(2)函数的定义域为 $\left( {-1, + \infty }\right)$ ,在 $\left( {-1, + \infty }\right)$ 内可导,且

$$
{y}^{\prime } = 1 - \frac{1}{1 + x},\;{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{1}{{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{2}}\left( {x >  - 1}\right) .
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ 得驻点 $x = 0$ . 由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 1 > 0$ 知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ 为极小值.

(3) ${y}^{\prime } =  - 4{x}^{3} + {4x} =  - {4x}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) ,{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - {12}{x}^{2} + 4$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ 得驻点 ${x}_{1} =  - 1,{x}_{2} = 1,{x}_{3} = 0$ .

由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x =  - 1} =  - 8 < 0$ 知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 1} = 1$ 为极大值,由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 1} =  - 8 < 0$ 知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = 1$ 为极大值,由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 4 > 0$ 知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ 为极小值.

(4)函数的定义域为 $( - \infty ,1\rbrack$ ,在 $\left( {-\infty , - 1}\right)$ 内可导,且

$$
{y}^{\prime } = 1 - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{1 - x}} = \frac{2\sqrt{1 - x} - 1}{2\sqrt{1 - x}},{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - \frac{1}{4} \cdot  \frac{1}{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{3/2}}.
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ 得驻点 $x = \frac{3}{4}$ ,由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = \frac{3}{4}} =  - 2 < 0$ 知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = \frac{3}{4}} = \frac{5}{4}$ 为极大值.

$$
\text{(5)}{y}^{\prime } = \frac{3\sqrt{4 + 5{x}^{2}} - \left( {1 + {3x}}\right)  \cdot  \frac{10x}{2\sqrt{4 + 5{x}^{2}}}}{4 + 5{x}^{2}} = \frac{{12} - {5x}}{{\left( 4 + 5{x}^{2}\right) }^{3/2}} = \frac{-5\left( {x - \frac{12}{5}}\right) }{{\left( 4 + 5{x}^{2}\right) }^{3/2}}\text{.}
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ 得驻点 $x = \frac{12}{5}$ .

当 $- \infty  < x < \frac{12}{5}$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } > 0$ ,因此函数在 $\left( {-\infty ,\frac{12}{5}}\right\rbrack$ 上单调增加; 当 $\frac{12}{5} < x <  + \infty$ 时 ${y}^{\prime } < 0$ ,因此函数在 $\left\lbrack  {\frac{12}{5}, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调减少,从而 $y\left( \frac{12}{5}\right)  = \frac{\sqrt{205}}{10}$ 为极大值.

(6) ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{\left( {{6x} + 4}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right)  - \left( {{2x} + 1}\right) \left( {3{x}^{2} + {4x} + 4}\right) }{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}} = \frac{-x\left( {x + 2}\right) }{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ 得驻点 ${x}_{1} =  - 2,{x}_{2} = 0$ .

当 $- \infty  < x <  - 2$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } < 0$ ,因此函数在 $( - \infty , - 2\rbrack$ 上单调减少; 当 $- 2 < x < 0$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } > 0$ ,因此函数在 $\left\lbrack  {-2,0}\right\rbrack$ 上单调增加; 当 $0 < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } < 0$ ,因此函数在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上单调减少. 从而可知 $y\left( {-2}\right)  = \frac{8}{3}$ 为极小值, $y\left( 0\right)  = 4$ 为极大值.

(7) ${y}^{\prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos x - {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin x = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\cos x - \sin x}\right) ,{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin x$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 ${x}_{k} = {2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{4},{x}^{\prime }{}_{k} = {2k\pi } + \frac{5}{4}\pi \left( {k = 0, \pm  1, \pm  2,\cdots }\right)$ .

由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = {2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{4}} =  - \sqrt{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{4}} < 0$ 知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = {2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{4}} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{2k\pi } + \frac{\pi }{4}}\left( {k = 0, \pm  1, \pm  2,\cdots }\right)$ 为极大值.

由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{{x}^{\prime } = {2k\pi } + \frac{5\pi }{4}} = \sqrt{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{2k\pi } + \frac{5\pi }{4}} > 0$ 知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = {2k\pi } + \frac{5\pi }{4}} = \frac{-\sqrt{2}}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{2k\pi } + \frac{5}{4}\pi }(k = 0, \pm  1$ , $\pm  2,\cdots )$ 为极小值.

(8) 函数的定义域为 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ ,在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内可导,且

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}\ln x}\right) }^{\prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}\ln x} \cdot  \frac{1 - \ln x}{{x}^{2}} = {x}^{\frac{1}{x} - 2}\left( {1 - \ln x}\right) ,
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = \mathrm{e}$ .

当 $0 < x < \mathrm{e}$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } > 0$ ,因此函数在 $(0,\mathrm{e}\rbrack$ 上单调增加；当 $\mathrm{e} < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } < 0$ ,因此函数在 $\lbrack \mathrm{e}, + \infty )$ 上单调减少,从而可知 $y\left( \mathrm{e}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}$ 为极大值.

(9) 当 $x \neq   - 1$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } =  - \frac{2}{3} \cdot  \frac{1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2/3}} < 0$ . 又 $x =  - 1$ 时函数有定义. 因此可知函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内单调减少,从而函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内无极值.

( 10 )由 ${y}^{\prime } = 1 + {\sec }^{2}x > 0$ 知所给函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内单调增加,从而函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内无极值.

2. 试证明：如果函数 $y = a{x}^{3} + b{x}^{2} + {cx} + d$ 满足条件 ${b}^{2} - {3ac} < 0$ ,那么这函数没有极值.

证 ${y}^{\prime } = {3a}{x}^{2} + {2bx} + c$ . 由 ${b}^{2} - {3ac} < 0$ 知 $a \neq  0,c \neq  0,{y}^{\prime }$ 是二次三项式,

$$
\Delta  = {\left( 2b\right) }^{2} - 4\left( {3a}\right)  \cdot  c = 4\left( {{b}^{2} - {3ac}}\right)  < 0.
$$

当 $a > 0$ 时, ${y}^{\prime }$ 的图像开口向上,且在 $x$ 轴上方,故 ${y}^{\prime } > 0$ ,从而所给函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内单调增加. 当 $a < 0$ 时, ${y}^{\prime }$ 的图像开口向下,且在 $x$ 轴下方,故 ${y}^{\prime } < 0$ ,从而所给函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内单调减少. 因此,只要条件 ${b}^{2} - {3ac} < 0$ 成立, 所给函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内单调,故函数在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内无极值.

3. 试问 $a$ 为何值时,函数 $f\left( x\right)  = a\sin x + \frac{1}{3}\sin {3x}$ 在 $x = \frac{\pi }{3}$ 处取得极值? 它是极大值还是极小值? 并求此极值.

解 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = a\cos x + \cos {3x}$ ,函数在 $x = \frac{\pi }{3}$ 处取得极值,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( \frac{\pi }{3}\right)  = 0$ ,即 $a\cos \frac{\pi }{3} +$ $\cos \pi  = 0$ ,故 $a = 2$ .

又 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  =  - 2\sin x - 3\sin {3x},{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \frac{\pi }{3}\right)  =  - 2\sin \frac{\pi }{3} - 3\sin \pi  =  - \sqrt{3} < 0$ ,因此 $f\left( \frac{\pi }{3}\right)  = 2\sin \frac{\pi }{3} + \frac{1}{3}\sin \pi  = \sqrt{3}$ 为极大值.

24. 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 处有 $n$ 阶导数,且 ${f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = \cdots  = {f}^{\left( n - 1\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 0$ , ${f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  \neq  0$ ,证明:

(1)当 $n$ 为奇数时, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 处不取得极值;

(2)当 $n$ 为偶数时, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 处取得极值,且当 ${f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  < 0$ 时, $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 为极大值,当 ${f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  > 0$ 时, $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 为极小值.

证 由含佩亚诺余项的 $n$ 阶泰勒公式及已知条件,得

$$
f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + \frac{{f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{n!}{\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n} + o\left( {\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n}\right) ,
$$

即 $f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = \frac{{f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{n!}{\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n} + o\left( {\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n}\right)$ ,由此式可知 $f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 某邻域内的符号由 $\frac{{f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{n!}{\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n}$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 某邻域内的符号决定.

(1) 当 $n$ 为奇数时, ${\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n}$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 两侧异号,所以 $\frac{{f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{n!}{\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n}$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 两侧异号,从而 $f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 两侧异号,故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 处不取得极值.

(2)当 $n$ 为偶数时,在 ${x}_{0}$ 两侧 ${\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n} > 0$ ,若 ${f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  < 0$ ,则 $\frac{{f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{n!}$ ${\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n} < 0$ ,从而 $f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  < 0$ ,即 $f\left( x\right)  < f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ ,故 $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 为极大值; 若 ${f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  > 0$ ,则 $\frac{{f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{n!}{\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{n} > 0$ ,从而 $f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  > 0$ ,即 $f\left( x\right)  > f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ ,故 $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 为极小值.

5. 试利用习题 4 的结论,讨论函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + 2\cos x$ 的极值.

解 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - 2\sin x,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - 2\cos x,{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} -$ ${\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + 2\sin x,{f}^{\left( 4\right) }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + 2\cos x$ ,故 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0,{f}^{\left( 4\right) }\left( 0\right)  = 4 > 0$ , 因此函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处有极小值,极小值为 4 .

26. 求下列函数的最大值、最小值：

(1) $y = 2{x}^{3} - 3{x}^{2}, - 1 \leq  x \leq  4$ ；

(2) $y = {x}^{4} - 8{x}^{2} + 2, - 1 \leq  x \leq  3$ ；

(3) $y = x + \sqrt{1 - x}, - 5 \leq  x \leq  1$ .

解 (1) 函数在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,4}\right\rbrack$ 上可导,且 ${y}^{\prime } = 6{x}^{2} - {6x} = {6x}\left( {x - 1}\right)$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 ${x}_{1} = 0,{x}_{2} = 1$ . 比较 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 1} =  - 5,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} =  - 1$ , ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 4} = {80}$ ,得函数的最大值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 4} = {80}$ ,最小值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 1} =  - 5$ .

(2)函数在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,3}\right\rbrack$ 上可导,且

$$
{y}^{\prime } = 4{x}^{3} - {16x} = {4x}\left( {x - 2}\right) \left( {x + 2}\right) .
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ 得驻点 ${x}_{1} =  - 2$ (舍去), ${x}_{2} = 0,{x}_{3} = 2$ .

比较 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 1} =  - 5,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 2,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 2} =  - {14},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 3} = {11}$ ,得函数的最大值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 3} = {11}$ ,最小值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 2} =  - {14}$ .

(3)函数在 $\lbrack  - 5,1)$ 上可导,且 ${y}^{\prime } = 1 - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{1 - x}} = \frac{2\sqrt{1 - x} - 1}{2\sqrt{1 - x}}$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = \frac{3}{4}$ . 比较 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 5} =  - 5 + \sqrt{6},{\left. y\right| }_{x = \frac{3}{4}} = \frac{5}{4},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = 1$ ,得函数的最大值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = \frac{3}{4}} = \frac{5}{4}$ ,最小值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 5} = \sqrt{6} - 5$ .

27. 问函数 $y = 2{x}^{3} - 6{x}^{2} - {18x} - 7\left( {1 \leq  x \leq  4}\right)$ 在何处取得最大值? 并求出它的最大值.

解 函数在 $\left\lbrack  {1,4}\right\rbrack$ 上可导,且 ${y}^{\prime } = 6{x}^{2} - {12x} - {18} = 6\left( {x + 1}\right) \left( {x - 3}\right)$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 ${x}_{1} =  - 1$ (舍去), ${x}_{2} = 3$ . 比较 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} =  - {29},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 3} =  - {61}$ , ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 4} =  - {47}$ ,得函数在 $x = 1$ 处取得最大值,且最大值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} =  - {29}$ .

8. 8. 问函数 $y = {x}^{2} - \frac{54}{x}\left( {x < 0}\right)$ 在何处取得最小值?

解 函数在 $\left( {-\infty ,0}\right)$ 内可导,且 ${y}^{\prime } = {2x} + \frac{54}{{x}^{2}} = \frac{2\left( {{x}^{3} + {27}}\right) }{{x}^{2}},{y}^{\prime \prime } = 2 - \frac{108}{{x}^{3}}$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x =  - 3$ . 由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x =  - 3} = 6 > 0$ 知 $x =  - 3$ 为极小值点. 又函数在 $\left( {-\infty ,0}\right)$ 内的驻点惟一,故极小值点就是最小值点,即 $x =  - 3$ 为最小值点,且最小值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 3} = {27}$ .

9. 问函数 $y = \frac{x}{{x}^{2} + 1}\left( {x \geq  0}\right)$ 在何处取得最大值?

解 函数在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上可导,且

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{{x}^{2} + 1 - x \cdot  {2x}}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}} = \frac{1 - {x}^{2}}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}},
$$

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{-{2x}\left( {3 - {x}^{2}}\right) }{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{3}}.
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x =  - 1$ (舍去), $x = 1$ . 由 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = \frac{-4}{8} =  - \frac{1}{2} < 0$ 知 $x = 1$ 为极大值点,又函数在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上的驻点惟一,故极大值点就是最大值点, 即 $x = 1$ 为最大值点,且最大值为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = \frac{1}{2}$ .

10. 某车间靠墙壁要盖一间长方形小屋,现有存砖只够砌 ${20}\mathrm{\;m}$ 长的墙壁. 问应围成怎样的长方形才能使这间小屋的面积最大?

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_120.jpg?x=595&y=188&w=381&h=243&r=0"/>

图 3-3

<!-- Media -->

解 如图 3-3,设这间小屋的宽为 $x$ ,长为 $y$ ,则小屋的面积为 $S = {xy}$ .

已知 ${2x} + y = {20}$ ,即 $y = {20} - {2x}$ . 故

$$
S = x\left( {{20} - {2x}}\right)  = {20x} - 2{x}^{2},x \in  \left( {0,{10}}\right) .
$$

${S}^{\prime } = {20} - {4x},{S}^{\prime \prime } =  - 4$ . 令 ${S}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = 5$ . 由 ${S}^{\prime \prime } < 0$ 知 $x = 5$ 为极大值点,又驻点惟一,故极大值点就是最大值点,即当宽为 $5\mathrm{\;m}$ ,长为 ${10}\mathrm{\;m}$ 时这间小屋的面积最大.

2011. 要造一圆柱形油罐,体积为 $V$ ,问底半径 $r$ 和高 $h$ 等于多少时,才能使表面积最小? 这时底直径与高的比是多少?

解 已知 $\pi {r}^{2}h = V$ ,即 $h = \frac{V}{\pi {r}^{2}}$ . 圆柱形油罐的表面积

$$
A = {2\pi }{r}^{2} + {2\pi rh} = {2\pi }{r}^{2} + {2\pi r} \cdot  \frac{V}{\pi {r}^{2}}
$$

$$
= {2\pi }{r}^{2} + \frac{2V}{r},\;r \in  \left( {0, + \infty }\right) .
$$

$$
{A}^{\prime } = {4\pi r} - \frac{2V}{{r}^{2}},\;{A}^{\prime \prime } = {4\pi } + \frac{4V}{{r}^{3}}.
$$

令 ${A}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 $r = \sqrt[3]{\frac{V}{2\pi }}$ . 由 ${A}^{\prime \prime }{}_{r = \sqrt{\frac{V}{2\pi }}} = {4\pi } + {8\pi } = {12\pi } > 0$ ,知 $r = \sqrt[3]{\frac{V}{2\pi }}$ 为极小值点, 又驻点惟一,故极小值点就是最小值点. 此时 $h = \frac{V}{\pi {r}^{2}} = 2\sqrt[3]{\frac{V}{2\pi }} = {2r}$ ,即 ${2r} : h = 1 : 1$ ,所以当底半径为 $r = \sqrt[3]{\frac{V}{2\pi }}$ 和高 $h = 2\sqrt[3]{\frac{V}{2\pi }}$ 时,才能使表面积最小. 这时底直径与高的比为 $1 : 1$ .

2012. 某地区防空洞的截面拟建成矩形加半圆 (图 3-4). 截面的面积为 $5{\mathrm{\;m}}^{2}$ . 问底宽 $x$ 为多少时才能使截面的周长最小, 从而使建造时所用的材料最省?

解 设截面的周长为 $l$ ,已知 $l = x + {2y} + \frac{\pi x}{2}$ 及 ${xy} + \frac{\pi }{2}{\left( \frac{x}{2}\right) }^{2} = 5$ ,即 $y = \frac{5}{x} - \frac{\pi x}{8}$ . 故

$$
l = x + \frac{\pi x}{4} + \frac{10}{x},\;x \in  \left( {0,\sqrt{\frac{40}{\pi }}}\right) .
$$

$$
{l}^{\prime } = 1 + \frac{\pi }{4} - \frac{10}{{x}^{2}},\;{l}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{20}{{x}^{3}}.
$$

令 ${l}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = \sqrt{\frac{40}{4 + \pi }}$ . 由 ${\left. {l}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = \sqrt{\frac{40}{4 + \pi }}} = \frac{20}{{\left( \frac{40}{4 + \pi }\right) }^{3/2}} > 0$ 知 $x = \sqrt{\frac{40}{4 + \pi }}$ 为极小值点,又驻点惟一,故极小值点就是最小值点. 所以当截面的底宽为 $x = \sqrt{\frac{40}{4 + \pi }}$ 时,才能使截面的周长最小, 从而使建造时所用的材料最省.

13. 设有质量为 $5\mathrm{\;{kg}}$ 的物体,置于水平面上,受力 $F$ 的作用而开始移动 (图 3-5). 设摩擦系数 $\mu  = {0.25}$ ,问力 $F$ 与水平线的交角 $\alpha$ 为多少时,才可使力 $F$ 的大小为最小.

解 如图 3-5,力 $F$ 的大小用 $\left| F\right|$ 表示,则由 $\left| F\right| \cos \alpha  = \left( {P - \left| F\right| \sin \alpha }\right) \mu$ 知

$$
\left| F\right|  = \frac{\mu P}{\cos \alpha  + \mu \sin \alpha },\;\alpha  \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{2}}\right) .
$$

设 $y = \cos \alpha  + \mu \sin \alpha ,\alpha  \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime } =  - \sin \alpha  + \mu \cos \alpha$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 ${\alpha }_{0} = \arctan \mu$ . 又 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{\alpha  = {\alpha }_{0}} =  - \cos {\alpha }_{0} - \mu \sin {\alpha }_{0} < 0$ ,所以驻点 ${\alpha }_{0}$ 为极大值点,又驻点惟一,因此 ${\alpha }_{0}$ 为函数 $y = y\left( \alpha \right)$ 的最大值点,这时, 即 $\alpha  = {\alpha }_{0} = \arctan \left( {0.25}\right)  \approx  {14}^{ \circ  }{2}^{\prime }$ 时,力 $F$ 的大小为最小.

1514. 有一杠杆,支点在它的一端. 在距支点 ${0.1}\mathrm{\;m}$ 处挂一质量为 ${49}\mathrm{\;{kg}}$ 的物体. 加力于杠杆的另一端使杠杆保持水平 (图 3-6). 如果杠杆的线密度为 $5\mathrm{\;{kg}}/\mathrm{m}$ ,求最省力的杆长?

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_121.jpg?x=187&y=1587&w=526&h=399&r=0"/>

图 3-5

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_121.jpg?x=889&y=1669&w=433&h=320&r=0"/>

图 3-6

<!-- Media -->

解 如图 3-6,设最省力的杆长为 $x\left( \mathrm{\;m}\right)$ ,则此时杠杆的重力为 $5\mathrm{\;g}x$ ,由力矩平衡公式

$$
x\left| F\right|  = {49g} \times  {0.1} + {5gx} \cdot  \frac{x}{2}\;\left( {x > 0}\right) ,
$$

知

$$
\left| F\right|  = \frac{4.9}{x}g + \frac{5}{2}{gx},\;{\left| F\right| }^{\prime } =  - \frac{4.9}{{x}^{2}}g + \frac{5}{2}g,
$$

$$
{\left| F\right| }^{\prime \prime } = \frac{9.8}{{x}^{3}}g.
$$

令 ${\left| F\right| }^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = {1.4}$ . 又 ${\left. {\left| F\right| }^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = {1.4}} = \frac{9.8}{{\left( {1.4}\right) }^{3}}g > 0$ ,故 $x = {1.4}$ 为极小值点,又驻点惟一,因此 $x = {1.4}$ 也是最小值点,即杆长为 ${1.4}\mathrm{\;m}$ 时最省力.

15. 从一块半径为 $R$ 的圆铁片上挖去一个扇形做成一个漏斗 (图 3-7). 问留下的扇形的中心角 $\varphi$ 取多大时,做成的漏斗的容积最大?

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_122.jpg?x=613&y=726&w=351&h=348&r=0"/>

图 3-7

<!-- Media -->

解 如图 3-7,设漏斗的高为 $h$ ,顶面的圆半径为 $r$ ,则漏斗的容积为 $V =$ $\frac{1}{3}\pi {r}^{2}h$ ,又

$$
{2\pi r} = {R\varphi },\;h = \sqrt{{R}^{2} - {r}^{2}}.
$$

故

$$
V = \frac{{R}^{3}}{{24}{\pi }^{2}}\sqrt{4{\pi }^{2}{\varphi }^{4} - {\varphi }^{6}}\;\left( {0 < \varphi  < {2\pi }}\right) ,
$$

$$
{V}^{\prime } = \frac{{R}^{3}}{{24}{\pi }^{2}} \cdot  \frac{{16}{\pi }^{2}{\varphi }^{3} - 6{\varphi }^{5}}{2\sqrt{4{\pi }^{2}{\varphi }^{4} - {\varphi }^{6}}} = \frac{{R}^{3}}{{24}{\pi }^{2}} \cdot  \frac{8{\pi }^{2}\varphi  - 3{\varphi }^{3}}{\sqrt{4{\pi }^{2} - {\varphi }^{2}}}.
$$

令 ${V}^{\prime } = 0$ 得 $\varphi  = \sqrt{\frac{8}{3}}\pi  = \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3}\pi$ . 当 $0 < \varphi  < \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3}\pi$ 时, ${V}^{\prime } > 0$ ,故 $V$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,\frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3}\pi }\right\rbrack$ 内单调增加; 当 $\frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3} < \varphi  < {2\pi }$ 时, ${V}^{\prime } < 0$ ,故 $V$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {\frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3}\pi ,{2\pi }}\right)$ 内单调减少. 因此 $\varphi  = \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3}\pi$ 为极大值点,又驻点惟一,从而 $\varphi  = \frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3}\pi$ 也是最大值点,即当 $\varphi$ 取 $\frac{2\sqrt{6}}{3}\pi$ 时,做成的漏斗的容积最大.

26 16. 某吊车的车身高为 ${1.5}\mathrm{\;m}$ ,吊臂长 ${15}\mathrm{\;m}$ . 现在要把一个 $6\mathrm{\;m}$ 宽、 $2\mathrm{\;m}$ 高的屋架,水平地吊到 $6\mathrm{\;m}$ 高的柱子上去 (图 3-8),问能否吊得上去?

解 如图 3-8,设吊臂对地面的倾角为 $\varphi$ ,屋架能够吊到最大的高度为 $h$ ,由

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_123.jpg?x=281&y=251&w=1039&h=513&r=0"/>

图 3-8

<!-- Media -->

${15}\sin \varphi  = h - {1.5} + 2 + 3\tan \varphi$ 知

$$
h = {15}\sin \varphi  - 3\tan \varphi  - \frac{1}{2},
$$

$$
{h}^{\prime } = {15}\cos \varphi  - \frac{3}{{\cos }^{2}\varphi },\;{h}^{\prime \prime } =  - {15}\sin \varphi  - \frac{6\sin \varphi }{{\cos }^{3}\varphi }.
$$

令 ${h}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 $\cos \varphi  = \sqrt[3]{\frac{1}{5}}$ ,即得惟一驻点 ${\varphi }_{0} = \arccos \sqrt[3]{\frac{1}{5}} \approx  {54}^{ \circ  }{13}^{\prime }$ . 又 ${\left. {h}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{\varphi  = {\varphi }_{0}} < 0$ ,

故 ${\varphi }_{0} \approx  {54}^{ \circ  }{13}^{\prime }$ 为极大值点也是最大值点. 即当 ${\varphi }_{0} \approx  {54}^{ \circ  }{13}^{\prime }$ 时, $h$ 达到最大值 ${h}_{0} =$ ${15}\sin {54}^{ \circ  }{13}^{\prime } - 3\tan {54}^{ \circ  }{13}^{\prime } - \frac{1}{2} \approx  {7.506}\mathrm{\;m}$ ,而柱子高只有 $6\mathrm{\;m}$ ,所以能吊得上去.

17. 一房地产公司有 50 套公寓要出租. 当月租金定为 4000 元时, 公寓会全部租出去. 当月租金每增加 200 元时, 就会多一套公寓租不出去. 而租出去的公寓平均每月需花费 400 元的维修费. 试问房租定为多少时可获得最大收入?

解 设每套月房租为 $x$ 元,则租不出去的房子套数为 $\frac{x - {4000}}{200} = \frac{x}{200} - {20}$ ,租出去的套数为 ${50} - \left( {\frac{x}{200} - {20}}\right)  = {70} - \frac{x}{200}$ ,租出的每套房子获利(x - 400)元. 故总利润为

$$
y = \left( {{70} - \frac{x}{200}}\right) \left( {x - {400}}\right)  =  - \frac{{x}^{2}}{200} + {72x} - {28000}.
$$

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - \frac{x}{100} + {72},\;{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{-1}{100}.
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = {7200}$ . 由 ${y}^{\prime \prime } < 0$ 知 $x = {7200}$ 为极大值点,又驻点惟一,这极大值点就是最大值点. 即当每套月房租定在 7200 元时, 可获得最大收入.

18. 已知制作一个背包的成本为 40 元,如果每一个背包的售出价为 $x$ 元,售出的背包数由

$$
n = \frac{a}{x - {40}} + b\left( {{80} - x}\right)
$$

给出,其中 $a,b$ 为正常数. 问什么样的售出价格能带来最大利润?

解 设利润函数为 $p\left( x\right)$ ,则

$$
p\left( x\right)  = \left( {x - {40}}\right) n = a + b\left( {x - {40}}\right) \left( {{80} - x}\right) .
$$

$$
{p}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = b\left( {{120} - {2x}}\right) ,
$$

令 ${p}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,得 $x = {60}$ (元). 由 ${p}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  =  - {2b} < 0$ 知 $x = {60}$ 为极大值点,又驻点惟一, 这极大值点就是最大值点, 即售出价格定在 60 元时能带来最大利润.

### 习题 3-6 函数图形的描绘



描绘下列函数的图形:

1. $y = \frac{1}{5}\left( {{x}^{4} - 6{x}^{2} + {8x} + 7}\right)$ ; 2. $y = \frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}$ ;

3. $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}}$ ; 4. $y = {x}^{2} + \frac{1}{x}$ ;

5. $y = \frac{\cos x}{\cos {2x}}$ .

解 1. (1) 所给函数 $y = \frac{1}{5}\left( {{x}^{4} - 6{x}^{2} + {8x} + 7}\right)$ 的定义域为 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ . 而 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{5}\left( {4{x}^{3} - {12x} + 8}\right)  = \frac{4}{5}\left( {x + 2}\right) {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2},{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{4}{5}\left( {3{x}^{2} - 3}\right)  = \frac{12}{5}\left( {x + 1}\right) \left( {x - 1}\right) .$

(2)令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 $x =  - 2,x = 1$ ,令 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = 0$ ,得 $x = 1,x =  - 1$ . 根据上述点将区间 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 分成下列四个部分区间:

$$
( - \infty , - 2\rbrack ,\left\lbrack  {-2, - 1}\right\rbrack  ,\left\lbrack  {-1,1}\right\rbrack  ,\lbrack 1, + \infty )\text{.}
$$

(3)在各部分区间内 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 及 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 的符号、相应曲线弧的升降及凹凸以及拐点等如下表:

<!-- Media -->

<table><tr><td>$x$</td><td>$\left( {-\infty , - 2}\right)$</td><td>-2</td><td>(-2,-1)</td><td>-1</td><td>(-1,1)</td><td>1</td><td>$\left( {1, + \infty }\right)$</td></tr><tr><td>${y}^{\prime }$</td><td>-</td><td>0</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>0</td><td>+</td></tr><tr><td>${y}^{\prime \prime }$</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>0</td><td>-</td><td>0</td><td>+</td></tr><tr><td>$y = f\left( x\right)$ 的图形</td><td> <img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_124.jpg?x=308&y=1912&w=82&h=79&r=0"/> </td><td>$\left( {-2, - \frac{17}{5}}\right)$</td><td> <img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_124.jpg?x=708&y=1914&w=87&h=77&r=0"/> </td><td>拐点</td><td> <img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_124.jpg?x=1036&y=1914&w=81&h=78&r=0"/> </td><td>拐点</td><td> <img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_124.jpg?x=1313&y=1914&w=89&h=79&r=0"/> </td></tr></table>

<!-- Media -->

(4) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   - \infty }}f\left( x\right)  =  + \infty$ ,图形没有铅直、水平、斜渐近线.

(5) 由 $f\left( {-2}\right)  =  - \frac{17}{5},f\left( {-1}\right)  =  - \frac{6}{5},f\left( 1\right)  = 2,f\left( 0\right)  = \frac{7}{5}$ 得图形上的四个点

$\left( {-2, - \frac{17}{5}}\right) ,\left( {-1, - \frac{6}{5}}\right) ,\left( {1,2}\right) ,\left( {0,\frac{7}{5}}\right)$ .

(6)作图如图 3-9.

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_125.jpg?x=491&y=371&w=610&h=387&r=0"/>

图 3-9

<!-- Media -->

2. (1) 所给函数 $y = \frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}$ 的定义域为 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ . 由于 $y = \frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}$ 是奇函数, 它的图形关于原点对称,因此可以只讨论 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上该函数的图形,求出

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{1 + {x}^{2} - x \cdot  {2x}}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}} = \frac{1 - {x}^{2}}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}},
$$

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{{2x}\left( {{x}^{2} - 3}\right) }{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{3}}.
$$

(2)在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 内, ${y}^{\prime }$ 的零点为 $x = 1$ , ${y}^{\prime \prime }$ 的零点为 $x = \sqrt{3}$ ,根据这两点把区间 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 分成三个区间: $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack  ,\left\lbrack  {1,\sqrt{3}}\right\rbrack  ,\left\lbrack  {\sqrt{3}, + \infty }\right)$ .

(3)在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 内的各部分区间内 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 及 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 的符号、相应曲线弧的升降及凹凸以及拐点等如下表:

(5) 由 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0,f\left( 1\right)  = \frac{1}{2},f\left( \sqrt{3}\right)  = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}$ 得在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 内图形上的点(0,0), $\left( {1,\frac{1}{2}}\right) ,\left( {\sqrt{3},\frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}}\right)$ .

5. (1) 所给函数 $y = \frac{\cos x}{\cos {2x}}$ 的定义域 $D = \left\{  {x\left| {\;x \neq  \frac{n\pi }{2} + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right. ,x \in  \mathbf{R},n = 0, \pm  1, \pm  2,\cdots }\right\}$ .

由于 $y = \frac{\cos x}{\cos {2x}}$ 是偶函数,它的图形关于 $y$ 轴对称,且由于函数是以 ${2\pi }$ 为周期的函数,因此可以只讨论 $\left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack$ 部分的图形. 求出

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{-\sin x\cos {2x} + \cos x \cdot  2\sin {2x}}{{\cos }^{2}\left( {2x}\right) } = \frac{\sin x\left( {3 - 2{\sin }^{2}x}\right) }{{\cos }^{2}\left( {2x}\right) },
$$

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{\cos x\left( {3 + {12}{\sin }^{2}x - 4{\sin }^{4}x}\right) }{{\cos }^{3}\left( {2x}\right) }.
$$

(2)令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 $x = 0,x = \pi$ ；令 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = 0$ ,得 $x = \frac{\pi }{2}$ ；又函数在点 $x = \frac{\pi }{4}$ 及 $x = \frac{3}{4}\pi$ 处无定义. 根据这些点把区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack$ 分成四个部分区间: $\left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{4}}\right) ,\left( {\frac{\pi }{4},\frac{\pi }{2}}\right\rbrack$ , $\left\lbrack  {\frac{\pi }{2},\frac{3\pi }{4}}\right) ,\left( {\frac{3\pi }{4},\pi }\right\rbrack$ .

(3) 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack$ 内的各部分区间内 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 及 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 的符号,相应曲线弧的升降及凹凸以及拐点等如下表:

### 习题 3-7 曲率

2. 1. 求椭圆 $4{x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = 4$ 在点(0,2)处的曲率.

解 由 ${8x} + {2y}{y}^{\prime } = 0$ 知 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{-{4x}}{y},{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{-{16}}{{y}^{3}}$ . 故 ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 0} =  - 2$ ,故在点

(0,2)处的曲率为

$$
K = {\left. \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}\right| }_{\left( 0,2\right) } = 2.
$$

2. 求曲线 $y = \ln \sec x$ 在点(x,y)处的曲率及曲率半径.

解 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{\sec x} \cdot  \sec x\tan x = \tan x,{y}^{\prime \prime } = {\sec }^{2}x$ . 故曲率

$$
K = \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{3/2}} = \frac{{\sec }^{2}x}{{\left( 1 + {\tan }^{2}x\right) }^{3/2}} = \left| {\cos x}\right| ,
$$

曲率半径 $\rho  = \frac{1}{K} = \left| {\sec x}\right|$ .

3. 求抛物线 $y = {x}^{2} - {4x} + 3$ 在其顶点处的曲率及曲率半径.

解 抛物线的顶点为 $\left( {2, - 1}\right) ,{y}^{\prime } = {2x} - 4,{y}^{\prime \prime } = 2$ .

抛物线 $y = {x}^{2} - {4x} + 3$ 在其顶点处的曲率

$$
K = {\left. \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{3/2}}\right| }_{\left( 2, - 1\right) } = 2,
$$

曲率半径 $\rho  = \frac{1}{K} = \frac{1}{2}$ .

24. 求曲线 $x = a{\cos }^{3}t,y = a{\sin }^{3}t$ 在 $t = {t}_{0}$ 处的曲率.

解 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t}}{\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t}} = \frac{{3a}{\sin }^{2}t\cos t}{-{3a}{\cos }^{2}t\sin t} =  - \tan t$ ,

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = \frac{\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right) }{\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t}} = \frac{-{\sec }^{2}t}{-{3a}{\cos }^{2}t\sin t} = \frac{1}{{3a}\sin t{\cos }^{4}t}.
$$

故曲线在 $t = {t}_{0}$ 处的曲率为

$$
K = {\left. \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{3/2}}\right| }_{t = {t}_{0}} = {\left. \frac{\left| \frac{1}{{3a}\sin t{\cos }^{4}t}\right| }{{\left\lbrack  1 + {\left( -\tan t\right) }^{2}\right\rbrack  }^{3/2}}\right| }_{t = {t}_{0}} = \frac{2}{\left| 3a\sin \left( 2{t}_{0}\right) \right| }.
$$

5. 对数曲线 $y = \ln x$ 上哪一点处的曲率半径最小? 求出该点处的曲率半径.

解 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{x},{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}$ . 曲线的曲率

$$
K = \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}} = \frac{\left| -\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\right| }{{\left\lbrack  1 + {\left( \frac{1}{x}\right) }^{2}\right\rbrack  }^{3/2}} = \frac{x}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{3/2}},
$$

曲率半径为

$$
\rho  = \frac{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{x}.
$$

又 ${\rho }^{\prime } = \frac{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}}\left( {2{x}^{2} - 1}\right) }{{x}^{2}}$ . 令 ${\rho }^{\prime } = 0$ 得驻点 ${x}_{1} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},{x}_{2} =  - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}$ (舍去).

当 $0 < x < \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}$ 时, ${\rho }^{\prime } < 0$ ,即 $\rho$ 在 $\left( {0,\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}}\right)$ 上单调减少; 当 $\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2} < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${\rho }^{\prime } > 0$ ,即 $\rho$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调增加. 因此在 $x = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}$ 处 $\rho$ 取得极小值; 驻点惟一,从而 $\rho$ 的极小值就是最小值, 因此最小的曲率半径为

$$
{\left. \rho \right| }_{x = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}} = \frac{{\left( 1 + \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}} = \frac{3\sqrt{3}}{2}.
$$

6. 证明曲线 $y = a\operatorname{ch}\frac{x}{a}$ 在点(x,y)处的曲率半径为 $\frac{{y}^{2}}{a}$ .

证 ${y}^{\prime } = \operatorname{sh}\frac{x}{a},{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{1}{a}\operatorname{ch}\frac{x}{a}$ ,曲线在点(x,y)处的曲率为

$$
K = \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}} = \frac{\left| \frac{1}{a}\operatorname{ch}\frac{x}{a}\right| }{{\left( 1 + {\operatorname{sh}}^{2}\frac{x}{a}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}} = \frac{1}{a{\operatorname{ch}}^{2}\frac{x}{a}},
$$

曲率半径为 $\rho  = \frac{1}{K} = a{\operatorname{ch}}^{2}\frac{x}{a} = \frac{{y}^{2}}{a}$ .

2. 7. 一飞机沿抛物线路径 $y = \frac{{x}^{2}}{10000}$ ( $y$ 轴铅直向上,单位为 $\mathrm{m}$ ) 作俯冲飞行. 在坐标原点 $O$ 处飞机的速度为 $v = {200}\mathrm{\;m}/\mathrm{s}$ ,飞行员体重 $G = {70}\mathrm{\;{kg}}$ . 求飞机俯冲至最低点即原点 $O$ 处时座椅对飞行员的反力.

解 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{2x}{10000} = \frac{x}{5000},{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{1}{5000}$ .

抛物线在坐标原点的曲率半径为

$$
\rho  = {\left. \frac{1}{K}\right| }_{x = 0} = {\left. \frac{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }\right| }_{x = 0} = {5000}.
$$

所以向心力为 ${F}_{1} = \frac{m{v}^{2}}{\rho } = \frac{{70} \times  {200}^{2}}{5000} = {560}\left( \mathrm{\;N}\right)$ .

座椅对飞行员的反力 $F$ 等于飞行员的离心力及飞行员本身的重量对座椅的压力之和, 因此

$$
F = {mg} + {F}_{1} = {70} \times  {9.8} + {560} = {1246}\left( \mathrm{\;N}\right) .
$$

8. 汽车连同载重共 $5\mathrm{t}$ ,在抛物线拱桥上行驶,速度为 ${21.6}\mathrm{\;{km}}/\mathrm{h}$ ,桥的跨度为 ${10}\mathrm{\;m}$ ,拱的矢高为 ${0.25}\mathrm{\;m}$ (图 3-14). 求汽车越过桥顶时对桥的压力. 解 设立直角坐标系如图 3-14 所示, 设抛物线拱桥方程为

$$
y = a{x}^{2}\text{.}
$$

由于抛物线过点(5,0.25),代入方程得 $a = {\left. \frac{y}{{x}^{2}}\right| }_{\left( 5,{0.25}\right) } = \frac{0.25}{25} = {0.01}$ .

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {2ax},\;{y}^{\prime \prime } = {2a},
$$

因此

$$
{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = {0.02},
$$

$$
{\left. \rho \right| }_{x = 0} = {\left. \frac{1}{K}\right| }_{x = 0} = {\left. \frac{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }\right| }_{x = 0} = {50}.
$$

汽车越过桥顶点时对桥的压力为

$$
F = {mg} - \frac{m{v}^{2}}{\rho } = 5 \times  {10}^{3} \times  {9.8} - \frac{5 \times  {10}^{3} \times  {\left( \frac{{21.6} \times  {10}^{3}}{3600}\right) }^{2}}{50} = {45400}\left( \mathrm{\;N}\right) .
$$

2 * 9. 求曲线 $y = \ln x$ 在与 $x$ 轴交点处的曲率圆方程. 解 解方程组 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} y = \ln x, \\  y = 0, \end{array}\right.$ 得曲线与 $x$ 轴的交点为(1,0).

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{x},{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\text{,故}{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 1} =  - 1\text{.}
$$

设曲线在点(1,0)处的曲率中心为 $\left( {\alpha ,\beta }\right)$ ,则

$$
\alpha  = {\left\lbrack  x - \frac{{y}^{\prime }\left( {1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\right) }{{y}^{\prime \prime }}\right\rbrack  }_{\left( 1,0\right) } = 1 - \frac{1 \cdot  \left( {1 + {1}^{2}}\right) }{-1} = 3,
$$

$$
\beta  = {\left\lbrack  y + \frac{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}{{y}^{\prime \prime }}\right\rbrack  }_{\left( 1,0\right) } = 0 + \frac{1 + {1}^{2}}{-1} =  - 2.
$$

曲率半径

$$
\rho  = {\left. \frac{1}{K}\right| }_{x = 1} = {\left. \frac{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }\right| }_{x = 1} = \frac{{\left( 1 + {1}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{1} = \sqrt{8},
$$

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_131.jpg?x=314&y=627&w=950&h=256&r=0"/>

图 3-14

<!-- Media -->

因此所求的曲率圆方程为 ${\left( \xi  - 3\right) }^{2} + {\left( \eta  + 2\right) }^{2} = 8$ .

9° 10. 求曲线 $y = \tan x$ 在点 $\left( {\frac{\pi }{4},1}\right)$ 处的曲率圆方程.

解 ${y}^{\prime } = {\sec }^{2}x,{y}^{\prime \prime } = 2{\sec }^{2}x\tan x$ ,故 ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = \frac{\pi }{4}} = 2,{\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = \frac{\pi }{4}} = 4$ .

设曲线在点 $\left( {\frac{\pi }{4},1}\right)$ 处的曲率中心的坐标为 $\left( {\alpha ,\beta }\right)$ ,则

$$
\alpha  = {\left\lbrack  x - \frac{{y}^{\prime }\left( {1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\right) }{{y}^{\prime \prime }}\right\rbrack  }_{\left( \frac{\pi }{4},1\right) } = \frac{\pi }{4} - \frac{2\left( {1 + 4}\right) }{4} = \frac{\pi  - {10}}{4},
$$

$$
\beta  = {\left\lbrack  y + \frac{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}{{y}^{\prime \prime }}\right\rbrack  }_{\left( \frac{\pi }{4},1\right) } = 1 + \frac{1 + 4}{4} = \frac{9}{4}.
$$

曲率半径

$$
\rho  = {\left. \frac{1}{K}\right| }_{x = \frac{\pi }{4}} = {\left. \frac{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }\right| }_{x = \frac{\pi }{4}} = \frac{{5}^{\frac{3}{2}}}{4},
$$

因此所求的曲率圆方程为 ${\left( \xi  - \frac{\pi  - {10}}{4}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \eta  - \frac{9}{4}\right) }^{2} = \frac{125}{16}$ .

9° 11. 求抛物线 ${y}^{2} = {2px}$ 的渐屈线方程.

解 由 ${2y}{y}^{\prime } = {2p}$ ,及 ${y}^{\prime 2} + y{y}^{\prime \prime } = 0$ 知 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{p}{y},{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - \frac{{p}^{2}}{{y}^{3}}$ .

故抛物线 ${y}^{2} = {2px}$ 的渐屈线方程为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \alpha  = x - \frac{{y}^{\prime }\left( {1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\right) }{{y}^{\prime \prime }} = x - \frac{\frac{p}{y}\left\lbrack  {1 + {\left( \frac{p}{y}\right) }^{2}}\right\rbrack  }{-\frac{{p}^{2}}{{y}^{3}}} = \frac{3{y}^{2}}{2p} + p, \\  \beta  = y + \frac{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}{{y}^{\prime \prime }} = y + \frac{1 + {\left( \frac{p}{y}\right) }^{2}}{-\frac{{p}^{2}}{{y}^{3}}} =  - \frac{{y}^{3}}{{p}^{2}}, \end{array}\right.
$$

其中 $y$ 为参数,消去参数 $y$ 得渐屈线方程为

$$
{27p}{\beta }^{2} = 8{\left( \alpha  - p\right) }^{3}.
$$

### 习题 3-8 方程的近似解



121. 试证明方程 ${x}^{3} - 3{x}^{2} + {6x} - 1 = 0$ 在区间(0,1)内有惟一的实根,并用二分法求这个根的近似值, 使误差不超过 0.01 .

解 设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} - 3{x}^{2} + {6x} - 1,f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( 0\right)  =  - 1 < 0$ , $f\left( 1\right)  = 3 > 0$ . 由零点定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {0,1}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,即方程 ${x}^{3} - 3{x}^{2} + {6x}$ $- 1 = 0$ 在(0,1)内至少有一个实根.

又 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 3{x}^{2} - {6x} + 6 = 3{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + 3 > 0$ ,故函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上单调增加,从而方程 $f\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,即 ${x}^{3} - 3{x}^{2} + {6x} - 1 = 0$ 在(0,1)内至多有一个实根. 因此方程 ${x}^{3} -$ $3{x}^{2} + {6x} - 1 = 0$ 在(0,1)内有惟一的实根.

现用二分法求这个实根的近似值:

<!-- Media -->

<table><tr><td>$n$</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>3</td><td>4</td><td>5</td><td>6</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>9</td><td>10</td><td>11</td></tr><tr><td>${a}_{n}$</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0</td><td>0.125</td><td>0.125</td><td>0.157</td><td>0.173</td><td>0.180</td><td>0.180</td><td>0.182</td><td>0.183</td></tr><tr><td>${b}_{n}$</td><td>1</td><td>0.5</td><td>0.25</td><td>0.25</td><td>0.188</td><td>0.188</td><td>0.188</td><td>0.188</td><td>0.184</td><td>0.184</td><td>0.184</td></tr><tr><td>中点 ${x}_{n}$</td><td>0.5</td><td>0.25</td><td>0.125</td><td>0.188</td><td>0.157</td><td>0.173</td><td>0.180</td><td>0.184</td><td>0.182</td><td>0.183</td><td>0.183</td></tr><tr><td>$f\left( {x}_{n}\right)$ 的符号</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>-</td><td>+</td><td>-</td><td>-</td><td>-</td><td>+</td><td>-</td><td>+</td><td>+</td></tr></table>

<!-- Media -->

故使误差不超过 0.01 的根的近似值为 $\xi  = {0.183}$ .

2. 试证明方程 ${x}^{5} + {5x} + 1 = 0$ 在区间(-1,0)内有惟一的实根,并用切线法求这个根的近似值, 使误差不超过 0.01 .

解 设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{5} + {5x} + 1.f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,0}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( {-1}\right)  =  - 5 < 0,f\left( 0\right)  =$ $1 > 0$ . 由零点定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {-1,0}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ 即方程 ${x}^{5} + {5x} + 1 = 0$ 在区间 (-1,0)内至少有一实根.

又 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 5{x}^{4} + 5 > 0$ ,故函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,0}\right\rbrack$ 上单调增加,从而方程 $f\left( x\right)  = 0$ 即 ${x}^{5} + {5x} + 1 = 0$ 在(-1,0)内至多有一个实根,因此方程 ${x}^{5} + {5x} + 1 = 0$ 在区间(-1,0)内有惟一的实根.

现用切线法求这个实根的近似值:

由 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {20}{x}^{3},{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {-1}\right)  =  - {20} < 0$ 知取 ${x}_{0} =  - 1$ ,利用递推公式 ${x}_{n} = {x}_{n - 1} -$ $\frac{f\left( {x}_{n - 1}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{n - 1}\right) }$ ,得:

$$
{x}_{1} = {x}_{0} - \frac{f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) } =  - 1 - \frac{f\left( {-1}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {-1}\right) } =  - {0.5},
$$

$$
{x}_{2} = {x}_{1} - \frac{f\left( {x}_{1}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{1}\right) } =  - {0.5} - \frac{f\left( {-{0.5}}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {-{0.5}}\right) } \approx   - {0.21},
$$

$$
{x}_{3} = {x}_{2} - \frac{f\left( {x}_{2}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{2}\right) } =  - {0.21} - \frac{f\left( {-{0.21}}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {-{0.21}}\right) } \approx   - {0.20},
$$

$$
{x}_{4} = {x}_{3} - \frac{f\left( {x}_{3}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{3}\right) } =  - {0.20} - \frac{f\left( {-{0.20}}\right) }{{f}^{\prime }\left( {-{0.20}}\right) } \approx   - {0.20}.
$$

故使误差不超过 0.01 的根的近似值为 $\xi  =  - {0.20}$ .

3. 用割线法求方程 ${x}^{3} + {3x} - 1 = 0$ 的近似根,使误差不超过 0.01 .

解 设 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} + {3x} - 1,f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( 0\right)  =  - 1 < 0,f\left( 1\right)  = 3 > 0$ ,由零点定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {0,1}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ; 又 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 3{x}^{2} + 3 > 0$ ,故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上单调增加,从而方程 $f\left( x\right)  = 0$ 在(0,1)内有惟一实根.

现用割线法求这个根的近似值:

由 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {6x},{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 1\right)  = 6 > 0$ 知取 ${x}_{0} = 1$ . 又取 ${x}_{1} = {0.8}$ ,利用递推公式 ${x}_{n + 1} =$ ${x}_{n} - \frac{{x}_{n} - {x}_{n - 1}}{f\left( {x}_{n}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{n - 1}\right) } \cdot  f\left( {x}_{n}\right)$ ,得:

$$
{x}_{2} = {x}_{1} - \frac{{x}_{1} - {x}_{0}}{f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) } \cdot  f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = {0.8} - \frac{{0.8} - 1}{f\left( {0.8}\right)  - f\left( 1\right) } \cdot  f\left( {0.8}\right)
$$

$$
\approx  {0.449}\text{,}
$$

$$
{x}_{3} = {x}_{2} - \frac{{x}_{2} - {x}_{1}}{f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{1}\right) } \cdot  f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = {0.449} - \frac{{0.449} - {0.8}}{f\left( {0.449}\right)  - f\left( {0.8}\right) } \cdot  f\left( {0.449}\right)
$$

$$
\approx  {0.345}\text{,}
$$

$$
{x}_{4} = {x}_{3} - \frac{{x}_{3} - {x}_{2}}{f\left( {x}_{3}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{2}\right) } \cdot  f\left( {x}_{3}\right)  = {0.345} - \frac{{0.345} - {0.449}}{f\left( {0.345}\right)  - f\left( {0.449}\right) } \cdot  f({0.345} \tag{0.345}
$$

$$
\approx  {0.323}\text{,}
$$

$$
{x}_{5} = {x}_{4} - \frac{{x}_{4} - {x}_{3}}{f\left( {x}_{4}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{3}\right) } \cdot  f\left( {x}_{4}\right)  = {0.323} - \frac{{0.323} - {0.345}}{f\left( {0.323}\right)  - f\left( {0.345}\right) } \cdot  f\left( {0.323}\right)
$$

$$
\approx  {0.322}\text{.}
$$

至此,计算无需再继续,因 ${x}_{4}$ 与 ${x}_{5}$ 的前两位小数相同,故以 0.32 作为根的近似值, 其误差小于 0.01 .

24. 求方程 $x\lg x = 1$ 的近似根,使误差不超过 0.01 .

解 设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = x\lg x - 1.f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {1,3}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且

$$
f\left( 1\right)  =  - 1 < 0,\;f\left( 3\right)  = 3\lg 3 - 1 > 0,
$$

由零点定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {1,3}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,即方程 $x\lg x = 1$ 在区间(1,3)内至少有一实根.

又 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \lg x + x \cdot  \frac{1}{x\ln {10}} = \lg x + \frac{1}{\ln {10}} > 0\left( {x \geq  1}\right)$ ,故函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {1,3}\right\rbrack$ 上单调增加,从而方程 $f\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,即 $x\lg x = 1$ 在(1,3)内至多有一个实根,因此方程 $x\lg x = 1$ 在 (1,3)内有惟一的实根.

现用二分法求这个根的近似值:

<!-- Media -->

<table><tr><td>$n$</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>3</td><td>4</td><td>5</td><td>6</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>9</td></tr><tr><td>${a}_{n}$</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>2.50</td><td>2.50</td><td>2.50</td><td>2.50</td><td>2.50</td><td>2.50</td><td>2.50</td></tr><tr><td>${b}_{n}$</td><td>3</td><td>3</td><td>3</td><td>2.75</td><td>2.63</td><td>2.57</td><td>2.53</td><td>2. 52</td><td>2. 51</td></tr><tr><td>中点 ${x}_{n}$</td><td>2</td><td>2.50</td><td>2.75</td><td>2.63</td><td>2.57</td><td>2.53</td><td>2.52</td><td>2.51</td><td>2.51</td></tr><tr><td>$f\left( {x}_{n}\right)$ 的符号</td><td>-</td><td>-</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>+</td><td>+</td></tr></table>

<!-- Media -->

故误差不超过 0.01 的根的近似值为 $\xi  = {2.51}$ .

### 总习题三

21. 填空：

设常数 $k > 0$ ,函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \ln x - \frac{x}{\mathrm{e}} + k$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内零点的个数为_____.

解 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{\mathrm{e}} = \frac{\mathrm{e} - x}{x\mathrm{e}}$ ,令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = \mathrm{e}$ .

当 $0 < x < \mathrm{e}$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,故函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $(0,\mathrm{e}\rbrack$ 上单调增加；当 $\mathrm{e} < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,故函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack \mathrm{e}, + \infty )$ 上单调减少. 从而 $x = \mathrm{e}$ 为函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极大值点. 由于驻点惟一,极大值也是最大值且最大值 $f\left( \mathrm{e}\right)  = k > 0$ . 又

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  =  - \infty ,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  =  - \infty ,
$$

故曲线 $y = \ln x - \frac{x}{\mathrm{e}} + k$ 与 $x$ 轴有两个交点,因此函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \ln x - \frac{x}{\mathrm{e}} + k$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内的零点的个数为 2 .

2. 以下两题中给出了四个结论, 从中选出一个正确的结论:

(1) 设在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) ,{f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right) ,f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( 0\right)$ 或 $f\left( 0\right)  - f\left( 1\right)$ 几个数的大小顺序为 (   ).

(A) ${f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  > f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( 0\right)$ (B) ${f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  > f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$

(C) $f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ (D) ${f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  > f\left( 0\right)  - f\left( 1\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$

(2)设 ${f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 0,{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  > 0$ ,则 (   ).

(A) ${f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 是 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 的极大值 (B) $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极大值

(C) $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极小值 (D) $\left( {{x}_{0},f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }\right)$ 是曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的拐点

解 (1) 由拉格朗日中值定理知 $f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)$ ,其中 $\xi  \in  \left( {0,1}\right)$ . 由于 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0,{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 单调增加,故 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)$ . 即

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  < f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right) .
$$

因此应填 (B).

(2)解法一 取 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3},{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 3{x}^{2},{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {6x},{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = 6 > 0,{x}_{0} = 0$ ,符合题意,但明显排除 $\left( \mathrm{A}\right) \text{、}\left( \mathrm{B}\right) \text{、}\left( \mathrm{C}\right)$ . 因此应填(D).

解法二 由已知条件及 ${f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {x}_{0}}}\frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  - {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{x - {x}_{0}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {x}_{0}}}\frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right) }{x - {x}_{0}} > 0$ 知,在 ${x}_{0}$ 某邻域内,当 $x < {x}_{0}$ 时, ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ; 当 $x > {x}_{0}$ 时, ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,所以 $\left( {{x}_{0},f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }\right)$ 是曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的拐点.

由此可知,在 ${x}_{0}$ 的某去心邻域内有 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 0$ ,所以 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 的某邻域内是单调增加的,从而 $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 不是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极值. 再由已知条件及极值的第二充分判别法知, ${f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 是 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 的极小值. 综上所述,本题只能选 (D).

23. 列举一个函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 满足: $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(a,b)内除某一点外处处可导, 但在(a,b)内不存在点 $\xi$ ,使 $f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left( {b - a}\right)$ .

解 取 $f\left( x\right)  = \left| x\right|$ ,区间为 $\left\lbrack  {-1,1}\right\rbrack$ . 函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(-1,1)内除点 $x = 0$ 外处处可导,但 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(-1,1)内不存在点 $\xi$ ,使 ${f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,即不存在 $\xi  \in$ (-1,1),使 $f\left( 1\right)  - f\left( {-1}\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left\lbrack  {1 - \left( {-1}\right) }\right\rbrack$ .

24. 设 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = k$ ,求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {x + a}\right)  - f\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$ .

解 由拉格朗日中值定理知

$$
f\left( {x + a}\right)  - f\left( x\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) a,
$$

$\xi$ 介于 $x$ 与 $x + a$ 之间,当 $x \rightarrow  \infty$ 时, $\xi  \rightarrow  \infty$ . 故

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {x + a}\right)  - f\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{\xi  \rightarrow  \infty }}{f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) a = {ka}.
$$

5. 证明多项式 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} - {3x} + a$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上不可能有两个零点.

证 假设多项式 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} - {3x} + a$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上有两个零点,即存在 ${x}_{1},{x}_{2} \in  \left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ ,使 $f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = 0$ ,不妨设 ${x}_{1} < {x}_{2}$ .

函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {{x}_{1},{x}_{2}}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在 $\left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2}}\right)$ 内可导,由罗尔定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {{x}_{1},{x}_{2}}\right)  \subset  \left( {0,1}\right)$ ,使 ${f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,但 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 3{x}^{2} - 3$ 在(0,1)内恒不等于零,故多项式 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} - {3x} + a$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上不可能有两个零点.

26. 设 ${a}_{0} + \frac{{a}_{1}}{2} + \cdots  + \frac{{a}_{n}}{n + 1} = 0$ ,证明多项式 $f\left( x\right)  = {a}_{0} + {a}_{1}x + \cdots  + {a}_{n}{x}^{n}$ 在(0,1)内至少有一个零点.

证 取函数 $F\left( x\right)  = {a}_{0}x + \frac{{a}_{1}}{2}{x}^{2} + \cdots  + \frac{{a}_{n}}{n + 1}{x}^{n + 1}.F\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(0,1) 内可导,且 $F\left( 0\right)  = 0,F\left( 1\right)  = {a}_{0} + \frac{{a}_{1}}{2} + \cdots  + \frac{{a}_{n}}{n + 1} = 0$ ,由罗尔定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {0,1}\right)$ ,使 ${F}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,即多项式 $f\left( x\right)  = {F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {a}_{0} + {a}_{1}x + \cdots  + {a}_{n}{x}^{n}$ 在(0,1)内至少有一个零点.

27. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,a}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(0,a)内可导,且 $f\left( a\right)  = 0$ ,证明存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {0,a}\right)$ , 使 $f\left( \xi \right)  + \xi {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ .

证 取函数 $F\left( x\right)  = {xf}\left( x\right) .F\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,a}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(0,a)内可导,且 $F\left( 0\right)  = 0$ , $F\left( a\right)  = {af}\left( a\right)  = 0$ ,由罗尔定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {0,a}\right)$ ,使

$$
{F}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = {\left. {\left\lbrack  xf\left( x\right) \right\rbrack  }^{\prime }\right| }_{x = \xi } = f\left( \xi \right)  + \xi {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0.
$$

2. 8. 设 $0 < a < b$ ,函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(a,b)内可导,试利用柯西中值定理, 证明存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使

$$
f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  = \xi {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \ln \frac{b}{a}.
$$

证 取函数 $F\left( x\right)  = \ln x,f\left( x\right) \text{、}F\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(a,b)内可导,且 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  =$ $\frac{1}{x} \neq  0,x \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ . 由柯西中值定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使

$$
\frac{f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right) }{F\left( b\right)  - F\left( a\right) } = \frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) }{{F}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) }.
$$

即

$$
\frac{f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right) }{\ln b - \ln a} = \frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) }{\frac{1}{\xi }},
$$

亦即 $f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  = \xi {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \ln \frac{b}{a}$ .

9. 设 $f\left( x\right) ,g\left( x\right)$ 都是可导函数,且 $\left| {{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) }\right|  < {g}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ ,证明：当 $x > a$ 时,

$$
\left| {f\left( x\right)  - f\left( a\right) }\right|  < g\left( x\right)  - g\left( a\right) .
$$

分析 要证 $x > a$ 时, $\left| {f\left( x\right)  - f\left( a\right) }\right|  < g\left( x\right)  - g\left( a\right)$ ,即要证

$$
- \left\lbrack  {g\left( x\right)  - g\left( a\right) }\right\rbrack   < f\left( x\right)  - f\left( a\right)  < g\left( x\right)  - g\left( a\right) ,
$$

亦即要证

$$
f\left( x\right)  - g\left( x\right)  < f\left( a\right)  - g\left( a\right) ,
$$

$$
f\left( x\right)  + g\left( x\right)  > f\left( a\right)  + g\left( a\right) .
$$

证 取 $F\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - g\left( x\right) ,G\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + g\left( x\right) ,x \in  \left( {a, + \infty }\right)$ . 由 $\left| {{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) }\right|  <$ ${g}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 知

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - {g}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0,\;{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  + {g}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0,
$$

故 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - {g}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0,{G}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  + {g}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,即当 $x > a$ 时函数 $F\left( x\right)$ 单调减少, $G\left( x\right)$ 单调增加. 因此

$$
F\left( x\right)  < F\left( a\right) ,\;G\left( x\right)  > G\left( a\right) \left( {x > a}\right) .
$$

从而

$$
f\left( x\right)  - g\left( x\right)  < f\left( a\right)  - g\left( a\right) ,f\left( x\right)  + g\left( x\right)  > f\left( a\right)  + g\left( a\right) \;\left( {x > a}\right) .
$$

即当 $x > a$ 时, $\left| {f\left( x\right)  - f\left( a\right) }\right|  < g\left( x\right)  - g\left( a\right)$ .

210. 求下列极限:

(1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{x - {x}^{x}}{1 - x + \ln x}$ ;

(2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } - \frac{1}{x}}\right\rbrack$ ;

(3) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{\left( \frac{2}{\pi }\arctan x\right) }^{x}$ ;

(4) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left\lbrack  \left( {a}_{1}{}^{\frac{1}{x}} + {a}_{2}{}^{\frac{1}{x}} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}{}^{\frac{1}{x}}\right) /n\right\rbrack  }^{nx}\;\left( \right.$ 其中 $\left. {{a}_{1},{a}_{2},\cdots ,{a}_{n} > 0}\right)$ .

解 (1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{x - {x}^{x}}{1 - x + \ln x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{1 - {x}^{x}\left( {1 + \ln x}\right) }{-1 + \frac{1}{x}}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{{x}^{x}\ln x + {x}^{x} - 1}{x - 1} \cdot  x
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{{x}^{x}\left( {\ln x + 1}\right) \ln x + {x}^{x - 1} + {x}^{x}\left( {\ln x + 1}\right) }{1}
$$

$$
= 2\text{.}
$$

(2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } - \frac{1}{x}}\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x - \ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }{x\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x - \ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }{{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - \frac{1}{1 + x}}{2x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{2\left( {1 + x}\right) } = \frac{1}{2}\text{.}
$$

(3) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{\left( \frac{2}{\pi }\arctan x\right) }^{x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}x\ln \left( {\frac{2}{\pi }\arctan x}\right) }$ ,而

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}x\ln \left( {\frac{2}{\pi }\arctan x}\right)
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{\ln \frac{2}{\pi } + \ln \arctan x}{\frac{1}{x}}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left( {\frac{1}{\arctan x} \cdot  \frac{-{x}^{2}}{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right)  =  - \frac{2}{\pi },
$$

故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{\left( \frac{2}{\pi }\arctan x\right) }^{x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{2}{\pi }}$ .

(4) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left\lbrack  \left( {a}_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}} + {a}_{2}^{\frac{1}{x}} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}^{\frac{1}{x}}\right) /n\right\rbrack  }^{nx} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\left\lbrack  {\ln \left( {{a}_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}} + {a}_{2}^{\frac{1}{x}} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}^{\frac{1}{x}}}\right)  - \ln n}\right\rbrack  }$ ,

而

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{nx}\left\lbrack  {\ln \left( {{a}_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}} + {a}_{2}^{\frac{1}{x}} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}^{\frac{1}{x}}}\right)  - \ln n}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= n\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{\ln \left( {{a}_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}} + {a}_{2}^{\frac{1}{x}} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}^{\frac{1}{x}}}\right)  - \ln n}{\frac{1}{x}}
$$

$$
= n\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{\frac{1}{{a}_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}} + {a}_{2}^{\frac{1}{x}} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}^{\frac{1}{x}}}\left\lbrack  {{a}_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}}\ln {a}_{1} + {a}_{2}^{\frac{1}{x}}\ln {a}_{2} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}^{\frac{1}{x}}\ln {a}_{n}}\right\rbrack  {\left( \frac{1}{x}\right) }^{\prime }}{{\left( \frac{1}{x}\right) }^{\prime }}
$$

$$
= n \cdot  \frac{1}{n}\left( {\ln {a}_{1} + \ln {a}_{2} + \cdots  + \ln {a}_{n}}\right)  = \ln \left( {{a}_{1}{a}_{2}\cdots {a}_{n}}\right) ,
$$

故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left\lbrack  \left( {a}_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}} + {a}_{2}^{\frac{1}{x}} + \cdots  + {a}_{n}^{\frac{1}{x}}\right) /n\right\rbrack  }^{nx} = {a}_{1}{a}_{2}\cdots {a}_{n}$ .

1211. 求下列函数在指定的 ${x}_{0}$ 处具有指定阶数及余项的泰勒公式:

(1) $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3}\ln x,{x}_{0} = 1,n = 4$ ,拉格朗日余项；

(2) $f\left( x\right)  = \arctan x,{x}_{0} = 0,n = 3$ ,佩亚诺余项;

(3) $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x},{x}_{0} = 0,n = 3$ ,佩亚诺余项;

(4) $f\left( x\right)  = \ln \cos x,{x}_{0} = 0,n = 6$ ,佩亚诺余项.

解 (1) $f\left( 1\right)  = 0,{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 3{x}^{2}\ln x + {x}^{2},{f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  = 1$ ;

${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {6x}\ln x + {5x},{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 1\right)  = 5;{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = 6\ln x + {11},{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( 1\right)  = {11}$ ;

${f}^{\left( 4\right) }\left( x\right)  = \frac{6}{x},{f}^{\left( 4\right) }\left( 1\right)  = 6;{f}^{\left( 5\right) }\left( x\right)  =  - \frac{6}{{x}^{2}},{f}^{\left( 5\right) }\left( \xi \right)  =  - \frac{6}{{\xi }^{2}}$ ,

因此,

$$
{x}^{3}\ln x = \left( {x - 1}\right)  + \frac{5}{2!}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + \frac{11}{3!}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{3} + \frac{6}{4!}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{4} - \frac{6}{5!{\xi }^{2}}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{5},
$$

其中 $\xi$ 介于 1 和 $x$ 之间.

(2) $f\left( 0\right)  = 0,{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{2}},{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 1;{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  =  - \frac{2x}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}},{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0;{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  =$

$- \frac{2\left( {1 - 3{x}^{2}}\right) }{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{3}},{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  =  - 2;$

因此,

$$
\arctan x = x - \frac{{x}^{2}}{3} + o\left( {x}^{4}\right) .
$$

注: 也可用下列方法求 $y = \arctan x$ 在 $x = 0$ 处的导数.

对 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{2}}$ ,即 $\left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) {y}^{\prime } = 1$ ,求 $n$ 阶导数:

$$
\left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) {y}^{\left( n + 1\right) } + {2nx}{y}^{\left( n\right) } + n\left( {n - 1}\right) {y}^{\left( n - 1\right) } = 0,
$$

令 $x = 0$ 得

$$
{y}^{\left( n + 1\right) }\left( 0\right)  =  - n\left( {n - 1}\right) {y}^{\left( n - 1\right) }\left( 0\right) ,
$$

由 ${y}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0,{y}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 1$ 得

$$
{y}^{\left( 2m\right) }\left( 0\right)  = 0,
$$

$$
{y}^{\left( 2m + 1\right) }\left( 0\right)  =  - {2m}\left( {{2m} - 1}\right) {y}^{\left( 2m - 1\right) }\left( 0\right)  = \left( {-1}\right) \left( {2m}\right) !.
$$

(3) ${\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x} = 1 + \sin x + \frac{1}{2!}{\sin }^{2}x + \frac{1}{3!}{\sin }^{3}x + o\left( {x}^{3}\right)$ ,又, $\sin x = x - \frac{1}{3!}{x}^{3} + o\left( {x}^{4}\right)$ ,故

$$
{\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x} = 1 + \left( {x - \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3}}\right)  + \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + o\left( {x}^{3}\right)  = 1 + x + \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2} + o\left( {x}^{3}\right) .
$$

(4) $\ln \cos x = \ln \left\lbrack  {1 + \left( {\cos x - 1}\right) }\right\rbrack   = \cos x - 1 - \frac{1}{2}{\left( \cos x - 1\right) }^{2} + \frac{1}{3}{\left( \cos x - 1\right) }^{3} +$

$o\left( {x}^{6}\right)$ ,又, $\cos x - 1 =  - \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{24}{x}^{4} - \frac{1}{720}{x}^{6} + o\left( {x}^{7}\right)$ ,因此, $\ln \cos x = \left( {-\frac{1}{2}{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{24}{x}^{4} - \frac{1}{720}{x}^{6}}\right)  - \frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{4}{x}^{4} - \frac{1}{24}{x}^{6}}\right)  + \frac{1}{3}\left( {-\frac{1}{8}{x}^{6}}\right)  + o\left( {x}^{6}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2} - \frac{1}{12}{x}^{4} - \frac{1}{45}{x}^{6} + o\left( {x}^{6}\right) .
$$

272. 证明下列不等式:

(1)当 $0 < {x}_{1} < {x}_{2} < \frac{\pi }{2}$ 时, $\frac{\tan {x}_{2}}{\tan {x}_{1}} > \frac{{x}_{2}}{{x}_{1}}$ ；

(2)当 $x > 0$ 时, $\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  > \frac{\arctan x}{1 + x}$ ；

(3) 当 $\mathrm{e} < a < b < {\mathrm{e}}^{2}$ 时, ${\ln }^{2}b - {\ln }^{2}a > \frac{4}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}}\left( {b - a}\right)$ .

证 (1) 取函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{\tan x}{x},0 < x < \frac{\pi }{2}$ .

当 $0 < x < \frac{\pi }{2}$ 时,

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{x{\sec }^{2}x - \tan x}{{x}^{2}} > 0\left( {x{\sec }^{2}x - \tan x > x - \tan x > 0}\right)
$$

故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0,\frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ 内单调增加,因此,当 $0 < {x}_{1} < {x}_{2} < \frac{\pi }{2}$ 时,

$$
f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  > f\left( {x}_{1}\right) ,
$$

即

$$
\frac{\tan {x}_{2}}{{x}_{2}} > \frac{\tan {x}_{1}}{{x}_{1}}
$$

亦即

$$
\frac{\tan {x}_{2}}{\tan {x}_{1}} > \frac{{x}_{2}}{{x}_{1}}.
$$

(2)取函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \left( {1 + x}\right) \ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - \arctan x\left( {x > 0}\right)$ .

当 $x > 0$ 时,

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  + 1 - \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{2}} > 0,
$$

故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内单调增加,因此,当 $x > 0$ 时,

$$
f\left( x\right)  > f\left( 0\right) ,
$$

即 $\left( {1 + x}\right) \ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - \arctan x > 0$ ,亦即

$$
\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  > \frac{\arctan x}{1 + x}.
$$

(3) 设 $f\left( x\right)  = {\ln }^{2}x\left( {\mathrm{e} < a < x < b < {\mathrm{e}}^{2}}\right)$ .

$f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(a,b)内可导,由拉格朗日中值定理知,至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使

$$
{\ln }^{2}b - {\ln }^{2}a = \frac{2\ln \xi }{\xi }\left( {b - a}\right) .
$$

设 $\varphi \left( t\right)  = \frac{\ln t}{t}$ ,则 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( t\right)  = \frac{1 - \ln t}{{t}^{2}}$ . 当 $t > \mathrm{e}$ 时, ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( t\right)  < 0$ ,所以 $\varphi \left( t\right)$ 在 $\lbrack \mathrm{e}, + \infty )$ 上单调减少,而 $\mathrm{e} < a < \xi  < b < {\mathrm{e}}^{2}$ ,从而 $\varphi \left( \xi \right)  > \varphi \left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2}\right)$ ,即

$$
\frac{\ln \xi }{\xi } > \frac{\ln {\mathrm{e}}^{2}}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}} = \frac{2}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}},
$$

因此, ${\ln }^{2}b - {\ln }^{2}a > \frac{4}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}}\left( {b - a}\right)$ .

13. 设 $a > 1,f\left( x\right)  = {a}^{x} - {ax}$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内的驻点为 $x\left( a\right)$ . 问 $a$ 为何值时, $x\left( a\right)$ 最小? 并求出最小值.

解 由 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {a}^{x}\ln a - a = 0$ ,得惟一驻点

$$
x\left( a\right)  = 1 - \frac{\ln \ln a}{\ln a}.
$$

考察函数 $x\left( a\right)  = 1 - \frac{\ln \ln a}{\ln a}$ 在 $a > 1$ 时的最小值. 令

$$
{x}^{\prime }\left( a\right)  =  - \frac{\frac{1}{a} - \frac{1}{a}\ln \ln a}{{\left( \ln a\right) }^{2}} =  - \frac{1 - \ln \ln a}{a{\left( \ln a\right) }^{2}} = 0,
$$

得惟一驻点, $a = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathrm{e}}$ . 当 $a > {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathrm{e}}$ 时, ${x}^{\prime }\left( a\right)  > 0$ ; 当 $a < {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathrm{e}}$ 时, ${x}^{\prime }\left( a\right)  < 0$ ,因此

$$
x\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathrm{e}}\right)  = 1 - \frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}
$$

为极小值, 也是最小值.

24. 求椭圆 ${x}^{2} - {xy} + {y}^{2} = 3$ 上纵坐标最大和最小的点.

解 在椭圆方程两端分别对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
{2x} - y - x{y}^{\prime } + {2y}{y}^{\prime } = 0,
$$

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{y - {2x}}{{2y} - x}.
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 $y = {2x}$ . 将 $y = {2x}$ 代入椭圆方程后得 ${x}^{2} = 1$ ,故 $x =  \pm  1$ . 从而得到椭圆上的点 $\left( {1,2}\right) ,\left( {-1, - 2}\right)$ . 根据题意即知点 $\left( {1,2}\right) ,\left( {-1, - 2}\right)$ 为椭圆 ${x}^{2} - {xy} + {y}^{2} = 3$ 上纵坐标最大和最小的点.

1215. 求数列 $\left\{  \sqrt[n]{n}\right\}$ 的最大项.

解 取函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{\frac{1}{x}}\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,则

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {x}^{\frac{1}{x} - 2}\left( {1 - \ln x}\right) .
$$

令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,得驻点 $x = \mathrm{e}$ . 当 $0 < x < \mathrm{e}$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ; 当 $\mathrm{e} < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,因此点 $x = \mathrm{e}$ 为 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极大值点. 由于驻点惟一,极大值点也是最大值点且最大值为 $f\left( \mathrm{e}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}$ .

由 $1 < \sqrt{2}$ 及 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {\mathrm{e}, + \infty }\right)$ 内单调减少,知

$$
\sqrt[3]{3} > \sqrt[4]{4} > \cdots  > \sqrt[n]{n} > \cdots
$$

又 $\max \left\{  {\sqrt{2},\sqrt[3]{3}}\right\}   = \sqrt[3]{3}$ ,故数列 $\left\{  \sqrt[n]{n}\right\}$ 的最大项为 $\sqrt[3]{3}$ .

26. 由线弧 $y = \sin x\left( {0 < x < \pi }\right)$ 上哪一点处的曲率半径最小? 求出该点处的曲率半径.

解 ${y}^{\prime } = \cos x,{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - \sin x$ ,曲线 $y = \sin x\left( {0 < x < \pi }\right)$ 的曲率为

$$
K = \frac{\left| -\sin x\right| }{{\left( 1 + {\cos }^{2}x\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}} = \frac{\sin x}{{\left( 1 + {\cos }^{2}x\right) }^{3/2}},
$$

由 ${K}^{\prime } = \frac{2\cos x\left( {1 + {\sin }^{2}x}\right) }{{\left( 1 + {\cos }^{2}x\right) }^{\frac{5}{2}}} = 0$ 知 $x = \frac{\pi }{2}$ .

当 $0 < x < \frac{\pi }{2}$ 时, ${K}^{\prime } > 0$ ; 当 $\frac{\pi }{2} < x < \pi$ 时, ${K}^{\prime } < 0$ . 因此 $x = \frac{\pi }{2}$ 为 $K$ 的极大值点. 又驻点惟一,故极大值点也是最大值点,且 $K$ 的最大值为

$$
K = {\left. \frac{\sin x}{{\left( 1 + {\cos }^{2}x\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}\right| }_{x = \frac{\pi }{2}} = 1.
$$

此时曲率半径 $\rho  = 1$ 最小,故曲线弧 $y = \sin x\left( {0 < x < \pi }\right)$ 上点 $x = \frac{\pi }{2}$ 处的曲率半径最小且曲率半径为 $\rho  = 1$ .

1217. 证明方程 ${x}^{3} - {5x} - 2 = 0$ 只有一个正根,并求此正根的近似值,精确到 ${10}^{-3}$ .

证 取函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} - {5x} - 2,{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 3{x}^{2} - 5$ .

令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$ 得驻点 $x = \sqrt{\frac{5}{3}}$ .

当 $0 < x < \sqrt{\frac{5}{3}}$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}}}\right\rbrack$ 上单调减少,又

$$
f\left( 0\right)  =  - 2 < 0,f\left( \sqrt{\frac{5}{3}}\right)  = {\left( \frac{5}{3}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}} - 5\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}} - 2 < 0.
$$

因此方程 $f\left( x\right)  = 0$ 即 ${x}^{3} - {5x} - 2 = 0$ 在 $\left( {0,\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}}}\right)$ 内没有实根.

当 $\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}} < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}}, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调增加,因此方程 $f\left( x\right)  = 0$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}}, + \infty }\right)$ 上至多有一实根,又 $f\left( 3\right)  = {10} > 0$ ,由零点定理知至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left( {\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}},3}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,即方程 $f\left( x\right)  = 0$ 亦即 ${x}^{3} - {5x} - 2 = 0$ 在 $\left( {\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}},3}\right)$ 内至少有一实根,因此方程 ${x}^{3} - {5x} - 2 = 0$ 在 $\left( {\sqrt{\frac{5}{3}},3}\right)$ 内只有一正根.

综上,方程 ${x}^{3} - {5x} - 2 = 0$ 只有一个正根.

现在用二分法来求该方程正根的近似值,由 $f\left( 2\right)  =  - 4 < 0$ ,为了方便起见,取区间 $\left\lbrack  {2,3}\right\rbrack$ .

<!-- Media -->
