故误差不超过 ${10}^{-3}$ 的正根的近似值为 $\xi  = {2.415}$ .

1 * 18. 设 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ 存在,证明

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {{x}_{0} + h}\right)  + f\left( {{x}_{0} - h}\right)  - {2f}\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{{h}^{2}} = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) .
$$

证 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {{x}_{0} + h}\right)  + f\left( {{x}_{0} - h}\right)  - {2f}\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{{h}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {{x}_{0} + h}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( {{x}_{0} - h}\right) }{2h}$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {{x}_{0} + h}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{h} + \frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {{x}_{0} - h}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{-h}}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\left\lbrack  {{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \text{.}
$$

2. 19. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(a,b)内二阶可导,且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ . 证明对于(a,b)内任意两点 ${x}_{1},{x}_{2}$ 及 $0 \leq  t \leq  1$ ,有

$$
f\left\lbrack  {\left( {1 - t}\right) {x}_{1} + t{x}_{2}}\right\rbrack   \leq  \left( {1 - t}\right) f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + {tf}\left( {x}_{2}\right) .
$$

证 由 ${x}_{1},{x}_{2} \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ 知 ${x}_{0} = \left( {1 - t}\right) {x}_{1} + t{x}_{2} \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,利用泰勒公式有

$$
f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \left( {{x}_{1} - {x}_{0}}\right)  + \frac{1}{2!}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\xi }_{1}\right) {\left( {x}_{1} - {x}_{0}\right) }^{2},{\xi }_{1}\text{介于}{x}_{1}\text{与}{x}_{0}\text{之间;}
$$

$$
f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{0}}\right)  + \frac{1}{2!}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\xi }_{2}\right) {\left( {x}_{2} - {x}_{0}\right) }^{2},{\xi }_{2}\text{介于}{x}_{2}\text{与}{x}_{0}\text{之间.}
$$

由 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ 知 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\xi }_{1}\right)  \geq  0,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\xi }_{2}\right)  \geq  0$ ,故

$$
f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \geq  f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \left( {{x}_{1} - {x}_{0}}\right) \text{ 及 }f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  \geq  f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{0}}\right) ,
$$

因此,

$$
\left( {1 - t}\right) f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + {tf}\left( {x}_{2}\right)
$$

$$
\geq  \left( {1 - t}\right) f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {tf}\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \left\lbrack  {\left( {1 - t}\right) \left( {{x}_{1} - {x}_{0}}\right)  + t\left( {{x}_{2} - {x}_{0}}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) \left\lbrack  {\left( {1 - t}\right) {x}_{1} + t{x}_{2} - {x}_{0}}\right\rbrack   = f\left( {x}_{0}\right) ,
$$

即 $f\left\lbrack  {\left( {1 - t}\right) {x}_{1} + t{x}_{2}}\right\rbrack   \leq  \left( {1 - t}\right) f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  + {tf}\left( {x}_{2}\right)$ .

250. 试确定常数 $a$ 和 $b$ ; 使 $f\left( x\right)  = x - \left( {a + b\cos x}\right) \sin x$ 为当 $x \rightarrow  0$ 时关于 $x$ 的 5 阶无穷小.

解 利用泰勒公式

$$
f\left( x\right)  = x - a\sin x - \frac{b}{2}\sin {2x}
$$

$$
= x - a\left\lbrack  {x - \frac{{x}^{3}}{3!} + \frac{{x}^{5}}{5!} + o\left( {x}^{5}\right) }\right\rbrack   - \frac{b}{2}\left\lbrack  {{2x} - \frac{{\left( 2x\right) }^{3}}{3!} + \frac{{\left( 2x\right) }^{5}}{5!} + o\left( {x}^{5}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \left( {1 - a - b}\right) x + \left( {\frac{a}{6} + \frac{2b}{3}}\right) {x}^{3} - \left( {\frac{a}{120} + \frac{2b}{15}}\right) {x}^{5} + o\left( {x}^{5}\right) .
$$

按题意, 应有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} 1 - a - b = 0, \\  \frac{a}{6} + \frac{2b}{3} = 0, \\  \frac{a}{120} + \frac{2b}{15} \neq  0, \end{array}\right.
$$

得 $a = \frac{4}{3},b =  - \frac{1}{3}$ . 因此,当 $a = \frac{4}{3},b =  - \frac{1}{3}$ 时, $f\left( x\right)  = x - \left( {a + b\cos x}\right) \sin x$ 是 $x \rightarrow  0$ 时关于 $x$ 的 5 阶无穷小.

## 第四章 不定积分

### 习题 4-1 不定积分的概念与性质

21. 利用导数验证下列等式:

(1) $\int \frac{1}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \ln \left( {x + \sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}}\right)  + C$ ；

(2) $\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}{x} + C$ ；

(3) $\int \frac{2x}{\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) {\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \arctan x + \frac{1}{x + 1} + C$ ;

(4) $\int \sec x\mathrm{\;d}x = \ln \left| {\tan x + \sec x}\right|  + C$ ;

(5) $\int x\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = x\sin x + \cos x + C$ ;

(6) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right)  + C$ .

解 (1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left\lbrack  {\ln \left( {x + \sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}}\right)  + C}\right\rbrack   = \frac{1}{x + \sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}} \cdot  \left( {1 + \frac{x}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}}}\right)  = \frac{1}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}}$ .

(2) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( {\frac{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}{x} + C}\right)  = \frac{\frac{x}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}} \cdot  x - \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}{{x}^{2}} = \frac{1}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}$ .

(3) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( {\arctan x + \frac{1}{x + 1} + C}\right)  = \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 1} - \frac{1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}} = \frac{2x}{\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) {\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}}$ .

(4) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( {\ln \left| {\tan x + \sec x}\right|  + C}\right)  = \frac{1}{\tan x + \sec x} \cdot  \left( {{\sec }^{2}x + \sec x\tan x}\right)  = \sec x$ .

(5) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( {x\sin x + \cos x + C}\right)  = \sin x + x\cos x - \sin x = x\cos x$ .

(6) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right)  + C}\right\rbrack   = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right)  + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\cos x + \sin x}\right)$

$= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin x$ .

2. 求下列不定积分:

(1) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}}$ ; (2) $\int x\sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (3) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x}}$ ; (4) $\int {x}^{2}\sqrt[3]{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(5) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{x}}$ ; (6) $\int \sqrt[m]{{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(7) $\int 5{x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (8) $\int \left( {{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ;

(9) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\sqrt{2gh}}\left( {g\text{是常数}}\right)$ ； (10) $\int {\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

( 11 ) $\int \left( {\sqrt{x} + 1}\right) \left( {\sqrt{{x}^{3}} - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ； (12) $\int \frac{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}}{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(13) $\int \left( {2{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \frac{3}{x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ； (14) $\int \left( {\frac{3}{1 + {x}^{2}} - \frac{2}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ；

(15) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {1 - \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{\sqrt{x}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (16) $\int {3}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(17) $\int \frac{2 \cdot  {3}^{x} - 5 \cdot  {2}^{x}}{{3}^{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (18) $\int \sec x\left( {\sec x - \tan x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ;

(19) $\int {\cos }^{2}\frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (20) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \cos {2x}}$ ;

(21) $\int \frac{\cos {2x}}{\cos x - \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (22) $\int \frac{\cos {2x}}{{\cos }^{2}x{\sin }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(23) $\int {\cot }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (24) $\int \cos \theta \left( {\tan \theta  + \sec \theta }\right) \mathrm{d}\theta$ ;

(25) $\int \frac{{x}^{2}}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; ( 26 ) $\int \frac{3{x}^{4} + 2{x}^{2}}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 (1) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}} = \int {x}^{-2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{-2 + 1}{x}^{-2 + 1} + C =  - \frac{1}{x} + C$ .

(2) $\int x\sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {x}^{\frac{3}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{\frac{3}{2} + 1}{x}^{\frac{3}{2} + 1} + C = \frac{2}{5}{x}^{\frac{5}{2}} + C$ .

(3) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x}} = \int {x}^{-\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{-\frac{1}{2} + 1}{x}^{-\frac{1}{2} + 1} + C = 2\sqrt{x} + C$ .

(4) $\int {x}^{2}\sqrt[3]{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {x}^{\frac{7}{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{\frac{7}{3} + 1}{x}^{\frac{7}{3} + 1} + C = \frac{3}{10}{x}^{\frac{10}{3}} + C$ .

(5) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{x}} = \int {x}^{-\frac{5}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{-\frac{5}{2} + 1}{x}^{-\frac{5}{2} + 1} + C =  - \frac{2}{3}{x}^{-\frac{3}{2}} + C$ . (6) $\int \sqrt[m]{{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{\frac{n}{m} + 1}{x}^{\frac{n}{m} + 1} + C = \frac{m}{m + n}{x}^{\frac{m + n}{m}} + C$ .

(7) $\int 5{x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{5}{3 + 1}{x}^{3 + 1} + C = \frac{5}{4}{x}^{4} + C$ .

(8) $\int \left( {{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \int {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x - 3\int x\mathrm{\;d}x + 2\int \mathrm{d}x = \frac{{x}^{3}}{3} - \frac{3}{2}{x}^{2} + {2x} + C$ .

(9) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\sqrt{2gh}} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2g}}\int {h}^{-\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}h = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2g}} \times  2\sqrt{h} + C = \sqrt{\frac{2h}{g}} + C$ .

(10) $\int {\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {{x}^{4} + 2{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \int {x}^{4}\mathrm{\;d}x + 2\int {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x + \int \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{5}}{5} + \frac{2}{3}{x}^{3} + x + C.
$$

(11) $\int \left( {\sqrt{x} + 1}\right) \left( {\sqrt{{x}^{3}} - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \int \left( {{x}^{2} + {x}^{\frac{3}{2}} - {x}^{\frac{1}{2}} - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \int {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x + \int {x}^{\frac{3}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x - \int {x}^{\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x - \int \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{3}}{3} + \frac{2}{5}{x}^{\frac{5}{2}} - \frac{2}{3}{x}^{\frac{3}{2}} - x + C.
$$

(12) $\int \frac{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}}{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {{x}^{\frac{3}{2}} - 2{x}^{\frac{1}{2}} + {x}^{-\frac{1}{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \int {x}^{\frac{3}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x - 2\int {x}^{\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + \int {x}^{-\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{5}{x}^{\frac{5}{2}} - \frac{4}{3}{x}^{\frac{3}{2}} + 2{x}^{\frac{1}{2}} + C.
$$

(13) $\int \left( {2{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \frac{3}{x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = 2\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x + 3\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x} = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 3\ln \left| x\right|  + C$ .

(14) $\int \left( {\frac{3}{1 + {x}^{2}} - \frac{2}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = 3\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{2}} - 2\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}$

$$
= 3\arctan x - 2\arcsin x + C\text{.}
$$

( 15 ) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {1 - \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{\sqrt{x}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x - \int {x}^{-\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 2{x}^{\frac{1}{2}} + C$ .

( 16 ) $\int {3}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {\left( 3\mathrm{e}\right) }^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{{\left( 3\mathrm{e}\right) }^{x}}{\ln \left( {3\mathrm{e}}\right) } + C = \frac{{3}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{\ln 3 + 1} + C$ .

(1) $\int \frac{2 \cdot  {3}^{x} - 5 \cdot  {2}^{x}}{{3}^{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = 2\int \mathrm{d}x - 5\int {\left( \frac{2}{3}\right) }^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {2x} - \frac{5}{\ln \frac{2}{3}}{\left( \frac{2}{3}\right) }^{x} + C$

$$
= {2x} - \frac{5}{\ln 2 - \ln 3}{\left( \frac{2}{3}\right) }^{x} + C.
$$

(18) $\int \sec x\left( {\sec x - \tan x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \int {\sec }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x - \int \sec x\tan x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \tan x - \sec x + C\text{.}
$$

(19) $\int {\cos }^{2}\frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1 + \cos x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{x + \sin x}{2} + C$ .

( 20 ) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \cos {2x}} = \int \frac{{\sec }^{2}x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{\tan x}{2} + C$ .

( 21 ) $\int \frac{\cos {2x}}{\cos x - \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{{\cos }^{2}x - {\sin }^{2}x}{\cos x - \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \sin x - \cos x + C$ .

( 22 ) $\int \frac{\cos {2x}}{{\cos }^{2}x{\sin }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{{\cos }^{2}x - {\sin }^{2}x}{{\cos }^{2}x{\sin }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {{\csc }^{2}x - {\sec }^{2}x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \int {\csc }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x - \int {\sec }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \left( {\cot x + \tan x}\right)  + C.
$$

( 23 ) $\int {\cot }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {\csc }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x - \int \mathrm{d}x =  - \cot x - x + C$ .

(24) $\int \cos \theta \left( {\tan \theta  + \sec \theta }\right) \mathrm{d}\theta  = \int \sin \theta \mathrm{d}\theta  + \int \mathrm{d}\theta  =  - \cos \theta  + \theta  + C$ .

( 25 ) $\int \frac{{x}^{2}}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \mathrm{d}x - \int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = x - \arctan x + C$ .

( 26 ) $\int \frac{3{x}^{4} + 2{x}^{2}}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int 3{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x - \int \mathrm{d}x + \int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = {x}^{3} - x + \arctan x + C$ .

3. 含有未知函数的导数的方程称为微分方程,例如方程 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = f\left( x\right)$ ,其中 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ 为未知函数的导数, $f\left( x\right)$ 为已知函数. 如果将函数 $y = \varphi \left( x\right)$ 代入微分方程,使微分方程成为恒等式,那么函数 $y = \varphi \left( x\right)$ 就称为这个微分方程的解. 求下列微分方程满足所给条件的解:

(1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 2} = 0$ ;

(2) $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = \frac{2}{{t}^{3}},{\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t}\right| }_{t = 1} = 1,{\left. x\right| }_{t = 1} = 1$ .

解 (1)

$$
y = \int {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{3}{\left( x - 2\right) }^{3} + C,
$$

由 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 2} = 0$ ,得 $C = 0$ ,于是所求的解为 $y = \frac{1}{3}{\left( x - 2\right) }^{3}$ .

(2)

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \int \frac{2}{{t}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}t =  - \frac{1}{{t}^{2}} + {C}_{1},
$$

由 ${\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t}\right| }_{t = 1} = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 2$ ,故 $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} =  - \frac{1}{{t}^{2}} + 2$ ,

$$
x = \int \left( {-\frac{1}{{t}^{2}} + 2}\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{t} + {2t} + {C}_{2},
$$

由 ${\left. x\right| }_{t = 1} = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{2} =  - 2$ ,于是所求的解为 $x = \frac{1}{t} + {2t} - 2$ .

14. 汽车以 ${20}\mathrm{\;m}/\mathrm{s}$ 的速度行驶,刹车后匀减速行驶了 ${50}\mathrm{\;m}$ 停住,求刹车加速度. 可执行下列步骤:

(1)求微分方程 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}s}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} =  - k$ 满足条件 ${\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t}\right| }_{t = 0} = {20}$ 及 ${\left. s\right| }_{t = 0} = 0$ 的解；

(2)求使 $\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = 0$ 的 $t$ 值；

(3)求使 $s = {50}$ 的 $k$ 值.

解 (1)

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \int  - k\mathrm{\;d}t =  - {kt} + {C}_{1},
$$

由 ${\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t}\right| }_{t = 0} = {20}$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = {20}$ ,故

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} =  - {kt} + {20},
$$

$$
s = \int \left( {-{kt} + {20}}\right) \mathrm{d}t =  - \frac{1}{2}k{t}^{2} + {20t} + {C}_{2},
$$

由 ${\left. s\right| }_{t = 0} = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 0$ ,于是所求的解为

$$
s =  - \frac{1}{2}k{t}^{2} + {20t}
$$

(2)令 $\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = 0$ ,解得 $t = \frac{20}{k}$ .

(3)根据题意,当 $t = \frac{20}{k}$ 时, $s = {50}$ ,即

$$
- \frac{1}{2}k{\left( \frac{20}{k}\right) }^{2} + \frac{400}{k} = {50},
$$

解得 $k = 4$ ,即得刹车加速度为 $- 4\mathrm{\;m}/{\mathrm{s}}^{2}$ .

5. 一曲线通过点 $\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2},3}\right)$ ,且在任一点处的切线的斜率等于该点横坐标的倒数,求该曲线的方程.

解 设曲线方程为 $y = f\left( x\right)$ ,则点(x,y)处的切线斜率为 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ ,由条件得

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x},
$$

因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 为 $\frac{1}{x}$ 的一个原函数,故有 $f\left( x\right)  = \int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \ln \left| x\right|  + C$ .

又,根据条件曲线过点 $\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2},3}\right)$ ,有 $f\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2}\right)  = 3$ 解得 $C = 1$ ,即得所求曲线方程为

$$
y = \ln x + 1\text{.}
$$

26. 一物体由静止开始运动,经 $t$ 秒后的速度是 $3{t}^{2}\left( {\mathrm{\;m}/\mathrm{s}}\right)$ ,问

(1)在 3 秒后物体离开出发点的距离是多少?

(2)物体走完 ${360}\mathrm{\;m}$ 需要多少时间？

解 (1) 设此物体自原点沿横轴正向由静止开始运动,位移函数为 $s = s\left( t\right)$ ,则

$$
s\left( t\right)  = \int v\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \int 3{t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t = {t}^{3} + C,
$$

由假设可知 $s\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,故 $s\left( t\right)  = {t}^{3}$ ,于是所求距离为 $s\left( 3\right)  = {27}\left( \mathrm{\;m}\right)$ .

(2) 由 ${t}^{3} = {360}$ ,得 $t = \sqrt[3]{360} \approx  {7.11}\left( \mathrm{\;s}\right)$ .

297. 证明函数 $\arcsin \left( {{2x} - 1}\right) ,\arccos \left( {1 - {2x}}\right)$ 和 $2\arctan \sqrt{\frac{x}{1 - x}}$ 都是 $\frac{1}{\sqrt{x - {x}^{2}}}$ 的原函数.

证 ${\left\lbrack  \arcsin \left( 2x - 1\right) \right\rbrack  }^{\prime } = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - {\left( 2x - 1\right) }^{2}}} \cdot  2 = \frac{1}{\sqrt{x - {x}^{2}}}$ ,

$$
{\left\lbrack  \arccos \left( 1 - 2x\right) \right\rbrack  }^{\prime } =  - \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - {\left( 1 - 2x\right) }^{2}}} \cdot  \left( {-2}\right)  = \frac{1}{\sqrt{x - {x}^{2}}},
$$

$$
{\left( 2\arctan \sqrt{\frac{x}{1 - x}}\right) }^{\prime } = 2\frac{1}{1 + \frac{x}{1 - x}} \cdot  \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{x}} \cdot  \frac{1}{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{x - {x}^{2}}}.
$$

故结论成立.

### 习题4-2 换元积分法


5 1. 在下列各式等号右端的空白处填入适当的系数,使等式成立 (例如: $\mathrm{d}x =$ $\frac{1}{4}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {{4x} + 7}\right) )$ :

(1) $\mathrm{d}x = \underline{}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {ax}\right)$ ; (2) $\mathrm{d}x = \underline{}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {{7x} - 3}\right)$ ；

(3) $x\mathrm{\;d}x = \underline{}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x}^{2}\right)$ ; (4) $x\mathrm{\;d}x = \underline{}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {5{x}^{2}}\right)$ ；

(5) $x\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \mathrm{d}\left( {1 - {x}^{2}}\right)$ ; (6) ${x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \mathrm{d}\left( {3{x}^{4} - 2}\right)$ ;

(7) ${\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \underline{}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\right)$ ; (8) ${\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{x}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \underline{}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{x}{2}}}\right)$ ;

(9) $\sin \frac{3}{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = x\left( {\cos \frac{3}{2}x}\right)$ ; (10) $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x} =  - \mathrm{d}\left( {5\ln \left| x\right| }\right)$ ;

( 11 ) $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x} =  - \mathrm{d}\left( {3 - 5\ln \left| x\right| }\right)$ ； (12) $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + 9{x}^{2}} =  - \mathrm{d}\left( {\arctan {3x}}\right)$ ;

(13) $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} =  - \mathrm{d}\left( {1 - \arcsin x}\right)$ ； (14) $\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = d\left( \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\right)$ .

解 (1) $\frac{1}{a}$ ; (2) $\frac{1}{7}$ ; (3) $\frac{1}{2}$ ; (4) $\frac{1}{10}$ ; (5) $- \frac{1}{2}$ ;

(6) $\frac{1}{12}$ ; (7) $\frac{1}{2}$ ; (8)-2 ; (9) $- \frac{2}{3}$ ; (10) $\frac{1}{5}$ ;

(11) $- \frac{1}{5}$ ; (12) $\frac{1}{3}$ ; (13) -1 ; (14) -1 .

2. 求下列不定积分 (其中 $a$ 、 $b$ 、 $\omega$ 、 $\varphi$ 均为常数):

(1) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ; (2) $\int {\left( 3 - 2x\right) }^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(3) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 - {2x}}$ ; (4) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{2 - {3x}}}$ ;

(5) $\int \left( {\sin {ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{b}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (6) $\int \frac{\sin \sqrt{t}}{\sqrt{t}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ;

(7) $\int x{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (8) $\int x\cos \left( {x}^{2}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ;

(9) $\int \frac{x}{\sqrt{2 - 3{x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (10) $\int \frac{3{x}^{3}}{1 - {x}^{4}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(11) $\int \frac{x + 1}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 5}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (12) $\int {\cos }^{2}\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) \sin \left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ；

(13) $\int \frac{\sin x}{{\cos }^{3}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (14) $\int \frac{\sin x + \cos x}{\sqrt[3]{\sin x - \cos x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(15) $\int {\tan }^{10}x \cdot  {\sec }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (16) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\ln x\ln \ln x}$ ;

(17) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}$ ; (18) $\int \frac{{10}^{2\arccos x}}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(19) $\int \tan \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}} \cdot  \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}$ ; (20) $\int \frac{\arctan \sqrt{x}}{\sqrt{x}\left( {1 + x}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$ ；

(21) $\int \frac{1 + \ln x}{{\left( x\ln x\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (22) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x\cos x}$ ;

(23) $\int \frac{\ln \tan x}{\cos x\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (24) $\int {\cos }^{3}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(25) $\int {\cos }^{2}\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ； (26) $\int \sin {2x}\cos {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(27) $\int \cos x\cos \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (28) $\int \sin {5x}\sin {7x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(29) $\int {\tan }^{3}x\sec x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； ( 30 ) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}$ ;

(31) $\int \frac{1 - x}{\sqrt{9 - 4{x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (32) $\int \frac{{x}^{3}}{9 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(33) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2{x}^{2} - 1}$ ; (34) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {x + 1}\right) \left( {x - 2}\right) }$ ;

(35) $\int \frac{x}{{x}^{2} - x - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (36) $\int \frac{{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}\left( {a > 0}\right)$ ;

(37) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}$ ; (38) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{3}}}$ ;

(39) $\int \frac{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9}}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; ( 40 ) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{2x}}$ ;

(41) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}$ ; (42) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}$ ;

(43) $\int \frac{x - 1}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (44) $\int \frac{{x}^{3} + 1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 (1) 令 $u = {5t}$ ,由第一类换元法得

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{1}{5}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{1}{5}{\mathrm{e}}^{u} + C = \frac{1}{5}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t} + C.
$$

(2)令 $u = 3 - {2x}$ ,由第一类换元法得

$$
\int {\left( 3 - 2x\right) }^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2}\int {u}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \frac{{u}^{4}}{8} + C =  - \frac{{\left( 3 - 2x\right) }^{4}}{8} + C.
$$

(3)令 $u = 1 - {2x}$ ,由第一类换元法得

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 - {2x}} =  - \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{u} =  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| u\right|  + C =  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {1 - {2x}}\right|  + C.
$$

(4) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{2 - {3x}}} = \int  - \frac{1}{3}{\left( 2 - 3x\right) }^{-\frac{1}{3}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {2 - {3x}}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{3} \cdot  \frac{3}{2}{\left( 2 - 3x\right) }^{\frac{2}{3}} + C =  - \frac{1}{2}{\left( 2 - 3x\right) }^{\frac{2}{3}} + C.
$$

(5) $\int \left( {\sin {ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{b}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \int \sin {ax}\mathrm{\;d}x - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{b}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \int \frac{1}{a}\sin {ax}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {ax}\right)  - \int b{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{b}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{x}{b}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{a}\left( {-\cos {ax}}\right)  - b{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{b}} + C =  - \frac{\cos {ax}}{a} - b{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{b}} + C.
$$

(6) $\int \frac{\sin \sqrt{t}}{\sqrt{t}}\mathrm{\;d}t = \int 2\sin \sqrt{t}\mathrm{\;d}\sqrt{t} =  - 2\cos \sqrt{t} + C$ .

(7) $\int x{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {-{x}^{2}}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}} + C$ .

(8) $\int x\cos \left( {x}^{2}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \cos \left( {x}^{2}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {x}^{2}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\sin \left( {x}^{2}\right)  + C$ .

(9) $\int \frac{x}{\sqrt{2 - 3{x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{6}\int {\left( 2 - 3{x}^{2}\right) }^{-\frac{1}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {2 - 3{x}^{2}}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{6} \cdot  2{\left( 2 - 3{x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}} + C =  - \frac{\sqrt{2 - 3{x}^{2}}}{3} + C.
$$

( 10 ) $\int \frac{3{x}^{3}}{1 - {x}^{4}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{3}{4}\int \frac{1}{1 - {x}^{4}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {1 - {x}^{4}}\right)  =  - \frac{3}{4}\ln \left| {1 - {x}^{4}}\right|  + C$ .

(1) $\int \frac{x + 1}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 5}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{x}^{2} + {2x} + 5}\right) }{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 5} = \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + {2x} + 5}\right)  + C$ .

2) $\int {\cos }^{2}\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) \sin \left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) \mathrm{d}t =  - \frac{1}{\omega }\int {\cos }^{2}\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) \mathrm{d}\left\lbrack  {\cos \left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) }\right\rbrack$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{3\omega }{\cos }^{3}\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right)  + C.
$$

(13) $\int \frac{\sin x}{{\cos }^{3}x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int \frac{1}{{\cos }^{3}x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos x}\right)  = \frac{1}{2{\cos }^{2}x} + C$ .

(14) $\int \frac{\sin x + \cos x}{\sqrt[3]{\sin x - \cos x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right) }{\sqrt[3]{\sin x - \cos x}} = \frac{3}{2}{\left( \sin x - \cos x\right) }^{\frac{2}{3}} + C$ .

(15) $\int {\tan }^{10}x \cdot  {\sec }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {\tan }^{10}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\tan x}\right)  = \frac{1}{11}{\tan }^{11}x + C$ .

16) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\ln x\ln \ln x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\ln x}\right) }{\ln x\ln \ln x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\ln \ln x}\right) }{\ln \ln x} = \ln \left| {\ln \ln x}\right|  + C$ .

(17) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\arcsin x}\right) }{{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}} =  - \frac{1}{\arcsin x} + C$ .

(18) $\int \frac{{10}^{2\arccos x}}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int  - {10}^{2\arccos x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\arccos x}\right)  =  - \frac{{10}^{2\arccos x}}{2\ln {10}} + C$ .

( 19 ) $\int \tan \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}} \cdot  \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \tan \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}} \cdot  \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) }{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}$

$$
= \int \tan \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \ln \left| {\cos \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right|  + C\text{.}
$$

$\int \frac{\arctan \sqrt{x}}{\sqrt{x}\left( {1 + x}\right) }\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{2\arctan \sqrt{x}}{1 + x}\mathrm{\;d}\sqrt{x} = \int 2\arctan \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\arctan \sqrt{x}}\right)$

$$
= {\left( \arctan \sqrt{x}\right) }^{2} + C\text{.}
$$

( 21 ) $\int \frac{1 + \ln x}{{\left( x\ln x\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {x\ln x}\right) }{{\left( x\ln x\right) }^{2}} =  - \frac{1}{x\ln x} + C$ .

(22) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x\cos x} = \int \csc {2x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {2x}\right)  = \ln \left| {\csc {2x} - \cot {2x}}\right|  + C = \ln \left| {\tan x}\right|  + C$ .

(23) $\int \frac{\ln \tan x}{\cos x\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\ln \tan x}{\tan x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\tan x}\right)  = \int \ln \tan x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\ln \tan x}\right)$

$$
= \frac{{\left( \ln \tan x\right) }^{2}}{2} + C\text{.}
$$

( 24 ) $\int {\cos }^{3}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {1 - {\sin }^{2}x}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\sin x}\right)  = \sin x - \frac{1}{3}{\sin }^{3}x + C$ .

( 25 ) $\int {\cos }^{2}\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) \mathrm{d}t = \int \frac{\cos 2\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right)  + 1}{2}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{\sin 2\left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) }{4\omega } + \frac{t}{2} + C$ .

(26) $\int \sin {2x}\cos {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{2}\left( {\sin {5x} - \sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - \frac{1}{10}\cos {5x} + \frac{1}{2}\cos x + C$ .

( 27 ) $\int \cos x\cos \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{2}\left( {\cos \frac{3}{2}x + \cos \frac{1}{2}x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}\sin \frac{3}{2}x + \sin \frac{1}{2}x + C.
$$

(28) $\int \sin {5x}\sin {7x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int  - \frac{1}{2}\left( {\cos {12x} - \cos {2x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{24}\sin {12x} + \frac{1}{4}\sin {2x} + C.
$$

(29) $\int {\tan }^{3}x\sec x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {{\sec }^{2}x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\sec x}\right)  = \frac{1}{3}{\sec }^{3}x - \sec x + C$ .

(30) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}} = \int \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + 1} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right) }{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + 1} = \arctan \left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right)  + C$ .

(31) $\int \frac{1 - x}{\sqrt{9 - 4{x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( \frac{2x}{3}\right) }{\sqrt{1 - {\left( \frac{2x}{3}\right) }^{2}}} + \frac{1}{8}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {9 - 4{x}^{2}}\right) }{\sqrt{9 - 4{x}^{2}}}$

$$
= \frac{\arcsin \frac{2x}{3}}{2} + \frac{\sqrt{9 - 4{x}^{2}}}{4} + C.
$$

(32) $\int \frac{{x}^{3}}{9 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int x\mathrm{\;d}x - \frac{9}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {9 + {x}^{2}}\right) }{9 + {x}^{2}} = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{9}{2}\ln \left( {9 + {x}^{2}}\right)  + C$ .

(33) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2{x}^{2} - 1} = \frac{1}{2}\int \left( {\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}x - 1} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}x + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2\sqrt{2}}\ln \left| \frac{\sqrt{2}x - 1}{\sqrt{2}x + 1}\right|  + C$ .

(34) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {x + 1}\right) \left( {x - 2}\right) } = \int \frac{1}{3}\left( {\frac{1}{x - 2} - \frac{1}{x + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}\ln \left| \frac{x - 2}{x + 1}\right|  + C\text{.}
$$

5) $\int \frac{x}{{x}^{2} - x - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{x}{\left( {x - 2}\right) \left( {x + 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{1}{3}\left( {\frac{2}{x - 2} + \frac{1}{x + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{2}{3}\ln \left| {x - 2}\right|  + \frac{1}{3}\ln \left| {x + 1}\right|  + C.
$$

(36) 设 $x = a\sin u\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < u < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 $\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}} = a\cos u,\mathrm{\;d}x = a\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,于是

$$
\int \frac{{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}} = \int {a}^{2}{\sin }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = {a}^{2}\int \frac{1 - \cos {2u}}{2}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{{a}^{2}}{2}\left( {u - \frac{\sin {2u}}{2}}\right)  + C
$$

$$
= \frac{{a}^{2}}{2}\arcsin \frac{x}{a} - \frac{x\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}{2} + C.
$$

(37) 当 $x > 1$ 时,

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}\frac{x = \frac{1}{t}}{} - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 - {t}^{2}}} =  - \arcsin t + C
$$

$$
=  - \arcsin \frac{1}{x} + C,
$$

当 $x <  - 1$ 时,

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}} = \frac{1}{t}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 - {t}^{2}}} = \arcsin t + C = \arcsin \frac{1}{x} + C,
$$

故在 $\left( {-\infty , - 1}\right)$ 或 $\left( {1, + \infty }\right)$ 内,有

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}} =  - \arcsin \frac{1}{\left| x\right| } + C.
$$

(38) 设 $x = \tan u\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < u < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 $\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1} = \sec u,\mathrm{\;d}x = {\sec }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,于是

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{3}}} = \int \cos u\mathrm{\;d}u = \sin u + C = \frac{x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}} + C.
$$

(39) 当 $x > 3$ 时,令 $x = 3\sec u\left( {0 \leq  u < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,

$$
\int \frac{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9}}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int 3{\tan }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = 3\int \left( {{\sec }^{2}u - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}u = 3\tan u - {3u} + C
$$

$$
= \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9} - 3\arccos \frac{3}{x} + C;
$$

当 $x <  - 3$ 时,令 $x = 3\sec u\left( {\frac{\pi }{2} < u \leq  \pi }\right)$ ,

$$
\int \frac{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9}}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int 3{\tan }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u =  - 3\int \left( {{\sec }^{2}u - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}u =  - 3\tan u + {3u} + {C}^{\prime }
$$

$$
= \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9} + 3\arccos \frac{3}{x} + {C}^{\prime }
$$

$$
= \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9} - 3\arccos \frac{3}{-x} + {C}^{\prime } + {3\pi }\text{,}
$$

故可统一写作 $\int \frac{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9}}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 9} - 3\arccos \frac{3}{\left| x\right| } + C$ .

( 40 ) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{2x}}\frac{x = \frac{{u}^{2}}{2}}{}\int \frac{u\mathrm{\;d}u}{1 + u} = u - \ln \left( {1 + u}\right)  + C = \sqrt{2x} - \ln \left( {1 + \sqrt{2x}}\right)  + C$ .

(41)令 $x = \sin t\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < t < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 $\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} = \cos t,\mathrm{\;d}x = \cos t\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,于是

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = \int \frac{\cos t}{1 + \cos t}\mathrm{\;d}t = \int \frac{2{\cos }^{2}\frac{t}{2} - 1}{2{\cos }^{2}\frac{t}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = t - \tan \frac{t}{2} + C
$$

$$
= t - \frac{\sin t}{1 + \cos t} + C = \arcsin x - \frac{x}{1 + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} + C.
$$

(42)设 $x = \sin t\left( {-\frac{\pi }{4} < t < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 $\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} = \cos t,\mathrm{\;d}x = \cos t\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,于是

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = \int \frac{\cos t\mathrm{\;d}t}{\sin t + \cos t},
$$

记 ${I}_{1} = \int \frac{\cos t\mathrm{\;d}t}{\sin t + \cos t},{I}_{2} = \int \frac{\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t}{\sin t + \cos t}$ ,利用

$$
{I}_{1} + {I}_{2} = \int \mathrm{d}t = t + C,
$$

$$
{I}_{1} - {I}_{2} = \int \frac{\cos t - \sin t}{\sin t + \cos t}\mathrm{\;d}t = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\sin t + \cos t}\right) }{\sin t + \cos t} = \ln \left| {\sin t + \cos t}\right|  + C,
$$

求得

$$
{I}_{1} = \int \frac{\cos t\mathrm{\;d}t}{\sin t + \cos t} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {t + \ln \left| {\sin t + \cos t}\right| }\right)  + C,
$$

即求得在 $\left( {-\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},1}\right)$ 内,有

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\arcsin x + \ln \left| {x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\right| }\right)  + C;
$$

再设 $x = \sin t\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < t <  - \frac{\pi }{4}}\right)$ ,重复上面的过程,可得在 $\left( {-1, - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}}\right)$ 内有与上面不

定积分形式相同的结果. 从而在 $\left( {-1, - \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}}\right)$ 或 $\left( {-\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},1}\right)$ 内,有

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\arcsin x + \ln \left| {x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\right| }\right)  + C.
$$

( 43 ) $\int \frac{x - 1}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 3}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{x + 1 - 2}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + 2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left\lbrack  {{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + 2}\right\rbrack  }{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + 2} - \sqrt{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( \frac{x + 1}{\sqrt{2}}\right) }{{\left( \frac{x + 1}{\sqrt{2}}\right) }^{2} + 1}$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + {2x} + 3}\right)  - \sqrt{2}\arctan \frac{x + 1}{\sqrt{2}} + C.
$$

(44)设 $x = \tan t\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < t < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 ${x}^{2} + 1 = {\sec }^{2}t,\mathrm{\;d}x = {\sec }^{2}t\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,于是

$$
\int \frac{{x}^{3} + 1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{{\tan }^{3}t + 1}{{\sec }^{2}t}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= \int \frac{{\cos }^{2}t - 1}{\cos t}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos t}\right)  + \int \frac{1 + \cos {2t}}{2}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\cos }^{2}t - \ln \cos t + \frac{t}{2} + \frac{1}{4}\sin {2t} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\cos }^{2}t - \ln \cos t + \frac{t}{2} + \frac{1}{2}\sin t\cos t + C.
$$

按 $\tan t = x$ 作辅助三角形 (图 4-1),便有

$$
\cos t = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}},\;\sin t = \frac{x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}},
$$
