于是

$$
\int \frac{{x}^{3} + 1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1 + x}{2\left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) } + \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)  + \frac{1}{2}\arctan x + C.
$$

### 习题 4-3 分部积分法



求下列不定积分:

1. $\int x\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 2. $\int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

3. $\int \arcsin x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 4. $\int x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

5. $\int {x}^{2}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 6. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 7. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 8. $\int x\cos \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

9. $\int {x}^{2}\arctan x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 10. $\int x{\tan }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

11. $\int {x}^{2}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 12. $\int t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ .

13. $\int {\ln }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 14. $\int x\sin x\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

15. $\int {x}^{2}{\cos }^{2}\frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 16. $\int x\ln \left( {x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

17. $\int \left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \sin {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 18. $\int \frac{{\ln }^{3}x}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

19. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt[3]{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 20. $\int \cos \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

21. $\int {\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 22. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}{\sin }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

23. $\int x{\ln }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 24. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{{3x} + 9}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 1. $\int x\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos x}\right)  =  - x\cos x + \int \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$=  - x\cos x + \sin x + C$ .

2. $\int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x = x\ln x - \int x \cdot  \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = x\ln x - x + C$ .

3. $\int \arcsin x\mathrm{\;d}x = x\arcsin x - \int x \cdot  \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = x\arcsin x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} + C$ .

4. $\int x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int x{\mathrm{{de}}}^{-x} =  - x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + \int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + C$ .

5. $\int {x}^{2}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{3}\int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x}^{3}\right)  = \frac{{x}^{3}\ln x}{3} - \frac{1}{3}\int {x}^{3} \cdot  \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{{x}^{3}\ln x}{3} - \frac{{x}^{3}}{9} + C$ .

6. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int \cos x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right)  =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x + \int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {-\sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$=  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x + \int \sin x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right)$

$=  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\sin x - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,

故有

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right) }{2} + C.
$$

7. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2}\int \sin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin \frac{x}{2} + \frac{1}{2}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} \cdot  \frac{1}{2}\cos \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin \frac{x}{2} - \frac{1}{8}\int \cos \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin \frac{x}{2} - \frac{1}{8}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\cos \frac{x}{2} + \frac{1}{8}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} \cdot  \left( {-\frac{1}{2}\sin \frac{x}{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{8}\left( {4\sin \frac{x}{2} + \cos \frac{x}{2}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} - \frac{1}{16}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x\text{,}
$$

故

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{2}{17}\left( {4\sin \frac{x}{2} + \cos \frac{x}{2}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} + C.
$$

8. $\int x\cos \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = 2\int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin \frac{x}{2}}\right)  = {2x}\sin \frac{x}{2} - 2\int \sin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {2x}\sin \frac{x}{2} + 4\cos \frac{x}{2} + C\text{.}
$$

9. $\int {x}^{2}\arctan x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{3}\int \arctan x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x}^{3}\right)  = \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3}\arctan x - \frac{1}{3}\int \frac{{x}^{3}}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3}\arctan x - \frac{1}{3}\int \left( {x - \frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3}\arctan x - \frac{1}{6}{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{6}\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)  + C.
$$

10. $\int x{\tan }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int x\left( {{\sec }^{2}x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\tan x}\right)  - \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}$

$$
= x\tan x + \ln \left| {\cos x}\right|  - \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} + C.
$$

11. $\int {x}^{2}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin x}\right)  = {x}^{2}\sin x - \int {2x}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {x}^{2}\sin x + \int {2x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos x}\right)
$$

$$
= {x}^{2}\sin x + {2x}\cos x - \int 2\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= {x}^{2}\sin x + {2x}\cos x - 2\sin x + C\text{.}
$$

12. $\int t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}}\mathrm{\;d}t =  - \frac{1}{2}\int t\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{2}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + \frac{1}{2}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}}\mathrm{\;d}t$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} - \frac{1}{4}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + C.
$$

13. $\int {\ln }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = x{\ln }^{2}x - \int 2\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x = x{\ln }^{2}x - {2x}\ln x + \int 2\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= x{\ln }^{2}x - {2x}\ln x + {2x} + C\text{.}
$$

14. $\int x\sin x\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int  - \frac{x}{4}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos {2x}}\right)  =  - \frac{x\cos {2x}}{4} + \frac{1}{4}\int \cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
=  - \frac{x\cos {2x}}{4} + \frac{\sin {2x}}{8} + C.
$$

15. $\int {x}^{2}{\cos }^{2}\frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int {x}^{2}\left( {1 + \cos x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + \frac{1}{2}\int {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin x}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}\sin x - \int x\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}\sin x + \int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos x}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}\sin x + x\cos x - \int \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}\sin x + x\cos x - \sin x + C.
$$

16. $\int x\ln \left( {x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \ln \left( {x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln \left( {x - 1}\right)  - \frac{1}{2}\int \left( {x + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln \left( {x - 1}\right)  - \frac{1}{4}{x}^{2} - \frac{1}{2}x + C.
$$

17. $\int \left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \sin {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2}\int \left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\cos {2x}}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \cos {2x} + \int x\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \cos {2x} + \frac{1}{2}\int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin {2x}}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \cos {2x} + \frac{1}{2}x\sin {2x} - \frac{1}{2}\int \sin {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}^{2} - \frac{3}{2}}\right) \cos {2x} + \frac{1}{2}x\sin {2x} + C.
$$

18. $\int \frac{{\ln }^{3}x}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int  - {\ln }^{3}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{1}{x}\right)  =  - \frac{{\ln }^{3}x}{x} - 3\int {\ln }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{1}{x}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{{\ln }^{3}x}{x} - 3\left\lbrack  {\frac{{\ln }^{2}x}{x} + 2\int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{1}{x}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
=  - \frac{{\ln }^{3}x + 3{\ln }^{2}x + 6\ln x + 6}{x} + C.
$$

19. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x\overset{x = {u}^{3}}{ = }\int 3{u}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int 3{u}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\right)  = 3{u}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{u} - \int {6u}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\right)$

$$
= \left( {3{u}^{2} - {6u} + 6}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{u} + C = 3{\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt[3]{x}}\left( {{x}^{2/3} - 2{x}^{1/3} + 2}\right)  + C.
$$

20. $\int \cos \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x\overset{x = {\mathrm{e}}^{u}}{ = }\int {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,

而

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \cos u\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u + \int {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u + \int \sin u\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u + {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\sin u - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u,
$$

因此 $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\left( {\cos u + \sin u}\right) }{2} + C$ ,故有

$$
\int \cos \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{x\left( {\cos \ln x + \sin \ln x}\right) }{2} + C.
$$

$$
\text{21.}\int {\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = x{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2} - \int \frac{{2x}\arcsin x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= x{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2} + \int 2\arcsin x\mathrm{\;d}\left( \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\right)
$$

$$
= x{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2} + 2\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\arcsin x - {2x} + C.
$$

$$
\text{22.}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}{\sin }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {1 - \cos {2x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \frac{1}{2}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x\text{,}
$$

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x} + 2\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x} + 2\int \sin {2x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin {2x} - 4\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x\text{,}
$$

得 $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin {2x}}{5} + C$ ,因此有

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}{\sin }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \frac{1}{5}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin {2x} - \frac{1}{10}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x} + C.
$$

$$
\text{23.}\int x{\ln }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {\ln }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}\right)  = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}{\ln }^{2}x - \int x\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}{\ln }^{2}x - \int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}\right)  = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}{\ln }^{2}x - \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}\ln x + \int \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{2}}{4}\left( {2{\ln }^{2}x - 2\ln x + 1}\right)  + C.
$$

24. 设 $\sqrt{{3x} + 9} = u$ ,即 $x = \frac{1}{3}\left( {{u}^{2} - 9}\right) ,\mathrm{d}x = \frac{2}{3}u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,则

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{{3x} + 9}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{2}{3}u{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \frac{2}{3}u\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{3}u{\mathrm{e}}^{u} - \int \frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{2}{3}u{\mathrm{e}}^{u} - \frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{u} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{{3x} + 9}}\left( {\sqrt{{3x} + 9} - 1}\right)  + C.
$$

### 习题 4-4 有理函数的积分



$$
\text{3.}\int \frac{x + 1}{{x}^{2} - {2x} + 5}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{x - 1}{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + 4}\mathrm{\;d}x + \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{1}{{\left( \frac{x - 1}{2}\right) }^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} - {2x} + 5}\right)  + \arctan \frac{x - 1}{2} + C.
$$

$$
\text{4.}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) } = \int \left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{x}{{x}^{2} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \ln \left| x\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }{{x}^{2} + 1}
$$

$$
= \ln \left| x\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right)  + C.
$$

<!-- Media -->

求下列不定积分:

1. $\int \frac{{x}^{3}}{x + 3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 2. $\int \frac{{2x} + 3}{{x}^{2} + {3x} - {10}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

3. $\int \frac{x + 1}{{x}^{2} - {2x} + 5}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 4. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }$ .

5. $\int \frac{3}{{x}^{3} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 6. $\int \frac{{x}^{2} + 1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}\left( {x - 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$ .

7. $\int \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\left( {x + 1}\right) \left( {x + 2}\right) \left( {x + 3}\right) }$ . 8. $\int \frac{{x}^{5} + {x}^{4} - 8}{{x}^{3} - x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

9. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} + x}\right) }$ . 10. $\int \frac{1}{{x}^{4} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

11. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) }$ . 12. $\int \frac{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

13. $\int \frac{-{x}^{2} - 2}{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 14. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3 + {\sin }^{2}x}$ .

15. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3 + \cos x}$ . 16. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2 + \sin x}$ .

17. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sin x + \cos x}$ . 18. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2\sin x - \cos x + 5}$ .

19. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt[3]{x + 1}}$ . 20. $\int \frac{{\left( \sqrt{x}\right) }^{3} - 1}{\sqrt{x} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

21. $\int \frac{\sqrt{x + 1} - 1}{\sqrt{x + 1} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 22. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x} + \sqrt[4]{x}}$ .

23. $\int \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x}$ . 24. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{4}}}$ .

解 1. $\int \frac{{x}^{3}}{x + 3}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {{x}^{2} - {3x} + 9 - \frac{27}{x + 3}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$= \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3} - \frac{3}{2}{x}^{2} + {9x} - {27}\ln \left| {x + 3}\right|  + C.$

2. $\int \frac{{2x} + 3}{{x}^{2} + {3x} - {10}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{x}^{2} + {3x} - {10}}\right) }{{x}^{2} + {3x} - {10}} = \ln \left| {{x}^{2} + {3x} - {10}}\right|  + C$ .

<!-- Media -->

5. $\int \frac{3}{1 + {x}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{3}{\left( {1 + x}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} - x + 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}x = \int \left( {\frac{1}{1 + x} + \frac{2 - x}{{x}^{2} - x + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \ln \left| {1 + x}\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{{\left( {x}^{2} - x + 1\right) }^{\prime }}{{x}^{2} - x + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x + \frac{3}{2}\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} - x + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \ln \left| {1 + x}\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} - x + 1}\right)  + \sqrt{3}\int \frac{1}{{\left( \frac{{2x} - 1}{\sqrt{3}}\right) }^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{{2x} - 1}{\sqrt{3}}\right)
$$

$$
= \ln \left| {1 + x}\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} - x + 1}\right)  + \sqrt{3}\arctan \frac{{2x} - 1}{\sqrt{3}} + C.
$$

$$
\text{6.}\int \frac{{x}^{2} + 1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}\left( {x - 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}x = \int \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{2\left( {x - 1}\right) } + \frac{1}{2\left( {x + 1}\right) } - \frac{1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {x - 1}\right|  + \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {x + 1}\right|  + \frac{1}{x + 1} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {{x}^{2} - 1}\right|  + \frac{1}{x + 1} + C.
$$

$$
\text{7.}\int \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\left( {x + 1}\right) \left( {x + 2}\right) \left( {x + 3}\right) } = \int \left\lbrack  {-\frac{1}{2\left( {x + 1}\right) } + \frac{2}{x + 2} - \frac{3}{2\left( {x + 3}\right) }}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {x + 1}\right|  + 2\ln \left| {x + 2}\right|  - \frac{3}{2}\ln \left| {x + 3}\right|  + C.
$$

8. $\int \frac{{x}^{5} + {x}^{4} - 8}{{x}^{3} - x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1 + \frac{8}{x} - \frac{3}{x - 1} - \frac{4}{x + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{3}}{3} + \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} + x + 8\ln \left| x\right|  - 3\ln \left| {x - 1}\right|  - 4\ln \left| {x + 1}\right|  + C.
$$

9. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} + x}\right) } = \int \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{2\left( {x + 1}\right) } - \frac{1 + x}{2\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$

2 ~ 5

$$
= \ln \left| x\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {x + 1}\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\arctan x - \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }{{x}^{2} + 1}
$$

$$
= \ln \left| x\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {x + 1}\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\arctan x - \frac{1}{4}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right)  + C.
$$

10. $\int \frac{1}{{x}^{4} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{\left( {x - 1}\right) \left( {x + 1}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{1}{x - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x - \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{1}{x + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x - \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\ln \left| \frac{x - 1}{x + 1}\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\arctan x + C.
$$

11. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) } = \int \left( {\frac{-x}{{x}^{2} + 1} + \frac{x + 1}{{x}^{2} + x + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
=  - \frac{\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }{2} + \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) }{{x}^{2} + x + 1} +
$$

$$
\frac{1}{2}\int \frac{1}{{\left( x + \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} + \frac{3}{4}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
=  - \frac{\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }{2} + \frac{\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) }{2} + \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{{2x} + 1}{\sqrt{3}} + C.
$$

12. $\int \frac{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{{x}^{2} + 1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + \int \frac{{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2}}$

$$
= \arctan x - \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 1} + C\text{.}
$$

13. $\int \frac{-{x}^{2} - 2}{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left\lbrack  {-\frac{1}{{x}^{2} + x + 1} + \frac{x - 1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$

$$
=  - \int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + x + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x + \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) }{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}} - \frac{3}{2}\int \frac{1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

令 $u = x + \frac{1}{2}$ ,并记 $a = \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{{\left( {u}^{2} + {a}^{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{1}{2{a}^{2}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{u}{{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}+\int \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{u}{2{a}^{2}\left( {{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\right) } + \frac{1}{2{a}^{2}}\int \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u,
$$

由此得

$$
\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + x + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x + \frac{3}{2}\int \frac{1}{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \int \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u + \frac{3}{2}\left\lbrack  {\frac{u}{2{a}^{2}\left( {{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\right) } + \frac{1}{2{a}^{2}}\int \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{3u}{4{a}^{2}\left( {{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\right) } + \left( {\frac{3}{4{a}^{2}} + 1}\right) \int \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{3u}{4{a}^{2}\left( {{u}^{2} + {a}^{2}}\right) } + \frac{1}{a}\left( {\frac{3}{4{a}^{2}} + 1}\right) \arctan \frac{u}{a} + {C}_{1}
$$

$$
= \frac{{2x} + 1}{2\left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) } + \frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{{2x} + 1}{\sqrt{3}} + {C}_{1},
$$

因此有

$$
\int \frac{-{x}^{2} - 2}{{\left( {x}^{2} + x + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2\left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) } - \frac{{2x} + 1}{2\left( {{x}^{2} + x + 1}\right) } -
$$

$$
\frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{{2x} + 1}{\sqrt{3}} + C
$$

$$
=  - \frac{x + 1}{{x}^{2} + x + 1} - \frac{4}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{{2x} + 1}{\sqrt{3}} + C.
$$

$$
\text{14.}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3 + {\sin }^{2}x} =  - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\cot x}\right) }{3{\csc }^{2}x + 1}\frac{u = \cot x}{} - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{3{u}^{2} + 4}
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{\sqrt{3}u}{2} + C
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{\sqrt{3}\cot x}{2} + C.
$$

15. 令 $u = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{3 + \cos x} = \int \frac{1}{3 + \frac{1 - {u}^{2}}{1 + {u}^{2}}} \cdot  \frac{2}{1 + {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \frac{1}{2 + {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\arctan \frac{u}{\sqrt{2}} + C = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\arctan \frac{\tan \frac{x}{2}}{\sqrt{2}} + C.
$$

16. 令 $u = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2 + \sin x} = \int \frac{1}{2 + \frac{2u}{1 + {u}^{2}}} \cdot  \frac{2}{1 + {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + u + 1}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \int \frac{1}{{\left( u + \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{{2u} + 1}{\sqrt{3}} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{2\tan \frac{x}{2} + 1}{\sqrt{3}} + C.
$$

17. 令 $u = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sin x + \cos x} = \int \frac{1}{1 + \frac{2u}{1 + {u}^{2}} + \frac{1 - {u}^{2}}{1 + {u}^{2}}} \cdot  \frac{2}{1 + {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{1 + u} = \ln \left| {1 + u}\right|  + C = \ln \left| {1 + \tan \frac{x}{2}}\right|  + C.
$$

18. 令 $u = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2\sin x - \cos x + 5} = \int \frac{1}{\frac{4u}{1 + {u}^{2}} - \frac{1 - {u}^{2}}{1 + {u}^{2}} + 5} \cdot  \frac{2}{1 + {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \int \frac{1}{3{u}^{2} + {2u} + 2}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}\int \frac{1}{{\left( u + \frac{1}{3}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \frac{\sqrt{5}}{3}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {u + \frac{1}{3}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}\arctan \frac{{3u} + 1}{\sqrt{5}} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}\arctan \frac{3\tan \frac{x}{2} + 1}{\sqrt{5}} + C.
$$

19. 令 $u = \sqrt[3]{x + 1}$ ,即 $x = {u}^{3} - 1$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt[3]{x + 1}} = \int \frac{3{u}^{2}}{1 + u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \left( {{3u} - 3 + \frac{3}{1 + u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{3}{2}{u}^{2} - {3u} + 3\ln \left| {1 + u}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= \frac{3}{2}\sqrt[3]{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}} - 3\sqrt[3]{x + 1} + 3\ln \left| {1 + \sqrt[3]{x + 1}}\right|  + C.
$$

20. $\int \frac{{\left( \sqrt{x}\right) }^{3} - 1}{\sqrt{x} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {x - \sqrt{x} + 1 - \frac{2}{\sqrt{x} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{2}{3}x\sqrt{x} + x - \int \frac{4t}{t + 1}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{2}{3}x\sqrt{x} + x - 4\int \left( {1 - \frac{1}{t + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}t
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{2}{3}x\sqrt{x} + x - 4\sqrt{x} + 4\ln \left( {\sqrt{x} + 1}\right)  + C.
$$

21. 令 $u = \sqrt{x + 1}$ ,即 $x = {u}^{2} - 1$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\sqrt{x + 1} - 1}{\sqrt{x + 1} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{u - 1}{u + 1} \cdot  {2u}\mathrm{\;d}u = 2\int \left( {u - 2 + \frac{2}{u + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= {u}^{2} - {4u} + 4\ln \left| {u + 1}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= x - 4\sqrt{x + 1} + 4\ln \left( {\sqrt{x + 1} + 1}\right)  + {C}_{1}\left( {{C}_{1} = C + 1}\right) .
$$

22. 令 $u = \sqrt[4]{x}$ ,即 $x = {u}^{4}$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x} + \sqrt[4]{x}} = \int \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + u} \cdot  4{u}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}u = 4\int \left( {u - 1 + \frac{1}{u + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= 2{u}^{2} - {4u} + 4\ln \left| {u + 1}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= 2\sqrt{x} - 4\sqrt[4]{x} + 4\ln \left( {\sqrt[4]{x} + 1}\right)  + C\text{.}
$$

23. 解法一

令 $u = \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}}$ ,即 $x = \frac{1 - {u}^{2}}{1 + {u}^{2}}$ ,则

$$
\int \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}} \cdot  \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x} = \int u \cdot  \frac{1 + {u}^{2}}{1 - {u}^{2}} \cdot  \frac{-{4u}}{{\left( 1 + {u}^{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \frac{-4{u}^{2}}{\left( {1 - {u}^{2}}\right) \left( {1 + {u}^{2}}\right) }\mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \int \left( {\frac{2}{1 + {u}^{2}} - \frac{1}{1 - u} - \frac{1}{1 + u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= 2\arctan u + \ln \left| {1 - u}\right|  - \ln \left| {1 + u}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= 2\arctan \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}} + \ln \left| \frac{\sqrt{1 + x} - \sqrt{1 - x}}{\sqrt{1 + x} + \sqrt{1 - x}}\right|  + C.
$$

解法二

$$
\int \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x} = \int \frac{1 - x}{x\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{x = \sin u}{}\int \frac{1 - \sin u}{\sin u}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \int \csc u\mathrm{\;d}u - \int \mathrm{d}u = \ln \left| {\csc u - \cot u}\right|  - u + C
$$

$$
= \ln \frac{1 - \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}{\left| x\right| } - \arcsin x + C.
$$

$$
\text{24.}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{4}}} = \int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} - 1}\sqrt[3]{\frac{x + 1}{x - 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x\text{,}
$$

令 $u = \sqrt[3]{\frac{x + 1}{x - 1}}$ ,即 $x = \frac{{u}^{3} + 1}{{u}^{3} - 1}$ ,得

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{4}}} = \int \frac{u}{{\left( \frac{{u}^{3} + 1}{{u}^{3} - 1}\right) }^{2} - 1} \cdot  \frac{-6{u}^{2}}{{\left( {u}^{3} - 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \frac{3}{2}\int \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
=  - \frac{3}{2}u + C =  - \frac{3}{2}\sqrt[3]{\frac{x + 1}{x - 1}} + C.
$$

### 习题 4-5 积分表的使用

利用积分表计算下列不定积分:

1. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{4{x}^{2} - 9}}$ . 2. $\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 5}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

3. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{5 - {4x} + {x}^{2}}}$ . 4. $\int \sqrt{2{x}^{2} + 9}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

5. $\int \sqrt{3{x}^{2} - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 6. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

7. $\int x\arcsin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 8. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 9\right) }^{2}}$ .

9. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\sin }^{3}x}$ . 10. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

11. $\int \sin {3x}\sin {5x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 12. $\int {\ln }^{3}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

13. $\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2}\left( {1 - x}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$ . 14. $\int \frac{\sqrt{x - 1}}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

15. $\int \frac{1}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 16. $\int \frac{1}{x\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

17. $\int \frac{x}{{\left( 2 + 3x\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 18. $\int {\cos }^{6}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

19. $\int {x}^{2}\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 20. $\int \frac{1}{2 + 5\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

21. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{{2x} - 1}}$ . 22. $\int \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

23. $\int \frac{x + 5}{{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 24. $\int \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 + x - {x}^{2}}}$ .

25. $\int \frac{{x}^{4}}{{25} + 4{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 注意:下列各题中最后括号内所标的是所用积分公式在教材上册附录 IV 积分表中的编号.

1. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{4{x}^{2} - 9}} = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {2x}\right) }{\sqrt{{\left( 2x\right) }^{2} - {3}^{2}}} = \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {{2x} + \sqrt{{\left( 2x\right) }^{2} - {3}^{2}}}\right|  + C$

$= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {{2x} + \sqrt{4{x}^{2} - 9}}\right|  + C$ .

2. $\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 5}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + {2}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x + 1}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\arctan \frac{x + 1}{2} + C$ . (19)

3. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{5 - {4x} + {x}^{2}}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {x - 2}\right) }{\sqrt{{\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} + 1}} = \ln \left\lbrack  {x - 2 + \sqrt{{\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} + 1}}\right\rbrack   + C$

$= \ln \left( {x - 2 + \sqrt{5 - {4x} + {x}^{2}}}\right)  + C$ . (3

$$
\text{4.}\int \sqrt{2{x}^{2} + 9}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\int \sqrt{{\left( \sqrt{2}x\right) }^{2} + {3}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sqrt{2}x}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\left\{  {\frac{\sqrt{2}x}{2}\sqrt{{\left( \sqrt{2}x\right) }^{2} + {3}^{2}} + \frac{{3}^{2}}{2}\ln \left\lbrack  {\sqrt{2}x + \sqrt{{\left( \sqrt{2}x\right) }^{2} + {3}^{2}}}\right\rbrack  }\right\}   + C
$$

$$
= \frac{x}{2}\sqrt{2{x}^{2} + 9} + \frac{9\sqrt{2}}{4}\ln \left( {\sqrt{2}x + \sqrt{2{x}^{2} + 9}}\right)  + C.\left( {39}\right)
$$

5. $\int \sqrt{3{x}^{2} - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\int \sqrt{{\left( \sqrt{3}x\right) }^{2} - {\left( \sqrt{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sqrt{3}x}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{\sqrt{3}x}{2}\sqrt{{\left( \sqrt{3}x\right) }^{2} - {\left( \sqrt{2}\right) }^{2}} - }\right.
$$

$$
\left. {\frac{{\left( \sqrt{2}\right) }^{2}}{2}\ln \left| {\sqrt{3}x + \sqrt{{\left( \sqrt{3}x\right) }^{2} - {\left( \sqrt{2}\right) }^{2}}}\right| }\right\rbrack   + C
$$

$$
= \frac{x}{2}\sqrt{3{x}^{2} - 2} - \frac{\sqrt{3}}{3}\ln \left| {\sqrt{3}x + \sqrt{3{x}^{2} - 2}}\right|  + C.(5 \tag{53}
$$

6. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{{2}^{2} + {1}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\left( {\sin x + 2\cos x}\right)  + C$

$$
= \frac{1}{5}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\left( {\sin x + 2\cos x}\right)  + C.\left( {129}\right)
$$

7. $\int x\arcsin \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \left( {\frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{{2}^{2}}{4}}\right) \arcsin \frac{x}{2} + \frac{x}{4}\sqrt{{2}^{2} - {x}^{2}} + C$

$$
= \left( {\frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - 1}\right) \arcsin \frac{x}{2} + \frac{x}{4}\sqrt{4 - {x}^{2}} + C.\left( {114}\right.
$$

8. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( {x}^{2} + 9\right) }^{2}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( {x}^{2} + {3}^{2}\right) }^{2}}$

$$
= \frac{x}{2\left( {2 - 1}\right) {3}^{2}\left( {{x}^{2} + {3}^{2}}\right) } + \frac{2 \times  2 - 3}{2\left( {2 - 1}\right) {3}^{2}}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + {3}^{2}}
$$

$$
= \frac{x}{{18}\left( {{x}^{2} + 9}\right) } + \frac{1}{18} \cdot  \frac{1}{3}\arctan \frac{x}{3} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{x}{{18}\left( {{x}^{2} + 9}\right) } + \frac{1}{54}\arctan \frac{x}{3} + C.\left( {{20},{19}}\right)
$$

9. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\sin }^{3}x} =  - \frac{1}{2} \cdot  \frac{\cos x}{{\sin }^{2}x} + \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin x}$

$$
=  - \frac{\cos x}{2{\sin }^{2}x} + \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {\csc x - \cot x}\right|  + C.\left( {{97},{88}}\right)
$$

10. $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{{\left( -2\right) }^{2} + {3}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\left( {-2\sin {3x} - 3\cos {3x}}\right)  + C$

$$
=  - \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}}{13}\left( {2\sin {3x} + 3\cos {3x}}\right)  + C.\left( {128}\right)
$$

11. $\int \sin {3x}\sin {5x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2\left( {3 + 5}\right) }\sin \left( {3 + 5}\right) x + \frac{1}{2\left( {3 - 5}\right) }\sin \left( {3 - 5}\right) x + C$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{16}\sin {8x} + \frac{1}{4}\sin {2x} + C.\left( {101}\right)
$$

12. $\int {\ln }^{3}x\mathrm{\;d}x = x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{3} - 3\int {\ln }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{3} - 3\left\lbrack  {x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{2} - 2\int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{3} - {3x}{\left( \ln x\right) }^{2} + 6\int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{3} - {3x}{\left( \ln x\right) }^{2} + 6\left( {x\ln x - x}\right)  + C
$$

$$
= x{\ln }^{3}x - {3x}{\ln }^{2}x + {6x}\ln x - {6x} + C.\left( {{135},{132}}\right)
$$

13. $\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2}\left( {1 - x}\right) }\mathrm{d}x =  - \frac{1}{x} - \ln \left| \frac{1 - x}{x}\right|  + C$ . (6)

14. $\int \frac{\sqrt{x - 1}}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = 2\sqrt{x - 1} - \int \frac{1}{x\sqrt{x - 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= 2\sqrt{x - 1} - 2\arctan \sqrt{x - 1} + C.\left( {{17},{15}}\right)
$$

15. $\int \frac{1}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{x}{2\left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) } + \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \frac{x}{2\left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) } + \frac{1}{2}\arctan x + C.\left( {{20},{19}}\right)
$$

16. $\int \frac{1}{x\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \arccos \frac{1}{\left| x\right| } + C.\left( {51}\right)$

17. $\int \frac{x}{{\left( 2 + 3x\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{9}\left( {\ln \left| {2 + {3x}}\right|  + \frac{2}{2 + {3x}}}\right)  + C$ . (7)

18. $\int {\cos }^{6}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{6}{\cos }^{5}x\sin x + \frac{5}{6}\int {\cos }^{4}x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{\cos }^{5}x\sin x + \frac{5}{6}\left( {\frac{1}{4}{\cos }^{3}x\sin x + \frac{3}{4}\int {\cos }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{\cos }^{5}x\sin x + \frac{5}{24}{\cos }^{3}x\sin x + \frac{5}{8}\int {\cos }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{\cos }^{5}x\sin x + \frac{5}{24}{\cos }^{3}x\sin x + \frac{5}{8}\left( {\frac{1}{2}\cos x\sin x + \frac{1}{2}\int \mathrm{d}x}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}{\cos }^{5}x\sin x + \frac{5}{24}{\cos }^{3}x\sin x + \frac{5}{16}\cos x\sin x + \frac{5}{16}x + C.\left( {96}\right)  \tag{96}
$$

19. $\int {x}^{2}\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{x}{8}\left( {2{x}^{2} - 2}\right) \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 2} - \frac{4}{8}\ln \left| {x + \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 2}}\right|  + C$

$$
= \frac{x}{4}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 2} - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {x + \sqrt{{x}^{2} - 2}}\right|  + C\text{. (56)}
$$

$$
\text{20.}\int \frac{1}{2 + 5\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{7}\sqrt{\frac{7}{3}}\ln \left| \frac{\tan \frac{x}{2} + \sqrt{\frac{7}{3}}}{\tan \frac{x}{2} - \sqrt{\frac{7}{3}}}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{21}}\ln \left| \frac{\sqrt{3}\tan \frac{x}{2} + \sqrt{7}}{\sqrt{3}\tan \frac{x}{2} - \sqrt{7}}\right|  + C.\left( {106}\right)
$$

21. $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{{2x} - 1}} =  - \frac{\sqrt{{2x} - 1}}{-x} - \frac{2}{-2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{{2x} - 1}}$

$$
= \frac{\sqrt{{2x} - 1}}{x} + 2\arctan \sqrt{{2x} - 1} + C.\left( {{16},{15}}\right)
$$

22. 解法一

$$
\int \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1 - x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x - \int \frac{x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \arcsin x + \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} + C.\left( {{59},{61}}\right)
$$

解法二

$$
\int \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \left( {x + 1}\right) \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{1 + x}} - 2\arcsin \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{2}} + C
$$

$$
= \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} - 2\arcsin \sqrt{\frac{1 - x}{2}} + C.\left( {80}\right)
$$

23. $\int \frac{x + 5}{{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{x}{{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x + 5\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\right|  - \frac{-2}{2}\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x + 5\int \frac{1}{{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\right|  + 6 \cdot  \frac{1}{\sqrt{{\left( -2\right) }^{2} - 4 \cdot  1 \cdot  \left( {-1}\right) }}.
$$

$$
\ln \left| \frac{{2x} - 2 - \sqrt{{\left( -2\right) }^{2} - 4 \cdot  1 \cdot  \left( {-1}\right) }}{{2x} - 2 + \sqrt{{\left( -2\right) }^{2} - 4 \cdot  1 \cdot  \left( {-1}\right) }}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1}\right|  + \frac{3}{\sqrt{2}}\ln \left| \frac{x - \left( {\sqrt{2} + 1}\right) }{x + \left( {\sqrt{2} - 1}\right) }\right|  + C.\left( {{30},{29}}\right)  \tag{30,29}
$$

24. $\int \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 + x - {x}^{2}}} =  - \sqrt{1 + x - {x}^{2}} + \frac{1}{2}\arcsin \frac{{2x} - 1}{\sqrt{5}} + C$ . (78)

25. $\int \frac{{x}^{4}}{{25} + 4{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \left( {\frac{1}{4}{x}^{2} - \frac{25}{16} + \frac{625}{16} \cdot  \frac{1}{{25} + 4{x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{3}}{12} - \frac{25}{16}x + \frac{625}{32}\int \frac{1}{{5}^{2} + {\left( 2x\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {2x}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{3}}{12} - \frac{25}{16}x + \frac{625}{32} \cdot  \frac{1}{5}\arctan \frac{2x}{5} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{3}}{12} - \frac{25}{16}x + \frac{125}{32}\arctan \frac{2x}{5} + C.
$$

### 总习题四

21. 填空：

(1) $\int {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x =$ _____；

( 2 ) $\int \frac{x + 5}{{x}^{2} - {6x} + {13}}\mathrm{\;d}x =$ _____.

解 (1) $\int {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right)  = {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 3\int {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right)$

$$
= {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 3\left\lbrack  {{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}-\int {2x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right) }\right\rbrack   = {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 3{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 6\left( {x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}-\int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)
$$

$= {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 3{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {6x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 6{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + C,$

因此,应填 ${x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 3{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {6x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 6{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + C$ .

(2) $\int \frac{x + 5}{{x}^{2} - {6x} + {13}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{{\left( {x}^{2} - 6x + {13}\right) }^{\prime }}{{x}^{2} - {6x} + {13}}\mathrm{\;d}x + \int \frac{8}{{x}^{2} - {6x} + {13}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} - {6x} + {13}}\right)  + \int \frac{8}{{\left( x - 3\right) }^{2} + 4}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} - {6x} + {13}}\right)  + 4\arctan \frac{x - 3}{2} + C,
$$

因此,应填 $\frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} - {6x} + {13}}\right)  + 4\arctan \frac{x - 3}{2} + C$ .

2. 以下两题中给出了四个结论, 从中选出一个正确的结论:

(1)已知 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x\left( {1 + 2\ln x}\right) }$ ,且 $f\left( 1\right)  = 1$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 等于(   ).

(A) $\ln \left( {1 + 2\ln x}\right)  + 1$ (B) $\frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + 2\ln x}\right)  + 1$

(C) $\frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + 2\ln x}\right)  + \frac{1}{2}$ (D) $2\ln \left( {1 + 2\ln x}\right)  + 1$

(2)在下列等式中,正确的结果是(   ).

(A) $\int {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( x\right)$ (B) $\int \mathrm{d}f\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)$

(C) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\int f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( x\right)$ (D) $\mathrm{d}\int f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( x\right)$

解 (1) 由微积分基本定理, 有

$$
f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 1\right)  = {\int }_{1}^{x}{f}^{\prime }\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{1}^{x}\frac{1}{t\left( {1 + 2\ln t}\right) }\mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{1}^{x}\frac{1}{1 + 2\ln t}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {1 + 2\ln t}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + 2\ln t\right) \right\rbrack  }_{1}^{x} = \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + 2\ln x}\right) ,
$$

根据条件 $f\left( 1\right)  = 1$ ,得 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + 2\ln x}\right)  + 1$ . 故选 (B).

(2)根据微分运算与积分运算的关系,可知

$$
\int \mathrm{d}f\left( x\right)  = \int {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( x\right)  + C,
$$

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\int f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( x\right) ,
$$

$$
\mathrm{d}\int f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \left( {\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\int f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x,
$$

故选 (C).

3. 已知 $\frac{\sin x}{x}$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的一个原函数,求 $\int {x}^{3}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

解 根据条件,有 $\int f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{\sin x}{x} + C$ ,即 $f\left( x\right)  = {\left( \frac{\sin x}{x}\right) }^{\prime } = \frac{x\cos x - \sin x}{{x}^{2}}$ ,因

此

$$
\int {x}^{3}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {x}^{3}f\left( x\right)  - \int 3{x}^{2}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = x\left( {x\cos x - \sin x}\right)  - 3\int {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{\sin x}{x}\right)
$$

$$
= {x}^{2}\cos x - x\sin x - 3\left( {{x}^{2} \cdot  \frac{\sin x}{x}-\int \frac{\sin x}{x} \cdot  {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)
$$

$$
= {x}^{2}\cos x - {4x}\sin x - 6\cos x + C\text{.}
$$

14. 求下列不定积分 (其中 $a,b$ 为常数):

(1) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}$ ; (2) $\int \frac{x}{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(3) $\int \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{6} - {x}^{6}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {a > 0}\right)$ ; (4) $\int \frac{1 + \cos x}{x + \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(5) $\int \frac{\ln \ln x}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (6) $\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{1 + {\sin }^{4}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(7) $\int {\tan }^{4}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (8) $\int \sin x\sin {2x}\sin {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(9) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\left( {{x}^{6} + 4}\right) }$ ; ( 10 ) $\int \sqrt{\frac{a + x}{a - x}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {a > 0}\right)$ ；

(11) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }}$ ; (12) $\int x{\cos }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(13) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (14) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}}$ ;

(15) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}$ ; (16) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( {a}^{2} - {x}^{2}\right) }^{5/2}}$ ;

(17) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{4}\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}$ ; (18) $\int \sqrt{x}\sin \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(19) $\int \ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (20) $\int \frac{{\sin }^{2}x}{{\cos }^{3}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(21) $\int \arctan \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (22) $\int \frac{\sqrt{1 + \cos x}}{\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(23) $\int \frac{{x}^{3}}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{8}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (24) $\int \frac{{x}^{11}}{{x}^{8} + 3{x}^{4} + 2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(25) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{16} - {x}^{4}}$ ; (26) $\int \frac{\sin x}{1 + \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(27) $\int \frac{x + \sin x}{1 + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (28) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\frac{x{\cos }^{3}x - \sin x}{{\cos }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(29) $\int \frac{\sqrt[3]{x}}{x\left( {\sqrt{x} + \sqrt[3]{x}}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$ ; (30) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( 1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right) }^{2}}$ ;

(31) $\int \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{3x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{{\mathrm{e}}^{4x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (32) $\int \frac{x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(33) $\int {\ln }^{2}\left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (34) $\int \frac{\ln x}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(35) $\int \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\arcsin x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (36) $\int \frac{{x}^{3}\arccos x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(37) $\int \frac{\cot x}{1 + \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (38) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\sin }^{3}x\cos x}$ ;

(39) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {2 + \cos x}\right) \sin x}$ ; (40) $\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 (1) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}} = \int \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1} = \frac{1}{2}\int \left( {\frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1} - \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \frac{\left| {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1\right| }{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} + C.
$$

( 2 ) $\int \frac{x}{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{u = 1 - x}{}\int \left( {\frac{1}{{u}^{2}} - \frac{1}{{u}^{3}}}\right) \mathrm{d}u =  - \frac{1}{u} + \frac{1}{2{u}^{2}} + C$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{1 - x} + \frac{1}{2{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}} + C.
$$

(3) $\int \frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{6} - {x}^{6}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {x}^{3}\right) }{3\left( {{a}^{6} - {x}^{6}}\right) }\frac{u = {x}^{3}}{}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{3\left( {{a}^{6} - {u}^{2}}\right) }$

$$
= \frac{1}{6{a}^{3}}\int \left( {\frac{1}{{a}^{3} + u} + \frac{1}{{a}^{3} - u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6{a}^{3}}\ln \left| \frac{{a}^{3} + u}{{a}^{3} - u}\right|  + C = \frac{1}{6{a}^{3}}\ln \left| \frac{{a}^{3} + {x}^{3}}{{a}^{3} - {x}^{3}}\right|  + C.
$$

(4) $\int \frac{1 + \cos x}{x + \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {x + \sin x}\right) }{x + \sin x} = \ln \left| {x + \sin x}\right|  + C$ .

(5) $\int \frac{\ln \ln x}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \ln \ln x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\ln x}\right)  = \ln x\ln \ln x - \int \ln x \cdot  \frac{1}{x\ln x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \ln x\left( {\ln \ln x - 1}\right)  + C\text{.}
$$

(6) $\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{1 + {\sin }^{4}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{\sin }^{2}x}\right) }{1 + {\sin }^{4}x} = \frac{\arctan \left( {{\sin }^{2}x}\right) }{2} + C$ .

(7) $\int {\tan }^{4}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {\tan }^{2}x\left( {{\sec }^{2}x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \int {\tan }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\tan x}\right)  - \int \left( {{\sec }^{2}x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}{\tan }^{3}x - \tan x + x + C.
$$

(8) $\int \sin x\sin {2x}\sin {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{2}\left( {\cos x - \cos {3x}}\right) \sin {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\int \cos x\sin {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x - \frac{1}{2}\int \cos {3x}\sin {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\int \left( {\sin {2x} + \sin {4x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{12}{\sin }^{2}{3x}
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{16}\cos {4x} - \frac{1}{8}\cos {2x} - \frac{1}{12}{\sin }^{2}{3x} + C.
$$

(9) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\left( {{x}^{6} + 4}\right) } = \frac{1}{}\int \frac{-{u}^{5}\mathrm{\;d}u}{1 + 4{u}^{6}} =  - \frac{1}{24}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {1 + 4{u}^{6}}\right) }{1 + 4{u}^{6}}$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{24}\ln \left( {1 + 4{u}^{6}}\right)  + C =  - \frac{1}{24}\ln \frac{{x}^{6} + 4}{{x}^{6}} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\ln \left| x\right|  - \frac{1}{24}\ln \left( {{x}^{6} + 4}\right)  + C.
$$

(10)解法一

$$
\int \sqrt{\frac{a + x}{a - x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{a + x}{\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = a\int \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - {\left( \frac{x}{a}\right) }^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{x}{a}\right)  - \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right) }{\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}
$$

$$
= a\arcsin \frac{x}{a} - \sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}} + C.
$$

解法二 令 $u = \sqrt{\frac{a + x}{a - x}}$ ,即 $x = a\frac{{u}^{2} - 1}{{u}^{2} + 1}$ ,则

$$
\int \sqrt{\frac{a + x}{a - x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int u \cdot  \frac{4au}{{\left( 1 + {u}^{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int  - {2au}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{1}{1 + {u}^{2}}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{2au}{1 + {u}^{2}} + \int \frac{2a}{1 + {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
=  - \frac{2au}{1 + {u}^{2}} + {2a}\arctan u + C
$$

$$
= \left( {x - a}\right) \sqrt{\frac{a + x}{a - x}} + {2a}\arctan \sqrt{\frac{a + x}{a - x}} + C
$$

$$
=  - \sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}} + {2a}\arctan \sqrt{\frac{a + x}{a - x}} + C.
$$

(11)解法一

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{{\left( x + \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} - {\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2}}}
$$

$$
\overset{x =  - \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{2}\sec u}{ = }\int \sec u\mathrm{\;d}u = \ln \left| {\sec u + \tan u}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= \ln \left| {{2x} + 1 + 2\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }}\right|  + C\text{.}
$$

解法二 当 $x > 0$ 时,因为 $\frac{1}{\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }} = \frac{1}{x}\sqrt{\frac{x}{1 + x}}$ ,故令 $u = \sqrt{\frac{x}{1 + x}}$ ,即 $x = \frac{{u}^{2}}{1 - {u}^{2}}$ ,则

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }} = \int \frac{2}{1 - {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \left( {\frac{1}{1 - u} + \frac{1}{1 + u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \ln \left| \frac{1 + u}{1 - u}\right|  + C = \ln \left| \frac{\sqrt{1 + x} + \sqrt{x}}{\sqrt{1 + x} - \sqrt{x}}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= \ln \left| {{2x} + 1 + 2\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }}\right|  + C\text{,}
$$

当 $x <  - 1$ 时,同样可得 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }} = \ln \left| {{2x} + 1 + 2\sqrt{x\left( {1 + x}\right) }}\right|  + C$ .

$$
\text{)}\int x{\cos }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\int x\left( {1 + \cos {2x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{4}\int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {{2x} + \sin {2x}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{x\left( {{2x} + \sin {2x}}\right) }{4} - \frac{1}{4}\int \left( {{2x} + \sin {2x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} + \frac{x\sin {2x}}{4} + \frac{\cos {2x}}{8} + C.
$$

(13) 当 $a \neq  0$ 时,

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{a}\int \cos {bx}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{a}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx} + \frac{b}{a}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\sin {bx}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{a}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx} + \frac{b}{{a}^{2}}\int \sin {bx}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{a}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx} + \frac{b}{{a}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\sin {bx} - \frac{{b}^{2}}{{a}^{2}}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx}\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

因此有

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{{a}^{2} + {b}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\left( {a\cos {bx} + b\sin {bx}}\right)  + C,
$$

当 $a = 0$ 时,

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\cos {bx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \left\{  \begin{matrix} \frac{\sin {bx}}{b} + C, & b \neq  0, \\  x + C, & b = 0. \end{matrix}\right.
$$

(14)令 $u = \sqrt{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}$ ,即作换元 $x = \ln \left( {{u}^{2} - 1}\right)$ ,得

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}} = \int \frac{2\mathrm{\;d}u}{{u}^{2} - 1} = \ln \left| \frac{u - 1}{u + 1}\right|  + C = \ln \frac{\sqrt{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}} - 1}{\sqrt{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}} + 1} + C.
$$

$\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}} = \frac{x = \frac{1}{u}}{} - \int \frac{u\mathrm{\;d}u}{\sqrt{1 - {u}^{2}}} = \sqrt{1 - {u}^{2}} + C = \frac{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - 1}}{x} + C,$

易知当 $x < 0$ 和 $x > 0$ 时的结果相同.

( 16 )设 $x = a\sin u\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < u < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 $\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}} = a\cos u,\mathrm{\;d}x = a\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,

于是

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( {a}^{2} - {x}^{2}\right) }^{5/2}} = \frac{1}{{a}^{4}}\int {\sec }^{4}u\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{1}{{a}^{4}}\int \left( {{\tan }^{2}u + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\tan u}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{{\tan }^{3}u}{3{a}^{4}} + \frac{\tan u}{{a}^{4}} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{3{a}^{4}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{{x}^{3}}{\sqrt{{\left( {a}^{2} - {x}^{2}\right) }^{3}}} + \frac{3x}{\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}}\right\rbrack   + C.
$$

17) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{4}\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\overset{x = \frac{1}{u}}{ = }\int \frac{-{u}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}u}{\sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}}} =  - \int \left( {u\sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}} - \frac{u}{\sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}}}}\right) \mathrm{d}u$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{3}{\left( 1 + {u}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}} + \sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}} + C
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{3}\frac{\sqrt{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{3}}}{{x}^{3}} + \frac{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}{x} + C,
$$

易知当 $x < 0$ 和 $x > 0$ 时结果相同. (18) $\int \sqrt{x}\sin \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x\overset{x = {u}^{2}}{ = }\int 2{u}^{2}\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \int 2{u}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos u}\right)$

$$
=  - 2{u}^{2}\cos u + \int {4u}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
=  - 2{u}^{2}\cos u + \int {4u}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin u}\right)
$$

$$
=  - 2{u}^{2}\cos u + {4u}\sin u - \int 4\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
=  - 2{u}^{2}\cos u + {4u}\sin u + 4\cos u + C
$$

$$
=  - {2x}\cos \sqrt{x} + 4\sqrt{x}\sin \sqrt{x} + 4\cos \sqrt{x} + C\text{.}
$$

(19) $\int \ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = x\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)  - \int \frac{2{x}^{2}}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= x\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)  - {2x} + 2\arctan x + C.
$$

(20) $\int \frac{{\sin }^{2}x}{{\cos }^{3}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {\tan }^{2}x\sec x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int {\sec }^{3}x\mathrm{\;d}x - \int \sec x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \left( {\frac{1}{2}\sec x\tan x + \frac{1}{2}\int \sec x\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)  - \int \sec x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\sec x\tan x - \frac{1}{2}\int \sec x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\sec x\tan x - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {\sec x + \tan x}\right|  + C.
$$

$$
\int \arctan \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \arctan \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {1 + x}\right)  = \left( {1 + x}\right) \arctan \sqrt{x} - \int \frac{1}{2\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \left( {1 + x}\right) \arctan \sqrt{x} - \sqrt{x} + C.
$$

(22) $\int \frac{\sqrt{1 + \cos x}}{\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\sqrt{2}\left| {\cos \frac{x}{2}}\right| }{2\sin \frac{x}{2}\cos \frac{x}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  \pm  \sqrt{2}\int \csc \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{x}{2}\right)$

$$
=  \pm  \sqrt{2}\ln \left| {\csc \frac{x}{2} - \cot \frac{x}{2}}\right|  + C,
$$

上式当 $\cos \frac{x}{2} > 0$ 时取正,当 $\cos \frac{x}{2} < 0$ 时取负.

当 $\cos \frac{x}{2} > 0$ 时, $\ln \left| {\csc \frac{x}{2} - \cot \frac{x}{2}}\right|  = \ln \frac{1 - \cos \frac{x}{2}}{\left| \sin \frac{x}{2}\right| }$

$$
= \ln \left( {\left| {\csc \frac{x}{2}}\right|  - \left| {\cot \frac{x}{2}}\right| }\right) ,
$$

当 $\cos \frac{x}{2} < 0$ 时, $\ln \left| {\csc \frac{x}{2} - \cot \frac{x}{2}}\right|  = \ln \frac{1 - \cos \frac{x}{2}}{\left| \sin \frac{x}{2}\right| }$

$$
= \ln \left( {\left| {\csc \frac{x}{2}}\right|  + \left| {\cot \frac{x}{2}}\right| }\right)  =  - \ln \left( {\left| {\csc \frac{x}{2}}\right|  - \left| {\cot \frac{x}{2}}\right| }\right) ,
$$

因此有

$$
\int \frac{\sqrt{1 + \cos x}}{\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \sqrt{2}\ln \left( {\left| {\csc \frac{x}{2}}\right|  - \left| {\cot \frac{x}{2}}\right| }\right)  + C.
$$

) $\int \frac{{x}^{3}}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{8}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{1}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{8}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x}^{4}\right) \overset{u = {x}^{4}}{ = }\frac{1}{4}\int \frac{1}{{\left( 1 + {u}^{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,

设 $u = \tan t\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < t < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 $1 + {u}^{2} = {\sec }^{2}t,\mathrm{\;d}u = {\sec }^{2}t\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,于是

$$
\text{ 原式 } = \frac{1}{4}\int {\cos }^{2}t\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{{2t} + \sin {2t}}{16} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{\arctan {x}^{4}}{8} + \frac{{x}^{4}}{8\left( {1 + {x}^{8}}\right) } + C.
$$

(24) $\int \frac{{x}^{11}}{{x}^{8} + 3{x}^{4} + 2}\mathrm{\;d}x\overset{u = {x}^{4}}{ = }\frac{1}{4}\int \frac{{u}^{2}}{{u}^{2} + {3u} + 2}\mathrm{\;d}u$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\int \left( {1 + \frac{1}{u + 1} - \frac{4}{u + 2}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}u + \frac{1}{4}\ln \left| {1 + u}\right|  - \ln \left| {2 + u}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{4}}{4} + \ln \frac{\sqrt[4]{1 + {x}^{4}}}{2 + {x}^{4}} + C.
$$

( 25 ) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{16} - {x}^{4}} = \int \frac{1}{\left( {2 - x}\right) \left( {2 + x}\right) \left( {4 + {x}^{2}}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \int \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{{32}\left( {2 - x}\right) } + \frac{1}{{32}\left( {2 + x}\right) } + \frac{1}{8\left( {4 + {x}^{2}}\right) }}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{32}\ln \left| \frac{2 + x}{2 - x}\right|  + \frac{1}{16}\arctan \frac{x}{2} + C.
$$

( 26 )解法一

令 $u = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ,得

$$
\int \frac{\sin x}{1 + \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{4u}{{\left( 1 + u\right) }^{2}\left( {1 + {u}^{2}}\right) }\mathrm{d}u = \int \left\lbrack  {\frac{-2}{{\left( 1 + u\right) }^{2}} + \frac{2}{1 + {u}^{2}}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{1 + u} + 2\arctan u + C = \frac{2}{1 + \tan \frac{x}{2}} + x + C.
$$

解法二

$$
\int \frac{\sin x}{1 + \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\sin x\left( {1 - \sin x}\right) }{{\cos }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
=  - \int \frac{1}{{\cos }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos x}\right)  - \int \left( {{\sec }^{2}x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \sec x - \tan x + x + C\text{.}
$$

( 27 ) $\int \frac{x + \sin x}{1 + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{x}{2}{\sec }^{2}\frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x + \int \tan \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\tan \frac{x}{2}}\right)  + \int \tan \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= x\tan \frac{x}{2} + C\text{.}
$$

(28) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\frac{x{\cos }^{3}x - \sin x}{{\cos }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int x{\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\tan x\sec x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\right)  - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sec x}\right)
$$

$$
= x{\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x} - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x - \left( {\sec x{\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}-\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)
$$

$$
= \left( {x - \sec x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x} + C\text{.}
$$

(29) $\int \frac{\sqrt[3]{x}}{x\left( {\sqrt{x} + \sqrt[3]{x}}\right) }\mathrm{d}x\overset{x = {u}^{6}}{ = }\int \frac{6}{u\left( {u + 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}u = 6\int \left( {\frac{1}{u} - \frac{1}{u + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u$

$$
= 6\ln \left| \frac{u}{1 + u}\right|  + C = \ln \frac{x}{{\left( \sqrt[6]{x} + 1\right) }^{6}} + C.
$$

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( 1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\right) }^{2}} = \frac{x = \ln u}{}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{u{\left( 1 + u\right) }^{2}} = \int \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{u} - \frac{1}{1 + u} - \frac{1}{{\left( 1 + u\right) }^{2}}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \ln u - \ln \left( {1 + u}\right)  + \frac{1}{1 + u} + C
$$

$$
= x - \ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right)  + \frac{1}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}} + C.
$$

(31) $\int \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{3x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{{\mathrm{e}}^{4x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right) }{{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right) }^{2} + 1}$

$$
= \arctan \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right)  + C.
$$

(32)$\int \frac{x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int x\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1}\right)  =  - \frac{x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} + \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1}$

$$
=  - \frac{x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} + \int \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}
$$

$$
=  - \frac{x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} - \ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right)  + C.
$$

$$
\int {\ln }^{2}\left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = x{\ln }^{2}\left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right)  - \int \frac{{2x}\ln \left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right) }{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= x{\ln }^{2}\left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right)  - \int 2\ln \left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}\right)
$$

$$
= x{\ln }^{2}\left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right)  - 2\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}\ln \left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right)  + {2x} + C.
$$

(34) $\int \frac{\ln x}{{\left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x\overset{x = \frac{1}{u}}{ = }\int \frac{u\ln u}{{\left( 1 + {u}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \int \ln u\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\left( 1 + {u}^{2}\right) }^{-\frac{1}{2}}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{\ln u}{\sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}}} + \int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{u\sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}}}
$$

$$
= \frac{x\ln x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}} - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}
$$

$$
= \frac{x\ln x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}} - \ln \left( {x + \sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right)  + C.
$$

(35) 设 $x = \sin u\left( {-\frac{\pi }{2} < u < \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)$ ,则 $\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} = \cos u,\mathrm{\;d}x = \cos u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,于是

$$
\int \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\arcsin x\mathrm{\;d}x = \int u{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{1}{2}\int u\left( {1 + \cos {2u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\int u\mathrm{\;d}\left( {{2u} + \sin {2u}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{u\left( {{2u} + \sin {2u}}\right) }{4} - \frac{1}{4}\int \left( {{2u} + \sin {2u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{{u}^{2}}{4} + \frac{u}{4}\sin {2u} - \frac{{\sin }^{2}u}{4} + C
$$

$$
= \frac{{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}}{4} + \frac{x}{2}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\arcsin x - \frac{{x}^{2}}{4} + C.
$$

(36) 设 $x = \cos u\left( {0 < u < \pi }\right)$ ,则 $\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} = \sin u,\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \sin u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,于是

$$
\int \frac{{x}^{3}\arccos x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int u{\cos }^{3}u\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \int u\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin u - \frac{1}{3}{\sin }^{3}u}\right)
$$

$$
=  - u\left( {\sin u - \frac{1}{3}{\sin }^{3}u}\right)  + \int \left( {\sin u - \frac{1}{3}{\sin }^{3}u}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
=  - u\left( {\sin u - \frac{1}{3}{\sin }^{3}u}\right)  - \frac{1}{3}\int \left( {2 + {\cos }^{2}u}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\cos u}\right)
$$

$$
=  - u\left( {\sin u - \frac{1}{3}{\sin }^{3}u}\right)  - \frac{2}{3}\cos u - \frac{1}{9}{\cos }^{3}u + C
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{3}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\left( {2 + {x}^{2}}\right) \arccos x - \frac{1}{9}x\left( {6 + {x}^{2}}\right)  + C.
$$

$$
\int \frac{\cot x}{1 + \sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\cos x}{\sin x\left( {1 + \sin x}\right) }\mathrm{d}x = \int \left( {\frac{1}{\sin x} - \frac{1}{1 + \sin x}}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\sin x}\right)
$$

$$
= \ln \left| \frac{\sin x}{1 + \sin x}\right|  + C.
$$

$\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\sin }^{3}x\cos x} =  - \int \cot x{\sec }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cot x}\right) \overset{u = \cot x}{ = } - \int u\left( {1 + \frac{1}{{u}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}u$

$$
=  - \frac{{u}^{2}}{2} - \ln \left| u\right|  + C =  - \frac{{\cot }^{2}x}{2} - \ln \left| {\cot x}\right|  + C.
$$

(39) $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {2 + \cos x}\right) \sin x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\cos x}\right) }{\left( {2 + \cos x}\right) \left( {{\cos }^{2}x - 1}\right) }$

$$
\overset{u = \cos x}{ = }\int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\left( {2 + u}\right) \left( {{u}^{2} - 1}\right) }
$$

$$
= \int \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{6\left( {u - 1}\right) } - \frac{1}{2\left( {u + 1}\right) } + \frac{1}{3\left( {u + 2}\right) }}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}\ln \left| {u - 1}\right|  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {u + 1}\right|  + \frac{1}{3}\ln \left| {u + 2}\right|  + C
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{6}\ln \left( {1 - \cos x}\right)  - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + \cos x}\right)  + \frac{1}{3}\ln \left( {2 + \cos x}\right)  + C.
$$

(40)解法一

$$
\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\frac{1}{2}{\left( \sin x + \cos x\right) }^{2} - \frac{1}{2}}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\int \left( {\sin x + \cos x}\right) \mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{1}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\left( {-\cos x + \sin x}\right)  - \frac{1}{2}\int \frac{1}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x\text{,}
$$

令 $u = \tan \frac{x}{2}$ ,则 $\sin x = \frac{2u}{1 + {u}^{2}},\cos x = \frac{1 - {u}^{2}}{1 + {u}^{2}},\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{2}{1 + {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,故有

$$
\int \frac{1}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{2}{{2u} + 1 - {u}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \int \frac{2}{{\left( u - 1\right) }^{2} - {\left( \sqrt{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\int \frac{1}{u - 1 - \sqrt{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u + \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\int \frac{1}{u - 1 + \sqrt{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\ln \left| \frac{u - 1 + \sqrt{2}}{u - 1 - \sqrt{2}}\right|  + {C}^{\prime },
$$

因此有

$$
\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right)  - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{2}}\ln \left| \frac{\tan \frac{x}{2} - 1 + \sqrt{2}}{\tan \frac{x}{2} - 1 - \sqrt{2}}\right|  + C.
$$

解法二

$$
\int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{\sin x + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\sin x\cos x}{\sqrt{2}\sin \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) }\mathrm{d}x\overset{u = x + \frac{\pi }{4}}{ = }\int \frac{2{\sin }^{2}u - 1}{2\sqrt{2}\sin u}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\int \sin u\mathrm{\;d}u - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{2}}\int \csc u\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
=  - \frac{\cos \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) }{\sqrt{2}} - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{2}}\ln \left| {\csc \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right)  - \cot \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) }\right|  + C.
$$

## 第五章 定积分

### 习题 5-1 定积分的概念与性质


2 -1 . 利用定积分定义计算由抛物线 $y = {x}^{2} + 1$ ,两直线 $x = a$ 、 $x = b\left( {b > a}\right)$ 及 $x$ 轴所围成的图形的面积.

解 由于函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} + 1$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,因此可积,为计算方便,不妨把 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 分成 $n$ 等份,则分点为 ${x}_{i} = a + \frac{i\left( {b - a}\right) }{n}\left( {i = 0,1,2,\cdots ,n}\right)$ ,每个小区间长度为 $\Delta {x}_{i} = \frac{b - a}{n}$ ,取 ${\xi }_{i}$ 为小区间的右端点 ${x}_{i}$ ,则

$$
\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}f\left( {\xi }_{i}\right) \Delta {x}_{i}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\left\lbrack  {{\left( a + \frac{i\left( {b - a}\right) }{n}\right) }^{2} + 1}\right\rbrack  \frac{b - a}{n}
$$

$$
= \frac{b - a}{n}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\left( {{a}^{2} + 1}\right)  + 2\frac{a{\left( b - a\right) }^{2}}{{n}^{2}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}i + \frac{{\left( b - a\right) }^{3}}{{n}^{3}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{i}^{2}
$$

$$
= \left( {b - a}\right) \left( {{a}^{2} + 1}\right)  + a{\left( b - a\right) }^{2}\frac{\left( n + 1\right) }{n} + {\left( b - a\right) }^{3}\frac{\left( {n + 1}\right) \left( {{2n} + 1}\right) }{6{n}^{2}}.
$$

当 $n \rightarrow  \infty$ 时,上式极限为

$$
\left( {b - a}\right) \left( {{a}^{2} + 1}\right)  + a{\left( b - a\right) }^{2} + \frac{1}{3}{\left( b - a\right) }^{3} = \frac{{b}^{3} - {a}^{3}}{3} + b - a,
$$

即为所求图形的面积.

8° 2. 利用定积分定义计算下列积分:

(1) ${\int }_{a}^{b}x\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {a < b}\right)$ ; (2) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 由于被积函数在积分区间上连续,因此把积分区间分成 $n$ 等份,并取 ${\xi }_{i}$ 为小区间的右端点, 得到

(1) ${\int }_{a}^{b}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\left\lbrack  {a + \frac{i\left( {b - a}\right) }{n}}\right\rbrack  \frac{b - a}{n}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left\lbrack  {a\left( {b - a}\right)  + \frac{{\left( b - a\right) }^{2}}{{n}^{2}}\frac{n\left( {n + 1}\right) }{2}}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= a\left( {b - a}\right)  + \frac{{\left( b - a\right) }^{2}}{2} = \frac{{b}^{2} - {a}^{2}}{2}.
$$

(2) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\frac{1}{n}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{i}{n}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{n}}\right) }^{n + 1} - 1}{n\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{n}} - 1}\right) }$

$$
= \frac{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{n + 1}{n}} - 1}\right) }{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}n\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{n}} - 1}\right) } = \mathrm{e} - 1.
$$

3. 利用定积分的几何意义, 证明下列等式:

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x = 1$ ; (2) ${\int }_{0}^{1}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{\pi }{4}$ ；

(3) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ ; (4) ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

证 (1)根据定积分的几何意义,定积分 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 表示由直线 $y = {2x}\text{、}x = 1$ 及 $x$ 轴围成的图形的面积,该图形是三角形,底边长为 1,高为 2,因此面积为 1,即 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x = 1$ .

( 2 )根据定积分的几何意义,定积分 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 表示的是由曲线 $y = \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}$ 以及 $x$ 轴、 $y$ 轴围成的在第 I 象限内的图形面积,即单位圆的四分之一的图形,因此有 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{\pi }{4}$ .

(3)由于函数 $y = \sin x$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack$ 上非负,在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-\pi ,0}\right\rbrack$ 上非正. 根据定积分的几何意义,定积分 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 表示曲线 $y = \sin x\left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack  }\right)$ 与 $x$ 轴所围成的图形 ${D}_{1}$ 的面积减去曲线 $y = \sin x\left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {-\pi ,0}\right\rbrack  }\right)$ 与 $x$ 轴所围成的图形 ${D}_{2}$ 的面积,显然图形 ${D}_{1}$ 与 ${D}_{2}$ 的面积是相等的,因此有 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

(4)由于函数 $y = \cos x$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-\frac{\pi }{2},\frac{\pi }{2}}\right\rbrack$ 上非负. 根据定积分的几何意义,定积分 ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 表示曲线 $y = \cos x\left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,\frac{\pi }{2}}\right\rbrack  }\right)$ 与 $x$ 轴和 $y$ 轴所围成的图形 ${D}_{1}$ 的面积加上曲线 $y = \cos x\left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {-\frac{\pi }{2},0}\right\rbrack  }\right)$ 与 $x$ 轴和 $y$ 轴所围成的图形 ${D}_{2}$ 的面积,而图形 ${D}_{1}$ 的面积和图形 ${D}_{2}$ 的面积显然相等,因此有 ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

14. 利用定积分的几何意义, 求下列积分:

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{t}x\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {t > 0}\right)$ ; (2) ${\int }_{-2}^{4}\left( {\frac{x}{2} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{-1}^{2}\left| x\right| \mathrm{d}x$ ; (4) ${\int }_{-3}^{3}\sqrt{9 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 (1) 根据定积分的几何意义, ${\int }_{0}^{t}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 表示的是由直线 $y = x,x = t$ 以及 $x$ 轴所围成的直角三角形面积,该直角三角形的两条直角边的长均为 $t$ ,因此面积为 $\frac{{t}^{2}}{2}$ ,故有 ${\int }_{0}^{t}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{{t}^{2}}{2}$ .

( 2 )根据定积分的几何意义, ${\int }_{-2}^{4}\left( {\frac{x}{2} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 表示的是由直线 $y = \frac{x}{2} + 3,x =  - 2,x =$ 4 以及 $x$ 轴所围成的梯形的面积,该梯形的两底长分别为 $\frac{-2}{2} + 3 = 2$ 和 $\frac{4}{2} + 3 = 5$ ,梯形的高为 $4 - \left( {-2}\right)  = 6$ ,因此面积为 21 . 故有 ${\int }_{-2}^{4}\left( {\frac{x}{2} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {21}$ .

(3)根据定积分的几何意义, ${\int }_{-1}^{2}\left| x\right| \mathrm{d}x$ 表示的是由折线 $y = \left| x\right|$ 和直线 $x =$ $- 1,x = 2$ 以及 $x$ 轴所围成的图形的面积. 该图形由两个等腰直角三角形组成,一个由直线 $y =  - x,x =  - 1$ 和 $x$ 轴所围成,其直角边长为 1,面积为 $\frac{1}{2}$ ; 另一个由直线 $y =$ $x,x = 2$ 和 $x$ 轴所围成,其直角边长为 2,面积为 2 . 因此 ${\int }_{-1}^{2}\left| x\right| \mathrm{d}x = \frac{5}{2}$ .

( 4 )根据定积分的几何意义, ${\int }_{-3}^{3}\sqrt{9 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 表示的是由上半圆周 $y = \sqrt{9 - {x}^{2}}$ 以及 $x$ 轴所围成的半圆的面积,因此有 ${\int }_{-3}^{3}\sqrt{9 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{9}{2}\pi$ .

5. 设 $a < b$ ,问 $a$ 、 $b$ 取什么值时,积分 ${\int }_{a}^{b}\left( {x - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 取得最大值？

解 根据定积分几何意义, ${\int }_{a}^{b}\left( {x - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 表示的是由 $y = x - {x}^{2},x = a,x = b$ ,以及 $x$ 轴所围成的图形在 $x$ 轴上方部分的面积减去 $x$ 轴下方部分面积. 因此如果下方部分面积为 0,上方部分面积为最大时, ${\int }_{a}^{b}\left( {x - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 的值最大,即当 $a = 0,b = 1$ 时,积分 ${\int }_{a}^{b}\left( {x - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 取得最大值.

26. 已知 $\ln 2 = {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{1}{1 + x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,试用抛物线法公式(1 - 6)求出 $\ln 2$ 的近似值(取 $n = {10}$ , 计算时取 4 位小数).

解 计算 ${y}_{i}$ 并列表

<table><tr><td>$i$</td><td>0</td><td>1</td><td>2</td><td>3</td><td>4</td><td>5</td><td>6</td><td>7</td><td>8</td><td>9</td><td>10</td></tr><tr><td>${x}_{i}$</td><td>0.0000</td><td>0.1000</td><td>0.2000</td><td>0.3000</td><td>0.4000</td><td>0.5000</td><td>0.6000</td><td>0.7000</td><td>0.8000</td><td>0.9000</td><td>1.0000</td></tr><tr><td>${y}_{i}$</td><td>1.000 0</td><td>0.9091</td><td>0.8333</td><td>0.7692</td><td>0.7143</td><td>0.6667</td><td>0.6250</td><td>0.5882</td><td>0.5556</td><td>0.5263</td><td>0.5000</td></tr></table>

按抛物线法公式(1 - 6),求得

$$
s = \frac{1}{30}\left\lbrack  {\left( {{y}_{0} + {y}_{10}}\right)  + 2\left( {{y}_{2} + {y}_{4} + {y}_{6} + {y}_{8}}\right)  + 4\left( {{y}_{1} + {y}_{3} + {y}_{5} + {y}_{7} + {y}_{9}}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$\approx  {0.6931}$ .

2. 7. 设 ${\int }_{-1}^{1}{3f}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {18},{\int }_{-1}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 4,{\int }_{-1}^{3}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 3$ . 求

(1) ${\int }_{-1}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (2) ${\int }_{1}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{3}^{-1}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (4) ${\int }_{-1}^{3}\frac{1}{5}\left\lbrack  {{4f}\left( x\right)  + {3g}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$ .

解 (1) ${\int }_{-1}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{3}{\int }_{-1}^{1}{3f}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 6$ .

(2) ${\int }_{1}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{-1}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x - {\int }_{-1}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - 2$ .

(3) ${\int }_{3}^{-1}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - {\int }_{-1}^{3}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - 3$ .

(4) ${\int }_{-1}^{3}\frac{1}{5}\left\lbrack  {{4f}\left( x\right)  + {3g}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x = \frac{4}{5}{\int }_{-1}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + \frac{3}{5}{\int }_{-1}^{3}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 5$ .

8 8. 水利工程中要计算拦水闸门所受的水压力. 已知闸门上水的压强 $p$ 与水深 $h$ 存在函数关系,且有 $p = {9.8h}\left( {\mathrm{{kN}}/{\mathrm{m}}^{2}}\right)$ . 若闸门高 $H = 3\mathrm{\;m}$ ,宽 $L = 2\mathrm{\;m}$ ,求水面与闸门顶相齐时闸门所受的水压力 $P$ .

解 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,3}\right\rbrack$ 上插入 $n - 1$ 个分点 $0 = {h}_{0} < {h}_{1} < \cdots  < {h}_{n} = 3$ ,取 ${\xi }_{i} \in  \left\lbrack  {h}_{i - 1}\right.$ , $\left. {h}_{i}\right\rbrack$ ,并记 $\Delta {h}_{i} = {h}_{i} - {h}_{i - 1}$ ,得到闸门所受水压力的近似值为 $\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}p\left( {\xi }_{i}\right) {2\Delta }{h}_{i}$ ,根据定积分的定义可知闸门所受的水压力为

$$
P = {\int }_{0}^{3}{2p}\left( h\right) \mathrm{d}h = {19.6}{\int }_{0}^{3}h\mathrm{\;d}h,
$$

由于被积函数连续,而连续函数是可积的,因此积分值与积分区间的分法和 ${\xi }_{i}$ 的取法无关. 为方便计算,对区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,3}\right\rbrack$ 进行 $n$ 等分,并取 ${\xi }_{i}$ 为小区间的端点 ${h}_{i} = \frac{3i}{n}$ , 于是

$$
{\int }_{0}^{3}h\mathrm{\;d}h = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\frac{9i}{{n}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{9\left( {n + 1}\right) }{2n} = \frac{9}{2},
$$

故

$$
P = {19.6}{\int }_{0}^{3}h\mathrm{\;d}h = {88.2}\left( \mathrm{{kN}}\right) .
$$

29. 证明定积分性质:

(1) ${\int }_{a}^{b}{kf}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = k{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\left( {k\text{是常数}}\right)$ ; (2) ${\int }_{a}^{b}1 \cdot  \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{a}^{b}\mathrm{\;d}x = b - a$ .

证 根据定积分的定义,在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 中插入 $n - 1$ 个点 $a = {x}_{0} < {x}_{1} < {x}_{2} < \cdots$ $< {x}_{n} = b$ ,记 $\Delta {x}_{i} = {x}_{i} - {x}_{i - 1}$ ,任取 ${\xi }_{i} \in  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{i - 1},{x}_{i}}\right\rbrack$ ,则

(1) ${\int }_{a}^{b}{kf}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{\lambda  \rightarrow  0}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{kf}\left( {\xi }_{i}\right) \Delta {x}_{i} = k\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{\lambda  \rightarrow  0}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}f\left( {\xi }_{i}\right) \Delta {x}_{i} = k{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

(2) ${\int }_{a}^{b}1 \cdot  \mathrm{d}x = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{\lambda  \rightarrow  0}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\Delta {x}_{i} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{\lambda  \rightarrow  0}}\left( {b - a}\right)  = b - a$ .

1210. 估计下列各积分的值:

(1) ${\int }_{1}^{4}\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (2) ${\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{5}{4}\pi }\left( {1 + {\sin }^{2}x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ；

(3) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}^{\sqrt{3}}x\arctan x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (4) ${\int }_{2}^{0}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2} - x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 (1) 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {1,4}\right\rbrack$ 上, $2 \leq  {x}^{2} + 1 \leq  {17}$ ,因此有

$$
6 = {\int }_{1}^{4}2\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{1}^{4}\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  {\int }_{1}^{4}{17}\mathrm{\;d}x = {51}.
$$

( 2 )在区间 $\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{4}\pi ,\frac{5}{4}\pi }\right\rbrack$ 上, $1 = 1 + 0 \leq  1 + {\sin }^{2}x \leq  1 + 1 = 2$ ,因此有

$$
\pi  = {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{5}{4}\pi }\mathrm{d}x \leq  {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{5}{4}\pi }\left( {1 + {\sin }^{2}x}\right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{5}{4}\pi }2\mathrm{\;d}x = {2\pi }.
$$

(3)在区间 $\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}},\sqrt{3}}\right\rbrack$ 上,函数 $f\left( x\right)  = x\arctan x$ 是单调增加的,因此 $f\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}\right)  \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq$ $f\left( \sqrt{3}\right)$ ,即 $\frac{\pi }{6\sqrt{3}} \leq  x\arctan x \leq  \frac{\pi }{\sqrt{3}}$ ,故有

$$
\frac{\pi }{9} = {\int }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}^{\sqrt{3}}\frac{\pi }{6\sqrt{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}^{\sqrt{3}}x\arctan x\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}^{\sqrt{3}}\frac{\pi }{\sqrt{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{2}{3}\pi .
$$

(4)设 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} - x,x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {2x} - 1,f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack$ 上的最大值、 最小值必为 $f\left( 0\right) ,f\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) ,f\left( 2\right)$ 中的最大值和最小值,即最大值和最小值分别为 $f\left( 2\right)  =$ 2 和 $f\left( \frac{1}{2}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{4}$ ,因此有

$$
2{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{4}} = {\int }_{0}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{4}}\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{0}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2} - x}\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{0}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{2},
$$

而 ${\int }_{2}^{0}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2} - x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - {\int }_{0}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2} - x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,故 $- 2{\mathrm{e}}^{2} \leq  {\int }_{2}^{0}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2} - x}\mathrm{\;d}x \leq   - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{4}}$ .

2011. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,证明 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \geq  {\left( {\int }_{0}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{2}$ .

证 记 $a = {\int }_{0}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ,则由定积分性质 5,得

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}{\left\lbrack  f\left( x\right)  - a\right\rbrack  }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x \geq  0,
$$

即

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}{\left\lbrack  f\left( x\right)  - a\right\rbrack  }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{1}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x - {2a}{\int }_{0}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + {a}^{2}
$$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{1}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x - {\left\lbrack  {\int }_{0}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right\rbrack  }^{2} \geq  0,
$$

由此结论成立.

12. 12. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 及 $g\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,证明

(1)若在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上, $f\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,且 $f\left( x\right)  ≢ 0$ ,则 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x > 0$ ;

(2)若在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上, $f\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,且 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 0$ ,则在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上, $f\left( x\right)  \equiv  0$ ；

(3) 若在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上, $f\left( x\right)  \leq  g\left( x\right)$ ,且 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ,则在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上, $f\left( x\right)  \equiv  g\left( x\right) .$

证 (1) 根据条件必定存在 ${x}_{0} \in  \left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ ,使得 $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  > 0$ . 由函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 连续可知,存在 $a \leq  \alpha  < \beta  \leq  b$ ,使得当 $x \in  \left\lbrack  {\alpha ,\beta }\right\rbrack$ 时 $f\left( x\right)  \geq  \frac{f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{2}$ . 因此有

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{a}^{\alpha }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + {\int }_{\alpha }^{\beta }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + {\int }_{\beta }^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x,
$$

由定积分性质得到:

$$
{\int }_{a}^{\alpha }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \geq  0,\;{\int }_{\alpha }^{\beta }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \geq  {\int }_{\alpha }^{\beta }\frac{f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{\beta  - \alpha }{2}f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  > 0,\;{\int }_{\beta }^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \geq  0,
$$

故得到结论 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x > 0$ .

(2)用反证法. 如果 $f\left( x\right)  ≢ 0$ ,则由 (1) 得到 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x > 0$ ,与假设条件矛盾,因此结论成立.

(3) 因为 $h\left( x\right)  = g\left( x\right)  - f\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,且

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}h\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x - {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 0,
$$

由 (2) 可得在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上

$$
h\left( x\right)  \equiv  0,
$$

从而结论成立.

13. 根据定积分的性质及第 12 题的结论,说明下列各对积分哪一个的值较大：

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 还是 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ?

(2) ${\int }_{1}^{2}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 还是 ${\int }_{1}^{2}{x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ?

(3) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 还是 ${\int }_{1}^{2}{\left( \ln x\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ?

(4) ${\int }_{0}^{1}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 还是 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ?

(5) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 还是 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\left( {1 + x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ?

解 (1)在区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上 ${x}^{2} \geq  {x}^{3}$ ,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 比 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 大.

( 2 )在区间 $\left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack$ 上 ${x}^{2} \leq  {x}^{3}$ ,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{2}{x}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 比 ${\int }_{1}^{2}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 大.

(3)在区间 $\left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack$ 上由于 $0 \leq  \ln x \leq  1$ ,得 $\ln x \geq  {\left( \ln x\right) }^{2}$ ,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{2}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 比 ${\int }_{1}^{2}{\left( \ln x\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 大.

(4)由教材第三章第一节例 1 可知,当 $x > 0$ 时, $\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  < x$ ,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{1}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 比 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 大.

(5) 由于当 $x > 0$ 时 $\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  < x$ ,故此时有 $1 + x < {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 比 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\left( {1 + x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 大.

### 习题 5-2 微积分基本公式


3 1. 试求函数 $y = {\int }_{0}^{x}\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t$ 当 $x = 0$ 及 $x = \frac{\pi }{4}$ 时的导数.

解 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \sin x$ ,因此 ${\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right| }_{x = \frac{\pi }{4}} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}$ .

2. 求由参数表达式 $x = {\int }_{0}^{t}\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u,y = {\int }_{0}^{t}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u$ 所确定的函数对 $x$ 的导数 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ .

解 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t}/\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \frac{\cos t}{\sin t} = \cot t$ .

3. 求由 ${\int }_{0}^{y}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\mathrm{\;d}t + {\int }_{0}^{x}\cos t\mathrm{\;d}t = 0$ 所决定的隐函数对 $x$ 的导数 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ .

解 方程两端分别对 $x$ 求导,得 ${\mathrm{e}}^{y}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + \cos x = 0$ ,故 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-y}\cos x$ . 24. 当 $x$ 为何值时,函数 $I\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ 有极值?

解 容易知道 $I\left( x\right)$ 可导,而 ${I}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = x{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}} = 0$ 只有惟一解 $x = 0$ . 当 $x < 0$ 时 ${I}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,当 $x > 0$ 时 ${I}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,故 $x = 0$ 为函数 $I\left( x\right)$ 的惟一的极值点 (极小值点). 25. 计算下列各导数:

(1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{0}^{{x}^{2}}\sqrt{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ; (2) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{{x}^{2}}^{{x}^{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 + {t}^{4}}}$ ;
