(3) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{\sin x}^{\cos x}\cos \left( {\pi {t}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t$ .

解 (1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{0}^{{x}^{2}}\sqrt{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = {2x}\sqrt{1 + {x}^{4}}$ .

( 2 ) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{{x}^{2}}^{{x}^{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 + {t}^{4}}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( {{\int }_{0}^{{x}^{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 + {t}^{4}}} - {\int }_{0}^{{x}^{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{1 + {t}^{4}}}}\right)$

$$
= \frac{3{x}^{2}}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{12}}} - \frac{2x}{\sqrt{1 + {x}^{8}}}.
$$

(3) $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{\sin x}^{\cos x}\cos \left( {\pi {t}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left\lbrack  {{\int }_{0}^{\cos x}\cos \left( {\pi {t}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t - {\int }_{0}^{\sin x}\cos \left( {\pi {t}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t}\right\rbrack$

$$
=  - \sin x\cos \left( {\pi {\cos }^{2}x}\right)  - \cos x\cos \left( {\pi {\sin }^{2}x}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \sin x\cos \left( {\pi  - \pi {\sin }^{2}x}\right)  - \cos x\cos \left( {\pi {\sin }^{2}x}\right)
$$

$$
= \left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right) \cos \left( {\pi {\sin }^{2}x}\right) \text{.}
$$

26. 证明 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{1}^{x}\sqrt{1 + {t}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ 在 $\lbrack  - 1, + \infty )$ 上是单调增加函数,并求 ${\left( {f}^{-1}\right) }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ .

证 显然 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack  - 1, + \infty )$ 上可导,且当 $x >  - 1$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \sqrt{1 + {x}^{3}} > 0$ ,因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack  - 1, + \infty )$ 是单调增加函数.

注意到 $f\left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,故 ${\left( {f}^{-1}\right) }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \frac{1}{{f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right) } = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}$ .

17. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 具有三阶连续导数, $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的图形如图 5-1 所示. 问下列积分中的哪一个积分值为负?

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_191.jpg?x=529&y=1274&w=537&h=223&r=0"/>

图 5-1

<!-- Media -->

(A) ${\int }_{-1}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ (B) ${\int }_{-1}^{3}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$

(C) ${\int }_{-1}^{3}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ (D) ${\int }_{-1}^{3}{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$

解 根据 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的图形可知,在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-1,3}\right\rbrack$ 上 $f\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,且 $f\left( {-1}\right)  = f\left( 3\right)  =$ $0,{f}^{\prime }\left( {-1}\right)  > 0,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {-1}\right)  < 0,{f}^{\prime }\left( 3\right)  < 0,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 3\right)  > 0$ . 因此

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x > 0,\;{\int }_{-1}^{3}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( 3\right)  - f\left( {-1}\right)  = 0,
$$

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{3}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {f}^{\prime }\left( 3\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( {-1}\right)  < 0,{\int }_{-1}^{3}{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 3\right)  - {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {-1}\right)  > 0\text{. 故选 (C).}
$$

8. 8. 计算下列积分:

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{a}\left( {3{x}^{2} - x + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (2) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\left( {{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{{x}^{4}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ； (3) ${\int }_{4}^{9}\sqrt{x}\left( {1 + \sqrt{x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ; (4) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}^{\sqrt{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{2}}$ ;

(5) ${\int }_{-\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{1}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}$ ; (6) ${\int }_{0}^{\sqrt{3}a}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{a}^{2} + {x}^{2}}$ ;

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{4 - {x}^{2}}}$ ; (8) ${\int }_{-1}^{0}\frac{3{x}^{4} + 3{x}^{2} + 1}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(9) ${\int }_{-\mathrm{e} - 1}^{-2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x}$ ; (10) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}{\tan }^{2}\theta \mathrm{d}\theta$ ;

(11) ${\int }_{0}^{2\pi }\left| {\sin x}\right| \mathrm{d}x$ ；

(12) ${\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ,其中 $f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} x + 1, & x \leq  1, \\  \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}, & x > 1. \end{array}\right.$

解 (1) ${\int }_{0}^{a}\left( {3{x}^{2} - x + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\left\lbrack  {x}^{3} - \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2} + x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{a}$

$$
= {a}^{3} - \frac{1}{2}{a}^{2} + a = a\left( {{a}^{2} - \frac{1}{2}a + 1}\right) .
$$

(2) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\left( {{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{{x}^{4}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3} - \frac{1}{3{x}^{3}}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{2} = \frac{21}{8}$ .

(3) ${\int }_{4}^{9}\sqrt{x}\left( {1 + \sqrt{x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{4}^{9}\left( {\sqrt{x} + x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\left\lbrack  \frac{2}{3}{x}^{\frac{3}{2}} + \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}\right\rbrack  }_{4}^{9} = \frac{271}{6}$ .

(4) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}^{\sqrt{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{2}} = {\left\lbrack  \arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}^{\sqrt{3}} = \frac{\pi }{6}$ .

(5) ${\int }_{-\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{1}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = {\left\lbrack  \arcsin x\right\rbrack  }_{-\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{1}{2}} = \frac{\pi }{3}$ .

(6) ${\int }_{0}^{\sqrt{3}a}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{a}^{2} + {x}^{2}} = {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{a}\arctan \frac{x}{a}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\sqrt{3}a} = \frac{\pi }{3a}$ .

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{4 - {x}^{2}}} = {\left\lbrack  \arcsin \frac{x}{2}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = \frac{\pi }{6}$ .

(8) ${\int }_{-1}^{0}\frac{3{x}^{4} + 3{x}^{2} + 1}{{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{-1}^{0}\left( {3{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  {x}^{3} + \arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{-1}^{0} = 1 + \frac{\pi }{4}.
$$

(9) ${\int }_{-\mathrm{e} - 1}^{-2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x} = {\left\lbrack  \ln \left| 1 + x\right| \right\rbrack  }_{-\mathrm{e} - 1}^{-2} =  - 1$ .

(10) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}{\tan }^{2}\theta \mathrm{d}\theta  = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\left( {{\sec }^{2}\theta  - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}\theta  = {\left\lbrack  \tan \theta  - \theta \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}} = 1 - \frac{\pi }{4}$ .

(11) ${\int }_{0}^{2\pi }\left| {\sin x}\right| \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x + {\int }_{\pi }^{2\pi }\left( {-\sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  -\cos x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\pi } + {\left\lbrack  \cos x\right\rbrack  }_{\pi }^{2\pi } = 4\text{.}
$$

(12) ${\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{1}\left( {x + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x + {\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} + x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} + {\left\lbrack  \frac{{x}^{3}}{6}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{2} = \frac{8}{3}\text{.}
$$

9. 设 $k \in  {\mathbf{N}}_{ + }$ ,试证下列各题：

(1) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ ; (2) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin {kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\cos }^{2}{kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \pi$ ; (4) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\sin }^{2}{kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \pi$ .

解 (1) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{k}\sin kx\right\rbrack  }_{-\pi }^{\pi } = 0$ .

(2) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin {kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{k}\cos kx\right\rbrack  }_{-\pi }^{\pi } = 0$ .

(3) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\cos }^{2}{kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\left( {1 + \cos {2kx}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\mathrm{d}x = \pi$ ,其中由 (1) 得到 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {2kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

(4) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\sin }^{2}{kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\left( {1 - \cos {2kx}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\mathrm{d}x = \pi$ ,其中由 (1) 得到 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {2kx}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

120. 设 $k,l \in  {\mathbf{N}}_{ + }$ ,且 $k \neq  l$ . 证明：

(1) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {kx}\sin {lx}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ ; (2) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {kx}\cos {lx}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ ；

(3) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin {kx}\sin {lx}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

解 (1) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {kx}\sin {lx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\left\lbrack  {\sin \left( {k + l}\right) x - \sin \left( {k - l}\right) x}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$

$= \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin \left( {k + l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin \left( {k - l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= 0\text{,}
$$

其中由上一题 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin \left( {k + l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0,{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin \left( {k - l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

(2) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos {kx}\cos {lx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\left\lbrack  {\cos \left( {k + l}\right) x + \cos \left( {k - l}\right) x}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k + l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x + \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k - l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= 0\text{,}
$$

其中由上一题 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k + l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0,\;{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k - l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

(3) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\sin {kx}\sin {lx}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\left\lbrack  {\cos \left( {k + l}\right) x - \cos \left( {k - l}\right) x}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k + l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x + \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k - l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= 0\text{,}
$$

其中由上一题 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k + l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0,{\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }\cos \left( {k - l}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

271. 求下列极限:

(1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}\cos {t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t}{x}$ ; (2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\left( {\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t\right) }^{2}}{{\int }_{0}^{x}t{\mathrm{e}}^{2{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t}$ .

解 (1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}\cos {t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t}{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\cos {x}^{2}}{1} = 1$ .

(2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\left( {\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t\right) }^{2}}{{\int }_{0}^{x}t{\mathrm{e}}^{2{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{2{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}{\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t}{x{\mathrm{e}}^{2{x}^{2}}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{2{\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t}{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{2{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}}{1} = 2$ .

212. 设

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {x}^{2}, & x \in  \lbrack 0,1), \\  x, & x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  . \end{array}\right.
$$

求 $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack$ 上的表达式,并讨论 $\Phi \left( x\right)$ 在(0,2)内的连续性.

解 当 $x \in  \lbrack 0,1)$ 时, $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}{t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{{x}^{3}}{3}$ ; 当 $x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack$ 时, $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{1}{t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t +$ ${\int }_{1}^{x}t\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{1}{6}$ ,即

$$
\Phi \left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{{x}^{3}}{3}, & x \in  \lbrack 0,1), \\  \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{1}{6}, & x \in  \left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack  . \end{array}\right.
$$

由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}\Phi \left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}\frac{{x}^{3}}{3} = \frac{1}{3},\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}\Phi \left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}\left( {\frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \frac{1}{6}}\right)  = \frac{1}{3}$ ,且 $\Phi \left( 1\right)  = \frac{1}{3}$ ,故函数 $\Phi \left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 1$ 处连续,而在其他点处显然连续,因此函数 $\Phi \left( x\right)$ 在区间(0,2)内连续.

注 事实上,由于 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(0,2)内连续,故 $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 在(0,2)内可导, 因此 $\Phi \left( x\right)$ 必在(0,2)内连续. 我们甚至有以下更强的结论:

若 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上有界并可积,则 $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续. 按照连续

函数定义不难证明这一结论. 作为练习, 请读者自己证明之.

23. 设

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{2}\sin x, & 0 \leq  x \leq  \pi , \\  0, & x < 0\text{ 或 }x > \pi . \end{array}\right.
$$

求 $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内的表达式.

解 当 $x < 0$ 时, $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = 0$ ;

当 $0 \leq  x \leq  \pi$ 时, $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{1}{2}\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{1 - \cos x}{2}$ ;

当 $x > \pi$ 时, $\Phi \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{\pi }^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\frac{1}{2}\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t = 1\text{.}
$$

即

$$
\Phi \left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} 0, & x < 0, \\  \frac{1 - \cos x}{2}, & 0 \leq  x \leq  \pi , \\  1, & x > \pi . \end{array}\right.
$$

214. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(a,b)内可导且 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  \leq  0$ ,

$$
F\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x - a}{\int }_{a}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t.
$$

证明在(a,b)内有 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  \leq  0$ .

证 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{{\left( x - a\right) }^{2}}\left\lbrack  {\left( {x - a}\right) f\left( x\right)  - {\int }_{a}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}\right\rbrack$

$$
= \frac{1}{{\left( x - a\right) }^{2}}\left\lbrack  {\left( {x - a}\right) f\left( x\right)  - \left( {x - a}\right) f\left( \xi \right) }\right\rbrack  \;\left( {\xi  \in  \left( {a,x}\right)  \subset  \left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack  }\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{x - \xi }{x - a}{f}^{\prime }\left( \eta \right) \;\left( {\eta  \in  \left( {\xi ,x}\right)  \subset  \left( {a,b}\right) }\right) ,
$$

由条件可知结论成立.

15. 15. 设 $F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{\sin t}{t}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,求 ${F}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ .

解

$$
{F}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{F\left( x\right)  - F\left( 0\right) }{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{\sin t}{t}\mathrm{\;d}t}{x}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\frac{\sin x}{x}}{1} = 1.
$$

1216. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 内连续,且 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = 1$ . 证明函数

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}{\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t
$$

满足微分方程 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + y = f\left( x\right)$ ,并求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}y\left( x\right)$ .

证

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}{\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{x}f\left( x\right)
$$

$$
=  - y + f\left( x\right) ,
$$

因此 $y\left( x\right)$ 满足微分方程 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + y = f\left( x\right)$ .

由条件 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = 1$ ,从而存在 ${X}_{0} > 0$ ,当 $x > {X}_{0}$ 时,有

$$
f\left( x\right)  > \frac{1}{2}.
$$

因此,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{{X}_{0}}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{{X}_{0}}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t
$$

$$
\geq  {\int }_{0}^{{X}_{0}}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{{X}_{0}}^{x}\frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{X}_{0}}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{{X}_{0}}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{X}_{0}}\left( {x - {X}_{0}}\right) ,
$$

故,当 $x \rightarrow   + \infty$ 时, ${\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t \rightarrow   + \infty$ ,从而利用洛必达法则,有

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}y\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}f\left( x\right) }{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}} = 1.
$$

### 习题 5-3 定积分的换元法和分部积分法


21. 计算下列定积分:

(1) ${\int }_{\frac{\pi }{3}}^{\pi }\sin \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ； (2) ${\int }_{-2}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( {11} + 5x\right) }^{3}}$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sin \varphi {\cos }^{3}\varphi \mathrm{d}\varphi$ ; (4) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }\left( {1 - {\sin }^{3}\theta }\right) \mathrm{d}\theta$ ;

(5) ${\int }_{\frac{\pi }{6}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ; (6) ${\int }_{0}^{\sqrt{2}}\sqrt{2 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (7) ${\int }_{-\sqrt{2}}^{\sqrt{2}}\sqrt{8 - 2{y}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}y$ ; (8) ${\int }_{\sqrt{2}}^{1}\frac{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(9) ${\int }_{0}^{a}{x}^{2}\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {a > 0}\right)$ ; (10) ${\int }_{1}^{\sqrt{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}}$ ;

(11) ${\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{5 - {4x}}}$ ; (12) ${\int }_{1}^{4}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{x}}$ ;

(13) ${\int }_{\frac{3}{4}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - x} - 1}$ ; (14) ${\int }_{0}^{\sqrt{2}a}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{3{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}\left( {a > 0}\right)$ ；

(15) ${\int }_{0}^{1}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{t}^{2}}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ; (16) ${\int }_{1}^{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{1 + \ln x}}$ ;

(17) ${\int }_{-2}^{0}\frac{\left( {x + 2}\right) \mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 2}$ ; (18) ${\int }_{0}^{2}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{{\left( {x}^{2} - 2x + 2\right) }^{2}}$ ;

(19) ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{x}^{4}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (20) ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}4{\cos }^{4}\theta \mathrm{d}\theta$ ;

(21) ${\int }_{-\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{1}{2}}\frac{{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ； (22) ${\int }_{-5}^{5}\frac{{x}^{3}{\sin }^{2}x}{{x}^{4} + 2{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(23) ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (24) ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{\cos x - {\cos }^{3}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(25) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }\sqrt{1 + \cos {2x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; ( 26 ) ${\int }_{0}^{2\pi }\left| {\sin \left( {x + 1}\right) }\right| \mathrm{d}x$ .

解 (1) ${\int }_{\frac{\pi }{3}}^{\pi }\sin \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{3}}^{\pi }\sin \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {x + \frac{\pi }{3}}\right)$

$= {\left\lbrack  -\cos \left( x + \frac{\pi }{3}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{3}}^{\pi } = 0.$

(2) ${\int }_{-2}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( {11} + 5x\right) }^{3}} = {\int }_{-2}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{11} + {5x}}\right) }{5{\left( {11} + 5x\right) }^{3}} = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{{10}{\left( {11} + 5x\right) }^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{-2}^{1} = \frac{51}{512}$ .

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sin \varphi {\cos }^{3}\varphi \mathrm{d}\varphi  =  - {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{3}\varphi \mathrm{d}\left( {\cos \varphi }\right)  = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{4}{\cos }^{4}\varphi \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} = \frac{1}{4}$ .

(4) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }\left( {1 - {\sin }^{3}\theta }\right) \mathrm{d}\theta  = \pi  + {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\left( {1 - {\cos }^{2}\theta }\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\cos \theta }\right)$

$$
\overset{u = \cos \theta }{ = }\pi  + {\int }_{1}^{-1}\left( {1 - {u}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}u = \pi  - \frac{4}{3}.
$$

(5) ${\int }_{\frac{\pi }{6}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{\frac{\pi }{6}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\left( {1 + \cos {2u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\left\lbrack  u + \frac{1}{2}\sin 2u\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{6}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} = \frac{\pi }{6} - \frac{\sqrt{3}}{8}\text{.}
$$

(6) ${\int }_{0}^{\sqrt{2}}\sqrt{2 - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{x = \sqrt{2}\sin u}{}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}2{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = 2 \cdot  \frac{\pi }{4} = \frac{\pi }{2}$ . (7) ${\int }_{-\sqrt{2}}^{\sqrt{2}}\sqrt{8 - 2{y}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}y\overset{y = 2\sin u}{ = }{\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}4\sqrt{2}{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u$

$$
= 2\sqrt{2}{\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\left( {1 + \cos {2u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= 2\sqrt{2}{\left\lbrack  u + \frac{1}{2}\sin 2u\right\rbrack  }_{-\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{4}} = \sqrt{2}\left( {\pi  + 2}\right) .
$$

(8) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}^{1}\frac{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = x\sin u{\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{{\cos }^{2}u}{{\sin }^{2}u}\mathrm{\;d}u = {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\left( {{\csc }^{2}u - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}u$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  -\cot u - u\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} = 1 - \frac{\pi }{4}.
$$

(9) ${\int }_{0}^{a}{x}^{2}\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = a\sin u{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{a}^{4}{\sin }^{2}u{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{{a}^{4}}{8}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\left( \sin 2u\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {2u}\right)$

$$
\overset{t = {2u}}{ = }\frac{{a}^{4}}{8}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }{\sin }^{2}t\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{{a}^{4}}{4}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\sin }^{2}t\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= \frac{{a}^{4}}{4} \cdot  \frac{\pi }{4} = \frac{\pi }{16}{a}^{4}.
$$

(10) ${\int }_{1}^{\sqrt{3}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2}\sqrt{1 + {x}^{2}}} = \frac{1}{}{\int }_{1}^{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}\frac{-u}{\sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}u = {\left\lbrack  -\sqrt{1 + {u}^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}$

$$
= \sqrt{2} - \frac{2\sqrt{3}}{3}\text{.}
$$

(11)令 $u = \sqrt{5 - {4x}}$ ,即 $x = \frac{5 - {u}^{2}}{4}$ ,得

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{5 - {4x}}} = {\int }_{3}^{1}\frac{{u}^{2} - 5}{8}\mathrm{\;d}u = {\left\lbrack  \frac{{u}^{3}}{24} - \frac{5}{8}u\right\rbrack  }_{3}^{1} = \frac{1}{6}.
$$

(12)令 $u = \sqrt{x}$ ,即 $x = {u}^{2}$ ,得

$$
{\int }_{1}^{4}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + \sqrt{x}} = {\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{{2u}\mathrm{\;d}u}{1 + u} = {\left\lbrack  2u - 2\ln \left( 1 + u\right) \right\rbrack  }_{1}^{2} = 2 + 2\ln \frac{2}{3}.
$$

(13)令 $u = \sqrt{1 - x}$ ,即 $x = 1 - {u}^{2}$ ,得

$$
{\int }_{\frac{3}{4}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{1 - x} - 1} = {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{0}\frac{-{2u}\mathrm{\;d}u}{u - 1} =  - 2{\left\lbrack  u + \ln \left( 1 - u\right) \right\rbrack  }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{0} = 1 - 2\ln 2.
$$

(14) ${\int }_{0}^{\sqrt{2}a}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{3{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}} =  - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\sqrt{2}a}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {3{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right) }{\sqrt{3{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}$

$$
=  - {\left\lbrack  \sqrt{3{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\sqrt{2}a} = \left( {\sqrt{3} - 1}\right) a.
$$

5) ${\int }_{0}^{1}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{t}^{2}}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t =  - {\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{t}^{2}}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {-\frac{{t}^{2}}{2}}\right)  = {\left\lbrack  -{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{t}^{2}}{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = 1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{2}}$ .

16) ${\int }_{1}^{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{1 + \ln x}} = \frac{x = {\mathrm{e}}^{u}}{}{\int }_{0}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\sqrt{1 + u}} = {\left\lbrack  2\sqrt{1 + u}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{2} = 2\sqrt{3} - 2$ .

(17) ${\int }_{-2}^{0}\frac{\left( {x + 2}\right) \mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 2} = {\int }_{-2}^{0}\frac{\left( {x + 1}\right)  + 1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {x}^{2} + 2x + 2\right)  + \arctan \left( x + 1\right) \right\rbrack  }_{-2}^{0}
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{2}\text{.}
$$

(18) 令 $x = 1 + \tan u$ ,则 $\mathrm{d}x = {\sec }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u$ ,因此

$$
{\int }_{0}^{2}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{{\left( {x}^{2} - 2x + 2\right) }^{2}} = {\int }_{0}^{2}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{{\left\lbrack  {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} + 1\right\rbrack  }^{2}} = {\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\frac{\left( {1 + \tan u}\right) \mathrm{d}u}{{\sec }^{2}u}
$$

$$
= 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\left( {1 + \cos {2u}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{4} + \frac{1}{2}\text{. }
$$

(19)由于被积函数为奇函数,因此 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{x}^{4}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

(20)由于被积函数为偶函数, 因此

$$
{\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}4{\cos }^{4}\theta \mathrm{d}\theta  = 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}4{\cos }^{4}\theta \mathrm{d}\theta  = 8 \cdot  \frac{3}{4} \cdot  \frac{\pi }{4} = \frac{3}{2}\pi .
$$

(21)由于被积函数为偶函数, 因此有

$$
{\int }_{-\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{1}{2}}\frac{{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x = 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{1}{2}}\frac{{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{1}{2}}{\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\arcsin x}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{3}{\left\lbrack  {\left( \arcsin x\right) }^{3}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{1}{2}} = \frac{{\pi }^{3}}{324}.
$$

(22)由于被积函数为奇函数, 因此

$$
{\int }_{-5}^{5}\frac{{x}^{3}{\sin }^{2}x}{{x}^{4} + 2{x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0.
$$

(23) ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\left( {1 - 2{\sin }^{2}x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= {\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\left( {1 - 2{\sin }^{2}x}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {\sin x}\right)
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \sin x - \frac{2}{3}{\sin }^{3}x\right\rbrack  }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} = \frac{2}{3}\text{.}
$$

或者

$$
{\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\left( {\cos {3x} + \cos x}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{3}\sin 3x + \sin x\right\rbrack  }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} = \frac{2}{3}\text{.}
$$

(24) ${\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{\cos x - {\cos }^{3}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{\cos x}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
\overset{u = \cos x}{ = } - 2{\int }_{1}^{0}\sqrt{u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{4}{3}\text{.}
$$

(25) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }\sqrt{1 + \cos {2x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\sqrt{2}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = \sqrt{2}{\left\lbrack  -\cos x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\pi } = 2\sqrt{2}$ .

( 26 ) ${\int }_{0}^{2\pi }\left| {\sin \left( {x + 1}\right) }\right| \mathrm{d}x\overset{x = u - 1}{ = }{\int }_{1}^{{2\pi } + 1}\left| {\sin u}\right| \mathrm{d}u$ ,

由于 $\left| {\sin x}\right|$ 是以 $\pi$ 为周期的周期函数,因此

$$
\text{上式} = 2{\int }_{0}^{\pi }\left| {\sin u}\right| \mathrm{d}u = 4\text{.}
$$

2. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,证明

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( {a + b - x}\right) \mathrm{d}x.
$$

证 令 $x = a + b - u$ ,则

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - {\int }_{b}^{a}f\left( {a + b - u}\right) \mathrm{d}u = {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( {a + b - u}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( {a + b - x}\right) \mathrm{d}x.
$$

例 3. 证明: ${\int }_{x}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 + {t}^{2}} = {\int }_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 + {t}^{2}}\;\left( {x > 0}\right)$ .

证 ${\int }_{x}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 + {t}^{2}} = \frac{t = \frac{1}{u}}{} - {\int }_{\frac{1}{x}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{1 + {u}^{2}} = {\int }_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{1 + {u}^{2}} = {\int }_{1}^{\frac{1}{x}}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{1 + {t}^{2}}$ .

24. 证明: ${\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{m}{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{n}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{n}{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{m}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {m,n \in  \mathbf{N}}\right)$ .

证 令 $x = 1 - u$ ,则

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{m}{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{n}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{1}^{0} - {\left( 1 - u\right) }^{m}{u}^{n}\mathrm{\;d}u = {\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{n}{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{m}\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

5. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续, $n \in  \mathbf{Z}$ ,证明

$$
{\int }_{\frac{n}{2}\pi }^{\frac{n + 1}{2}\pi }f\left( \left| {\sin x}\right| \right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{\frac{n}{2}\pi }^{\frac{n + 1}{2}\pi }f\left( \left| {\cos x}\right| \right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( {\sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x.
$$

证 令 $x = u + \frac{n}{2}\pi$ ,则 $\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{d}u$ ,因此

$$
{\int }_{\frac{n}{2}\pi }^{\frac{n + 1}{2}\pi }f\left( \left| {\sin x}\right| \right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( \left| {\sin \left( {u + \frac{n}{2}\pi }\right) }\right| \right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( {\sin u}\right) \mathrm{d}u, & n\text{ 为偶数,} \\  {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( {\cos u}\right) \mathrm{d}u, & n\text{ 为奇数. } \end{array}\right.
$$

$$
{\int }_{\frac{n}{2}\pi }^{\frac{n + 1}{2}\pi }f\left( \left| {\cos x}\right| \right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( \left| {\cos \left( {u + \frac{n}{2}\pi }\right) }\right| \right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( {\cos u}\right) \mathrm{d}u, & n\text{ 为偶数,} \\  {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( {\sin u}\right) \mathrm{d}u, & n\text{ 为奇数. } \end{array}\right.
$$

由于 ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( {\sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}f\left( {\cos x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ,因此结论成立.

2. 6. 若 $f\left( x\right)$ 是连续的奇函数,证明 ${\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 是偶函数; 若 $f\left( x\right)$ 是连续的偶函数,证明 ${\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 是奇函数. 证 记 $F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,则有

$$
F\left( {-x}\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{-x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t\overset{t =  - u}{ = } - {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( {-u}\right) \mathrm{d}u,
$$

当 $f\left( x\right)$ 为奇函数时, $F\left( {-x}\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u = F\left( x\right)$ ,故 ${\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 是偶函数. 当 $f\left( x\right)$ 为偶函数时, $F\left( {-x}\right)  =  - {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u =  - F\left( x\right)$ ,故 ${\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 是奇函数. 17. 计算下列定积分:

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{1}x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (2) ${\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}x\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{2\pi }{\omega }}t\sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t\left( {\omega \text{为常数}}\right)$ ； (4) ${\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{3}}\frac{x}{{\sin }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(5) ${\int }_{1}^{4}\frac{\ln x}{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (6) ${\int }_{0}^{1}x\arctan x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (8) ${\int }_{1}^{2}x{\log }_{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(9) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }{\left( x\sin x\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (10) ${\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\sin \left( {\ln x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ;

(11) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{e}}^{e}\left| {\ln x}\right| \mathrm{d}x$ ; (12) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{\left( 1 - {x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{m}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {m \in  {\mathbf{N}}_{ + }}\right)$ ;

(13) ${J}_{m} = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }x{\sin }^{m}x\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {m \in  {\mathbf{N}}_{ + }}\right)$ . 解 (1) ${\int }_{0}^{1}x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - {\int }_{0}^{1}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right)  =  - {\left\lbrack  x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} + {\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
=  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-1} + {\left\lbrack  -{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = 1 - \frac{2}{\mathrm{e}}.
$$

(2) ${\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}x\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\frac{\ln x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x}^{2}\right)  = {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}\ln x\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}} - {\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{2} + 1}{4}$ .

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{2\pi }{\omega }}t\sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t =  - \frac{1}{\omega }{\int }_{0}^{\frac{2\pi }{\omega }}t\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos {\omega t}}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{\omega }{\left\lbrack  t\cos \omega t\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{2\pi }{\omega }} + \frac{1}{\omega }{\int }_{0}^{\frac{2\pi }{\omega }}\cos {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t$

$$
=  - \frac{2\pi }{{\omega }^{2}} + \frac{1}{{\omega }^{2}}{\left\lbrack  \sin \omega t\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{2\pi }{\omega }} =  - \frac{2\pi }{{\omega }^{2}}.
$$

(4) ${\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{3}}\frac{x}{{\sin }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{3}}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cot x}\right)  = {\left\lbrack  -x\cot x\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{3}} + {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{3}}\cot x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
=  - \frac{\pi }{3\sqrt{3}} + \frac{\pi }{4} + {\left\lbrack  \ln \sin x\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{3}}
$$

$$
= \left( {\frac{1}{4} - \frac{\sqrt{3}}{9}}\right) \pi  + \frac{1}{2}\ln \frac{3}{2}\text{.}
$$

(5) ${\int }_{1}^{4}\frac{\ln x}{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{1}^{4}2\ln x\mathrm{\;d}\sqrt{x} = {\left\lbrack  2\sqrt{x}\ln x\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{4} - {\int }_{1}^{4}\frac{2}{\sqrt{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= 8\ln 2 - {\left\lbrack  4\sqrt{x}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{4} = 4\left( {2\ln 2 - 1}\right) .
$$

(6) ${\int }_{0}^{1}x\arctan x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{1}\arctan x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x}^{2}\right)$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}\arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{{x}^{2}}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{8} - \frac{1}{2}{\left\lbrack  x - \arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = \frac{\pi }{4} - \frac{1}{2}\text{.}
$$

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\cos x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} + \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{4}{\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\sin x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} - \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x\text{,}
$$

因此有

$$
{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{5}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{\pi } - 2}\right) .
$$

(8) ${\int }_{1}^{2}x{\log }_{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{1}^{2}{\log }_{2}x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x}^{2}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\left\lbrack  {x}^{2}{\log }_{2}x\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{2} - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{x}{\ln 2}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= 2 - \frac{1}{4\ln 2}{\left\lbrack  {x}^{2}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{2} = 2 - \frac{3}{4\ln 2}\text{.}
$$

(9) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }{\left( x\sin x\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }{x}^{2}\left( {1 - \cos {2x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \frac{{\pi }^{3}}{6} - \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin {2x}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{{\pi }^{3}}{6} - \frac{1}{4}{\left\lbrack  {x}^{2}\sin 2x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\pi } + \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }x\sin {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{{\pi }^{3}}{6} - \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos {2x}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{{\pi }^{3}}{6} - \frac{1}{4}{\left\lbrack  x\cos 2x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\pi } + \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }\cos {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{{\pi }^{3}}{6} - \frac{\pi }{4}\text{.}
$$

0) ${\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\sin \left( {\ln x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\mathrm{e}}^{u}{\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u = {\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\sin u\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} - {\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u$

$$
= \operatorname{esin}1 - {\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{e}}^{u}\cos u\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} - {\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \mathrm{e}\left( {\sin 1 - \cos 1}\right)  + 1 - {\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{u}\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u,
$$

所以, ${\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\sin \left( {\ln x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{\mathrm{e}}{2}\left( {\sin 1 - \cos 1}\right)  + \frac{1}{2}$ .

(11) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}^{\mathrm{e}}\left| {\ln x}\right| \mathrm{d}x =  - {\int }_{\frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}^{1}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x + {\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
=  - {\left\lbrack  x\ln x\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}^{1} + {\int }_{\frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}^{1}\mathrm{\;d}x + {\left\lbrack  x\ln x\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}} - {\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= 2 - \frac{2}{\mathrm{e}}\text{.}
$$

(12) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{\left( 1 - {x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{m}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x\overset{x = \sin u}{ = }{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{m + 1}u\mathrm{\;d}u$

$$
= \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{m}{m + 1} \cdot  \frac{m - 2}{m - 1} \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \frac{1}{2} \cdot  \frac{\pi }{2}, & m\text{ 为奇数,} \\  \frac{m}{m + 1} \cdot  \frac{m - 2}{m - 1} \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \frac{2}{3}, & m\text{ 为偶数,} \end{array}\right.
$$

$$
= \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  m}{2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {m + 1}\right) } \cdot  \frac{\pi }{2}, & m\text{ 为奇数,} \\  \frac{2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  m}{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {m + 1}\right) }, & m\text{ 为偶数. } \end{array}\right.
$$

(13)由教材本节的例 6 , 可得

$$
{J}_{m} = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }x{\sin }^{m}x\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{\pi }{2}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }{\sin }^{m}x\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

而

$$
{\int }_{0}^{\pi }{\sin }^{m}x\mathrm{\;d}x\overset{x = \frac{\pi }{2} + t}{ = }{\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{m}t\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{m}t\mathrm{\;d}t = 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\sin }^{m}x\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

故

$$
{J}_{m} = \pi {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\sin }^{m}x\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

从而有

$$
{J}_{m} = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {m - 1}\right) }{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  m} \cdot  \pi , & m\text{ 为大于 }1\text{ 的奇数,} \\  \frac{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {m - 1}\right) }{2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  m} \cdot  \frac{{\pi }^{2}}{2}, & m\text{ 为偶数,} \end{array}\right.
$$

$$
{J}_{1} = \pi \text{.}
$$

### 习题 5-4 反常积分



11. 判定下列各反常积分的收敛性, 如果收敛, 计算反常积分的值:

(1) ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{4}}$ ; (2) ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x}}$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {a > 0}\right)$ ; (4) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {1 + x}\right) \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) }$ ;

(5) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t\left( {p > 0,\omega  > 0}\right)$ ; (6) ${\int }_{-\infty }^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 2}$ ;

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}$ ; (8) ${\int }_{0}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}}$ ;

(9) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{x - 1}}$ ; (10) ${\int }_{1}^{\mathrm{e}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{1 - {\left( \ln x\right) }^{2}}}$ .

解 (1) ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{4}} = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{3{x}^{3}}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{+\infty } = \frac{1}{3}$ .

(2) ${\int }_{1}^{t}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x}} = {\left\lbrack  2\sqrt{x}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{t} = 2\sqrt{t} - 2$ ,当 $t \rightarrow   + \infty$ 时,该极限不存在,故该反常积分发散.

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{a}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty } = \frac{1}{a}$ .

(4) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\left( {1 + x}\right) \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) } = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{1 + x} + \frac{1 - x}{1 + {x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{4}\ln \frac{{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{2}}{1 + {x}^{2}} + \frac{1}{2}\arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty }
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{4}\text{.}
$$

(5) $\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t =  - \frac{1}{p}\int \sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\right)$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{p}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t} + \frac{\omega }{p}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\cos {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{p}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t} - \frac{\omega }{{p}^{2}}\int \cos {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{p}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t} - \frac{\omega }{{p}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\cos {\omega t} - \frac{{\omega }^{2}}{{p}^{2}}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t\text{,}
$$

因此,

$$
\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{-p{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t} - \omega {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\cos {\omega t}}{{p}^{2} + {\omega }^{2}} + C,
$$

故

$$
{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t}\mathrm{\;d}t = {\left\lbrack  \frac{-p{\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\sin {\omega t} - \omega {\mathrm{e}}^{-{pt}}\cos {\omega t}}{{p}^{2} + {\omega }^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty }
$$

$$
= \frac{\omega }{{p}^{2} + {\omega }^{2}}\text{.}
$$

(6) ${\int }_{-\infty }^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + {2x} + 2} = {\int }_{-\infty }^{0}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {x + 1}\right) }{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + 1} + {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {x + 1}\right) }{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2} + 1}$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \arctan \left( x + 1\right) \right\rbrack  }_{-\infty }^{0} + {\left\lbrack  \arctan \left( x + 1\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty } = \pi .
$$

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = {\left\lbrack  -\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = 1$ .

(8) ${\int }_{0}^{t}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}} = {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{1 - x}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{t} = \frac{1}{1 - t} - 1$ ,当 $t \rightarrow  1$ 时极限不存在,故原反常积分发散.

(9) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{x\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{x - 1}} = \frac{x = {u}^{2} + 1}{2}2{\int }_{0}^{1}\left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}u = \frac{8}{3}$ .

(10) ${\int }_{1}^{e}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt{1 - {\left( \ln x\right) }^{2}}} = {\int }_{1}^{e}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\ln x}\right) }{\sqrt{1 - {\left( \ln x\right) }^{2}}} = {\left\lbrack  \arcsin \ln x\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{e} = \frac{\pi }{2}$ .

2. 当 $k$ 为何值时,反常积分 ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{k}}$ 收敛? 当 $k$ 为何值时,这反常积分发散? 又当

$k$ 为何值时,这反常积分取得最小值?

解 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{k}} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\ln x}\right) }{{\left( \ln x\right) }^{k}} = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \ln \ln x + C, & k = 1, \\   - \frac{1}{\left( {k - 1}\right) {\ln }^{k - 1}x} + C, & k \neq  1, \end{array}\right.$

因此当 $k \leq  1$ 时,反常积分发散; 当 $k > 1$ 时,该反常积分收敛,此时

$$
{\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x{\left( \ln x\right) }^{k}} = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{\left( {k - 1}\right) {\ln }^{k - 1}x}\right\rbrack  }_{2}^{+\infty } = \frac{1}{\left( {k - 1}\right) {\left( \ln 2\right) }^{k - 1}}.
$$

记 $f\left( k\right)  = \frac{1}{\left( {k - 1}\right) {\left( \ln 2\right) }^{k - 1}}$ ,则

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( k\right)  =  - \frac{1}{{\left( k - 1\right) }^{2}{\left( \ln 2\right) }^{{2k} - 2}}\left\lbrack  {{\left( \ln 2\right) }^{k - 1} + \left( {k - 1}\right) {\left( \ln 2\right) }^{k - 1}\ln \ln 2}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1 + \left( {k - 1}\right) \ln \ln 2}{{\left( k - 1\right) }^{2}{\left( \ln 2\right) }^{k - 1}},
$$

令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( k\right)  = 0$ ,得 $k = 1 - \frac{1}{\ln \ln 2}$ . 当 $1 < k < 1 - \frac{1}{\ln \ln 2}$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( k\right)  < 0$ ,当 $k > 1 - \frac{1}{\ln \ln 2}$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( k\right)  > 0$ ,故 $k = 1 - \frac{1}{\ln \ln 2}$ 为函数 $f\left( k\right)$ 的最小值点,即当 $k = 1 - \frac{1}{\ln \ln 2}$ 时所给反常积分取得最小值.

3. 利用递推公式计算反常积分 ${I}_{n} = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {n \in  \mathbf{N}}\right)$ .

解 ${I}_{0} = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  -{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty } = 1$ .

当 $n \geq  1$ 时,

$$
{I}_{n} =  - {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right)  =  - {\left\lbrack  {x}^{n}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty } + n{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n - 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x = n{I}_{n - 1},
$$

故有 ${I}_{n} = n!$ .

24. 计算反常积分 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解

$$
\int \ln x\mathrm{\;d}x = x\ln x - \int x \cdot  \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = x\ln x - x + C,
$$

因此

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}\ln x\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  x\ln x - x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} =  - 1 - \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\left( {x\ln x - x}\right)  =  - 1.
$$

### 习题 5-5 反常积分的审敛法 $\Gamma$ 函数



21. 判定下列反常积分的收敛性:

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{{x}^{2}}{{x}^{4} + {x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (2) ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} + 1}}$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\sin \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (4) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x\left| {\sin x}\right| }$ ；

(5) ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{x\arctan x}{1 + {x}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (6) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( \ln x\right) }^{3}}$ ;

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{{x}^{4}\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{4}}}$ ; (8) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ .

解 (1) 由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{x}^{2} \cdot  \frac{{x}^{2}}{{x}^{4} + {x}^{2} + 1} = 1$ ,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{{x}^{2}}{{x}^{4} + {x}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 收敛.

(2)由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{x}^{\frac{5}{3}} \cdot  \frac{1}{x\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} + 1}} = 1$ ,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} + 1}}$ 收敛.

(3) 由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{x}^{2} \cdot  \sin \frac{1}{{x}^{2}} = 1$ ,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\sin \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 收敛.

(4)由于当 $x \geq  0$ 时, $\frac{1}{1 + x\left| {\sin x}\right| } \geq  \frac{1}{1 + x}$ ,且 ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x}$ 发散,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + x\left| {\sin x}\right| }$ 发散.

(5) 由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{x}^{2} \cdot  \frac{x\arctan x}{1 + {x}^{3}} = \frac{\pi }{2}$ ,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{x\arctan x}{1 + {x}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 收敛.

(6) $x = 1$ 是被积函数的瑕点. 由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ + }}}\left( {x - 1}\right)  \cdot  \frac{1}{{\left( \ln x\right) }^{3}} =  + \infty$ ,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\left( \ln x\right) }^{3}}$ 发散.

(7) $x = 1$ 是被积函数的瑕点. 由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}} \cdot  \frac{{x}^{4}}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{4}}} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{{x}^{4}\mathrm{\;d}x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{4}}}$ 收敛.

(8) 被积函数有两个瑕点: $x = 1,x = 2$ . 由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ + }}}{\left( x - 1\right) }^{\frac{1}{3}}\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}} =$ -1,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{1 - 5}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ 收敛；又因为 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {2}^{ - }}}{\left( x - 2\right) }^{\frac{1}{3}}\frac{1}{\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}} = 1$ ,因此 ${\int }_{1.5}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ 收敛,故 ${\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ 收敛.

2. 设反常积分 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛,证明反常积分 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 绝对收敛.

解 因为 $\left| \frac{f\left( x\right) }{x}\right|  \leq  \frac{{f}^{2}\left( x\right)  + \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}{2}$ ,由于 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛, ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 也收敛,因此 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\left| \frac{f\left( x\right) }{x}\right| \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛. 即 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 绝对收敛.

3. 用 $\Gamma$ 函数表示下列积分,并指出这些积分的收敛范围：

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {n > 0}\right)$ ; (2) ${\int }_{0}^{1}{\left( \ln \frac{1}{x}\right) }^{p}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ；

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{m}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {n \neq  0}\right)$ .

解 (1) 令 $u = {x}^{n}$ ,即 $x = {u}^{\frac{1}{n}}$ ,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{n}{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{\mathrm{e}}^{-u}{u}^{\frac{1}{n} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{1}{n}\Gamma \left( \frac{1}{n}\right) ,
$$

在 $n > 0$ 时都收敛.

(2)令 $u = \ln \frac{1}{x}$ ,即 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{-u}$ ,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}{\left( \ln \frac{1}{x}\right) }^{p}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{+\infty }^{0} - {u}^{p}{\mathrm{e}}^{-u}\mathrm{\;d}u = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{u}^{p}{\mathrm{e}}^{-u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \Gamma \left( {p + 1}\right) ,
$$

当 $p >  - 1$ 时收敛.

(3)令 $u = {x}^{n}$ ,即 $x = {u}^{\frac{1}{n}}$ .

当 $n > 0$ 时, ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{m}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{n}{u}^{\frac{m + 1}{n} - 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-u}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{1}{n}\Gamma \left( \frac{m + 1}{n}\right)$ ,

当 $n < 0$ 时, ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{m}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{+\infty }^{0}\frac{1}{n}{u}^{\frac{m + 1}{n} - 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-u}\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \frac{1}{n}\Gamma \left( \frac{m + 1}{n}\right)$ ,

故 ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{m}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{n}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{\left| n\right| }\Gamma \left( \frac{m + 1}{n}\right)$ ,当 $\frac{m + 1}{n} > 0$ 时收敛.

24. 证明 $\Gamma \left( \frac{{2k} + 1}{2}\right)  = \frac{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2k} - 1}\right) \sqrt{\pi }}{{2}^{k}}$ ,其中 $k \in  {\mathbf{N}}_{ + }$ .

证 $\Gamma \left( \frac{{2k} + 1}{2}\right)  = \frac{{2k} - 1}{2}\Gamma \left( \frac{{2k} - 1}{2}\right)  = \frac{{2k} - 1}{2} \cdot  \frac{{2k} - 3}{2}\Gamma \left( \frac{{2k} - 3}{2}\right)$

$$
= \frac{{2k} - 1}{2} \cdot  \frac{{2k} - 3}{2} \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \frac{1}{2}\Gamma \left( \frac{1}{2}\right)  = \frac{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2k} - 1}\right) }{{2}^{k}}\sqrt{\pi }.
$$

25. 证明以下各式 (其中 $n \in  {\mathbf{N}}_{ + }$ ):

(1) $2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {2n}\right)  = {2}^{n}\Gamma \left( {n + 1}\right)$ ;

(2) $1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2n} - 1}\right)  = \frac{\Gamma \left( {2n}\right) }{{2}^{n - 1}\Gamma \left( n\right) }$ ；

(3) $\sqrt{\pi }\Gamma \left( {2n}\right)  = {2}^{{2n} - 1}\Gamma \left( n\right) \Gamma \left( {n + \frac{1}{2}}\right)$ .

证 $\left( 1\right) 2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {2n}\right)  = {2}^{n}n! = {2}^{n}\Gamma \left( {n + 1}\right)$ .

(2) $1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2n} - 1}\right)  = \frac{\left( {{2n} - 1}\right) !}{2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2n} - 2}\right) } = \frac{\Gamma \left( {2n}\right) }{{2}^{n - 1}\left( {n - 1}\right) !} = \frac{\Gamma \left( {2n}\right) }{{2}^{n - 1}\Gamma \left( n\right) }$ .

(3) 因为 $\sqrt{\pi }\Gamma \left( {2n}\right)  = \left( {{2n} - 1}\right) !\sqrt{\pi }$ ,

$$
\Gamma \left( n\right) \Gamma \left( {n + \frac{1}{2}}\right)  = \left( {n - 1}\right) !\frac{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2n} - 1}\right) \sqrt{\pi }}{{2}^{n}}
$$

$$
= \frac{2 \cdot  4 \cdot  6 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2n} - 2}\right) }{{2}^{n - 1}} \cdot  \frac{1 \cdot  3 \cdot  5 \cdot  \cdots  \cdot  \left( {{2n} - 1}\right) \sqrt{\pi }}{{2}^{n}}
$$

$$
= \frac{\left( {{2n} - 1}\right) !}{{2}^{{2n} - 1}}\sqrt{\pi },
$$

因此结论成立.

### 总习题五


21. 填空：
(1)函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上有界是 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上可积的_____条件,而 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续是 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上可积的_____条件；

(2)对 $\lbrack a, + \infty )$ 上非负、连续的函数 $f\left( x\right)$ ,它的变上限积分 ${\int }_{a}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 在 $\lbrack a, + \infty )$ 上有界是反常积分 ${\int }_{a}^{+\infty }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛的_____条件；

* (3) 绝对收敛的反常积分 ${\int }_{a}^{+\infty }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 一定_____；

(4)函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上有定义且 $\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上可积,此时积分 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ _____存在.

( 5 )设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 连续,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( {{t}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t =$ _____.

(2)充分必要. (3) 收敛.

(4) 不一定. 例如 $f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{l} 1,x\text{ 为有理数,} \\   - 1,x\text{ 为无理数,} \end{array}\right.$ 则 $\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|  = 1$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上可积,而 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 不存在.

(5) ${xf}\left( {-{x}^{2}}\right)$ . 作换元 $u = {t}^{2} - {x}^{2}$ ,则

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( {{t}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( {{t}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( {{t}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-{x}^{2}}^{0}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{-{x}^{2}}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u,
$$

因此

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}{\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( {{t}^{2} - {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t =  - \frac{1}{2}f\left( {-{x}^{2}}\right)  \cdot  \left( {-{2x}}\right)  = {xf}\left( {-{x}^{2}}\right) .
$$

2. 以下两题中给出了四个结论, 从中选出一个正确的结论:

(1)设 $I = {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{{x}^{4}}{\sqrt{1 + x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,则估计 $I$ 值的大致范围为(   ).

(A) $0 \leq  I \leq  \frac{\sqrt{2}}{10}$ (B) $\frac{\sqrt{2}}{10} \leq  I \leq  \frac{1}{5}$

(C) $\frac{1}{5} < I < 1$ (D) $I \geq  1$

(2)设 $F\left( x\right)$ 是连续函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 的一个原函数,则必有(   ).

(A) $F\left( x\right)$ 是偶函数 $\Leftrightarrow  f\left( x\right)$ 是奇函数

(B) $F\left( x\right)$ 是奇函数 $\Leftrightarrow  f\left( x\right)$ 是偶函数

(C) $F\left( x\right)$ 是周期函数 $\Leftrightarrow  f\left( x\right)$ 是周期函数

(D) $F\left( x\right)$ 是单调函数 $\Leftrightarrow  f\left( x\right)$ 是单调函数

解 (1) 当 $0 \leq  x \leq  1$ 时, $\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}{x}^{4} \leq  \frac{{x}^{4}}{\sqrt{1 + x}} \leq  {x}^{4}$ ,因此

$$
\frac{\sqrt{2}}{10} = {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}{x}^{4}\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{{x}^{4}}{\sqrt{1 + x}}\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{4}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{5},
$$

故选 (B).

(2) 记 $G\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,则 $G\left( x\right)$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的一个原函数,且

$G\left( x\right)$ 是奇 (偶) 函数 $\Leftrightarrow  f\left( x\right)$ 是偶 (奇) 函数,

又 $F\left( x\right)  = G\left( x\right)  + C$ ,其中 $C$ 是一常数,而常数是偶函数,故由奇、偶函数的性质知应选 (A).

取周期函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \cos x + 1$ ,则 $F\left( x\right)  = \sin x + x + C$ 不是周期函数,故 (C) 不成立; 取单调增加函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {2x},x \in  \mathbf{R}$ ,则 $F\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2} + C$ 在 $\mathbf{R}$ 上不是单调函数,故 (D) 不成立.

23. 回答下列问题：

(1)设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 及 $g\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( x\right)  \geq  g\left( x\right)$ ,那么 ${\int }_{a}^{b}\lbrack f\left( x\right)  -$ $g\left( x\right) \rbrack \mathrm{d}x$ 在几何上表示什么?

(2)设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,那么 ${\int }_{a}^{b}\pi {f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 在几何上表示什么?

(3)如果在时刻 $t$ 以 $\varphi \left( t\right)$ 的流量(单位时间内流过的流体的体积或质量)向一水池注水,那么 ${\int }_{{t}_{1}}^{{t}_{2}}\varphi \left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 表示什么?

(4)如果某国人口增长的速率为 $u\left( t\right)$ ,那么 ${\int }_{{T}_{1}}^{{T}_{2}}u\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 表示什么？

(5) 如果一公司经营某种产品的边际利润函数为 ${P}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ ,那么 ${\int }_{1000}^{2000}{P}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 表示什么?

解 (1) ${\int }_{a}^{b}\left\lbrack  {f\left( x\right)  - g\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$ 表示由曲线 $y = f\left( x\right) ,y = g\left( x\right)$ 以及直线 $x = a$ , $x = b$ 所围成的图形的面积.

( 2 ) ${\int }_{a}^{b}\pi {f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 表示 ${xOy}$ 面上,由曲线 $y = f\left( x\right) ,x = a,x = b$ 以及 $x$ 轴所围成的图形绕 $x$ 轴旋转一周而得到的旋转体的体积.

(3) ${\int }_{{t}_{1}}^{{t}_{2}}\varphi \left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 表示在时间段 $\left\lbrack  {{t}_{1},{t}_{2}}\right\rbrack$ 内向水池注入的水的总量.

(4) ${\int }_{{T}_{1}}^{{T}_{2}}u\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 表示该国在 $\left\lbrack  {{T}_{1},{T}_{2}}\right\rbrack$ 时间段内增加的人口总量.

(5) ${\int }_{1000}^{2000}{P}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 表示从经营第 1000 个产品起一直到第 2000 个产品的利润总量. 3°4. 利用定积分的定义计算下列极限：

(1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1}{n}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\sqrt{1 + \frac{i}{n}}$ ; (2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{1}^{p} + {2}^{p} + \cdots  + {n}^{p}}{{n}^{p + 1}}\left( {p > 0}\right)$ .

解 (1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1}{n}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}\sqrt{1 + \frac{i}{n}} = {\int }_{0}^{1}\sqrt{1 + x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  \frac{2}{3}{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = \frac{2}{3}\left( {2\sqrt{2} - 1}\right)$ .

(2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{1}^{p} + {2}^{p} + \cdots  + {n}^{p}}{{n}^{p + 1}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1}{n}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{i = 1}}^{n}{\left( \frac{i}{n}\right) }^{p} = {\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{p}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{p + 1}$ .

25. 求下列极限:

(1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  a}}\frac{x}{x - a}{\int }_{a}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,其中 $f\left( x\right)$ 连续； (2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}{\left( \arctan t\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}}$ .

解 (1) 记 $F\left( x\right)  = x{\int }_{a}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  a}}\frac{x}{x - a}{\int }_{a}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  a}}\frac{F\left( x\right)  - F\left( a\right) }{x - a} = {F}^{\prime }\left( a\right)  = {af}\left( a\right) .
$$

(2)先证明所求极限为未定式 $\frac{\infty }{\infty }$ . 由于当 $x > \tan 1$ 时, $\arctan x > 1$ ,记 $c = {\int }_{0}^{\tan 1}{\left( \arctan t\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,则当 $x > \tan 1$ 时,有

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}{\left( \arctan t\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t = c + {\int }_{\tan 1}^{x}{\left( \arctan t\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t > c + {\int }_{\tan 1}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}t = c + x - \tan 1;
$$

故有 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{\int }_{0}^{x}{\left( \arctan t\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t =  + \infty$ ,从而利用洛必达法则有

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}{\left( \arctan t\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{{\left( \arctan x\right) }^{2}}{\frac{x}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}}} = \frac{{\pi }^{2}}{4}.
$$

26. 下列计算是否正确, 试说明理由:

(1) ${\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{2}} =  - {\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( \frac{1}{x}\right) }{1 + {\left( \frac{1}{x}\right) }^{2}} = {\left\lbrack  -\arctan \frac{1}{x}\right\rbrack  }_{-1}^{1} =  - \frac{\pi }{2}$ ;

(2)因为

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + x + 1}\frac{x = \frac{1}{t}}{} - {\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{{t}^{2} + t + 1},
$$

所以

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + x + 1} = 0.
$$

(3) ${\int }_{-\infty }^{+\infty }\frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{A \rightarrow   + \infty }}{\int }_{-A}^{A}\frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ .

解 (1) 不对. 因为 $u = \frac{1}{x}$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,1}\right\rbrack$ 上有间断点 $x = 0$ ,不符合换元法的要求. 而由习题 5-1 的第 12 题可知该积分一定为正, 因此该积分计算不对. 事实上,

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{2}} = {\left\lbrack  \arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{-1}^{1} = \frac{\pi }{2}.
$$

(2)不对. 原因与(1)相同. 事实上,

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{x}^{2} + x + 1} = {\int }_{-1}^{1}\frac{1}{{\left( x + \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} + {\left( \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {x + \frac{1}{2}}\right)
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \frac{2}{\sqrt{3}}\arctan \frac{{2x} + 1}{\sqrt{3}}\right\rbrack  }_{-1}^{1} = \frac{\pi }{\sqrt{3}}.
$$

(3) 不对. 因为 ${\int }_{0}^{A}\frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + {A}^{2}}\right)$ ,当 $A \rightarrow   + \infty$ 时极限不存在,故 ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 发散,也就得到 ${\int }_{-\infty }^{+\infty }\frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 发散.

2.7. 设 $x > 0$ ,证明 ${\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{1}{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t + {\int }_{0}^{\frac{1}{x}}\frac{1}{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{\pi }{2}$ .

证 记 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{1}{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t + {\int }_{0}^{\frac{1}{x}}\frac{1}{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,则当 $x > 0$ 时,有

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{2}} + \frac{1}{1 + \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}} \cdot  \left( {-\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\right)  = 0,
$$

由拉格朗日中值定理的推论, 得

$$
f\left( x\right)  \equiv  C\;\left( {x > 0}\right) .
$$

而 $f\left( 1\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{1}{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t + {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{1}{1 + {t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{\pi }{2}$ ,故 $C = \frac{\pi }{2}$ ,从而结论成立.

2 8 . 设 $p > 0$ ,证明

$$
\frac{p}{1 + p} < {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{p}} < 1
$$

证 由于当 $p > 0,0 < x < 1$ 时, $0 < \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{p}} < 1$ ,因此有 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{p}} < 1$ . 又

$$
1 - {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{p}} = {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{{x}^{p}\mathrm{\;d}x}{1 + {x}^{p}} < {\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{p}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{1 + p},
$$

故有 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{p}} > \frac{p}{1 + p}$ ,原题得证.

2 9. 设 $f\left( x\right) \text{、}g\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上均连续,证明:

(1) ${\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{2} \leq  {\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \cdot  {\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ (柯西 - 施瓦茨不等式)；

(2) ${\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}{\left\lbrack  f\left( x\right)  + g\left( x\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}} \leq  {\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}} + {\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}}$ (闵可夫斯基不等式).

证 (1) 对任意实数 $\lambda$ ,有 ${\int }_{a}^{b}{\left\lbrack  f\left( x\right)  + \lambda g\left( x\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x \geq  0$ ,即

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + {2\lambda }{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + {\lambda }^{2}{\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \geq  0,
$$

上式左边是一个关于 $\lambda$ 的二次三项式,它非负的条件是其系数判别式非正,即有

$$
4{\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{2} - 4{\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \cdot  {\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  0,
$$

从而本题得证.

(2) ${\int }_{a}^{b}{\left\lbrack  f\left( x\right)  + g\left( x\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{a}^{b}\left\lbrack  {{f}^{2}\left( x\right)  + {2f}\left( x\right) g\left( x\right)  + {g}^{2}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= {\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + 2{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + {\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
\leq  {\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + 2{\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x{\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}} + {\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x.
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  {\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}} + {\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}{g}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}}\right\rbrack  }^{2},
$$

从而本题得证. 1910. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( x\right)  > 0$ . 证明

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \cdot  {\int }_{a}^{b}\frac{1}{f\left( x\right) }\mathrm{d}x \geq  {\left( b - a\right) }^{2}.
$$

证 根据上一题所证的柯西 - 施瓦茨不等式, 有

$$
{\left( {\int }_{a}^{b}\sqrt{f\left( x\right) } \cdot  \frac{1}{\sqrt{f\left( x\right) }}\mathrm{d}x\right) }^{2} \leq  {\int }_{a}^{b}{\left( \sqrt{f\left( x\right) }\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x \cdot  {\int }_{a}^{b}{\left( \frac{1}{\sqrt{f\left( x\right) }}\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

即得

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \cdot  {\int }_{a}^{b}\frac{1}{f\left( x\right) }\mathrm{d}x \geq  {\left( b - a\right) }^{2}.
$$

1211. 计算下列积分:

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{x + \sin x}{1 + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (2) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \left( {1 + \tan x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ；

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{a}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}\left( {a > 0}\right)$ ； (4) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{1 - \sin {2x}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(5) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {\cos }^{2}x}$ ; (6) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }x\sqrt{{\cos }^{2}x - {\cos }^{4}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ;

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }{x}^{2}\left| {\cos x}\right| \mathrm{d}x$ ; (8) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x + 1} + {\mathrm{e}}^{3 - x}}$ ;

(9) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| {x}^{2} - x\right| }}$ ; (10) ${\int }_{0}^{x}\max \left\{  {{t}^{3},{t}^{2},1}\right\}  \mathrm{d}t$ .

解 (1) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{x + \sin x}{1 + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{x}{1 + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x + {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\sin x}{1 + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{x}{2}{\sec }^{2}\frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x - {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{1}{1 + \cos x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {1 + \cos x}\right)
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  x\tan \frac{x}{2}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} - {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\tan \frac{x}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x - {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + \cos x\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{2} + {\left\lbrack  2\ln \cos \frac{x}{2}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} + \ln 2 = \frac{\pi }{2}.
$$

(2) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \left( {1 + \tan x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \frac{\cos x + \sin x}{\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \left( {\cos x + \sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x - {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x\text{,}
$$

而

$$
{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \left( {\cos x + \sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \left\lbrack  {\sqrt{2}\cos \left( {\frac{\pi }{4} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
\overset{x = \frac{\pi }{4} - u}{ = } - {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{0}\left( {\ln \sqrt{2} + \ln \cos u}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi \ln 2}{8} + {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

故

$$
{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \left( {1 + \tan x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{\pi \ln 2}{8}.
$$

(3) ${\int }_{0}^{a}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x + \sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}^{2}}}\frac{x = a\sin u}{}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u}{\sin u + \cos u} = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u}{\cos u + \sin u}$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\left( {{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u}{\sin u + \cos u} + {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u}{\cos u + \sin u}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{\pi }{4}.
$$

(4) ${\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{1 - \sin {2x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{{\sin }^{2}x + {\cos }^{2}x - 2\sin x\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\left| {\sin x - \cos x}\right| \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\left( {\cos x - \sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x + {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \sin x + \cos x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}} + {\left\lbrack  -\cos x - \sin x\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}
$$

$$
= 2\left( {\sqrt{2} - 1}\right) \text{.}
$$

(5) 注意到 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \frac{{\pi }^{ - }}{2}}}\arctan \frac{\tan x}{\sqrt{2}} = \frac{\pi }{2}$ ,因此有

$$
{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {\cos }^{2}x} = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{{\sec }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x}{{\sec }^{2}x + 1} = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\tan x}\right) }{{\tan }^{2}x + 2}
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\arctan \frac{\tan x}{\sqrt{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} = \frac{\pi }{2\sqrt{2}}.
$$

(6) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }x\sqrt{{\cos }^{2}x - {\cos }^{4}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }x\left| {\cos x}\right| \sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{2}{\int }_{0}^{\pi }\left| {\cos x}\right| \sin x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{2}\left\lbrack  {{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\cos x\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x - {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\pi }\cos x\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{2}{\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{2}{\sin }^{2}x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} - \frac{\pi }{2}{\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{2}{\sin }^{2}x\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\pi } = \frac{\pi }{2}.
$$

(7) ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }{x}^{2}\left| {\cos x}\right| \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{x}^{2}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x - {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\pi }{x}^{2}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  {x}^{2}\sin x + 2x\cos x - 2\sin x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} -
$$

$$
{\left\lbrack  {x}^{2}\sin x + 2x\cos x - 2\sin x\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\pi }
$$

$$
= \frac{{\pi }^{2}}{2} + {2\pi } - 4\text{.}
$$

(8) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x + 1} + {\mathrm{e}}^{3 - x}} = \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}}{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x - 1}\right) }{{\mathrm{e}}^{{2x} - 2} + 1} = \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}}{\left\lbrack  \arctan \left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x - 1}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty }$

$$
= \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{2}}\left( {\frac{\pi }{2} - \arctan \frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}\right) .
$$

(9) ${\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| {x}^{2} - x\right| }} = {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x - {x}^{2}}} = {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) }{\sqrt{1 - {\left( 2x - 1\right) }^{2}}}$ ;

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \arcsin \left( 2x - 1\right) \right\rbrack  }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1} = \frac{\pi }{2};
$$

$$
{\int }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| {x}^{2} - x\right| }} = {\int }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - x}} = {\int }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) }{\sqrt{{\left( 2x - 1\right) }^{2} - 1}}
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 2x - 1 + \sqrt{{\left( 2x - 1\right) }^{2} - 1}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}} = \ln \left( {2 + \sqrt{3}}\right) ,
$$

因此

$$
{\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| {x}^{2} - x\right| }} = {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| {x}^{2} - x\right| }} + {\int }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| {x}^{2} - x\right| }}
$$

$$
= \frac{\pi }{2} + \ln \left( {2 + \sqrt{3}}\right) \text{.}
$$

( 10 )当 $x <  - 1$ 时,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}\max \left\{  {{t}^{3},{t}^{2},1}\right\}  \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{-1}\mathrm{\;d}t + {\int }_{-1}^{x}{t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3} - \frac{2}{3};
$$

当 $- 1 \leq  x \leq  1$ 时,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}\max \left\{  {{t}^{3},{t}^{2},1}\right\}  \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}t = x;
$$

当 $x > 1$ 时,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}\max \left\{  {{t}^{3},{t}^{2},1}\right\}  \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{1}\mathrm{\;d}t + {\int }_{1}^{x}{t}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{1}{4}{x}^{4} + \frac{3}{4}.
$$

因此

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}\max \left\{  {{t}^{3},{t}^{2},1}\right\}  \mathrm{d}t = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3} - \frac{2}{3}, & x <  - 1, \\  x, &  - 1 \leq  x \leq  1, \\  \frac{1}{4}{x}^{4} + \frac{3}{4}, & x > 1. \end{array}\right.
$$

12. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 为连续函数,证明

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \left( {x - t}\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{x}\left( {{\int }_{0}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u}\right) \mathrm{d}t.
$$

证 ${\int }_{0}^{x}\left( {{\int }_{0}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u}\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\left\lbrack  t{\int }_{0}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{x} - {\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$

$$
= x{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u - {\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t
$$

$$
= x{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - {\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{x}\left( {x - t}\right) f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t.
$$

本题也可利用原函数性质来证明,记等式左端的函数为 $F\left( x\right)$ 、右端的函数为 $G\left( x\right)$ ,则

$$
{F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\left( x{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - {\int }_{0}^{x}tf\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t\right) }^{\prime } = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t,
$$

$$
{G}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t,
$$

即 $F\left( x\right) \text{、}G\left( x\right)$ 都为函数 ${\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 的原函数,因此它们至多只差一个常数,但由于 $F\left( 0\right)  = G\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,因此必有 $F\left( x\right)  = G\left( x\right)$ .

13. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,

$$
F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{a}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{b}^{x}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{f\left( t\right) },x \in  \left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack  .
$$

证明: (1) ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  \geq  2$ ; (2) 方程 $F\left( x\right)  = 0$ 在区间(a,b)内有且仅有一个根.

证 (1) ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  + \frac{1}{f\left( x\right) } \geq  2\sqrt{f\left( x\right)  \cdot  \frac{1}{f\left( x\right) }} = 2$ .

(2) $F\left( a\right)  = {\int }_{b}^{a}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{f\left( t\right) } =  - {\int }_{a}^{b}\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{f\left( t\right) } < 0,F\left( b\right)  = {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t > 0$ ,由闭区间上连续函数性质可知 $F\left( x\right)$ 在区间(a,b)内必有零点,根据 (1) 可知函数 $F\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上单调增加,从而零点惟一,即方程 $F\left( x\right)  = 0$ 在区间(a,b)内有且仅有一个根.

214. 求 ${\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( {x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ ,其中

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}, & x < 0, \\  \frac{1}{1 + x}, & x \geq  0. \end{array}\right.
$$

解 ${\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( {x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{x - u + 1}{}{\int }_{-1}^{1}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u = {\int }_{-1}^{0}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{u}} + {\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{1 + u}$

$$
= {\int }_{-1}^{0}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-u}\mathrm{\;d}u}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-u}} + {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + u\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1}
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  -\ln \left( 1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-u}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{-1}^{0} + \ln 2 = \ln \left( {1 + \mathrm{e}}\right) .
$$

25. 15. 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续, $g\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续不变号. 证明至少存在一点 $\xi  \in  \left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ ,使下式成立:

$$
{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( \xi \right) {\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\text{ (积分第一中值定理). }
$$

证 不妨设 $g\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,由定积分性质可知 ${\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \geq  0$ . 记 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上的最大值为 $M$ 、最小值为 $m$ ,则有

$$
{mg}\left( x\right)  \leq  f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right)  \leq  {Mg}\left( x\right) ,
$$

故有

$$
m{\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{a}^{b}{mg}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  {\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
\leq  {\int }_{a}^{b}{Mg}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = M{\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x.
$$

当 ${\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 0$ 时,由上述不等式可知 ${\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 0$ ,故结论成立.

当 ${\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x > 0$ 时,有

$$
m \leq  \frac{{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}{{\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x} \leq  M,
$$

由闭区间上连续函数性质,知存在 $\xi  \in  \left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ ,使得

$$
f\left( \xi \right)  = \frac{{\int }_{a}^{b}f\left( x\right) g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}{{\int }_{a}^{b}g\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x},
$$

从而结论成立.

12 *16. 证明: ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{n - 1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n - 2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {n > 1}\right)$ ,并用它证明:

$$
{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{{2n} + 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}\Gamma \left( {n + 1}\right) \;\left( {n \in  \mathbf{N}}\right) .
$$

证 当 $n > 1$ 时,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n - 1}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2}{\left\lbrack  {x}^{n - 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty } + \frac{n - 1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n - 2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{n - 1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{n - 2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

记 ${I}_{n} = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{{2n} + 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,则

$$
{I}_{n} = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{{2n} + 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{{2n} + 1 - 1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{{2n} - 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= n{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{x}^{{2n} - 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = n{I}_{n - 1},
$$

因此有

$$
{I}_{n} = n!{I}_{0} = n!{\int }_{0}^{+\infty }x{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = n!{\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{+\infty }
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}n! = \frac{1}{2}\Gamma \left( {n + 1}\right) \text{.}
$$

2° 17. 判断下列反常积分的收敛性：

(1) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\sin x}{\sqrt{{x}^{3}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (2) ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x \cdot  \sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ ;

(3) ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\cos x}{\ln x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ; (4) ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt[3]{{x}^{2}\left( {x - 1}\right) \left( {x - 2}\right) }}$ .

解 (1) $x = 0$ 为被积函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{\sin x}{\sqrt{{x}^{3}}}$ 的瑕点,而 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{x}^{\frac{1}{2}} \cdot  f\left( x\right)  = 1$ ,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛; 又由于 $\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|  \leq  \frac{1}{\sqrt{{x}^{3}}}$ ,而 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{\sqrt{{x}^{3}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 收敛,故 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛,因此 ${\int }_{0}^{+\infty }\frac{\sin x}{\sqrt{{x}^{3}}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 收敛.

( 2 ) $x = 2$ 为被积函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x \cdot  \sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ 的瑕点,而

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {2}^{ + }}}{\left( x - 2\right) }^{\frac{1}{3}} \cdot  f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2},
$$

因此 ${\int }_{2}^{3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛; 又由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{x}^{\frac{5}{3}} \cdot  f\left( x\right)  = 1$ ,因此 ${\int }_{3}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x \cdot  \sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ 收敛,故 ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x \cdot  \sqrt[3]{{x}^{2} - {3x} + 2}}$ 收敛.

(3) ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\cos x}{\ln x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{\ln x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sin x}\right)  = {\left\lbrack  \frac{\sin x}{\ln x}\right\rbrack  }_{2}^{+\infty } + {\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\sin x}{x{\ln }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$

$$
= {\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\sin x}{x{\ln }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x - \frac{\sin 2}{\ln 2},
$$

又由于 $\left| \frac{\sin x}{x{\ln }^{2}x}\right|  \leq  \frac{1}{x{\ln }^{2}x}$ ,而 ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{x{\ln }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 收敛,故 ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\left| \frac{\sin x}{x{\ln }^{2}x}\right| \mathrm{d}x$ 收敛,即 ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\sin x}{x{\ln }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 绝对收敛,因此 ${\int }_{2}^{+\infty }\frac{\cos x}{\ln x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 收敛.
