\int \frac{1 - {2u} - {u}^{2}}{{u}^{3} + {u}^{2} + u + 1}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \frac{1 - {2u} - {u}^{2}}{\left( {u + 1}\right) \left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}u = \int \left( {\frac{1}{u + 1} - \frac{2u}{{u}^{2} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \ln \frac{\left| u + 1\right| }{{u}^{2} + 1} = \ln \left| x\right|  + \ln C,
$$

故

$$
\frac{u + 1}{{u}^{2} + 1} = {Cx}
$$

代入 $u = \frac{y}{x}$ 并整理,得通解 $\frac{y + x}{{y}^{2} + {x}^{2}} = C$ . 以初值条件 $x = 1,y = 1$ 定出 $C = 1$ . 故所求特解为

$$
\frac{x + y}{{x}^{2} + {y}^{2}} = 1
$$

3. 设有连结点 $O\left( {0,0}\right)$ 和 $A\left( {1,1}\right)$ 的一段向上凸的曲线弧 $\overset{⏜}{OA}$ ,对于 $\overset{⏜}{OA}$ 上任一点 $P\left( {x,y}\right)$ ,曲线弧 $\overset{⏜}{OP}$ 与直线段 $\overline{OP}$ 所围图形的面积为 ${x}^{2}$ ,求曲线弧 $\overset{⏜}{OA}$ 的方程.

解 设曲线弧的方程为 $y = y\left( x\right)$ . 依题意,有

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}y\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x - \frac{1}{2}{xy}\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2}.
$$

上式两端对 $x$ 求导,

$$
y\left( x\right)  - \frac{1}{2}y\left( x\right)  - \frac{1}{2}x{y}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {2x},
$$

即得微分方程

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{y}{x} - 4\text{.}
$$

令 $u = \frac{y}{x}$ ,有 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = u + x\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ ,则微分方程成为

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} =  - \frac{4}{x}.
$$

积分得

$$
u =  - 4\ln x + C,
$$

因 $u = \frac{y}{x}$ ,故有

$$
y = x\left( {-4\ln x + C}\right) .
$$

又因曲线过点 $A\left( {1,1}\right)$ ,故 $1 = C$ . 于是得曲线弧的方程

$$
y = x\left( {1 - 4\ln x}\right) .
$$

13 *4. 化下列方程为齐次方程, 并求出通解:

(1) $\left( {{2x} - {5y} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}x - \left( {{2x} + {4y} - 6}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0$ ;

(2) $\left( {x - y - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x + \left( {{4y} + x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0$ ;

(3) $\left( {{3y} - {7x} + 7}\right) \mathrm{d}x + \left( {{7y} - {3x} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0$ ;

(4) $\left( {x + y}\right) \mathrm{d}x + \left( {{3x} + {3y} - 4}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0$ .

解 (1) 令 $x = X + h,y = Y + k$ ,则 $\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{d}X,\mathrm{\;d}y = \mathrm{d}Y$ ,且原方程成为

$$
\left( {{2X} - {5Y} + {2h} - {5k} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}X - \left( {{2X} + {4Y} + {2h} + {4k} - 6}\right) \mathrm{d}Y = 0.
$$

令

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {2h} - {5k} + 3 = 0, \\  {2h} + {4k} - 6 = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

解此方程组得 $h = 1,k = 1$ . 故在变换 $x = X + 1,y = Y + 1$ 下原方程化为 $\left( {{2X} - {5Y}}\right) \mathrm{d}X$ $- \left( {{2X} + {4Y}}\right) \mathrm{d}Y = 0$ ,即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}Y}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = \frac{{2X} - {5Y}}{{2X} + {4Y}} = \frac{2 - 5\frac{Y}{X}}{2 + 4\frac{Y}{X}}.
$$

又令 $u = \frac{Y}{X}$ ,有 $\frac{\mathrm{d}Y}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = u + X\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}X}$ ,则原方程成为

$$
u + X\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = \frac{2 - {5u}}{2 + {4u}},
$$

即

$$
\frac{{4u} + 2}{4{u}^{2} + {7u} - 2}\mathrm{\;d}u =  - \frac{1}{X}\mathrm{\;d}X.
$$

积分

$$
\int \frac{{4u} + 2}{4{u}^{2} + {7u} - 2}\mathrm{\;d}u = \int \left( {\frac{2}{3} \cdot  \frac{1}{u + 2} + \frac{4}{3} \cdot  \frac{1}{{4u} - 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{3}\ln \left| {u + 2}\right|  + \frac{1}{3}\ln \left| {{4u} - 1}\right|
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}\ln \left| {{\left( u + 2\right) }^{2}\left( {{4u} - 1}\right) }\right|
$$

$$
=  - \ln \left| X\right|  + \ln {C}_{1}\text{.}
$$

得

$$
\ln \left| {{\left( u + 2\right) }^{2}\left( {{4u} - 1}\right) }\right|  =  - \ln \left| {X}^{3}\right|  + \ln {C}_{2}\left( {{C}_{2} = {C}_{1}^{3}}\right) ,
$$

即

$$
{\left( u + 2\right) }^{2}\left( {{4u} - 1}\right) {X}^{3} =  \pm  {C}_{2},
$$

因 $u = \frac{Y}{X}$ ,故上式成为

$$
{\left( 2X + Y\right) }^{2}\left( {{4Y} - X}\right)  =  \pm  {C}_{2}.
$$

代入 $X = x - 1,Y = y - 1$ ,得原方程的通解

$$
{\left( 2x + y - 3\right) }^{2}\left( {{4y} - x - 3}\right)  = C.
$$

(2)将原方程写成

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{-x + y + 1}{{4y} + x - 1} = \frac{y - \left( {x - 1}\right) }{{4y} + \left( {x - 1}\right) },
$$

令 $X = x - 1,Y = y$ ,则 $\mathrm{d}y = \mathrm{d}Y,\mathrm{\;d}x = \mathrm{d}X$ ,且原方程化为

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}Y}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = \frac{Y - X}{{4Y} + X} = \frac{Y/X - 1}{{4Y}/X + 1}.
$$

又令 $u = \frac{Y}{X}$ ,有 $\frac{\mathrm{d}Y}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = u + X\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}X}$ ,则原方程成为

$$
\frac{{4u} + 1}{4{u}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}u + \frac{1}{X}\mathrm{\;d}X = 0.
$$

积分

$$
\int \left( {\frac{4u}{4{u}^{2} + 1} + \frac{1}{4{u}^{2} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u + \int \frac{\mathrm{d}X}{X}
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {4{u}^{2} + 1}\right)  + \frac{1}{2}\arctan \left( {2u}\right)  + \ln \left| X\right|  = {C}_{1},
$$

即 $\ln \left\lbrack  {{X}^{2}\left( {4{u}^{2} + 1}\right) }\right\rbrack   + \arctan \left( {2u}\right)  = C\left( {C = 2{C}_{1}}\right)$ . 将 $u = \frac{Y}{X} = \frac{y}{x - 1}$ 代入上式,得原方程的通解

$$
\ln \left\lbrack  {4{y}^{2} + {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}}\right\rbrack   + \arctan \frac{2y}{x - 1} = C.
$$

(3)令 $x = X + h,y = Y + k$ ,则 $\mathrm{d}x = \mathrm{d}X,\mathrm{\;d}y = \mathrm{d}Y$ ,且原方程成为

$$
\left( {{3Y} - {7X} + {3k} - {7h} + 7}\right) \mathrm{d}X + \left( {{7Y} - {3X} + {7k} - {3h} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}Y = 0.
$$

令

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {3k} - {7h} + 7 = 0, \\  {7k} - {3h} + 3 = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

解此方程组,得 $h = 1,k = 0$ . 故在变换 $x = X + 1,y = Y$ 下,原方程化为 $\left( {{3Y} - {7X}}\right) \mathrm{d}X +$ $\left( {{7Y} - {3X}}\right) \mathrm{d}Y = 0$ ,即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}Y}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = \frac{{7X} - {3Y}}{{7Y} - {3X}} = \frac{7 - {3Y}/X}{{7Y}/X - 3}
$$

又令 $u = \frac{Y}{X}$ ,有 $\frac{\mathrm{d}Y}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = u + X\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}X}$ ,则原方程成为

$$
u + X\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}X} = \frac{7 - {3u}}{{7u} - 3},
$$

即

$$
\frac{{7u} - 3}{{u}^{2} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}u =  - 7\frac{\mathrm{d}X}{X},
$$

积分

$$
\int \left( {\frac{2}{u - 1} + \frac{5}{u + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u =  - 7\int \frac{\mathrm{d}X}{X}
$$

得

$$
2\ln \left| {u - 1}\right|  + 5\ln \left| {u + 1}\right|  =  - 7\ln \left| X\right|  + \ln {C}_{1}.
$$

即 ${X}^{7}{\left( u - 1\right) }^{2}{\left( u + 1\right) }^{5} =  \pm  {C}_{1}$ . 将 $u = \frac{Y}{X} = \frac{y}{x - 1}$ 代入上式,得原方程的通解

$$
{\left( y - x + 1\right) }^{2}{\left( y + x - 1\right) }^{5} = C.
$$

( 4 )将原方程写成 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{x + y}{4 - 3\left( {x + y}\right) }$ (该方程属于 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = f\left( {{ax} + {by} + c}\right)$ 类型,解此

类方程,一般可令 $u = {ax} + {by} + c)$ . 令 $u = x + y$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - 1$ ,且原方程成为

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - 1 = \frac{u}{4 - {3u}},
$$

即

$$
\frac{{3u} - 4}{u - 2}\mathrm{\;d}u = 2\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

积分得 ${3u} + 2\ln \left| {u - 2}\right|  = {2x} + C$ . 将 $u = x + y$ 代入上式,得原方程的通解

$$
x + {3y} + 2\ln \left| {x + y - 2}\right|  = C.
$$

### 习题 7-4 一阶线性微分方程



121. 求下列微分方程的通解:

(1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ ; (2) $x{y}^{\prime } + y = {x}^{2} + {3x} + 2$ ;

(3) ${y}^{\prime } + y\cos x = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sin x}$ ; (4) ${y}^{\prime } + y\tan x = \sin {2x}$ ;

(5) $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) {y}^{\prime } + {2xy} - \cos x = 0$ ; (6) $\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{\mathrm{d}\theta } + {3\rho } = 2$ ;

(7) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + {2xy} = {4x}$ ; (8) $y\ln y\mathrm{\;d}x + \left( {x - \ln y}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0$ ;

(9) $\left( {x - 2}\right) \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = y + 2{\left( x - 2\right) }^{3}$ ； ( 10 ) $\left( {{y}^{2} - {6x}}\right) \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + {2y} = 0$ . 解 (1) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \mathrm{d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \mathrm{d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {x + C}\right) \text{.}
$$

(2)将方程改写成 ${y}^{\prime } + \frac{1}{x}y = x + 3 + \frac{2}{x}$ ,则

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {x + 3 + \frac{2}{x}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = \frac{1}{x}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {x + 3 + \frac{2}{x}}\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{x}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {{x}^{2} + {3x} + 2}\right) \mathrm{d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = \frac{1}{x}\left( {\frac{{x}^{3}}{3} + \frac{3}{2}{x}^{2} + {2x} + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{{x}^{2}}{3} + \frac{3x}{2} + 2 + \frac{C}{x}\text{.}
$$

(3) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sin x} \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sin x}\left( {\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sin x} \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{\sin x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sin x}\left( {x + C}\right) \text{.}
$$

(4) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \tan x\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int \sin {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \tan x\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= \cos x\left( {\int \frac{\sin {2x}}{\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = \cos x\left( {\int 2\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= C\cos x - 2{\cos }^{2}x\text{.}
$$

(5)将原方程写成 ${y}^{\prime } + \frac{2x}{{x}^{2} - 1}y = \frac{\cos x}{{x}^{2} - 1}$ ,则

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{2x}{{x}^{2} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int \frac{\cos x}{{x}^{2} - 1}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{2x}{{x}^{2} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{x}^{2} - 1}\left\lbrack  {\int \frac{\cos x}{{x}^{2} - 1}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = \frac{1}{{x}^{2} - 1}\left( {\int \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{\sin x + C}{{x}^{2} - 1}\text{.}
$$

(6) $\rho  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int 3\mathrm{\;d}\theta }\left( {\int 2{\mathrm{e}}^{\int 3\mathrm{\;d}\theta }\mathrm{d}\theta  + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{3\theta }}\left( {\int 2{\mathrm{e}}^{3\theta }\mathrm{d}\theta  + C}\right)$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-{3\theta }}\left( {\frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{3\theta } + C}\right)  = \frac{2}{3} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-{3\theta }}.
$$

(7) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int {{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}}\left( {\int {4x}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int {{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\left( {\int {4x}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\left( {2{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} + C}\right)  = 2 + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}.
$$

(8)将原方程写成 $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + \frac{1}{y\ln y}x = \frac{1}{y}$ ,则

$$
x = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y\ln y}}\left( {\int \frac{1}{y}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y\ln y}}\mathrm{\;d}y + {C}_{1}}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\ln \left| {\ln y}\right| }\left\lbrack  {\int \frac{1}{y}{\mathrm{e}}^{\ln \left| {\ln y}\right| }\mathrm{d}y + {C}_{1}}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\ln y}\left( {\int \frac{\ln y}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y + {C}_{1}}\right)  = \frac{1}{\ln y}\left( {\frac{1}{2}{\ln }^{2}y + {C}_{1}}\right) ,
$$

即 ${2x}\ln y = {\ln }^{2}y + C\left( {C = 2{C}_{1}}\right)$ .

(9)将原方程写成 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - \frac{1}{x - 2}y = 2{\left( x - 2\right) }^{2}$ ,则

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{1}{x - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int 2{\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{1}{x - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \left( {x - 2}\right) \left\lbrack  {\int 2{\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} \cdot  \frac{1}{x - 2}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \left( {x - 2}\right) \left\lbrack  {\int 2\left( {x - 2}\right) \mathrm{d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \left( {x - 2}\right) \left\lbrack  {{\left( x - 2\right) }^{2} + C}\right\rbrack   = {\left( x - 2\right) }^{3} + C\left( {x - 2}\right) .
$$

( 10 )将原方程改写成 $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \frac{3}{y}x =  - \frac{y}{2}$ ,则

$$
x = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{3}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\left( {\int  - \frac{y}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{3}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {y}^{3}\left( {\int  - \frac{y}{2} \cdot  \frac{1}{{y}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)  = {y}^{3}\left( {\int  - \frac{1}{2{y}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {y}^{3}\left( {\frac{1}{2y} + C}\right)  = \frac{{y}^{2}}{2} + C{y}^{3}.
$$

2. 求下列微分方程满足所给初值条件的特解:

(1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - y\tan x = \sec x,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ ; (2) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + \frac{y}{x} = {\left. \frac{\sin x}{x},y\right| }_{x = \pi } = 1$ ；

(3) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + y\cot x = {\left. 5{\mathrm{e}}^{\cos x},y\right| }_{x = \frac{\pi }{2}} =  - 4$ ; ( (4) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + {3y} = 8,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 2$ ;

(5) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + \frac{2 - 3{x}^{2}}{{x}^{3}}y = 1,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = 0$ .

解 (1) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \tan x\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int \sec x{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \tan x\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-\ln \left| {\cos x}\right| }\left( {\int \sec x{\mathrm{e}}^{\ln \left| {\cos x}\right| }\mathrm{d}x + C}\right)  = \frac{1}{\cos x}\left( {\int \sec x \cdot  \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{x + C}{\cos x}\text{,}
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 0$ ,得 $C = 0$ . 故所求特解为

$$
y = \frac{x}{\cos x}.
$$

(2) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int \frac{\sin x}{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = \frac{1}{x}\left( {\int \frac{\sin x}{x} \cdot  x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{x}\left( {-\cos x + C}\right) \text{,}
$$

代入初值条件 $x = \pi ,y = 1$ ,得 $C = \pi  - 1$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y = \frac{1}{x}\left( {\pi  - 1 - \cos x}\right) .
$$

(3) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \cot x\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int 5{\mathrm{e}}^{\cos x}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \cot x\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= \frac{1}{\sin x}\left( {\int 5{\mathrm{e}}^{\cos x} \cdot  \sin x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = \frac{1}{\sin x}\left( {-5{\mathrm{e}}^{\cos x} + C}\right) ,
$$

代入初值条件 $x = \frac{\pi }{2},y =  - 4$ ,得 $C = 1$ ,故所求特解为 $y = \frac{1 - 5{\mathrm{e}}^{\cos x}}{\sin x}$ ,即

$$
y\sin x + 5{\mathrm{e}}^{\cos x} = 1.
$$

(4) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int 3\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int 8{\mathrm{e}}^{\int 3\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}}\left( {\int 8{\mathrm{e}}^{3x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}}\left( {\frac{8}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{3x} + C}\right)  = \frac{8}{3} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}},
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 2$ ,得 $C =  - \frac{2}{3}$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y = \frac{2}{3}\left( {4 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}}}\right) .
$$

(5) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \left( {\frac{2}{{x}^{3}} - \frac{3}{x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \left( {\frac{2}{{x}^{3}} - \frac{3}{x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}} + 3\ln x}\left( {\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-\left( {\frac{1}{{x}^{2}} + 3\ln x}\right) }\mathrm{d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\left( {\int \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{{x}^{3}}}}{{x}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{2}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {-\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\right)  + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\left( {\frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}} + C}\right)  = \frac{{x}^{3}}{2} + C{x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}},
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 1,y = 0$ ,得 $C =  - \frac{1}{2\mathrm{e}}$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y = \frac{{x}^{3}}{2}\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}} - 1}}\right) .
$$

3. 求一曲线的方程,这曲线通过原点,并且它在点(x,y)处的切线斜率等于 ${2x} + y$ .

解 设曲线方程为 $y = y\left( x\right)$ ,依题意有 ${y}^{\prime } = {2x} + y$ ,即

$$
{y}^{\prime } - y = {\left. 2x,y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0.
$$

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \mathrm{d}x}\left( {\int {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \mathrm{d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\int {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {-{2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + C}\right)  =  - {2x} - 2 + C{\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

由 $x = 0,y = 0$ ,得 $C = 2$ . 故所求曲线的方程为

$$
y = 2\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - x - 1}\right) .
$$

14. 设有一质量为 $m$ 的质点作直线运动,从速度等于零的时刻起,有一个与运动方向一致、大小与时间成正比 (比例系数为 ${k}_{1}$ ) 的力作用于它,此外还受一与速度成正比

(比例系数为 ${k}_{2}$ ) 的阻力作用. 求质点运动的速度与时间的函数关系.

解 依题意,有 ${ma} = {k}_{1}t - {k}_{2}v,a = \frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}t}$ ,即

$$
m\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = {k}_{1}t - {\left. {k}_{2}v,v\right| }_{t = 0} = 0.
$$

将方程改写成 $\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + \frac{{k}_{2}}{m}v = \frac{{k}_{1}}{m}t$ ,则

$$
v = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{{k}_{2}}{m}\mathrm{\;d}t}\left( {\int \frac{{k}_{1}}{m}t \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{{k}_{2}}{m}\mathrm{\;d}t}\mathrm{\;d}t + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t}\left( {\frac{{k}_{1}}{m}\int t{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t}\mathrm{\;d}t + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t}\left( {\frac{{k}_{1}}{{k}_{2}}t{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t} - \frac{{k}_{1}}{{k}_{2}}\int {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t}\mathrm{\;d}t + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t}\left( {\frac{{k}_{1}}{{k}_{2}}t{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t} - \frac{{k}_{1}m}{{k}_{2}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t} + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{{k}_{1}}{{k}_{2}}t - \frac{{k}_{1}m}{{k}_{2}^{2}} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t}.
$$

由 $t = 0,v = 0$ ,得 $C = \frac{{k}_{1}m}{{k}_{2}^{2}}$ ,故速度与时间的关系为

$$
v = \frac{{k}_{1}}{{k}_{2}}t - \frac{{k}_{1}m}{{k}_{2}^{2}}\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{{k}_{2}}{m}t}}\right) .
$$

25. 设有一个由电阻 $R = {10\Omega }$ 、电感 $L = 2\mathrm{H}$ (亨) 和电源电压 $E = {20}\sin {5t}\mathrm{\;V}$ (伏) 串联组成的电路. 开关 $K$ 合上后,电路中有电流通过. 求电流 $i$ 与时间 $t$ 的函数关系.

解 依题意,有 ${20}\sin {5t} = {10i} + 2\frac{\mathrm{d}i}{\mathrm{\;d}t}$ ,即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}i}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {5i} = {\left. {10}\sin 5t,i\right| }_{t = 0} = 0.
$$

$$
i = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int 5\mathrm{\;d}t}\left( {\int {10}\sin {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int 5\mathrm{\;d}t}\mathrm{\;d}t + {C}_{1}}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}}\left( {\int {10}\sin {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\mathrm{\;d}t + {C}_{1}}\right) ,
$$

其中,记 $I = \int {10}\sin {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,则

$$
I = 2\int \sin {5t}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\right)  = 2\sin {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t} - 2\int {\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\cos {5t} \cdot  5\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= 2\sin {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t} - 2\int \cos {5t}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\right)
$$

$$
= 2\sin {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t} - 2\cos {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t} - {10}\int \sin {5t}{\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= 2{\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\left( {\sin {5t} - \cos {5t}}\right)  - I,
$$

故 $I = {\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\left( {\sin {5t} - \cos {5t}}\right)  + {C}_{2}$ ,于是

$$
i = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}} \cdot  \left\lbrack  {{\mathrm{e}}^{5t}\left( {\sin {5t} - \cos {5t}}\right)  + C}\right\rbrack  \;\left( {C = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}}\right)
$$

$$
= \sin {5t} - \cos {5t} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}}\text{.}
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,i = 0$ ,得 $C = 1$ ,故电流 $i$ 与时间 $t$ 的函数关系为

$$
i = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}} + \sin {5t} - \cos {5t},
$$

按电学的习惯,可写成

$$
i = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}} + \sqrt{2}\sin \left( {{5t} - \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) .
$$

5 6. 验证形如 ${yf}\left( {xy}\right) \mathrm{d}x + {xg}\left( {xy}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0$ 的微分方程,可经变量代换 $v = {xy}$ 化为可分离变量的方程, 并求其通解.

解 由 $v = {xy}$ ,即 $y = \frac{v}{x}$ ,得 $\mathrm{d}y = \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}v - v\mathrm{\;d}x}{{x}^{2}}$ . 又原方程改写成 ${xyf}\left( {xy}\right) \mathrm{d}x + {x}^{2}g\left( {xy}\right)$ $\mathrm{d}y = 0$ ,并将 $v = {xy},\mathrm{\;d}y = \frac{x\mathrm{\;d}v - v\mathrm{\;d}x}{{x}^{2}}$ 代入上式,得

$$
{vf}\left( v\right) \mathrm{d}x + g\left( v\right) \left( {x\mathrm{\;d}v - v\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)  = 0,
$$

可分离变量, 得

$$
\frac{g\left( v\right) \mathrm{d}v}{v\left\lbrack  {f\left( v\right)  - g\left( v\right) }\right\rbrack  } + \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x} = 0.
$$

积分得

$$
\int \frac{g\left( v\right) \mathrm{d}v}{v\left\lbrack  {f\left( v\right)  - g\left( v\right) }\right\rbrack  } + \ln \left| x\right|  = C,
$$

代入 $v = {xy}$ 后,便是原方程的通解.

27. 用适当的变量代换将下列方程化为可分离变量的方程, 然后求出通解:

(1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = {\left( x + y\right) }^{2}$ ; (2) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{1}{x - y} + 1$ ;

(3) $x{y}^{\prime } + y = y\left( {\ln x + \ln y}\right)$ ;

(4) ${y}^{\prime } = {y}^{2} + 2\left( {\sin x - 1}\right) y + {\sin }^{2}x - 2\sin x - \cos x + 1$ ;

(5) $y\left( {{xy} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x + x\left( {1 + {xy} + {x}^{2}{y}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0$ .

解 (1)令 $u = x + y$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = 1 + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ ,且原方程变为 $\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = {u}^{2} + 1$ ,分离变量,得

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{1 + {u}^{2}} = \mathrm{d}x.
$$

积分得 $\arctan u = x + C$ ,即 $u = \tan \left( {x + C}\right)$ ,代入 $u = x + y$ ,得原方程的通解

$$
y =  - x + \tan \left( {x + C}\right) .
$$

(2)令 $u = x - y$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = 1 - \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ ,且原方程变为 $\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} =  - \frac{1}{u}$ ,即

$$
u\mathrm{\;d}u + \mathrm{d}x = 0
$$

积分得

$$
\frac{{u}^{2}}{2} + x = {C}_{1},
$$

代入 $u = x - y$ ,得原方程的通解 ${\left( x - y\right) }^{2} + {2x} = C\left( {C = 2{C}_{1}}\right)$ .

(3)令 $u = {xy}$ ,则 ${u}^{\prime } = y + x{y}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程变为 ${u}^{\prime } = \frac{u}{x}\ln u$ ,即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{u\ln u} = \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x}.
$$

积分得 $\ln \left| {\ln u}\right|  = \ln \left| x\right|  + \ln {C}_{1}$ ,即 $u = {\mathrm{e}}^{Cx}$ . 代入 $u = {xy}$ ,得原方程的通解 ${xy} = {\mathrm{e}}^{Cx}$ , 即 $y = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{Cx}}{x}$ .

(4)将原方程写成 ${y}^{\prime } = {\left( y + \sin x - 1\right) }^{2} - \cos x$ ,令 $u = y + \sin x - 1$ ,则 ${u}^{\prime } = {y}^{\prime } +$ $\cos x$ ,且原方程变为 ${u}^{\prime } = {u}^{2}$ ,即 $\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{{u}^{2}} = \mathrm{d}x$ .

积分得 $- \frac{1}{u} = x + C$ ,即 $u =  - \frac{1}{x + C}$ . 代入 $u = y + \sin x - 1$ ,得原方程的通解

$$
y = 1 - \sin x - \frac{1}{x + C}.
$$

(5)原方程改写成 ${xy}\left( {{xy} + 1}\right)  + {x}^{2}\left( {1 + {xy} + {x}^{2}{y}^{2}}\right) \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = 0$ . 令 $u = {xy}$ ,即 $y = \frac{u}{x}$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{x\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - u}{{x}^{2}}$ ,且原方程变为

$$
u\left( {u + 1}\right)  + \left( {1 + u + {u}^{2}}\right) \left( {x\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - u}\right)  = 0,
$$

整理并分离变量,得 $\frac{1 + u + {u}^{2}}{{u}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x}$ . 积分得 $- \frac{1}{2{u}^{2}} - \frac{1}{u} + \ln \left| u\right|  = \ln \left| x\right|  + {C}_{1}$ ,代入 $u = {xy}$ ,并整理,得原方程的通解为

$$
2{x}^{2}{y}^{2}\ln \left| y\right|  - {2xy} - 1 = C{x}^{2}{y}^{2}\left( {C = 2{C}_{1}}\right) .
$$

8°8. 求下列伯努利方程的通解:

(1) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + y = {y}^{2}\left( {\cos x - \sin x}\right)$ ; (2) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - {3xy} = x{y}^{2}$ ;

(3) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + \frac{1}{3}y = \frac{1}{3}\left( {1 - {2x}}\right) {y}^{4}$ ; (4) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - y = x{y}^{5}$ ;

(5) $x\mathrm{\;d}y - \left\lbrack  {y + x{y}^{3}\left( {1 + \ln x}\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x = 0$ .

解 (1) 将原方程改写成 $\frac{1}{{y}^{2}}{y}^{\prime } + \frac{1}{y} = \cos x - \sin x$ ,并令 $z = \frac{1}{y}$ ,则 ${z}^{\prime } =  - \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}{y}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程化为

$$
{z}^{\prime } - z = \sin x - \cos x.
$$

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \mathrm{d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \mathrm{d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {\sin x - \cos x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\int \sin x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x-\int \cos x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right) ,
$$

其中 $\int \sin x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int \sin x\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\right)  =  - \sin x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + \int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,故

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {-\sin x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + C}\right)  = C{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \sin x,
$$

即 $\frac{1}{y} = C{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \sin x$ 为所求通解.

(2)将原方程改写成 ${y}^{-2}{y}^{\prime } - {3x}{y}^{-1} = x$ ,并令 $z = {y}^{-1}$ ,则 ${z}^{\prime } =  - {y}^{-2}{y}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程化为

$$
{z}^{\prime } + {3xz} =  - x,
$$

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int  - x{\mathrm{e}}^{\int {3x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2}}\left( {\int  - x{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2}}\left( {-\frac{1}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2}} + C}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{3} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2}},
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
{y}^{-1} =  - \frac{1}{3} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2}},
$$

或写成

$$
\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2} + \ln \left( {1 + \frac{3}{y}}\right)  = {C}_{1}\;\left( {{C}_{1} = \ln {3C}}\right) .
$$

(3)将原方程改写成 ${y}^{-4}{y}^{\prime } + \frac{1}{3}{y}^{-3} = \frac{1}{3}\left( {1 - {2x}}\right)$ ,并令 $z = {y}^{-3}$ ,则 ${z}^{\prime } =$ $- 3{y}^{-4}{y}^{\prime }$ ,于是原方程化为

$$
{z}^{\prime } - z = 1 - {2x}.
$$

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \mathrm{d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {1 - {2x}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \mathrm{d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {1 - {2x}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left\lbrack  {\left( {-{2x} - 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + C}\right\rbrack   =  - {2x} - 1 + C{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\text{,}
$$

即 ${y}^{-3} =  - {2x} - 1 + C{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 为所求通解.

(4)将原方程改写成 ${y}^{-5}{y}^{\prime } - {y}^{-4} = x$ ,并令 $z = {y}^{-4}$ ,则 ${z}^{\prime } =  - 4{y}^{-5}{y}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程化为

$$
{z}^{\prime } + {4z} =  - {4x},
$$

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int 4\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int  - {4x}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int {4x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{4x}}\left( {\int  - {4x}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-{4x}}\left( {-x{\mathrm{e}}^{4x} + \frac{1}{4}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x} + C}\right)  =  - x + \frac{1}{4} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-{4x}}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
{y}^{-4} =  - x + \frac{1}{4} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-{4x}}.
$$

(5) 原方程可写成 ${y}^{\prime } - \frac{1}{x}y = \left( {1 + \ln x}\right) {y}^{3}$ ,即 ${y}^{-3}{y}^{\prime } - \frac{1}{x}{y}^{-2} = 1 + \ln x$ ,令 $z = {y}^{-2}$ ,则 ${z}^{\prime } =  - 2{y}^{-3}{y}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程化为

$$
{z}^{\prime } + \frac{2}{x}z =  - 2\left( {1 + \ln x}\right) .
$$

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{2}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int  - 2\left( {1 + \ln x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{2}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {x}^{-2}\left\lbrack  {\int  - 2\left( {1 + \ln x}\right) {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {x}^{-2}\left\lbrack  {-\frac{2}{3}{x}^{3}\left( {1 + \ln x}\right)  + \frac{2}{3}\int {x}^{3} \cdot  \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {x}^{-2}\left\lbrack  {-\frac{2}{3}{x}^{3}\left( {1 + \ln x}\right)  + \frac{2}{9}{x}^{3} + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
=  - \frac{2}{3}x\left( {1 + \ln x}\right)  + \frac{2}{9}x + C{x}^{-2}.
$$

故原方程通解为

$$
{y}^{-2} =  - \frac{2}{3}x\left( {1 + \ln x}\right)  + \frac{2}{9}x + C{x}^{-2},
$$

或写成

$$
\frac{{x}^{2}}{{y}^{2}} =  - \frac{4}{9}{x}^{3} - \frac{2}{3}{x}^{3}\ln x + C.
$$

### 习题 7-5 可降阶的高阶微分方程


121. 求下列各微分方程的通解:

(1) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = x + \sin x$ ; (2) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ;

(3) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{2}}$ ; (4) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}$ ;

(5) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {y}^{\prime } + x$ ; (6) $x{y}^{\prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime } = 0$ ;

(7) $y{y}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}^{\prime 2} = 0$ ; (8) ${y}^{3}{y}^{\prime \prime } - 1 = 0$ ;

(9) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{1}{\sqrt{y}}$ ; (10) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {\left( {y}^{\prime }\right) }^{3} + {y}^{\prime }$ .

解 (1) ${y}^{\prime } = \int \left( {x + \sin x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \cos x + {C}_{1}$ ,

$$
y = \int \left( {\frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - \cos x + {C}_{1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{{x}^{3}}{6} - \sin x + {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}.
$$

(2) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = \int x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}^{\prime }{}_{1} = \left( {x - 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}^{\prime }{}_{1}$ ,

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \int \left\lbrack  {\left( {x - 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{1}^{\prime }}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x = \left( {x - 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x + {C}_{1}^{\prime }x + {C}_{2}
$$

$$
= \left( {x - 2}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{1}^{\prime }x + {C}_{2},
$$

$$
y = \int \left\lbrack  {\left( {x - 2}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{1}^{\prime }x + {C}_{2}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x = \left( {x - 2}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x + \frac{{C}_{1}^{\prime }}{2}{x}^{2} + {C}_{2}x + {C}_{3}
$$

$$
= \left( {x - 3}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{1}{x}^{2} + {C}_{2}x + {C}_{3}.
$$

(3) ${y}^{\prime } = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{1 + {x}^{2}} = \arctan x + {C}_{1}$ ,

$$
y = \int \left( {\arctan x + {C}_{1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = x\arctan x - \int \frac{x}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + {C}_{1}x
$$

$$
= x\arctan x - \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)  + {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}.
$$

(4)令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {p}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程化为 ${p}^{\prime } = 1 + {p}^{2}$ . 分离变量,得

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{1 + {p}^{2}} = \mathrm{d}x.
$$

积分得 $\arctan p = x + {C}_{1}$ ,即 $p = {y}^{\prime } = \tan \left( {x + {C}_{1}}\right)$ ,再积分得通解

$$
y = \int \tan \left( {x + {C}_{1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - \ln \left| {\cos \left( {x + {C}_{1}}\right) }\right|  + {C}_{2}.
$$

(5) 令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {p}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程可化为

$$
{p}^{\prime } - p = x.
$$

利用一阶线性方程的求解公式, 得

$$
p = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \mathrm{d}x}\left( {\int x{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \mathrm{d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + {C}_{1}}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {\int x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x + {C}_{1}}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {-x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{1}}\right)  =  - x - 1 + {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

积分得通解

$$
y = \int \left( {{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - x - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} - x + {C}_{2}.
$$

(6) 令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {p}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程化为 $x{p}^{\prime } + p = 0$ ,分离变量,得

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{p} =  - \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x},
$$

积分得 $\ln \left| p\right|  = \ln \left| \frac{1}{x}\right|  + \ln {C}_{1}$ ,即 $p = \frac{{C}_{1}}{x}$ . 再积分,得通解

$$
y = \int \frac{{C}_{1}}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {C}_{1}\ln \left| x\right|  + {C}_{2}.
$$

(7)令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {p}^{\prime } = \frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} \cdot  \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}p$ ,且原方程化为 ${yp}\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + 2{p}^{2} = 0$ . 分离变量, 得

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{p} =  - 2\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y},
$$

积分得 $\ln \left| p\right|  = \ln \frac{1}{{y}^{2}} + \ln {C}_{0}$ ,即 ${y}^{\prime } = p = \frac{{C}_{0}}{{y}^{2}}$ ,分离变量,得 ${y}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}y = {C}_{0}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,积分得 ${y}^{3} =$ $3{C}_{0}x + {C}_{2}$ ,即通解为 ${y}^{3} = {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}$ .

(8) 令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,且原方程化为 ${y}^{3}p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - 1 = 0$ . 分离变量,得

$$
p\mathrm{\;d}p = \frac{1}{{y}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}y,
$$

积分得 ${p}^{2} =  - \frac{1}{{y}^{2}} + {C}_{1}$ ,故

$$
{y}^{\prime } = p =  \pm  \sqrt{{C}_{1} - \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}} =  \pm  \frac{1}{\left| y\right| }\sqrt{{C}_{1}{y}^{2} - 1}.
$$

分离变量, 得

$$
\frac{\left| y\right| \mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{{C}_{1}{y}^{2} - 1}} =  \pm  \mathrm{d}x.
$$

由于 $\left| y\right|  = y\operatorname{sgn}\left( y\right)$ ,故上式两端积分,

$$
\operatorname{sgn}\left( y\right) \int \frac{y\mathrm{\;d}y}{\sqrt{{C}_{1}{y}^{2} - 1}} =  \pm  \int \mathrm{d}x,
$$

$$
\operatorname{sgn}\left( y\right) \sqrt{{C}_{1}{y}^{2} - 1} =  \pm  {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}.
$$

两边平方,得 ${C}_{1}{y}^{2} - 1 = {\left( {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}\right) }^{2}$ .

(9)方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{1}{\sqrt{y}}$ 属于 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = f\left( y\right)$ 型方程,除了设 ${y}^{\prime } = p,{y}^{\prime \prime } = p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ 来降阶求解外,还可以用如下方法求解:

在 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = f\left( y\right)$ 的两端乘以 $2{y}^{\prime }$ ,得

$$
2{y}^{\prime }{y}^{\prime \prime } = {2f}\left( y\right) {y}^{\prime },
$$

即 ${\left( {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\prime } = {2f}\left( y\right) {y}^{\prime }$ . 若 $F\left( y\right)$ 是 $f\left( y\right)$ 的原函数,则有

$$
{\left( {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\prime } = 2{\left\lbrack  F\left( y\right) \right\rbrack  }^{\prime },
$$

积分得到降阶的方程 ${y}^{\prime 2} = {2F}\left( y\right)  + {C}_{1}$ .

本小题按上述方法求解: 用 $2{y}^{\prime }$ 乘方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{1}{\sqrt{y}}$ 的两端,得

$$
2{y}^{\prime }{y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{2{y}^{\prime }}{\sqrt{y}}
$$

即 ${\left( {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\prime } = {\left( 4\sqrt{y}\right) }^{\prime }$ ,故 ${y}^{\prime 2} = 4\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}^{\prime }$ ,有 ${y}^{\prime } =  \pm  2\sqrt{\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}\left( {{C}_{1} = \frac{{C}_{1}^{\prime }}{4}}\right)$ .

分离变量, 得

$$
\mathrm{d}x =  \pm  \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{2\sqrt{\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}}.
$$

积分, 得

$$
x =  \pm  \int \frac{\mathrm{d}{\left( \sqrt{y}\right) }^{2}}{2\sqrt{\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}} =  \pm  \int \frac{\sqrt{y}\mathrm{\;d}\sqrt{y}}{\sqrt{\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}} =  \pm  \int \frac{\left( {\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}\right)  - {C}_{1}}{\sqrt{\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( \sqrt{y}\right)
$$

$$
=  \pm  \left\lbrack  {\int \sqrt{\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}\right)  - {C}_{1}\int \frac{1}{\sqrt{\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
=  \pm  \left\lbrack  {\frac{2}{3}{\left( \sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}} - 2{C}_{1}{\left( \sqrt{y} + {C}_{1}\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}}}\right\rbrack   + {C}_{2}.
$$

(10)令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,原方程化为 $p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} = {p}^{3} + p$ ,即

$$
p\left\lbrack  {\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \left( {1 + {p}^{2}}\right) }\right\rbrack   = 0.
$$

若 $p \equiv  0$ ,则 $y \equiv  C.y \equiv  C$ 是原方程的解,但不是通解.

若 $p ≢ 0$ ,由于 $p$ 的连续性,必在 $x$ 的某区间有 $p \neq  0$ . 于是

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \left( {1 + {p}^{2}}\right)  = 0.
$$

分离变量,得 $\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{1 + {p}^{2}} = \mathrm{d}y$ ,积分得 $\arctan p = y - {C}_{1}$ ,即 $p = \tan \left( {y - {C}_{1}}\right)$ ,亦即 $\cot \left( {y - {C}_{1}}\right)$ $\mathrm{d}y = \mathrm{d}x$ . 积分得 $\ln \sin \left( {y - {C}_{1}}\right)  = x + \ln {C}_{2}$ . 即 $\sin \left( {y - {C}_{1}}\right)  = {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,也可写成 $y =$ $\arcsin \left( {{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right)  + {C}_{1}$ .

由于当 ${C}_{2} = 0$ 时, $y = {C}_{1}$ ,故前面所得的解 $y \equiv  C$ 也包含在这个通解之内. 2. 求下列各微分方程满足所给初值条件的特解:

(1) ${y}^{3}{y}^{\prime \prime } + 1 = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = 0$ ;

(2) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - a{y}^{\prime 2} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} =  - 1$ ;

(3) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{ax},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = {\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = {\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = 0$ ;

(4) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{2y},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = {\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ ;

(5) ${y}^{\prime \prime } = 3\sqrt{y},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 2$ ;

(6) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {\left( {y}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} = 1,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ .

解 (1) 将原方程写成 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + \frac{1}{{y}^{3}} = 0$ ,两端乘以 $2{y}^{\prime }$ ,得

$$
2{y}^{\prime }{y}^{\prime \prime } + \frac{2{y}^{\prime }}{{y}^{3}} = 0,
$$

即 ${\left( {y}^{\prime 2} - \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}\right) }^{\prime } = 0$ ,由此得

$$
{y}^{\prime 2} - \frac{1}{{y}^{2}} = {C}_{1}.
$$

代入初值条件: $y = 1,{y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{1} =  - 1$ ,故有

$$
{y}^{\prime 2} = \frac{1}{{y}^{2}} - 1 = \frac{1 - {y}^{2}}{{y}^{2}},
$$

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  \pm  \frac{\sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}}}{y},
$$

分离变量, 得

$$
\frac{y\mathrm{\;d}y}{\sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}}} =  \pm  \mathrm{d}x,
$$

积分得 $- \sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}} =  \pm  x + {C}_{2}$ . 代入初值条件: $x = 1,y = 1$ ,得 $C =  \mp  1$ . 于是有

$$
- \sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}} =  \pm  \left( {x - 1}\right) .
$$

两边平方,得 ${x}^{2} + {y}^{2} = {2x}$ . 由于在点 $x = 1$ 处, $y = 1$ ,故在 $x = 1$ 的某邻域内 $y > 0$ ,因而特解可表示为

$$
y = \sqrt{{2x} - {x}^{2}}.
$$

(2)令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {p}^{\prime }$ ,原方程化为 ${p}^{\prime } - a{p}^{2} = 0$ ,分离变量即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{{p}^{2}} = a\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

积分得 $- \frac{1}{p} = {ax} + {C}_{1}$ . 代入初值条件 $x = 0,p = {y}^{\prime } =  - 1$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 1$ . 从而有 $- \frac{1}{{y}^{\prime }} =$ ${ax} + 1$ ,即

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - \frac{1}{{ax} + 1},
$$

又积分得

$$
y =  - \frac{1}{a}\ln \left( {{ax} + 1}\right)  + {C}_{2}.
$$

代入初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 0$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y =  - \frac{1}{a}\ln \left( {{ax} + 1}\right) .
$$

(3) 因 ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}$ ,并由初值条件 $x = 1,{y}^{\prime \prime } = 0$ ,故积分得

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } = {\int }_{1}^{x}{y}^{\prime \prime \prime }\mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{1}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{a}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{a}}\right) .
$$

又因 $x = 1$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,故积分得

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {\int }_{1}^{x}{y}^{\prime \prime }\mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{1}^{x}\frac{1}{a}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{a}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{a}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{a}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{a}}\right)  - {\mathrm{e}}^{a}\left( {x - 1}\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{a}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{a}x + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{a}\left( {1 - \frac{1}{a}}\right) .
$$

又因 $x = 1$ 时, $y = 0$ ,故再积分得

$$
y = {\int }_{1}^{x}{y}^{\prime }\mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{1}^{x}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{{a}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{a}x + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{a}\left( {1 - \frac{1}{a}}\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{a}^{3}}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{a}}\right)  - \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{2a}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right)  + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{a}\left( {1 - \frac{1}{a}}\right) \left( {x - 1}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{a}^{3}}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{2a}{x}^{2} + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{{a}^{2}}\left( {a - 1}\right) x + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{a}}{2{a}^{3}}\left( {{2a} - {a}^{2} - 2}\right) .
$$

(4)在原方程两端同乘以 $2{y}^{\prime }$ ,得 $2{y}^{\prime }{y}^{\prime \prime } = 2{y}^{\prime }{\mathrm{e}}^{2y}$ ,即 ${\left( {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\prime } = {\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2y}\right) }^{\prime }$ ,积分得

$$
{y}^{\prime 2} = {\mathrm{e}}^{2y} + {C}_{1}.
$$

代入初值条件: $x = 0,y = {y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{1} =  - 1$ ,从而有

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  \pm  \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2y} - 1}.
$$

分离变量后积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2y} - 1}} =  \pm  \int \mathrm{d}x
$$

即

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-y}\right) }{\sqrt{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2y}}}} =  \mp  \int \mathrm{d}x,
$$

得 $\arcsin \left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-y}\right)  =  \mp  x + {C}_{2}$ . 代入初值条件: $x = 0,y = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = \frac{\pi }{2}$ . 于是得特解

$$
{\mathrm{e}}^{-y} = \sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{2} \pm  x}\right)  = \cos x,
$$

即 $y =  - \ln \cos x = \ln \sec x$ .

(5) 在原方程两端同乘以 $2{y}^{\prime }$ ,得 $2{y}^{\prime }{y}^{\prime \prime } = 6{y}^{\prime }\sqrt{y}$ ,即 ${\left( {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\prime } = {\left( 4{y}^{\frac{3}{2}}\right) }^{\prime }$ ,积分得 ${y}^{\prime 2} =$ $4{y}^{\frac{3}{2}} + {C}_{1}$ . 代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 1,{y}^{\prime } = 2$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 0$ ,从而有 ${y}^{\prime } =  \pm  2{y}^{\frac{3}{4}}$ . 并由于 ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 2$ ,故取 ${y}^{\prime } = 2{y}^{\frac{3}{4}}$ . 分离变量后积分 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{{y}^{\frac{3}{4}}} = 2\int \mathrm{d}x$ 得 $4{y}^{\frac{1}{4}} = {2x} + {C}_{2}$ . 代入初值条件: $x = 0,y = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 4$ ,于是得特解

$$
y = {\left( \frac{x}{2} + 1\right) }^{4}.
$$

(6)令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,原方程变为 $p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + {p}^{2} = 1$ . 分离变量,得

$$
\frac{p\mathrm{\;d}p}{1 - {p}^{2}} = \mathrm{d}y.
$$

由初值条件: $y = 0,p = 0$ ,积分

$$
{\int }_{0}^{p}\frac{p\mathrm{\;d}p}{1 - {p}^{2}} = {\int }_{0}^{y}\mathrm{\;d}y
$$

得

$$
- \frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 - {p}^{2}}\right)  = y,
$$

即 $p =  \pm  \sqrt{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2y}}}$ . 又分离变量,得

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2y}}}} =  \pm  \mathrm{d}x
$$

由初值条件: $x = 0,y = 0$ ,积分

$$
{\int }_{0}^{y}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2y}}}} =  \pm  {\int }_{0}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

$$
{\int }_{0}^{y}\frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{y}\right) }{\sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2y} - 1}} =  \pm  {\int }_{0}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

得

$$
\ln \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{y} + \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2y} - 1}}\right)  =  \pm  x,
$$

即

$$
{\mathrm{e}}^{y} = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{2},
$$

或写成

$$
y = \ln \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{2}.
$$

2. 3. 试求 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = x$ 的经过点 $M\left( {0,1}\right)$ 且在此点与直线 $y = \frac{x}{2} + 1$ 相切的积分曲线.

解 由于直线 $y = \frac{x}{2} + 1$ 在(0,1)处的切线斜率为 $\frac{1}{2}$ ,依题设知,所求积分曲线是初值问题

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } = x,{\left. \;y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,{\left. \;{y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{1}{2}
$$

的解. 由 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = x$ ,积分得

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} + {C}_{1}.
$$

代入 $x = 0,{y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2}$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,即有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2} + \frac{1}{2}\text{.}
$$

再积分,得 $y = \frac{{x}^{3}}{6} + \frac{x}{2} + {C}_{2}$ ,代入 $x = 0,y = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 1$ ,于是所求积分曲线的方程为

$$
y = \frac{{x}^{3}}{6} + \frac{x}{2} + 1
$$

24. 设有一质量为 $m$ 的物体,在空中由静止开始下落,如果空气阻力为 $R = {cv}$ (其中 $c$ 为常数, $v$ 为物体运动的速度),试求物体下落的距离 $s$ 与时间 $t$ 的函数关系.

解 根据牛顿第二定律, 有关系式

$$
m\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}s}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = {mg} - c\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t},
$$

并依据题设条件, 得初值问题

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}s}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = g - \frac{c}{m}\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t},{\left. \;s\right| }_{t = 0} = 0,{\left. \;\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t}\right| }_{t = 0} = 0.
$$

令 $\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = v$ ,方程成为 $\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = g - \frac{c}{m}v$ ,分离变量后积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}v}{g - \frac{c}{m}v} = \int \mathrm{d}t
$$

得

$$
\ln \left( {g - \frac{c}{m}v}\right)  =  - \frac{c}{m}t + {C}_{1},
$$

代入初值条件 ${\left. v\right| }_{t = 0} = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = \ln g$ . 于是有

$$
v = \frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \frac{mg}{c}\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{c}{m}t}}\right) ;
$$

积分得

$$
s = \frac{mg}{c}\left( {t + \frac{m}{c}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{c}{m}t}}\right)  + {C}_{2}
$$

代入初值条件 ${\left. s\right| }_{t = 0} = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{2} =  - \frac{{m}^{2}g}{{c}^{2}}$ . 故所求特解 (即下落的距离与时间的关系) 为

$$
s = \frac{mg}{c}\left( {t + \frac{m}{c}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{c}{m}t} - \frac{m}{c}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{mg}{c}t + \frac{{m}^{2}g}{{c}^{2}}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{c}{m}t} - 1}\right) .
$$

### 习题 7-6 高阶线性微分方程



31. 下列函数组在其定义区间内哪些是线性无关的?

(1) $x,{x}^{2}$ ; (2) $x,{2x}$ ;

(3) ${\mathrm{e}}^{2x},3{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ ; (4) ${\mathrm{e}}^{-x},{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ;

(5) $\cos {2x},\sin {2x}$ ; (6) ${\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}},x{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}$ ;

(7) $\sin {2x},\cos x\sin x$ ; (8) ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x},{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin {2x}$ ;

(9) $\ln x,x\ln x$ ; (10) ${\mathrm{e}}^{ax},{\mathrm{e}}^{bx}\left( {a \neq  b}\right)$ .

解 对于两个函数构成的函数组, 如果两函数的比为常数, 则它们是线性相关的, 否则就线性无关, 因此本题中除了

(2) $\frac{x}{2x} = \frac{1}{2}$ ; (3) $\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}}{3{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}} = \frac{1}{3}$ ; (7) $\frac{\sin {2x}}{\cos x\sin x} = 2$ ,

即 (2) (3) (7) 中的函数组线性相关外, 其余的 7 个函数组中两函数之比不是常数, 从而线性无关.

2. 验证 ${y}_{1} = \cos {\omega x}$ 及 ${y}_{2} = \sin {\omega x}$ 都是方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {\omega }^{2}y = 0$ 的解,并写出该方程的通解.

解 由 ${y}_{1} = \cos {\omega x}$ ,得 ${y}_{1}^{\prime } =  - \omega \sin {\omega x},{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } =  - {\omega }^{2}\cos {\omega x}$ ; 由 ${y}_{2} = \sin {\omega x}$ ,得 ${y}_{2}^{\prime } =$ $\omega \cos {\omega x},{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } =  - {\omega }^{2}\sin {\omega x}$ ; 可见

$$
{y}_{i}^{\prime \prime } + {\omega }^{2}{y}_{i} = 0\left( {i = 1,2}\right) ,
$$

故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 都是方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {\omega }^{2}y = 0$ 的解.

又因 $\frac{{y}_{1}}{{y}_{2}} = \cot {\omega x} \neq$ 常数,故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 线性无关. 于是方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} = {C}_{1}\cos {\omega x} + {C}_{2}\sin {\omega x}.
$$

3. 验证 ${y}_{1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}$ 及 ${y}_{2} = x{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}$ 都是方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - {4x}{y}^{\prime } + \left( {4{x}^{2} - 2}\right) y = 0$ 的解,并写出该方程的通解.

解 由 ${y}_{1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}$ ,得 ${y}_{1}^{\prime } = {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}},{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } = \left( {2 + 4{x}^{2}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}$ ; 由 ${y}_{2} = x{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}$ ,得 ${y}_{2}^{\prime } = (1 +$ $\left. {2{x}^{2}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}},{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } = \left( {{6x} + 4{x}^{3}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}$ . 因

$$
{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } - {4x}{y}_{1}^{\prime } + \left( {4{x}^{2} - 2}\right) {y}_{1} = \left( {2 + 4{x}^{2}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} - {4x} \cdot  {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} + \left( {4{x}^{2} - 2}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} = 0,
$$

$$
{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } - {4x}{y}_{2}^{\prime } + \left( {4{x}^{2} - 2}\right) {y}_{2} = \left( {{6x} + 4{x}^{3}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} - {4x}\left( {1 + 2{x}^{2}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} + \left( {4{x}^{2} - 2}\right) x{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} = 0,
$$

故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 都是方程的解.

又因 $\frac{{y}_{2}}{{y}_{1}} = x \neq$ 常数,故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 线性无关,于是方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}.
$$

24. 验证:

(1) $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + \frac{1}{12}{\mathrm{e}}^{5x}$ ( ${C}_{1},{C}_{2}$ 是任意常数) 是方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 3{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = {\mathrm{e}}^{5x}$ 的通解;

(2) $y = {C}_{1}\cos {3x} + {C}_{2}\sin {3x} + \frac{1}{32}\left( {{4x}\cos x + \sin x}\right) \left( {{C}_{1},{C}_{2}}\right.$ 是任意常数) 是方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {9y} = x\cos x$ 的通解;

(3) $y = {C}_{1}{x}^{2} + {C}_{2}{x}^{2}\ln x\left( {{C}_{1},{C}_{2}}\right.$ 是任意常数) 是方程 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}^{\prime } + {4y} = 0$ 的通解;

(4) $y = {C}_{1}{x}^{5} + \frac{{C}_{2}}{x} - \frac{{x}^{2}}{9}\ln x\left( {{C}_{1},{C}_{2}}\right.$ 是任意常数 $)$ 是方程 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}^{\prime } - {5y} = {x}^{2}\ln x$ 的通解;

(5) $y = \frac{1}{x}\left( {{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right)  + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{2}\left( {{C}_{1},{C}_{2}}\right.$ 是任意常数 $)$ 是方程 $x{y}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}^{\prime } - {xy} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 的通解;

(6) $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{3}\cos x + {C}_{4}\sin x - {x}^{2}\left( {{C}_{1},{C}_{2},{C}_{3},{C}_{4}}\right.$ 是任意常数 $)$ 是方程 ${y}^{\left( 4\right) } - y = {x}^{2}$ 的通解.

解 (1) 记 ${y}_{1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},{y}_{2} = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x},{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{12}{\mathrm{e}}^{5x}$ ,则

$$
{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } - 3{y}_{1}^{\prime } + 2{y}_{1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 3{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x} = 0,
$$

$$
{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } - 3{y}_{2}^{\prime } + 2{y}_{2} = 4{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 6{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} = 0.
$$

故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 是原方程对应的齐次方程的解,易见 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 是线性无关的.

又因

$$
{y}^{*\prime } - 3{y}^{*\prime } + 2{y}^{ * } = \frac{25}{12}{\mathrm{e}}^{5x} - \frac{15}{12}{\mathrm{e}}^{5x} + \frac{2}{12}{\mathrm{e}}^{5x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{5x},
$$

故 ${y}^{ * }$ 是原方程的一个特解,所以

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + \frac{1}{12}{\mathrm{e}}^{5x}
$$

是原方程的通解.

( 2 )记 ${y}_{1} = \cos {3x},{y}_{2} = \sin {3x},{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{32}\left( {{4x}\cos x + \sin x}\right)$ . 因

$$
{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } + 9{y}_{1} =  - 9\cos {3x} + 9\cos {3x} = 0,
$$

$$
{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } + 9{y}_{2} =  - 9\sin {3x} + 9\sin {3x} = 0,
$$

故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 是原方程对应的齐次方程的解,易见它们是线性无关的.

又因

$$
{y}^{*\prime } = \frac{1}{32}\left( {4\cos x - {4x}\sin x + \cos x}\right)  = \frac{1}{32}\left( {5\cos x - {4x}\sin x}\right) ,
$$

$$
{y}^{*\prime } = \frac{1}{32}\left( {-5\sin x - 4\sin x - {4x}\cos x}\right)  = \frac{1}{32}\left( {-{4x}\cos x - 9\sin x}\right) ,
$$

有

$$
{y}^{*\prime \prime } + 9{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{32}\left( {-{4x}\cos x - 9\sin x}\right)  + \frac{9}{32}\left( {{4x}\cos x + \sin x}\right)  = x\cos x.
$$

故 ${y}^{ * }$ 是原方程的一个特解. 所以

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}\cos {3x} + {C}_{2}\sin {3x} + \frac{1}{32}\left( {{4x}\cos x + \sin x}\right)
$$

是原方程的通解. (3)记 ${y}_{1} = {x}^{2},{y}_{2} = {x}^{2}\ln x$ ,则

$$
{y}_{1}^{\prime } = {2x},\;{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } = 2;\;{y}_{2}^{\prime } = {2x}\ln x + x,\;{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } = 2\ln x + 3.
$$

且.

$$
{x}^{2}{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}_{1}^{\prime } + 4{y}_{1} = {x}^{2} \cdot  2 - {3x} \cdot  {2x} + 4{x}^{2} = 0,
$$

$$
{x}^{2}{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}_{2}^{\prime } + 4{y}_{2} = {x}^{2}\left( {2\ln x + 3}\right)  - {3x}\left( {{2x}\ln x + x}\right)  + 4{x}^{2}\ln x = 0,
$$

故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 是方程的解,易见 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 线性无关,所以

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} = {C}_{1}{x}^{2} + {C}_{2}{x}^{2}\ln x
$$

是方程的通解.

(4)记 ${y}_{1} = {x}^{5},{y}_{2} = \frac{1}{x},{y}^{ * } =  - \frac{1}{9}{x}^{2}\ln x$ ,则

$$
{x}^{2}{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}_{1}^{\prime } - 5{y}_{1} = {x}^{2} \cdot  {20}{x}^{3} - {3x} \cdot  5{x}^{4} - 5{x}^{5} = 0,
$$

$$
{x}^{2}{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}_{2}^{\prime } - 5{y}_{2} = {x}^{2}\left( \frac{2}{{x}^{3}}\right)  - {3x}\left( {-\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\right)  - \frac{5}{x} = 0,
$$

故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 是原方程对应的齐次方程的解,易见它们是线性无关的. 又因

$$
{x}^{2}{y}^{*\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}^{*\prime } - 5{y}^{ * } = {x}^{2} \cdot  \frac{2\ln x + 3}{9} - {3x}\frac{{2x}\ln x + x}{9} - 5 \cdot  \frac{{x}^{2}\ln x}{9}
$$

$$
= {x}^{2}\ln x,
$$

故 ${y}^{ * }$ 是原方程的一个特解. 所以

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}{x}^{5} + {C}_{2}\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{9}{x}^{2}\ln x
$$

是原方程的通解.

(5) 记 ${y}_{1} = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{x},{y}_{2} = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{x},{y}^{ * } = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{2}$ ,则

$$
{y}_{1}^{\prime } = \left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x},{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } = \left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{2}{{x}^{2}} + \frac{2}{{x}^{3}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x},
$$

$$
{y}_{2}^{\prime } = \left( {-\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x},{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } = \left( {\frac{1}{x} + \frac{2}{{x}^{2}} + \frac{2}{{x}^{3}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x},
$$

且.

$$
x{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}_{1}^{\prime } - x{y}_{1} = x\left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{2}{{x}^{2}} + \frac{2}{{x}^{3}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 2\left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - x \cdot  \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{x} = 0,
$$

$$
x{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}_{2}^{\prime } - x{y}_{2} = x\left( {\frac{1}{x} + \frac{2}{{x}^{2}} + \frac{2}{{x}^{3}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + 2\left( {-\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - x \cdot  \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{x} = 0,
$$

故 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 是原方程对应的齐次方程的解,易见它们是线性无关的.

又因 ${y}^{*\prime } = {y}^{*\prime \prime } = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{2}$ ,且

$$
x{y}^{*\prime } + 2{y}^{*\prime } - x{y}^{ * } = \frac{x}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \frac{x}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},
$$

故 ${y}^{ * }$ 是原方程的一个特解. 所以

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + {y}^{ * } = \frac{{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{x} + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{2}
$$

是原方程的通解.

(6) 令 ${y}_{1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},{y}_{2} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x},{y}_{3} = \cos x,{y}_{4} = \sin x$ ,易见

$$
{y}_{i}^{\left( 4\right) } = {y}_{i},i = 1,2,3,4.
$$

故 ${y}_{i}\left( {i = 1,2,3,4}\right)$ 是原方程对应的齐次方程 ${y}^{\left( 4\right) } - y = 0$ 的解.

下面说明 ${y}_{i}\left( {i = 1,2,3,4}\right)$ 在它们的定义域 $\mathbf{R}$ 中是线性无关的. 令

$$
{k}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {k}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {k}_{3}\cos x + {k}_{4}\sin x \equiv  0,
$$

分别取 $x = 0,\frac{\pi }{2}, - \frac{\pi }{2},\pi$ ,则有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {k}_{1} + {k}_{2} + {k}_{3} + 0 = 0, \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{k}_{1} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{\pi }{2}}{k}_{2} + 0 + {k}_{4} = 0, \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{\pi }{2}}{k}_{1} + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{k}_{2} + 0 - {k}_{4} = 0, \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{\pi }{k}_{1} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\pi }{k}_{2} - {k}_{3} + 0 = 0. \end{array}\right.
$$

根据线性代数的知识, 经计算, 上述齐次线性方程组的系数行列式

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} 1 & 1 & 1 & 0 \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} & {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{\pi }{2}} & 0 & 1 \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{\pi }{2}} & {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}} & 0 &  - 1 \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{\pi } & {\mathrm{e}}^{-\pi } &  - 1 & 0 \end{matrix}\right|  \neq  0,
$$

故齐次线性方程组仅有零解 ${k}_{1} = 0,{k}_{2} = 0,{k}_{3} = 0,{k}_{4} = 0$ . 这说明 ${y}_{1},{y}_{2},{y}_{3},{y}_{4}$ 是线性无关的.

又令 ${y}^{ * } =  - {x}^{2}$ ,则 ${y}^{*\left( 4\right) } = 0$ ,且 ${y}^{*\left( 4\right) } - {y}^{ * } = 0 - \left( {-{x}^{2}}\right)  = {x}^{2}$ ,故 ${y}^{ * }$ 是原方程的一个特解. 所以

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + {C}_{3}{y}_{3} + {C}_{4}{y}_{4} + {y}^{ * }
$$

$$
= {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{3}\cos x + {C}_{4}\sin x + {x}^{2}
$$

是原方程的通解.

2 *5. 已知 ${y}_{1}\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 是齐次线性方程

$$
\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) {y}^{\prime \prime } - \left( {{2x} + 1}\right) {y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 0
$$

的一个解, 求此方程的通解.

解 设 ${y}_{2}\left( x\right)  = {y}_{1}u = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}u$ 是方程的解,则 ${y}_{2}^{\prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {u + {u}^{\prime }}\right) ,{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {u + 2{u}^{\prime } + {u}^{\prime \prime }}\right)$ , 代入方程并整理, 得

$$
{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left\lbrack  {\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) {u}^{\prime \prime } + \left( {{2x} - 3}\right) {u}^{\prime }}\right\rbrack   = 0,
$$

即

$$
\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) {u}^{\prime \prime } + \left( {{2x} - 3}\right) {u}^{\prime } = 0,
$$

令 ${u}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${u}^{\prime \prime } = {p}^{\prime }$ ,且上式成为

$$
\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) {p}^{\prime } + \left( {{2x} - 3}\right) p = 0.
$$

分离变量后积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}p}{p} =  - \int \frac{{2x} - 3}{{2x} - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

得

$$
\ln \left| p\right|  =  - x + \ln \left| {{2x} - 1}\right|  + \ln C,
$$

取 $C = 1$ ,即 $p = \left( {{2x} - 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ . 再积分得

$$
u = \int \left( {{2x} - 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \left\lbrack  {\left( {{2x} - 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{0}}\right\rbrack  ,
$$

取 ${C}_{0} = 0$ ,即 $u =  - \left( {{2x} + 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ ,故

$$
{y}_{2} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}u =  - \left( {{2x} + 1}\right) .
$$

${y}_{2}$ 与 ${y}_{1}$ 线性无关,故原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}\left( {{2x} + 1}\right)  + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

2° 6. 已知 ${y}_{1}\left( x\right)  = x$ 是齐次线性方程 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {2x}{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 0$ 的一个解,求非齐次线性方程 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {2x}{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 2{x}^{3}$ 的通解.

解 设 ${y}_{2} = {y}_{1}u = {xu}$ 是非齐次线性方程的解,则 ${y}_{2}^{\prime } = u + x{u}^{\prime },{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } = 2{u}^{\prime } + x{u}^{\prime \prime }$ ,代入方程并整理, 得

$$
{u}^{\prime \prime } = 0\text{.}
$$

不妨取 $u = x$ ,则 ${y}_{2} = {y}_{1}u = {x}^{2}$ ,且 ${y}_{2}$ 与 ${y}_{1}$ 线性无关.

将非齐次方程化为标准形

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } - \frac{2}{x}{y}^{\prime } + \frac{2}{{x}^{2}}y = {2x},
$$

则它的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} - {y}_{1}\int \frac{{y}_{2}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x + {y}_{2}\int \frac{{y}_{1}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

其中 $f = {2x},W = \left| \begin{array}{ll} {y}_{1} & {y}_{2} \\  {y}_{1}^{\prime } & {y}_{2}^{\prime } \end{array}\right|  = \left| \begin{array}{ll} x & {x}^{2} \\  1 & {2x} \end{array}\right|  = {x}^{2}$ .

故

$$
y = {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}{x}^{2} - x\int \frac{2{x}^{3}}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + {x}^{2}\int \frac{2{x}^{2}}{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}{x}^{2} + {x}^{3}\text{.}
$$

9 7. 已知齐次线性方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y = 0$ 的通解为 $Y\left( x\right)  = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x$ ,求非齐次线性方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y = \sec x$ 的通解.

解 由题设知, ${y}_{1} = \cos x$ 与 ${y}_{2} = \sin x$ 都是齐次方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y = 0$ 的解,且 ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$

线性无关,则非齐次方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y = \sec x$ 的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x - {y}_{1}\int \frac{{y}_{2}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x + {y}_{2}\int \frac{{y}_{1}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

其中

$$
f = \sec x,\;W = \left| \begin{array}{ll} {y}_{1} & {y}_{2} \\  {y}_{1}^{\prime } & {y}_{2}^{\prime } \end{array}\right|  = \left| \begin{matrix} \cos x & \sin x \\   - \sin x & \cos x \end{matrix}\right|  = 1.
$$

故

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x - \cos x\int \frac{\sin x}{\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x + \sin x\int \frac{\cos x}{\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x + \cos x\ln \left| {\cos x}\right|  + x\sin x.
$$

8 8. 已知齐次线性方程 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - x{y}^{\prime } + y = 0$ 的通解为 $Y\left( x\right)  = {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}x\ln \left| x\right|$ ,求非齐次线性方程 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - x{y}^{\prime } + y = x$ 的通解.

解 由题设知 ${y}_{1} = x$ 与 ${y}_{2} = x\ln \left| x\right|$ 都是齐次方程的解, ${y}_{1}$ 与 ${y}_{2}$ 显然是线性无关的. 将非齐次方程化为标准形 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - \frac{1}{x}{y}^{\prime } + \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}y = \frac{1}{x}$ ,则方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} - {y}_{1}\int \frac{{y}_{2}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x + {y}_{2}\int \frac{{y}_{1}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

其中

$$
f = \frac{1}{x},W = \left| \begin{array}{ll} {y}_{1} & {y}_{2} \\  {y}_{1}^{\prime } & {y}_{2}^{\prime } \end{array}\right|  = \left| \begin{matrix} x & x\ln \left| x\right| \\  1 & \ln \left| x\right|  + 1 \end{matrix}\right|  = x.
$$

因

$$
\int \frac{{y}_{2}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\ln \left| x\right| }{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\ln }^{2}\left| x\right| ,
$$

$$
\int \frac{{y}_{1}f}{W}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \ln \left| x\right| ,
$$

故非齐次方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}x\ln \left| x\right|  - x\frac{1}{2}{\ln }^{2}\left| x\right|  + x\ln \left| x\right|  \cdot  \ln \left| x\right|
$$

$$
= {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}x\ln \left| x\right|  + \frac{x}{2}{\ln }^{2}\left| x\right| .
$$

### 习题 7-7 常系数齐次线性微分方程



21. 求下列微分方程的通解:

(1) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime } - {2y} = 0$ ; (2) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } = 0$ ;

(3) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y = 0$ ; (4) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + 6{y}^{\prime } + {13y} = 0$ ;

(5) $4\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} - {20}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {25x} = 0$ ; (6) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } + {5y} = 0$ ;

(7) ${y}^{\left( 4\right) } - y = 0$ ; (8) ${y}^{\left( 4\right) } + 2{y}^{\prime \prime } + y = 0$ ;

(9) ${y}^{\left( 4\right) } - 2{y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } = 0$ ; (10) ${y}^{\left( 4\right) } + 5{y}^{\prime \prime } - {36y} = 0$ .

解 (1) 特征方程为 ${r}^{2} + r - 2 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2} =  - 2$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}.
$$

(2)特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {4r} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1} = 0,{r}_{2} = 4$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x}.
$$

(3)特征方程为 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1} = \mathrm{i},{r}_{2} =  - \mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x.
$$

(4)特征方程为 ${r}^{2} + {6r} + {13} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 3 \pm  2\mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x}}\right) .
$$

(5)特征方程为 $4{r}^{2} - {20r} + {25} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1} = {r}_{2} = \frac{5}{2}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
x = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{5}{2}t}.
$$

(6) 特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {4r} + 5 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} = 2 \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x}\right) .
$$

(7) 特征方程为 ${r}^{4} - 1 = 0$ ,即 $\left( {{r}^{2} - 1}\right) \left( {{r}^{2} + 1}\right)  = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1,{r}_{3,4} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{3}\cos x + {C}_{4}\sin x.
$$

(8) 特征方程为 ${r}^{4} + 2{r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ ,即 ${\left( {r}^{2} + 1\right) }^{2} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} = \mathrm{i},{r}_{3,4} =  - \mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) \cos x + \left( {{C}_{3} + {C}_{4}x}\right) \sin x.
$$

(9) 特征方程为 ${r}^{4} - 2{r}^{3} + {r}^{2} = 0$ ,即 ${r}^{2}{\left( r - 1\right) }^{2} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} = 0,{r}_{3,4} = 1$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x + \left( {{C}_{3} + {C}_{4}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

(10)特征方程为 ${r}^{4} + 5{r}^{2} - {36} = 0$ ,即 $\left( {{r}^{2} + 9}\right) \left( {{r}^{2} - 4}\right)  = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  2,{r}_{3,4} =$ $\pm  3\mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} + {C}_{3}\cos {3x} + {C}_{4}\sin {3x}.
$$

2. 求下列微分方程满足所给初值条件的特解:

(1) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } + {3y} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 6,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = {10}$ ;

(2) $4{y}^{\prime \prime } + 4{y}^{\prime } + y = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 2,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ ;

(3) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 3{y}^{\prime } - {4y} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} =  - 5$ ;

(4) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + 4{y}^{\prime } + {29y} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = {15}$ ;

(5) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {25y} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 2,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 5$ ;

(6) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } + {13y} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 3$ .

解 (1) 解特征方程 ${r}^{2} - {4r} + 3 = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2} = 3$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{3x},
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 3{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{3x}.
$$

代入初值条件,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = 6, \\  {C}_{1} + 3{C}_{2} = {10}, \end{array}\right.$ 解得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 4, \\  {C}_{2} = 2. \end{array}\right.$ 故所求特解为

$$
y = 4{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}.
$$

(2)解特征方程 $4{r}^{2} + {4r} + 1 = 0$ ,即 ${\left( 2r + 1\right) }^{2} = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1,2} =  - \frac{1}{2}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{x}{2}},
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \left( {-\frac{{C}_{1}}{2} + {C}_{2} - \frac{{C}_{2}}{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{x}{2}}.
$$

代入初值条件,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 2, \\   - \frac{{C}_{1}}{2} + {C}_{2} = 0, \end{array}\right.$ 解得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 2, \\  {C}_{2} = 1. \end{array}\right.$ 故所求特解为

$$
y = \left( {2 + x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{x}{2}}.
$$

(3)解特征方程 ${r}^{2} - {3r} - 4 = 0$ ,即 $\left( {r + 1}\right) \left( {r - 4}\right)  = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1} =  - 1,{r}_{2} = 4$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x},
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + 4{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x}.
$$

代入初值条件,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = 0, \\   - {C}_{1} + 4{C}_{2} =  - 5, \end{array}\right.$ 解得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 1, \\  {C}_{2} =  - 1. \end{array}\right.$ 故所求特解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{4x}.
$$

(4)解特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {4r} + {29} = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 2 \pm  5\mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos {5x} + {C}_{2}\sin {5x}}\right) ,
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\left\lbrack  {\left( {5{C}_{2} - 2{C}_{1}}\right) \cos {5x} + \left( {-5{C}_{1} - 2{C}_{2}}\right) \sin {5x}}\right\rbrack  .
$$

代入初值条件,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 0, \\  5{C}_{2} - 2{C}_{1} = {15}, \end{array}\right.$ 即 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 0, \\  {C}_{2} = 3. \end{array}\right.$ 故所求特解为

$$
y = 3{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}\sin {5x}.
$$

(5) 解特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {25} = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  5\mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos {5x} + {C}_{2}\sin {5x},
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - 5{C}_{1}\sin {5x} + 5{C}_{2}\cos {5x}.
$$

代入初值条件,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 2, \\  5{C}_{2} = 5, \end{array}\right.$ 即 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 2, \\  {C}_{2} = 1. \end{array}\right.$ 故所求特解为

$$
y = 2\cos {5x} + \sin {5x}.
$$

(6)解特征方程 ${r}^{2} - {4r} + {13} = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1,2} = 2 \pm  3\mathrm{i}$ ,故方程的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos {3x} + {C}_{2}\sin {3x}}\right) ,
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\left\lbrack  {\left( {2{C}_{1} + 3{C}_{2}}\right) \cos {3x} + \left( {2{C}_{2} - 3{C}_{1}}\right) \sin {3x}}\right\rbrack  .
$$

代入初值条件,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 0, \\  2{C}_{1} + 3{C}_{2} = 3, \end{array}\right.$ 即 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 0, \\  {C}_{2} = 1. \end{array}\right.$ 故所求特解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\sin {3x}.
$$

3. 一个单位质量的质点在数轴上运动,开始时质点在原点 $O$ 处且速度为 ${v}_{0}$ ,在运动过程中, 它受到一个力的作用, 这个力的大小与质点到原点的距离成正比 (比例系数 ${k}_{1} > 0)$ 而方向与初速一致. 又介质的阻力与速度成正比 (比例系数 ${k}_{2} > 0$ ). 求反映这质点的运动规律的函数.

解 设质点的位置函数为 $x = x\left( t\right)$ . 由题意得

$$
{x}^{\prime \prime } = {k}_{1}x - {k}_{2}{x}^{\prime },
$$

即 ${x}^{\prime \prime } + {k}_{2}{x}^{\prime } - {k}_{1}x = 0$ ,且 ${\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = 0,{\left. {x}^{\prime }\right| }_{t = 0} = {v}_{0}$ .

解特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {k}_{2}r - {k}_{1} = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1,2} = \frac{-{k}_{2} \pm  \sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}{2}$ ,故有通解

$$
x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{{r}_{1}t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{r}_{2}t},
$$

且有

$$
{x}^{\prime } = {r}_{1}{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{{r}_{1}t} + {r}_{2}{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{{r}_{2}t},
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = 0,{x}^{\prime } = {v}_{0}$ ,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = 0, \\  {r}_{1}{C}_{1} + {r}_{2}{C}_{2} = {v}_{0}, \end{array}\right.$ 解得

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = \frac{-{v}_{0}}{{r}_{2} - {r}_{1}} = \frac{{v}_{0}}{\sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}, \\  {C}_{2} = \frac{{v}_{0}}{{r}_{2} - {r}_{1}} =  - \frac{{v}_{0}}{\sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}. \end{array}\right.
$$

故

$$
x = \frac{{v}_{0}}{\sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{-{k}_{2} + \sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}{2}t} - {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{-{k}_{2} - \sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}{2}t}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{{v}_{0}}{\sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{-{k}_{2} + \sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}t}{2}}\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-t\sqrt{{k}_{2}^{2} + 4{k}_{1}}}}\right) .
$$

24. 在图 7-3 所示的电路中先将开关 $K$ 拨向 $A$ ,达到稳定状态后再将开关 $K$ 拨向 $B$ , 求电压 ${u}_{C}\left( t\right)$ 及电流 $i\left( t\right)$ . 已知 $E = {20}\mathrm{\;V},C = {0.5} \times  {10}^{-6}\mathrm{\;F}$ (法), $L = {0.1}\mathrm{H}$ (亨), $R =$ ${2000\Omega }$ . 解 由回路定律, 得

$$
L\frac{\mathrm{d}i}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + \frac{q}{C} + {Ri} = 0.
$$

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_289.jpg?x=566&y=531&w=430&h=293&r=0"/>

图 7-3

<!-- Media -->

因 $\frac{q}{C} = {u}_{C}$ ,即 $q = C{u}_{C},i = \frac{\mathrm{d}q}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = C\frac{\mathrm{d}{u}_{C}}{\mathrm{\;d}t}$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}i}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = C\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}{u}_{C}}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}}$ . 于是有

$$
{LC}\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}{u}_{C}}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} + {u}_{C} + {RC}\frac{\mathrm{d}{u}_{C}}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = 0,
$$

即

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}{u}_{C}}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} + \frac{R}{L}\frac{\mathrm{d}{u}_{C}}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + \frac{1}{LC}{u}_{C} = 0,
$$

且

$$
{\left. {u}_{C}\right| }_{t = 0} = E,{\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}{u}_{C}}{\mathrm{\;d}t}\right| }_{t = 0} = 0.
$$

已知

$$
\frac{R}{L} = \frac{2000}{0.1} = 2 \times  {10}^{4},\frac{1}{LC} = \frac{1}{{0.1} \times  {0.5} \times  {10}^{-6}} = 2 \times  {10}^{7},
$$

故微分方程为

$$
{u}_{C}^{\prime \prime } + 2 \times  {10}^{4}{u}_{C}^{\prime } + 2 \times  {10}^{7}{u}_{C} = 0.
$$

其特征方程为

$$
{r}^{2} + 2 \times  {10}^{4}r + 2 \times  {10}^{7} = 0,
$$

解得 ${r}_{1} \approx   - {1.9} \times  {10}^{4},{r}_{2} \approx   - {10}^{3}$ ,故 ${u}_{C} = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{1.9} \times  {10}^{4}t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{10}^{3}t}$ ,且有

$$
{u}_{C}^{\prime } =  - {1.9} \times  {10}^{4}{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{1.9} \times  {10}^{4}t} - {10}^{3}{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{10}^{3}t}.
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,{u}_{C} = {20},{u}_{C}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = {20}, \\   - {1.9} \times  {10}^{4}{C}_{1} - {10}^{3}{C}_{2} = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得

$$
{C}_{1} =  - \frac{10}{9},{C}_{2} = \frac{190}{9}.
$$

故

$$
{u}_{C} = \frac{10}{9}\left( {{19}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{10}^{3}t} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{1.9} \times  {10}^{4}t}}\right) ,
$$

$$
i = C{u}_{C}^{\prime } = {0.5} \times  {10}^{-6} \times  \frac{10}{9}\left( {-{19} \times  {10}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{10}^{3}t} + {1.9} \times  {10}^{4}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{1.9} \times  {10}^{4}t}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{19}{18} \times  {10}^{-2}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{-{1.9} \times  {10}^{4}t} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{10}^{3}t}}\right) .
$$

5. 设底面直径为 ${0.5}\mathrm{\;m}$ 的圆柱形浮筒铅直放在水中,当稍向下压后突然放开,浮筒在水中上下振动的周期为 $2\mathrm{\;s}$ ,求浮筒的质量.

解 设 $x$ 轴的正向铅直向下,原点在水面处. 平衡状态下浮筒上一点 $A$ 在水平面处,又设在时刻 $t$ ,点 $A$ 的位置为 $x = x\left( t\right)$ ,此时它受到的恢复力的大小为 ${1000g\pi }{R}^{2}\left| x\right|$ ( $R$ 是浮筒的半径),恢复力的方向与位移方向相反,故有

$$
m{x}^{\prime \prime } =  - {1000g\pi }{R}^{2}x,
$$

其中 $m$ 是浮筒的质量.

记 ${\omega }^{2} = \frac{{1000g\pi }{R}^{2}}{m}$ ,则得微分方程

$$
{x}^{\prime \prime } + {\omega }^{2}x = 0.
$$

解特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {\omega }^{2} = 0$ ,得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \omega \mathrm{i}$ ,故

$$
x = {C}_{1}\cos {\omega t} + {C}_{2}\sin {\omega t} = A\sin \left( {{\omega t} + \varphi }\right) ,A = \sqrt{{C}_{1}^{2} + {C}_{2}^{2}},\sin \varphi  = \frac{{C}_{1}}{A}.
$$

由于振动周期 $T = \frac{2\pi }{\omega } = 2$ ,故 $\omega  = \pi$ ,即

$$
\frac{{1000g\pi }{R}^{2}}{m} = {\pi }^{2},
$$

从中解出

$$
m = \frac{{1000g}{R}^{2}}{\pi } \approx  {195}\left( \mathrm{\;{kg}}\right) .
$$

### 习题 7-8 常系数非齐次线性微分方程



121. 求下列各微分方程的通解:

(1) $2{y}^{\prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime } - y = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ; (2) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {a}^{2}y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ;

(3) $2{y}^{\prime \prime } + 5{y}^{\prime } = 5{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1$ ; (4) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + 3{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = {3x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ ;

(5) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } + {5y} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin {2x}$ ; (6) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 6{y}^{\prime } + {9y} = \left( {x + 1}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{3x}$ ;

(7) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + 5{y}^{\prime } + {4y} = 3 - {2x}$ ; (8) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {4y} = x\cos x$ ;

(9) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \cos x$ ; (10) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = {\sin }^{2}x$ .

解 (1) 由 $2{r}^{2} + r - 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1} = \frac{1}{2},{r}^{2} =  - 1$ . 故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{2}} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x},\lambda  = 1$ 不是特征方程的根,故可设 ${y}^{ * } = a{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 是原方程的一个特解,代入原方程得

$$
{2a}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + a{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - a{\mathrm{e}}^{x} = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,有 $a = 1$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{2}} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

(2)由 ${r}^{2} + {a}^{2} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  a\mathrm{i}$ . 故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}\cos {ax} + {C}_{2}\sin {ax}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},\lambda  = 1$ 不是特征方程的根,故设 ${y}^{ * } = b{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 是原方程的一个特解,代入方程得

$$
b{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {a}^{2}b{\mathrm{e}}^{x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},
$$

消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,有 $b = \frac{1}{1 + {a}^{2}}$ ,即 ${y}^{ * } = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{1 + {a}^{2}}$ . 故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}\cos {ax} + {C}_{2}\sin {ax} + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{1 + {a}^{2}}.
$$

(3) 由 $2{r}^{2} + {5r} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1} = 0,{r}_{2} =  - \frac{5}{2}$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{5}{2}x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = 5{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1,\lambda  = 0$ 是特征方程的单根,故设 ${y}^{ * } = x\left( {{b}_{0}{x}^{2} + {b}_{1}x + {b}_{2}}\right)$ 是原方程的一个特解, 代入方程并整理, 得

$$
{15}{b}_{0}{x}^{2} + \left( {{12}{b}_{0} + {10}{b}_{1}}\right) x + 4{b}_{1} + 5{b}_{2} = 5{x}^{2} - {2x} - 1.
$$

比较系数得 ${b}_{0} = \frac{1}{3},{b}_{1} =  - \frac{3}{5},{b}_{2} = \frac{7}{25}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3} - \frac{3}{5}{x}^{2} + \frac{7}{25}x.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{5}{2}x} + \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3} - \frac{3}{5}{x}^{2} + \frac{7}{25}x.
$$

(4) 由 ${r}^{2} + {3r} + 2 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1} =  - 1,{r}_{2} =  - 2$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {3x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x},\lambda  =  - 1$ 是特征方程的单根,故可设

$$
{y}^{ * } = x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {{ax} + b}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {a{x}^{2} + {bx}}\right)
$$

是原方程的一个特解,代入方程并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ ,得

$$
{2ax} + \left( {{2a} + b}\right)  = {3x}.
$$

比较系数,得 $a = \frac{3}{2},b =  - 3$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2} - {3x}}\right) .
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {\frac{3}{2}{x}^{2} - {3x}}\right) .
$$

(5) 由 ${r}^{2} - {2r} + 5 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} = 1 \pm  2\mathrm{i}$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x}}\right) .
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin {2x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {0 \cdot  \cos {2x} + 1 \cdot  \sin {2x}}\right) ,\lambda  + \mathrm{i}\omega  = 1 + 2\mathrm{i}$ 是特征方程的单根,故可设

$$
{y}^{ * } = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {a\cos {2x} + b\sin {2x}}\right)
$$

是原方程的一个特解,代入方程并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,得

$$
{4b}\cos {2x} - {4a}\sin {2x} = \sin {2x}.
$$

比较系数,得 $a =  - \frac{1}{4},b = 0$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {-\frac{1}{4}\cos {2x}}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{4}x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x}}\right)  - \frac{1}{4}x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\cos {2x}.
$$

(6)由 ${r}^{2} - {6r} + 9 = 0$ 得 ${r}_{1,2} = 3$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {\mathrm{e}}^{3x}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) .
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{3x}\left( {x + 1}\right) ,\lambda  = 3$ 是特征方程的 (二重) 根,故可设

$$
{y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{3x}\left( {{ax} + b}\right) {x}^{2}
$$

是原方程的一个特解,代入方程并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{3x}$ ,得

$$
{6ax} + {2b} = x + 1\text{.}
$$

比较系数,得 $a = \frac{1}{6},b = \frac{1}{2}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{3x}\left( {\frac{1}{6}x + \frac{1}{2}}\right) {x}^{2}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{3x}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right)  + {\mathrm{e}}^{3x}\left( {\frac{1}{6}x + \frac{1}{2}}\right) {x}^{2}.
$$

(7)由 ${r}^{2} + {5r} + 4 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1} =  - 1,{r}_{2} =  - 4$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{4x}}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = 3 - {2x},\lambda  = 0$ 不是特征方程的根,故可设

$$
{y}^{ * } = {ax} + b
$$

是原方程的一个特解, 代入方程, 得

$$
{4ax} + {5a} + {4b} =  - {2x} + 3.
$$

比较系数得 $a =  - \frac{1}{2},b = \frac{11}{8}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } =  - \frac{1}{2}x + \frac{11}{8}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{4x}} - \frac{1}{2}x + \frac{11}{8}.
$$

(8) 由 ${r}^{2} + 4 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  2\mathrm{i}$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = x\cos x,\lambda  + \mathrm{i}\omega  = \mathrm{i}$ 不是特征方程的根,故可设

$$
{y}^{ * } = \left( {{ax} + b}\right) \cos x + \left( {{cx} + d}\right) \sin x
$$

是原方程的一个特解, 代入方程, 得

$$
\left( {{3ax} + {3b} + {2c}}\right) \cos x + \left( {{3cx} + {3d} - {2a}}\right) \sin x = x\cos x.
$$

比较系数有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {3a} = 1, \\  {3b} + {2c} = 0, \\  {3c} = 0, \\  {3d} - {2a} = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} a = \frac{1}{3}, \\  b = 0, \\  c = 0, \\  d = \frac{2}{9}, \end{array}\right.
$$

即 ${y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{3}x\cos x + \frac{2}{9}\sin x$ . 故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x} + \frac{1}{3}x\cos x + \frac{2}{9}\sin x.
$$

(9) 由 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \cos x$ ,对应于方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,可设特解 ${y}_{1}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ; 对应于方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y =$ $\cos x(\lambda  + \mathrm{i}\omega  = \mathrm{i}$ 是特征方程的根) 可设特解 ${y}_{2}^{ * } = x\left( {B\cos x + C\sin x}\right)$ ,故由叠加原理, 设

$$
{y}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + x\left( {B\cos x + C\sin x}\right)
$$

是原方程的一个特解, 代入方程, 得

$$
{2A}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {2C}\cos x - {2B}\sin x = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \cos x.
$$

比较系数,得 $A = \frac{1}{2},B = 0,C = \frac{1}{2}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \frac{1}{2}x\sin x.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \frac{1}{2}x\sin x.
$$

( 10 )由 ${r}^{2} - 1 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {\sin }^{2}x = \frac{1}{2} - \frac{1}{2}\cos {2x}$ ,对应于方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = \frac{1}{2}$ ,可设特解 ${y}_{1}^{ * } = A$ ; 对应于方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y =  - \frac{1}{2}\cos {2x}$ ,可设特解 ${y}_{2}^{ * } = B\cos {2x} + C\sin {2x}$ ,故由叠加原理,设

$$
{y}^{ * } = A + B\cos {2x} + C\sin {2x}
$$

是原方程的一个特解, 代入方程, 得

$$
- A - {5B}\cos {2x} - {5C}\sin {2x} = \frac{1}{2} - \frac{1}{2}\cos {2x}.
$$

比较系数得 $A =  - \frac{1}{2},B = \frac{1}{10},C = 0$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } =  - \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{10}\cos {2x}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{10}\cos {2x}.
$$

2. 求下列各微分方程满足已给初值条件的特解:

(1) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + y + \sin {2x} = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{x = \pi } = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = \pi } = 1$ ;

(2) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 3{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 5,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 2$ ;

(3) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - {10}{y}^{\prime } + {9y} = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{6}{7},{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{33}{7}$ ;

(4) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = \left. 4x{\mathrm{e}}^{x},{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 1\right|$ ;

(5) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } = 5,{\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ .

解 (1) 由 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  =  - \sin {2x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{0x}\left( {0 \cdot  \cos {2x} - \sin {2x}}\right) ,\lambda  + \mathrm{i}\omega  = 2\mathrm{i}$ 不是特征方程的根,故可设

$$
{y}^{ * } = A\cos {2x} + B\sin {2x}
$$

是原方程的一个特解, 代入方程得

$$
- {3A}\cos {2x} - {3B}\sin {2x} =  - \sin {2x}.
$$

比较系数得 $A = 0,B = \frac{1}{3}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{3}\sin {2x}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x + \frac{1}{3}\sin {2x}.
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - {C}_{1}\sin x + {C}_{2}\cos x + \frac{2}{3}\cos {2x}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = \pi ,y = 1,{y}^{\prime } = 1$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l}  - {C}_{1} = 1, \\   - {C}_{2} + \frac{2}{3} = 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} =  - 1,{C}_{2} =  - \frac{1}{3}$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y =  - \cos x - \frac{1}{3}\sin x + \frac{1}{3}\sin {2x}.
$$

(2)由 ${r}^{2} - {3r} + 2 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2} = 2$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = 5,\lambda  = 0$ 不是特征方程的根,故可设 ${y}^{ * } = A$ 是原方程的一个特解,代入方程

得 $A = \frac{5}{2}$ ,即 ${y}^{ * } = \frac{5}{2}$ . 于是原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + \frac{5}{2},
$$

且有 ${y}^{\prime } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 2{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ . 代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 1,{y}^{\prime } = 2$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} + \frac{5}{2} = 1, \\  {C}_{1} + 2{C}_{2} = 2, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} =  - 5,{C}_{2} = \frac{7}{2}$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y =  - 5{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \frac{7}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + \frac{5}{2}.
$$

(3) 由 ${r}^{2} - {10r} + 9 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2} = 9$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{9x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x},\lambda  = 2$ 不是特征方程的根,故可设 ${y}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ 是原方程的一个特解,代入方程并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ ,得 $A =  - \frac{1}{7}$ ,即 ${y}^{ * } =  - \frac{1}{7}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ . 于是原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{9x} - \frac{1}{7}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x},
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 9{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{9x} - \frac{2}{7}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = \frac{6}{7},{y}^{\prime } = \frac{33}{7}$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} - \frac{1}{7} = \frac{6}{7}, \\  {C}_{1} + 9{C}_{2} - \frac{2}{7} = \frac{33}{7}, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} = \frac{1}{2},{C}_{2} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{9x} - \frac{1}{7}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}.
$$
