(4)由 ${r}^{2} - 1 = 0$ 得特征根 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {4x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x},\lambda  = 1$ 是特征方程的单根,故可设 ${y}^{ * } = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{Ax} + B}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {A{x}^{2} + {Bx}}\right)$ 是原方程的一个特解,代入方程并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,得

$$
{4Ax} + {2A} + {2B} = {4x}.
$$

比较系数得 $A = 1,B =  - 1$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{x}^{2} - x}\right) .
$$

于是原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{x}^{2} - x}\right) ,
$$

即

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{x}^{2} - x + {C}_{1}}\right)  + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x},
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{x}^{2} + x - 1 + {C}_{1}}\right)  - {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 0,{y}^{\prime } = 1$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = 0, \\  {C}_{1} - {C}_{2} - 1 = 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} = 1,{C}_{2} =  - 1$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{x}^{2} - x + 1}\right)  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

(5) 由 ${r}^{2} - {4r} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1} = 0,{r}_{2} = 4$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x}.
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = 5 = 5 \cdot  {\mathrm{e}}^{0x},\lambda  = 0$ 是特征方程的单根,故可设 ${y}^{ * } = {Ax}$ 是原方程的一个特解, 代入方程得 $A =  - \frac{5}{4}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } =  - \frac{5}{4}x
$$

于是原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x} - \frac{5}{4}x,
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = 4{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x} - \frac{5}{4}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 1,{y}^{\prime } = 0$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = 1, \\  4{C}_{2} - \frac{5}{4} = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} = \frac{11}{16},{C}_{2} = \frac{5}{16}$ ,故所求特解为

$$
y = \frac{11}{16} + \frac{5}{16}{\mathrm{e}}^{4x} - \frac{5}{4}x.
$$

3. 大炮以仰角 $\alpha$ 、初速 ${v}_{0}$ 发射炮弹,若不计空气阻力,求弹道曲线.

解 取炮口在原点,炮弹前进的水平方向为 $x$ 轴,铅直向上为 $y$ 轴,设在时刻 $t$ , 炮弹位于 $\left( {x\left( t\right) ,y\left( t\right) }\right)$ . 按题意,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} =  - g, \\  \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = 0, \end{array}\right.  \tag{1}
$$

(2)

且

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {\left. y\right| }_{t = 0} = 0, & {\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{t = 0} = {v}_{0}\sin \alpha , \\  {\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = 0, & {\left. {x}^{\prime }\right| }_{t = 0} = {v}_{0}\cos \alpha . \end{array}\right.
$$

解方程 (1), 得

$$
y =  - \frac{g}{2}{t}^{2} + {C}_{1}t + {C}_{2},
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,y = 0,{y}^{\prime } = {v}_{0}\sin \alpha$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 0,{C}_{1} = {v}_{0}\sin \alpha$ ,即

$$
y = {v}_{0}\sin \alpha  \cdot  t - \frac{g}{2}{t}^{2};
$$

解方程 (2), 得

$$
x = {C}_{3}t + {C}_{4},
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = 0,{x}^{\prime } = {v}_{0}\cos \alpha$ ,得 ${C}_{4} = 0,{C}_{3} = {v}_{0}\cos \alpha$ ,即

$$
x = {v}_{0}\cos \alpha  \cdot  t.
$$

故弹道曲线为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {v}_{0}\cos \alpha  \cdot  t, \\  y = {v}_{0}\sin \alpha  \cdot  t - \frac{g}{2}{t}^{2}. \end{array}\right.
$$

24. 在 $R\text{、}L\text{、}C$ 含源串联电路中,电动势为 $E$ 的电源对电容器 $C$ 充电. 已知 $E = {20}\mathrm{\;V}$ , $C = {0.2\mu }\mathrm{F}$ (微法), $L = {0.1}\mathrm{H}$ (亨), $R = {1000\Omega }$ ,试求合上开关 $K$ 后的电流 $i\left( t\right)$ 及电压 ${u}_{C}\left( t\right)$ .

解 由回路定律知

$$
{LC}{u}_{C}^{\prime \prime } + {RC}{u}_{C}^{\prime } + {u}_{C} = E.
$$

即

$$
{u}_{C}^{\prime \prime } + \frac{R}{L}{u}_{C}^{\prime } + \frac{1}{LC}{u}_{C} = \frac{E}{LC}.
$$

且依题意,有初值条件, ${\left. {u}_{C}\right| }_{t = 0} = 0,{\left. {u}_{C}^{\prime }\right| }_{t = 0} = 0$ .

已知 $R = {1000}\left( \Omega \right) ,L = {0.1}\left( \mathrm{H}\right) ,C = {0.2}\left( \mathrm{{mF}}\right)  = {0.2} \times  {10}^{-6}\left( \mathrm{\;F}\right) ,E = {20}\left( \mathrm{\;V}\right)$ ,故微分方程为

$$
{u}_{C}^{\prime \prime } + {10}^{4}{u}_{C}^{\prime } + 5 \times  {10}^{7}{u}_{C} = {10}^{9},
$$

其对应的齐次方程的特征方程为

$$
{r}^{2} + {10}^{4}r + 5 \times  {10}^{7} = 0,
$$

解得

$$
{r}_{1,2} =  - \frac{{10}^{4}}{2} \pm  \frac{{10}^{4}}{2}\mathrm{i} =  - 5 \times  {10}^{3} \pm  5 \times  {10}^{3}\mathrm{i}.
$$

因 $f\left( t\right)  = {10}^{9}$ . 可令 ${u}_{C}^{ * } = A$ 是原方程的特解,代入方程,得 $A = {20}$ ,即 ${u}_{C}^{ * } = {20}$ . 故方程的通解为

$$
{u}_{C} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\left\lbrack  {{C}_{1}\cos \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right)  + {C}_{2}\sin \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right) }\right\rbrack   + {20},
$$

代入初值条件, $t = 0,{u}_{C} = 0$ ,有 ${C}_{1} + {20} = 0$ ,即 ${C}_{1} =  - {20}$ . 又

$$
{u}_{C}^{\prime } =  - 5 \times  {10}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\left\lbrack  {-{20}\cos \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right)  + {C}_{2}\sin \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right) }\right\rbrack   +
$$

$$
{\mathrm{e}}^{-5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\left\lbrack  {{20} \times  5 \times  {10}^{3}\sin \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right)  + 5 \times  {10}^{3}{C}_{2}\cos \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right) }\right\rbrack  ,
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,{u}_{C}^{\prime } = 0$ ,有 $- 5 \times  {10}^{3}\left( {-{20}}\right)  + 5 \times  {10}^{3}{C}_{2} = 0$ ,即 ${C}_{2} =  - {20}$ . 故

$$
{u}_{C} = {20} - {20}{\mathrm{e}}^{-5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\left\lbrack  {\cos \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right)  + \sin \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right) }\right\rbrack  \left( \mathrm{V}\right) ,
$$

$$
i = C{u}_{C}^{\prime } = {0.2} \times  {10}^{-6}{u}_{C}^{\prime }
$$

$$
= 4 \times  {10}^{-2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\sin \left( {5 \times  {10}^{3}t}\right) \left( \mathrm{A}\right) \text{.}
$$

5. 一链条悬挂在一钉子上,起动时一端离开钉子 $8\mathrm{\;m}$ ,另一端离开钉子 ${12}\mathrm{\;m}$ ,分别在以下两种情况下求链条滑下来所需要的时间：

(1)若不计钉子对链条所产生的摩擦力;

(2)若摩擦力为 $1\mathrm{\;m}$ 长的链条的重量.

解 设链条的线密度为 $\rho \left( {\mathrm{{kg}}/\mathrm{m}}\right)$ ,则链条的质量为 ${20\rho }\left( \mathrm{{kg}}\right)$ . 又设在时刻 $t$ ,链条的一端离钉子 $x = x\left( t\right)$ ,则另一端离钉子 ${20} - x\left( \text{图 7-4}\right)$ ,当 $t = 0$ 时, $x = {12}$ .

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_299.jpg?x=692&y=1032&w=213&h=344&r=0"/>

图 7-4

<!-- Media -->

(1)若不计摩擦力,则运动过程中的链条所受力的大小为 $\left\lbrack  {x - \left( {{20} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack  {\rho g}$ ,按牛顿定律, 有

$$
{20\rho }{x}^{\prime \prime } = \left\lbrack  {x - \left( {{20} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack  {\rho g},
$$

即

$$
{x}^{\prime \prime } - \frac{g}{10}x =  - g.
$$

且有初值条件

$$
{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = {12},{\left. {x}^{\prime }\right| }_{t = 0} = 0\text{.}
$$

由特征方程 ${r}^{2} - \frac{g}{10} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}$ ,又将 ${x}^{ * } = A$ 代入方程,得 $A = {10}$ ,即 ${x}^{ * } = {10}$ . 求得方程通解

$$
x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t} + {10},
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = {12},{x}^{\prime } = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = {C}_{2} = 1$ ,故

$$
x = {\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t} + {10}\;\left( {\text{ 或 }x = 2\operatorname{ch}\left( {\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t}\right)  + {10}}\right) .
$$

取 $x = {20}$ ,得 ${\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{\frac{8}{10}}t} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sqrt{\frac{8}{10}}t} = {10}\left( \right.$ 或 $\left. {\operatorname{ch}\left( {\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t}\right)  = 5}\right)$ ,即

$$
t = \sqrt{\frac{10}{g}}\ln \left( {5 + 2\sqrt{6}}\right) \left( \mathrm{s}\right) \;\left( {\text{ 或 }t = \sqrt{\frac{10}{g}}\operatorname{arch}5\left( \mathrm{\;s}\right) }\right) .
$$

(2)摩擦力为 $1\mathrm{\;m}$ 长链条的重量即为 ${\rho g}$ ,则运动过程中的链条所受力的大小为 $\left\lbrack  {x - \left( {{20} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack  {\rho g} - {\rho g}$ ,按牛顿定律,有

$$
{20\rho }{x}^{\prime \prime } = \left\lbrack  {x - \left( {{20} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack  {\rho g} - {\rho g},
$$

即

$$
{x}^{\prime \prime } - \frac{g}{10}x =  - \frac{21}{10}g,
$$

且有初值条件

$$
{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = {12},{\left. {x}^{\prime }\right| }_{t = 0} = 0\text{.}
$$

满足该条件的特解为

$$
x = \frac{3}{4}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t}}\right)  + \frac{21}{2}\left( {\text{ 或 }x = \frac{3}{2}\operatorname{ch}\left( {\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t}\right)  + \frac{21}{2}}\right) .
$$

取 $x = {20}$ ,得 ${\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{\frac{R}{10}}t} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\sqrt{\frac{R}{10}}t} = \frac{38}{3}$ (或 $\operatorname{ch}\left( {\sqrt{\frac{g}{10}}t}\right)  = \frac{19}{3}$ ),即

$$
t = \sqrt{\frac{10}{g}}\ln \left( {\frac{19}{3} + \frac{4}{3}\sqrt{22}}\right) \left( \mathrm{s}\right) \left( {\text{ 或 }t = \sqrt{\frac{10}{g}}\operatorname{arch}\frac{19}{3}\left( \mathrm{\;s}\right) }\right) .
$$

26. 设函数 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ 连续,且满足

$$
\varphi \left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\int }_{0}^{x}{t\varphi }\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - x{\int }_{0}^{x}\varphi \left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t,
$$

求 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ .

解 由所给方程可得 $\varphi \left( 0\right)  = 1$ ,在该方程两端对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {x\varphi }\left( x\right)  - {\int }_{0}^{x}\varphi \left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - {x\varphi }\left( x\right) ,
$$

即

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\int }_{0}^{x}\varphi \left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t.
$$

可见 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 1$ .

又在方程 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\int }_{0}^{x}\varphi \left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 的两端对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \varphi \left( x\right) .
$$

若记 $\varphi \left( x\right)  = y$ ,则有初值问题

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {y}^{\prime \prime } + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}, \\  {\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,{\left. \;{y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 1. \end{array}\right.  \tag{1}
$$

上述非齐次方程对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,而 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},\lambda  = 1$ 不是特征方程的根,故令 ${y}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 是方程 (1) 的特解,代入方程 (1) 并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,得 $A = \frac{1}{2}$ ,于是方程 (1) 有通解

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x},
$$

且有

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - {C}_{1}\sin x + {C}_{2}\cos x + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 1,{y}^{\prime } = 1$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + \frac{1}{2} = 1, \\  {C}_{2} + \frac{1}{2} = 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

即 ${C}_{1} = {C}_{2} = \frac{1}{2}$ . 于是得

$$
y = \varphi \left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\left( {\cos x + \sin x + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right) .
$$

### 习题 7-9 欧拉方程



求下列欧拉方程的通解:

1. ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } + x{y}^{\prime } - y = 0$ ; 2. ${y}^{\prime \prime } - \frac{{y}^{\prime }}{x} + \frac{y}{{x}^{2}} = \frac{2}{x}$ ;

3. ${x}^{3}{y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + 3{x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {2x}{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 0$ ; 4. ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {2x}{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = {\ln }^{2}x - 2\ln x$ ;

5. ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } + x{y}^{\prime } - {4y} = {x}^{3}$ ; 6. ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - x{y}^{\prime } + {4y} = x\sin \left( {\ln x}\right)$ ;

7. ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {3x}{y}^{\prime } + {4y} = x + {x}^{2}\ln x$ ; 8. ${x}^{3}{y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {2x}{y}^{\prime } - {2y} = {x}^{2}\ln x + {3x}$ .

说明 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ 或 $t = \ln x$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{1}{x}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t}$ ,即 $x\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t}$ . 记 $\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t} = \mathrm{D},\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = {\mathrm{D}}^{2},\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{3}}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{3}} =$ ${\mathrm{D}}^{3}$ ,则

$$
x\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \mathrm{D}y,
$$

$$
{x}^{2}\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = \mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) y,
$$

$$
{x}^{3}\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{3}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{3}} = \mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) \left( {\mathrm{D} - 2}\right) y.
$$

本节习题中 8 个欧拉方程均用此法转化为常系数线性微分方程求解.

解 1. 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则原方程化为

$$
\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  + \mathrm{D} - 1}\right\rbrack  y = 0, \tag{1}
$$

特征方程为 $r\left( {r - 1}\right)  + r - 1 = 0$ ,即 ${r}^{2} - 1 = 0$ ,有特征根 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1$ ,故方程 (1) 有通解

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t},
$$

即原方程的通解为 $y = {C}_{1}x + \frac{{C}_{2}}{x}$ .

2. 原方程可改写成 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - x{y}^{\prime } + y = {2x}$ . 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则方程化为

$$
\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  - \mathrm{D} + 1}\right\rbrack  y = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{t}. \tag{2}
$$

方程 (2) 对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 $r\left( {r - 1}\right)  - r + 1 = 0$ ,即 ${r}^{2} - {2r} + 1 = 0$ ,有特征根 ${r}_{1,2} = 1$ . 故方程 (2) 对应的齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right) .
$$

因 $f\left( t\right)  = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{t},\lambda  = 1$ 是特征 (二重) 根. 设 ${y}^{ * } = A{t}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,则

$$
\mathrm{D}y = A\left( {{t}^{2} + {2t}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{t},{\mathrm{D}}^{2}y = A\left( {{t}^{2} + {4t} + 2}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{t},
$$

代入方程 (2) 中可得 $A = 1$ ,即 ${y}^{ * } = {t}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,故方程 (2) 的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right)  + {t}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t},
$$

即原方程的通解为

$$
y = x\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}\ln x}\right)  + x{\ln }^{2}x.
$$

3. 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则方程可化为

$$
\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) \left( {\mathrm{D} - 2}\right)  + 3\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  - 2\mathrm{D} + 2}\right\rbrack  y = 0. \tag{3}
$$

其特征方程为 $r\left( {r - 1}\right) \left( {r - 2}\right)  + {3r}\left( {r - 1}\right)  - {2r} + 2 = 0$ ,即 ${\left( r - 1\right) }^{2}\left( {r + 2}\right)  = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1,2} = 1,{r}_{3} =  - 2$ . 故方程 (3) 的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right)  + {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}},
$$

即原方程的通解为

$$
y = x\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}\ln x}\right)  + \frac{{C}_{3}}{{x}^{2}}.
$$

4. 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则方程可化为 $\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  - 2\mathrm{D} + 2}\right\rbrack  y = {t}^{2} - {2t}$ ,即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 3\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) y = {t}^{2} - {2t}, \tag{4}
$$

方程 (4) 对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {3r} + 2 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2} = 2$ ,故齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}.
$$

因 $f\left( t\right)  = {t}^{2} - {2t},\lambda  = 0$ 不是特征方程的根,故可令 ${y}^{ * } = A{t}^{2} + {Bt} + C$ 是 (4) 的特解,代

入方程 (4),比较系数得 $A = B = \frac{1}{2},C = \frac{1}{4}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{2}{t}^{2} + \frac{1}{2}t + \frac{1}{4}.
$$

于是方程 (4) 的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + \frac{1}{2}{t}^{2} + \frac{1}{2}t + \frac{1}{4},
$$

即原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}{x}^{2} + \frac{1}{2}{\ln }^{2}x + \frac{1}{2}\ln x + \frac{1}{4}.
$$

5. 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则方程可化为 $\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  + \mathrm{D} - 4}\right\rbrack  y = {\mathrm{e}}^{3t}$ ,即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 4}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{3t}. \tag{5}
$$

方程 (5) 对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - 4 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  2$ ,故齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} = {C}_{1}{x}^{2} + \frac{{C}_{2}}{{x}^{2}}.
$$

因 $f\left( t\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{3t},\lambda  = 3$ 不是特征方程的根,故可令 ${y}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{3t}$ 是方程 (5) 的特解,即 ${y}^{ * } = A{x}^{3}$ 是原方程的特解,代入原方程 ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } + x{y}^{\prime } - {4y} = {x}^{3}$ 中,得 $A = \frac{1}{5}$ ,即 ${y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{5}{x}^{3}$ . 故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1}{x}^{2} + \frac{{C}_{2}}{{x}^{2}} + \frac{1}{5}{x}^{3}.
$$

6. 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}y}$ ,则原方程化为 $\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  - \mathrm{D} + 4}\right\rbrack  y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin t$ ,即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 2\mathrm{D} + 4}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin t. \tag{6}
$$

方程 (6) 对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {2r} + 4 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1,2} = 1 \pm  \sqrt{3}\mathrm{i}$ ,故齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\left\lbrack  {{C}_{1}\cos \left( {\sqrt{3}t}\right)  + {C}_{2}\sin \left( {\sqrt{3}t}\right) }\right\rbrack  .
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin t,\lambda  + \mathrm{i}\omega  = 1 + \mathrm{i}$ 不是特征方程的根,故可令 ${y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}(A\cos t +$ $B\sin t)$ 是方程 (6) 的特解,代入方程 (6) 并比较系数,可得 $A = 0,B = \frac{1}{2}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{t}}{2}\sin t,
$$

于是方程 (6) 的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\left\lbrack  {{C}_{1}\cos \left( {\sqrt{3}t}\right)  + {C}_{2}\sin \left( {\sqrt{3}t}\right) }\right\rbrack   + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{t}}{2}\sin t,
$$

即原方程的通解为

$$
y = x\left\lbrack  {{C}_{1}\cos \left( {\sqrt{3}\ln x}\right)  + {C}_{2}\sin \left( {\sqrt{3}\ln x}\right) }\right\rbrack   + \frac{x}{2}\sin \left( {\ln x}\right) .
$$

7. 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}y}$ ,则原方程可化为 $\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  - 3\mathrm{D} + 4}\right\rbrack  y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t} + t{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}$ ,即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 4\mathrm{D} + 4}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t} + t{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}. \tag{7}
$$

方程 (7) 对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {4r} + 4 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1,2} = 2$ ,故齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right) .
$$

因 $\lambda  = 1$ 不是特征方程的根,故方程 $\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 4\mathrm{D} + 4}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ 的特解 ${y}_{1}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ; 而 $\lambda  = 2$ 是特征方程的(二重)根,故方程 $\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 4\mathrm{D} + 4}\right) y = t{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}$ 的特解可令作 ${y}_{2}^{ * } =$ ${t}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}\left( {{Bt} + C}\right)$ . 由叠加原理知,可令 ${y}^{ * } = {y}_{1}^{ * } + {y}_{2}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + \left( {B{t}^{3} + C{t}^{2}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}$ 是方程 (7) 的特解,代入方程 (7), 得

$$
A{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + \left( {{6Bt} + {2C}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} = {\mathrm{e}}^{t} + t{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}.
$$

比较系数,得 $A = 1,B = \frac{1}{6},C = 0$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = {\mathrm{e}}^{t} + \frac{{t}^{3}}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}.
$$

于是方程 (7) 的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right)  + {\mathrm{e}}^{t} + \frac{{t}^{3}}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t},
$$

即原方程的通解为

$$
y = {x}^{2}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}\ln x}\right)  + x + \frac{1}{6}{x}^{2}{\ln }^{3}x.
$$

8. 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则原方程可化为 $\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) \left( {\mathrm{D} - 2}\right)  + 2\mathrm{D} - 2}\right\rbrack  y = t{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} +$

$3{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,即

$$
\left\lbrack  {\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) \left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 2\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) }\right\rbrack  y = t{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + 3{\mathrm{e}}^{t}. \tag{8}
$$

方程 (8) 对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 $\left( {r - 1}\right) \left( {{r}^{2} - {2r} + 2}\right)  = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2,3} =$ $1 \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,故齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}\cos t + {C}_{3}\sin t}\right) .
$$

对方程 $\left\lbrack  {\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) \left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 2\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) }\right\rbrack  y = t{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}$ ,因 $\lambda  = 2$ 不是特征方程的根,可令 ${y}_{1}^{ * } =$ $\left( {{At} + B}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}$ ; 对方程 $\left\lbrack  {\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) \left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 2\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) }\right\rbrack  y = 3{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,因 $\lambda  = 1$ 是特征方程的单根,可令 ${y}_{2}^{ * } = {Ct}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ . 由叠加原理,可令 ${y}^{ * } = {y}_{1}^{ * } + {y}_{2}^{ * } = \left( {{At} + B}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + {Ct}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ 是方程 (8) 的特解, 即令

$$
{y}^{ * } = {x}^{2}\left( {A\ln x + B}\right)  + {Cx}\ln x
$$

是原方程的特解, 并有

$$
{y}^{*\prime } = {2Ax}\ln x + \left( {A + {2B}}\right) x + C\ln x + C,
$$

$$
{y}^{*\prime } = {2A}\ln x + \left( {{3A} + {2B}}\right)  + \frac{C}{x},
$$

$$
{y}^{*{\prime \prime \prime }} = \frac{2A}{x} - \frac{C}{{x}^{2}}.
$$

代入原方程 ${x}^{3}{y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {2x}{y}^{\prime } - {2y} = {x}^{2}\ln x + {3x}$ 中,得

$$
{2A}{x}^{2}\ln x + \left( {{4A} + {2B}}\right) {x}^{2} + {Cx} = {x}^{2}\ln x + {3x}.
$$

比较系数得 $A = \frac{1}{2},B =  - 1,C = 3$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = {x}^{2}\left( {\frac{1}{2}\ln x - 1}\right)  + {3x}\ln x.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = x\left\lbrack  {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}\cos \left( {\ln x}\right)  + {C}_{3}\sin \left( {\ln x}\right) }\right\rbrack   + {x}^{2}\left( {\frac{1}{2}\ln x - 1}\right)  + {3x}\ln x.
$$

### 习题 7-10 常系数线性微分方程组解法举例


121. 求下列微分方程组的通解:

(1) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = z, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}z}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = y; \end{array}\right.$ ( 2 ) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = y, \\  \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = x; \end{array}\right.$ (3) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} =  - x + y + 3, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = x + y - 3; \end{array}\right.$ ( 4 ) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {5x} + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - x - {3y} = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}; \end{array}\right.$ (5) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {2x} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + y = t, \\  {5x} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {3y} = {t}^{2}; \end{array}\right.$ (6) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - {3x} + 2\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {4y} = 2\sin t, \\  2\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {2x} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - y = \cos t. \end{array}\right.$ 说明 求解线性微分方程组一般采用 “消去法”: ${1}^{ \circ  }$ 从方程组中消去一些未知函数及其各阶导数,得到只含一个未知函数的线性微分方程, 然后求出该线性微分方程的通解, 本题的 (1) (2) (3) 题采用这种方法来解; 对于学过 “线性代数” 的读者,可以记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,将微分方程组写成代数线性方程组的形式, 然后用类似于克拉默法则的方法, 消去一些未知函数而获得一个未知函数的微分方程, 本题的 (4) (5) (6) 题采用这种方法来解.

${2}^{ \circ  }$ 当用“消去法”求得一个未知函数的通解后,求另一未知函数的通解时,一般不必再积分, 否则会出现新的任意常数. 解 (1) 将

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = z, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}z}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = y, \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

中①式的两端关于 $x$ 求导,得 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}z}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ ,代入 ② 式得 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = y$ ,即

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} - y = 0.
$$

由它的特征方程 ${r}^{2} - 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1$ . 于是得

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

从而由①, 得

$$
z = \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

故方程组的通解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}, \\  z = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}. \end{array}\right.
$$

(2)将

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = y, \\  \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = x, \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

中①式两端关于 $t$ 求二阶导数,得 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{4}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{4}} = \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}}$ ,代入 ② 式得 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{4}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{4}} = x$ ,即

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{4}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{4}} - x = 0.
$$

由它的特征方程 ${r}^{4} - 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1,{r}_{3,4} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ . 于是得

$$
x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + {C}_{3}\cos t + {C}_{4}\sin t.
$$

再由①, 得

$$
y = \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - {C}_{3}\cos t - {C}_{4}\sin t.
$$

故方程组的通解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + {C}_{3}\cos t + {C}_{4}\sin t, \\  y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - {C}_{3}\cos t - {C}_{4}\sin t. \end{array}\right.
$$

(3)将

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {x}^{\prime } + {y}^{\prime } =  - x + y + 3, \\  {x}^{\prime } - {y}^{\prime } = x + y - 3, \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

的① + ②得

$$
{x}^{\prime } = y,
$$

③

代入①式,得 ${x}^{\prime } + {x}^{\prime \prime } =  - x + {x}^{\prime } + 3$ ,即

$$
{x}^{\prime \prime } + x = 3\text{.}
$$

④

由它对应的齐次方程的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,且易见 ${x}^{ * } = 3$ 是④的特解, 于是

$$
x = {C}_{1}\cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t + 3.
$$

由③得

$$
y = {x}^{\prime } =  - {C}_{1}\sin t + {C}_{2}\cos t,
$$

故方程组的通解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {C}_{1}\cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t + 3, \\  y =  - {C}_{1}\sin t + {C}_{2}\cos t. \end{array}\right.
$$

(4)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则方程组可表示为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {\mathrm{D} + 5}\right) x + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \\   - x + \left( {\mathrm{D} - 3}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}, \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

记 $\Delta  = \left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} + 5 & 1 \\   - 1 & \mathrm{D} - 3 \end{matrix}\right| ,{\Delta }_{x} = \left| \begin{matrix} {\mathrm{e}}^{t} & 1 \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} & \mathrm{D} - 3 \end{matrix}\right|$ ,则有 ${\Delta x} = {\Delta }_{x}$ ,即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 2\mathrm{D} - {14}}\right) x =  - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{t} - {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}.
$$

③

由其对应的齐次方程的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {2r} - {14} = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 1 \pm  \sqrt{15}$ ,并令 ${x}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ $+ B{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}$ 是方程③的特解,代入③并比较系数,得

$$
{x}^{ * } = \frac{2}{11}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + \frac{1}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t},
$$

于是得

$$
x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{\left( {-1 + \sqrt{15}}\right) t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{\left( {-1 - \sqrt{15}}\right) t} + \frac{2}{11}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + \frac{1}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t},
$$

并由①得

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t} - \left( {\mathrm{D} + 5}\right) x,
$$

即

$$
y = \left( {-4 - \sqrt{15}}\right) {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{\left( {-1 + \sqrt{15}}\right) t} - \left( {4 - \sqrt{15}}\right) {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{\left( {-1 - \sqrt{15}}\right) t} - \frac{1}{11}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} - \frac{7}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}.
$$

(5)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组可表示为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) x + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = t, \\  {5x} + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) y = {t}^{2}, \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} + 2 & \mathrm{D} + 1 \\  5 & \mathrm{D} + 3 \end{matrix}\right| y = \left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} + 2 & t \\  5 & {t}^{2} \end{matrix}\right| ,
$$

即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 1}\right) y = 2{t}^{2} - {3t}.
$$

③

③ 所对应的齐次方程的特征方程的根为 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,令 ${y}^{ * } = A{t}^{2} + {Bt} + C$ ,代入 ③ 并比较系数,可得 $A = 2,B =  - 3,C =  - 4$ . 于是

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t + 2{t}^{2} - {3t} - 4.
$$

再由 ② 得 $x = \frac{1}{5}\left\lbrack  {{t}^{2} - \left( {\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) y}\right\rbrack$ ,即

$$
x =  - \frac{3{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}}{5}\cos t + \frac{{C}_{1} - 3{C}_{2}}{5}\sin t - {t}^{2} + t + 3.
$$

(6)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组可表示为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {\mathrm{D} - 3}\right) x + \left( {2\mathrm{D} + 4}\right) y = 2\sin t, \\  \left( {2\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) x + \left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) y = \cos t, \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} - 3 & 2\mathrm{D} + 4 \\  2\mathrm{D} + 2 & \mathrm{D} - 1 \end{matrix}\right| x = \left| \begin{matrix} 2\sin t & 2\mathrm{D} + 4 \\  \cos t & \mathrm{D} - 1 \end{matrix}\right| ,
$$

即

$$
\left( {3{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + {16}\mathrm{D} + 5}\right) x = 2\cos t.
$$

③

③ 所对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 $3{r}^{2} + {16r} + 5 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1} =  - 5,{r}_{2} =  - \frac{1}{3}$ . 令 ③ 的特解 ${x}^{ * } = A\cos t + B\sin t$ ,代入 ③ 并比较系数,可得 $A = \frac{1}{65},B = \frac{8}{65}$ . 于是

$$
x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{3}t} + \frac{1}{65}\cos t + \frac{8}{65}\sin t.
$$

再由① $- 2 \times$ ②,得

$$
- \left( {3\mathrm{D} + 7}\right) x + {6y} = 2\sin t - 2\cos t,
$$

即

$$
y = \frac{1}{6}\left\lbrack  {2\sin t - 2\cos t + \left( {3\mathrm{D} + 7}\right) x}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
=  - \frac{4}{3}{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{3}t} + \frac{{61}\sin t - {33}\cos t}{130}.
$$

2. 求下列微分方程组满足所给初值条件的特解:

(1) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = y,{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = 0, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} =  - {\left. x,y\right| }_{t = 0} = 1; \end{array}\right.$ ( 2 ) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} + 2\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - x = 0,{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = 1, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + y = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{t = 0} = 0; \end{array}\right.$

(3) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {3x} - y = 0,{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = 1, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - {8x} + y = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{t = 0} = 4; \end{array}\right.$ (4) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} 2\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - {4x} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t},{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = \frac{3}{2}, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {3x} + y = 0,{\left. y\right| }_{t = 0} = 0; \end{array}\right.$

(5) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {2x} - \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = {10}\cos t,{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = 2, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {2y} = 4{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}},{\left. y\right| }_{t = 0} = 0; \end{array}\right.$

(6) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} - x + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {3y} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - 1,{\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = \frac{48}{49}, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {2x} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + t,{\left. y\right| }_{t = 0} = \frac{95}{98}. \end{array}\right.$

解 (1) 记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,原方程组即为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \mathrm{D}x - y = 0, \\  x + \mathrm{D}y = 0. \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} &  - 1 \\  1 & \mathrm{D} \end{matrix}\right| x = 0,
$$

即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 1}\right) x = 0.
$$

③

由③的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,于是

$$
x = {C}_{1}\cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t.
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 0$ . 故 $x = {C}_{2}\sin t$ . 又由①得

$$
y = \mathrm{D}x = {C}_{2}\cos t,
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,y = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 1$ . 故方程组的特解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = \sin t, \\  y = \cos t. \end{array}\right.
$$

(2)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,原方程组即为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 1}\right) x + 2\mathrm{D}y = 0, \\  \mathrm{D}x + y = 0. \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} {\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 1 & 2\mathrm{D} \\  \mathrm{D} & 1 \end{matrix}\right| x = 0,
$$

即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 1}\right) x = 0.
$$

③

由③的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,于是

$$
x = {C}_{1}\cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t.
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 1$ ,即 $x = \cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t$ . 又由②得

$$
y =  - \mathrm{D}x = \sin t - {C}_{2}\cos t,
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,y = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 0$ . 故方程组的特解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = \cos t, \\  y = \sin t. \end{array}\right.
$$

(3)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组即为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) x - y = 0, \\   - {8x} + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = 0. \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} + 3 &  - 1 \\   - 8 & \mathrm{D} + 1 \end{matrix}\right| x = 0,
$$

即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 4\mathrm{D} - 5}\right) x = 0.
$$

③

由③的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {4r} - 5 = 0$ 解得 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2} =  - 5$ . 于是

$$
x = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}}.
$$

又由①得

$$
y = \left( {\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) x = 4{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} - 2{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{5t}}.
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = 1,y = 4$ ,就有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = 1, \\  4{C}_{1} - 2{C}_{2} = 4, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} = 1,{C}_{2} = 0$ . 故方程组的特解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \\  y = 4{\mathrm{e}}^{t}. \end{array}\right.
$$

(4)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组即为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {2\mathrm{D} - 4}\right) x + \left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \\  \left( {\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) x + y = 0. \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} 2\mathrm{D} - 4 & \mathrm{D} - 1 \\  \mathrm{D} + 3 & 1 \end{matrix}\right| x = \left| \begin{matrix} {\mathrm{e}}^{t} & \mathrm{D} - 1 \\  0 & 1 \end{matrix}\right|
$$

即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 1}\right) x =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{t}.
$$

③

由方程③对应的齐次方程的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + 1 = 0$ 解得

$$
{r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}\text{.}
$$

令 ${x}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,代入方程③并比较系数得 $A =  - \frac{1}{2}$ ,即 ${x}^{ * } =  - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ . 于是

$$
x = {C}_{1}\cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}.
$$

又由②得

$$
y =  - \left( {\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) x = \left( {{C}_{1} - 3{C}_{2}}\right) \sin t - \left( {3{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}}\right) \cos t + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{t}.
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = \frac{3}{2},y = 0$ ,就有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} - \frac{1}{2} = \frac{3}{2}, \\   - 3{C}_{1} - {C}_{2} + 2 = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} = 2,{C}_{2} =  - 4$ . 故方程组的特解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 2\cos t - 4\sin t - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \\  y = {14}\sin t - 2\cos t + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{t}. \end{array}\right.
$$

(5)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组即为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) x - \mathrm{D}y = {10}\cos t, \\  \mathrm{D}x + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) y = 4{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}}. \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} + 2 &  - \mathrm{D} \\  \mathrm{D} & \mathrm{D} + 2 \end{matrix}\right| y = \left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} + 2 & {10}\cos t \\  \mathrm{D} & 4{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} \end{matrix}\right| ,
$$

即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 2\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) y = 5\sin t.
$$

③

由方程③对应的齐次方程的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {2r} + 2 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 1 \pm  \mathrm{i}$ . 令 ${y}^{ * } =$ $A\cos t + B\sin t$ ,代入方程③并比较系数,得 $A =  - 2,B = 1$ . 于是

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-t}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos t + {C}_{2}\sin t}\right)  - 2\cos t + \sin t.
$$

又由① - ②得

$$
x = 5\cos t - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-t}\left( {{C}_{2}\cos t - {C}_{1}\sin t}\right)  + 4\cos t + 3\sin t - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}}.
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = 2,y = 0$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{2} + 4 - 2 = 2, \\  {C}_{1} - 2 = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

解得 ${C}_{1} = 2,{C}_{2} = 0$ ,故方程组的特解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = 4\cos t + 3\sin t - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} - 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-t}\sin t, \\  y =  - 2\cos t + \sin t + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-t}\cos t. \end{array}\right.
$$

(6)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组即为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) x + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - 1, \\  \left( {\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) x + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + t. \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{array}{ll} \mathrm{D} - 1 & \mathrm{D} + 3 \\  \mathrm{D} + 2 & \mathrm{D} + 1 \end{array}\right| x = \left| \begin{matrix} {\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - 1 & \mathrm{D} + 3 \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + t & \mathrm{D} + 1 \end{matrix}\right| ,
$$

即

$$
\left( {5\mathrm{D} + 7}\right) x = 5{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + {3t} + 2,
$$

③

亦即

$$
\mathrm{D}x + \frac{7}{5}x = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + \frac{3}{5}t + \frac{2}{5}.
$$

由一阶线性方程的通解公式, 得

$$
x = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{7}{5}\mathrm{\;d}t}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + \frac{3}{5}t + \frac{2}{5}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{7}{5}\mathrm{\;d}t}\mathrm{\;d}t + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= C{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{7}{5}t} + \frac{5}{17}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + \frac{3}{7}t - \frac{1}{49}.
$$

代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = \frac{48}{49}$ ,得 $C = \frac{12}{17}$ . 于是

$$
x = \frac{12}{17}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{7}{5}t} + \frac{5}{17}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + \frac{3}{7}t - \frac{1}{49}.
$$

由① - ②得

$$
y = \frac{3}{2}x + \frac{1}{2}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} - t - 1}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{18}{17}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{7}{5}t} - \frac{1}{17}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + \frac{1}{7}t - \frac{26}{49}.
$$

### 总习题七

20. 填空

( 1 ) $x{y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + 2{x}^{2}{y}^{\prime 2} + {x}^{3}y = {x}^{4} + 1$ 是_____阶微分方程；

( 2 )一阶线性微分方程 ${y}^{\prime } + P\left( x\right) y = Q\left( x\right)$ 的通解为_____；

( 3 )与积分方程 $y = {\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}f\left( {x,y}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 等价的微分方程初值问题是_____；

(4)已知 $y = 1,y = x,y = {x}^{2}$ 是某二阶非齐次线性微分方程的三个解,则该方程的通解为_____.

解 (1) 3 .

(2) $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int P\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}\left( {\int Q\left( x\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\int P\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)$ .

(3) ${y}^{\prime } = f\left( {x,y}\right) ,{\left. y\right| }_{x = {x}_{0}} = 0$ .

注 ${1}^{ \circ  }$ 方程 $y = {\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}f\left( {x,y}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 的积分上限 $x$ 是积分方程的变量,它是与 $y$ 相对应的; 而积分表达式中 $f\left( {x,y}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ 中的 $x$ 是积分变量,不能将它与积分上限相混淆,故积分方程应理解为 $y = {\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}f\left( {t,y}\right) \mathrm{d}t$ .

${2}^{ \circ  }$ 由于积分方程 $y = {\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}f\left( {t,y}\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 确定了隐函数 $y = y\left( x\right)$ ,因此积分方程中的 $y$ 取 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 后,有恒等式

$$
y\left( x\right)  \equiv  {\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}f\left\lbrack  {t,y\left( t\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}t.
$$

于是上式两端对 $x$ 求导,就得 ${y}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = f\left\lbrack  {x,y\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$ ,即 ${y}^{\prime } = f\left( {x,y}\right)$ . 显然,当 $x = {x}_{0}$ 时, $y = {\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{{x}_{0}}f\left( {x,y}\right) \mathrm{d}x = 0$ ,即 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = {x}_{0}} = 0$ .

(4) $y = {C}_{1}\left( {x - 1}\right)  + {C}_{2}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right)  + 1$ .

因为由叠加原理知 $x - 1$ 与 ${x}^{2} - 1$ 是非齐次方程对应的齐次方程的解,且它们是线性无关的, 于是根据线性方程通解结构得出以上结论.

2. 以下两题中给出了四个结论, 从中选出一个正确的结论:

(1)设非齐次线性微分方程 ${y}^{\prime } + P\left( x\right) y = Q\left( x\right)$ 有两个不同的解: ${y}_{1}\left( x\right)$ 与 ${y}_{2}\left( x\right) ,C$ 为任意常数,则该方程的通解是 (   ).

(A) $C\left\lbrack  {{y}_{1}\left( x\right)  - {y}_{2}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$

(B) ${y}_{1}\left( x\right)  + C\left\lbrack  {{y}_{1}\left( x\right)  - {y}_{2}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$

(C) $C\left\lbrack  {{y}_{1}\left( x\right)  + {y}_{2}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$

(D) ${y}_{1}\left( x\right)  + C\left\lbrack  {{y}_{1}\left( x\right)  + {y}_{2}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$

解 ${y}_{1}\left( x\right)  - {y}_{2}\left( x\right)$ 是对应的齐次方程 ${y}^{\prime } + P\left( x\right) y = 0$ 的非零解,从而由线性微分方程解的性质定理知 $C\left\lbrack  {{y}_{1}\left( x\right)  - {y}_{2}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$ 是齐次方程的通解,再由非齐次线性方程解的结构定理知 ${y}_{1}\left( x\right)  + C\left\lbrack  {{y}_{1}\left( x\right)  - {y}_{2}\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack$ 是原方程的通解. 故选 (B).

(2)具有特解 ${y}_{1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x},{y}_{2} = {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x},{y}_{3} = 3{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 的三阶常系数齐次线性微分方程是 (   ).

(A) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime } + y = 0$

(B) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime } - y = 0$

(C) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - 6{y}^{\prime \prime } + {11}{y}^{\prime } - {6y} = 0$

(D) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 0$

解 由题设知 $r =  - 1, - 1,1$ 为所求齐次线性微分方程对应的特征方程的 3 个根,而 ${\left( r + 1\right) }^{2}\left( {r - 1}\right)  = {r}^{3} + {r}^{2} - r - 1$ ,故应选 (B). 3. 求以下列各式所表示的函数为通解的微分方程:

(1) ${\left( x + C\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1$ (其中 $C$ 为任意常数)；

(2) $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ (其中 ${C}_{1},{C}_{2}$ 为任意常数).

解 (1) 将 ${\left( x + C\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1$ 两端关于 $x$ 求导,得

$$
x + C + y{y}^{\prime } = 0,
$$

即有

$$
C =  - x - y{y}^{\prime },
$$

将其代入 ${\left( x + C\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = 1$ 中,得

$$
{y}^{2}\left( {1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\right)  = 1.
$$

(2)将 $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ 关于 $x$ 求二次导数,得

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {y}^{\prime } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 2{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}, \\  {y}^{\prime \prime } = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 4{C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}. \end{array}\right.
$$

把以上两式看成是以 ${C}_{1}$ 与 ${C}_{2}$ 为未知量的线性方程组,解得

$$
{C}_{1} = \left( {2{y}^{\prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime }}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x},\;{C}_{2} = \frac{1}{2}\left( {{y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime }}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}},
$$

代入 $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ 中,得

$$
y = \left( {2{y}^{\prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime }}\right)  + \frac{1}{2}\left( {{y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime }}\right) ,
$$

即 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 3{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 0$ .

24. 求下列微分方程的通解:

(1) $x{y}^{\prime } + y = 2\sqrt{xy}$ ; (2) $x{y}^{\prime }\ln x + y = {ax}\left( {\ln x + 1}\right)$ ；

(3) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{y}{2\left( {\ln y - x}\right) }$ ; * (4) $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + {xy} - {x}^{3}{y}^{3} = 0$ ;

(5) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime 2} + 1 = 0$ ; (6) $y{y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime 2} - 1 = 0$ ;

(7) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}^{\prime } + {5y} = \sin {2x}$ ; (8) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } = x\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 4}\right)$ ;

* (9) $\left( {{y}^{4} - 3{x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}y + {xy}\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ ; (10) ${y}^{\prime } + x = \sqrt{{x}^{2} + y}$ .

解 (1) 将方程化为 ${y}^{\prime } + \frac{y}{x} = 2\sqrt{\frac{y}{x}}$ ,并令 $\frac{y}{x} = u$ ,则方程成为

$$
x{u}^{\prime } = 2\sqrt{u} - {2u}.
$$

分离变量后有

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{2\sqrt{u}\left( {1 - \sqrt{u}}\right) } = \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x},
$$

积分得

$$
\ln \left| {1 - \sqrt{u}}\right|  =  - \ln \left| x\right|  + \ln {C}_{1},
$$

即 $x\left( {1 - \sqrt{u}}\right)  = C$ ,代入 $u = \frac{y}{x}$ ,得原方程的通解 $x - \sqrt{xy} = C$ .

( 2 )原方程可化为 ${y}^{\prime } + \frac{1}{x\ln x}y = a\left( {1 + \frac{1}{\ln x}}\right)$ ,由一阶线性方程的通解公式,得

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{1}{x\ln x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int a\left( {1 + \frac{1}{\ln x}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{1}{x\ln x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{\ln x}\left\lbrack  {\int a\left( {\ln x + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = \frac{1}{\ln x}\left( {{ax}\ln x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {ax} + \frac{C}{\ln x}\text{.}
$$

故方程的通解为 $y = {ax} + \frac{C}{\ln x}$ .

(3)原方程可表示为 $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + \frac{2}{y}x = \frac{2\ln y}{y}$ ,由一阶线性方程的通解公式,得

$$
x = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{2}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\left( {\int \frac{2\ln y}{y}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{2}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}\left( {\int {2y}\ln y\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)  = \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}\left( {{y}^{2}\ln y - \frac{1}{2}{y}^{2} + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \ln y - \frac{1}{2} + \frac{C}{{y}^{2}}\text{.}
$$

故方程的通解为 $x = \frac{C}{{y}^{2}} + \ln y - \frac{1}{2}$ .

* (4) 原方程为伯努利方程 ${y}^{\prime } + {xy} = {x}^{3}{y}^{3}$ . 该方程两端同除以 ${y}^{3}$ 后成为

$$
\frac{{y}^{\prime }}{{y}^{3}} + x\frac{1}{{y}^{2}} = {x}^{3}.
$$

令 $\frac{1}{{y}^{2}} = z$ ,则 $- 2\frac{{y}^{\prime }}{{y}^{3}} = {z}^{\prime }$ ,且原方程化为

$$
{z}^{\prime } - {2xz} =  - 2{x}^{3}.
$$

得

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int  - 2{x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int {2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\left( {\int  - 2{x}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\left( {{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}-\int {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\left( {{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{2}} + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {x}^{2} + 1 + C{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\text{.}
$$

代入 $z = \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}$ ,即得原方程的通解

$$
\frac{1}{{y}^{2}} = C{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} + {x}^{2} + 1.
$$

(5) 令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = {p}^{\prime }$ 且方程成为

$$
{p}^{\prime } + {p}^{2} + 1 = 0.
$$

分离变量并积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}p}{1 + {p}^{2}} =  - \int \mathrm{d}x,
$$

得 $\arctan p =  - x + {C}_{1}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{\prime } = p = \tan \left( {-x + {C}_{1}}\right) ,
$$

于是得通解

$$
y = \int  - \tan \left( {x - {C}_{1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \ln \left| {\cos \left( {x - {C}_{1}}\right) }\right|  + {C}_{2}\text{,}
$$

或写成 $y = \ln \left| {\cos \left( {x + {C}_{1}}\right) }\right|  + {C}_{2}$ .

(6)此方程不显含 $x$ ,令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,且原方程化为

$$
{yp}\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - {p}^{2} - 1 = 0.
$$

分离变量

$$
\frac{p\mathrm{\;d}p}{{p}^{2} + 1} = \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y},
$$

积分得

$$
\frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {{p}^{2} + 1}\right)  = \ln y + \ln {C}_{1},
$$

即 ${p}^{2} + 1 = {\left( {C}_{1}y\right) }^{2}$ ,故 $p =  \pm  \sqrt{{\left( {C}_{1}y\right) }^{2} - 1}$ . 取 ${y}^{\prime } = \sqrt{{\left( {C}_{1}y\right) }^{2} - 1}$ ,分离变量并积分

$$
x = \int \mathrm{d}x = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{{\left( {C}_{1}y\right) }^{2} - 1}} = \frac{1}{{C}_{1}}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {{C}_{1}y}\right) }{\sqrt{{\left( {C}_{1}y\right) }^{2} - 1}}
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{C}_{1}}\left\{  {\ln \left\lbrack  {{C}_{1}y + \sqrt{{\left( {C}_{1}y\right) }^{2} - 1}}\right\rbrack   - {C}_{2}}\right\}  ,
$$

即 ${C}_{1}y = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{{C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\left( {{C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}}\right) }}{2}$ .

对于 ${y}^{\prime } =  - \sqrt{{\left( {C}_{1}y\right) }^{2} - 1}$ ,可得相同的结果,故原方程的通解为

$$
y = \frac{1}{2{C}_{1}}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{{C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-{C}_{1}x - {C}_{2}}}\right) .
$$

(7)原方程对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} + {2r} + 5 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 1 \pm  2\mathrm{i}$ ,故对应齐次方程的通解为 $Y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x}}\right)$ .

因 $f\left( x\right)  = \sin {2x},\lambda  + \mathrm{i}\omega  = 2\mathrm{i}$ 不是特征方程的根,故令 ${y}^{ * } = A\cos {2x} +$ $B\sin {2x}$ 是原方程的特解. 将 ${y}^{ * }$ 代入原方程,可得

$$
\left( {A + {4B}}\right) \cos {2x} + \left( {B - {4A}}\right) \sin {2x} = \sin {2x}.
$$

比较系数,得 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} A + {4B} = 0, \\  B - {4A} = 1, \end{array}\right.$ 即 $A =  - \frac{4}{17},B = \frac{1}{17}$ . 于是

$$
{y}^{ * } =  - \frac{4}{17}\cos {2x} + \frac{1}{17}\sin {2x}.
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {{C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x}}\right)  - \frac{4}{17}\cos {2x} + \frac{1}{17}\sin {2x}.
$$

(8)原方程对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{3} + {r}^{2} - {2r} = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1} = 0,{r}_{2} = 1,{r}_{3} =$ -2,故对应齐次方程的通解为 $Y = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}}$ .

对于方程

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x},
$$

①

因 ${f}_{1}\left( x\right)  = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,其中 $\lambda  = 1$ 是特征方程的 (单) 根,故令 ${y}_{1}^{ * } = x\left( {{A}_{1}x + {B}_{1}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,代入①中并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,得 $6{A}_{1}x + 8{A}_{1} + 3{B}_{1} = x$ ,比较系数得

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} 6{A}_{1} = 1, \\  8{A}_{1} + 3{B}_{1} = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

即 ${A}_{1} = \frac{1}{6},{B}_{1} =  - \frac{4}{9}$ . 于是 ${y}_{1}^{ * } = \left( {\frac{1}{6}{x}^{2} - \frac{4}{9}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ .

对于方程

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } = {4x},
$$

②

因 ${f}_{2}\left( x\right)  = {4x}$ ,其中 $\lambda  = 0$ 是特征方程的 (单) 根,故令 ${y}_{2}^{ * } = x\left( {{A}_{2}x + {B}_{2}}\right)$ ,代入 ② 中, 得 $- 4{A}_{2}x + 2{A}_{2} - 2{B}_{2} = {4x}$ . 比较系数得 ${A}_{2} =  - 1,{B}_{2} =  - 1$ . 于是 ${y}_{2}^{ * } =  - {x}^{2} - x$ .

根据线性方程解的叠加原理知 ${y}^{ * } = {y}_{1}^{ * } + {y}_{2}^{ * }$ 是原方程的特解,故原方程的通解为

$$
y = Y + {y}^{ * } = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} + \left( {\frac{1}{6}{x}^{2} - \frac{4}{9}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {x}^{2} - x.
$$

* (9) 原方程可改写成 $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \frac{3}{y}x =  - {y}^{3}{x}^{-1}$ ,这是伯努利方程. 在此方程两端同乘以 $x$ ,得 $x\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \frac{3}{y}{x}^{2} =  - {y}^{3}$ .

令 ${x}^{2} = z$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}z}{\mathrm{\;d}y} = {2x}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,且原方程化为

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}z}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \frac{6}{y}z =  - 2{y}^{3},
$$

解得

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{6}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\left( {\int  - 2{y}^{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{6}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)  = {y}^{6}\left( {\int  - \frac{2}{{y}^{3}}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {y}^{6}\left( {\frac{1}{{y}^{2}} + C}\right)  = {y}^{4} + C{y}^{6}.
$$

代入 $z = {x}^{2}$ ,得原方程的通解 ${x}^{2} = {y}^{4} + C{y}^{6}$ .

( 10 )令 $u = \sqrt{{x}^{2} + y}$ ,即 $y = {u}^{2} - {x}^{2}$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = {2u}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - {2x}$ . 且原方程化为 ${2u}\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - x =$

$u$ ,即 $\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - \frac{1}{2}\left( \frac{x}{u}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}$ .

又令 $\frac{u}{x} = v$ ,即 $u = {xv}$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}u}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = v + x\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}x}$ . 且原方程化为

$$
v + x\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - \frac{1}{2v} = \frac{1}{2}.
$$

分离变量得 $\frac{v\mathrm{\;d}v}{2{v}^{2} - v - 1} =  - \frac{1}{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x}$ . 积分

$$
- \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| x\right|  = \int \frac{v\mathrm{\;d}v}{2{v}^{2} - v - 1} = \frac{1}{3}\left( {\int \frac{1}{v - 1}\mathrm{\;d}v+\int \frac{1}{{2v} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}v}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{3}\left\lbrack  {\ln \left| {v - 1}\right|  + \frac{1}{2}\ln \left| {{2v} - 1}\right| }\right\rbrack   + {C}_{1},
$$

即 ${\left( v - 1\right) }^{2}\left( {{2v} - 1}\right) {x}^{3} = {C}_{2}\left( {{C}_{2} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-6{C}_{1}}}\right)$ . 代入 $v = \frac{u}{x}$ ,得

$$
2{u}^{3} - {3x}{u}^{2} + {x}^{3} = {C}_{2}.
$$

再代入 $u = \sqrt{{x}^{2} + y}$ ,得原方程的通解

$$
2{\left( {x}^{2} + y\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}} - {3x}\left( {{x}^{2} + y}\right)  + {x}^{3} = {C}_{2},
$$

即 ${\left( {x}^{2} + y\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}} = {x}^{3} + \frac{3}{2}{xy} + C\left( {C = \frac{{C}_{2}}{2}}\right)$ .

5. 求下列微分方程满足所给初值条件的特解:

* (1) ${y}^{3}\mathrm{\;d}x + 2\left( {{x}^{2} - x{y}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}y = 0,x = 1$ 时 $y = 1$ ;

(2) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - a{y}^{\prime 2} = 0,x = 0$ 时 $y = 0,{y}^{\prime } =  - 1$ ；

(3) $2{y}^{\prime \prime } - \sin {2y} = 0,x = 0$ 时 $y = \frac{\pi }{2},{y}^{\prime } = 1$ ;

(4) ${y}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}^{\prime } + y = \cos x,x = 0$ 时 $y = 0,{y}^{\prime } = \frac{3}{2}$ .

解 * (1) 原方程可以表示成伯努利方程

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \frac{2}{y}x =  - \frac{2}{{y}^{3}}{x}^{2},
$$

即

$$
{x}^{-2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} - \frac{2}{y}{x}^{-1} =  - \frac{2}{{y}^{3}}.
$$

令 $z = {x}^{-1}$ ,则 $\frac{\mathrm{d}z}{\mathrm{\;d}y} =  - {x}^{-2}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,且原方程化为一阶线性方程

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}z}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + \frac{2}{y}z = \frac{2}{{y}^{3}}.
$$

解得

$$
z = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{2}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\left( {\int \frac{2}{{y}^{3}}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{2}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)  = \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}\left( {\int \frac{2}{y}\mathrm{\;d}y + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}\left( {2\ln \left| y\right|  + C}\right) \text{.}
$$

将 $z = {x}^{-1}$ 代入上式,得 ${x}^{-1} = \frac{1}{{y}^{2}}\left( {2\ln \left| y\right|  + C}\right)$ ,即原方程的通解

$$
{y}^{2} = x\left( {2\ln \left| y\right|  + C}\right) .
$$

由初值条件 $x = 1,y = 1$ ,得 $C = 1$ ,故所求特解为

$$
{y}^{2} = x\left( {2\ln \left| y\right|  + 1}\right) .
$$

(2)令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则原方程化为 ${p}^{\prime } - a{p}^{2} = 0$ . 分离变量并积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}p}{{p}^{2}} = \int a\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

得

$$
- \frac{1}{p} = {ax} + {C}_{1},
$$

即 $p =  - \frac{1}{{ax} + {C}_{1}}$ . 代入初值条件 $x = 0,p =  - 1$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 1$ ,从而有

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - \frac{1}{{ax} + 1},
$$

于是

$$
y =  - \int \frac{1}{{ax} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \frac{1}{a}\ln \left( {{ax} + 1}\right)  + {C}_{2}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 0$ . 故所求特解为

$$
y =  - \frac{1}{a}\ln \left( {{ax} + 1}\right) .
$$

(3)在方程 $2{y}^{\prime \prime } - \sin {2y} = 0$ 两端同乘以 ${y}^{\prime }$ ,则有

$$
2{y}^{\prime }{y}^{\prime \prime } - \sin {2y}{y}^{\prime } = 0,
$$

即

$$
{\left( {y}^{\prime 2} + \frac{1}{2}\cos 2y\right) }^{\prime } = 0,
$$

于是

$$
{y}^{\prime 2} + \frac{1}{2}\cos {2y} = {C}_{1}.
$$

代入初值条件 $y = \frac{\pi }{2},{y}^{\prime } = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = \frac{1}{2}$ . 故有 ${y}^{\prime 2} + \frac{1}{2}\cos {2y} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{\prime 2} = \frac{1}{2} - \frac{1}{2}\cos {2y} = {\sin }^{2}y,
$$

并因 $y = \frac{\pi }{2}$ 时, ${y}^{\prime } = 1$ ,故上式开方后取

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \sin y\text{.}
$$

分离变量并积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\sin y} = \int \mathrm{d}x,
$$

得

$$
\ln \tan \frac{y}{2} = x + {C}_{2}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = \frac{\pi }{2}$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 0$ ,故所求特解为 $\ln \tan \frac{y}{2} = x$ ,即

$$
y = 2\arctan {\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

(4)由原方程对应齐次方程的特征方程 ${r}^{2} + {2r} + 1 = 0$ ,解得 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 1$ ,故对应齐次方程的通解为 $Y = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ .

因 $f\left( x\right)  = \cos x,\lambda  + \mathrm{i}\omega  = 0 + \mathrm{i}$ 不是特征方程的根,故令 ${y}^{ * } = A\cos x + B\sin x$ 是原方程的特解, 并代入原方程, 得

$$
- {2A}\sin x + {2B}\cos x = \cos x.
$$

比较系数得 $A = 0,B = \frac{1}{2}$ ,故 ${y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{2}\sin x$ ,且原方程的通解为

$$
y = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + \frac{1}{2}\sin x,
$$

并有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \left( {{C}_{2} - {C}_{1} - {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + \frac{1}{2}\cos x.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,y = 0,{y}^{\prime } = \frac{3}{2}$ ,有

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 0, \\  {C}_{2} - {C}_{1} + \frac{1}{2} = \frac{3}{2}, \end{array}\right.
$$

即 ${C}_{1} = 0,{C}_{2} = 1$ . 故所求特解为

$$
y = x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} + \frac{1}{2}\sin x.
$$

26. 已知某曲线经过点(1,1),它的切线在纵轴上的截距等于切点的横坐标,求它的方程.

解 设(x,y)为曲线上的点,则曲线在该点处的切线方程为

$$
Y - y = {y}^{\prime }\left( {X - x}\right) ,
$$

切线在纵轴上的截距为 $y - x{y}^{\prime }$ . 并依题意,有

$$
y - x{y}^{\prime } = x,{\left. \;y\right| }_{x = 1} = 1.
$$

将上述方程写成 ${y}^{\prime } - \frac{1}{x}y =  - 1$ ,可解得

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x} + C}\right)  = x\left( {\int  - \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= x\left( {C - \ln \left| x\right| }\right) \text{.}
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 1,y = 1$ ,得 $C = 1$ . 故所求曲线的方程为

$$
y = x\left( {1 - \ln \left| x\right| }\right) .
$$

27. 已知某车间的容积为 ${30} \times  {30} \times  6{\mathrm{\;m}}^{3}$ ,其中的空气含 ${0.12}\%$ 的 ${\mathrm{{CO}}}_{2}$ (以容积计算). 现以含 ${\mathrm{{CO}}}_{2}{0.04}\%$ 的新鲜空气输入,问每分钟应输入多少,才能在 30 min 后使车间空气中 ${\mathrm{{CO}}}_{2}$ 的含量不超过 0.06%? (假定输入的新鲜空气与原有空气很快混合均匀后, 以相同的流量排出. )

解 设每分钟输入 $v\left( {\mathrm{\;m}}^{3}\right)$ 的空气. 又设在时刻 $t$ 车间中 ${\mathrm{{CO}}}_{2}$ 的浓度为 $x =$ $x\left( t\right) \left( \% \right)$ ,则在时间间隔 $\left\lbrack  {t,t + \mathrm{d}t}\right\rbrack$ 内,车间内 ${\mathrm{{CO}}}_{2}$ 的含量的改变量为

$$
{30} \times  {30} \times  6\mathrm{\;d}x = {0.04} \times  {10}^{-2}v\mathrm{\;d}t - {vx}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x - {0.0004}} =  - \frac{v}{5400}\mathrm{\;d}t,
$$

且 ${\left. x\right| }_{t = 0} = {0.0012}$ .

将上述微分方程两端积分, 得

$$
\ln \left( {x - {0.0004}}\right)  =  - \frac{v}{5400}t + \ln C,
$$

即 $x = {0.0004} + C{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{v}{5400}t}$ . 代入初值条件 $t = 0,x = {0.0012}$ ,可得 $C = {0.0008}$ . 于是有

$$
x = {0.0004} + {0.0008}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{v}{5400}t}.
$$

依题意,当 $t = {30}$ 时, $x \leq  {0.0006}$ ,将 $t = {30},x = {0.0006}$ 代入上式,解得

$$
v = {180}\ln 4 \approx  {250}\left( {\mathrm{\;m}}^{3}\right) .
$$

故每分钟至少输入新鲜空气 ${250}{\mathrm{\;m}}^{3}$ .

2. 8. 设可导函数 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ 满足

$$
\varphi \left( x\right) \cos x + 2{\int }_{0}^{x}\varphi \left( t\right) \sin t\mathrm{\;d}t = x + 1,
$$

求 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ .

解 在方程 $\varphi \left( x\right) \cos x + 2{\int }_{0}^{x}\varphi \left( t\right) \sin t\mathrm{\;d}t = x + 1$ 两端关于 $x$ 求导,得

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right) \cos x - \varphi \left( x\right) \sin x + {2\varphi }\left( x\right) \sin x = 1,
$$

即 ${\varphi }^{\prime } + \tan x \cdot  \varphi  = \sec x$ ,且在原方程中取 $x = 0$ ,可得 $\varphi \left( 0\right)  = 1$ .

由一阶线性方程的通解公式, 得

$$
\varphi  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \tan x\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int \sec x{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \tan x\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \cos x\left( {\int {\sec }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = \cos x\left( {\tan x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \sin x + C\cos x\text{.}
$$

代入初值条件 $x = 0,\varphi  = 1$ ,可得 $C = 1$ ,故

$$
\varphi \left( x\right)  = \sin x + \cos x.
$$

9. 设光滑曲线 $y = \varphi \left( x\right)$ 过原点,且当 $x > 0$ 时 $\varphi \left( x\right)  > 0$ ,对应于 $\left\lbrack  {0,x}\right\rbrack$ 一段曲线的弧长为 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1$ ,求 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ .

解 根据题设条件得

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1,{\left. \;y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0.
$$

在积分方程两端对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},
$$

即 ${y}^{\prime } =  \pm  \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}$ . 取 ${y}^{\prime } = \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}$ ,积分得

$$
y = \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1} - \arctan \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1} + C,
$$

由初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ 知 $C = 0$ ,故

$$
y = \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1} - \arctan \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}.
$$

注: 此函数满足题设条件: $x > 0$ 时, $y = \varphi \left( x\right)  > 0$ . 若取 ${y}^{\prime } =  - \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}$ ,则积分所得的函数不满足这个题设条件.

1910. 设 ${y}_{1}\left( x\right) \text{、}{y}_{2}\left( x\right)$ 是二阶齐次线性方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + p\left( x\right) {y}^{\prime } + q\left( x\right) y = 0$ 的两个解,令

$$
W\left( x\right)  = \left| \begin{matrix} {y}_{1}\left( x\right) & {y}_{2}\left( x\right) \\  {y}_{1}^{\prime }\left( x\right) & {y}_{2}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  \end{matrix}\right|  = {y}_{1}\left( x\right) {y}_{2}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - {y}_{1}^{\prime }\left( x\right) {y}_{2}\left( x\right) ,
$$

证明: (1) $W\left( x\right)$ 满足方程 ${W}^{\prime } + p\left( x\right) W = 0$ ;

(2) $W\left( x\right)  = W\left( {x}_{0}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}p\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}$ .

证 (1) 依题意,对 $i = 1,2$ ,有

$$
{y}_{i}^{\prime \prime } + p\left( x\right) {y}_{i}^{\prime } + q\left( x\right) {y}_{i} = 0,
$$

即 ${y}_{i}^{\prime \prime } + p\left( x\right) {y}_{i}^{\prime } =  - q\left( x\right) {y}_{i}$ . 于是

$$
{W}^{\prime } + p\left( x\right) W
$$

$$
= \left( {{y}_{1}^{\prime }{}_{1}{y}^{\prime }{}_{2} + {y}_{1}{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } - {y}_{1}^{\prime \prime }{y}_{2} - {y}^{\prime }{}_{1}{y}^{\prime }{}_{2}}\right)  + p\left( x\right) \left( {{y}_{1}{y}^{\prime }{}_{2} - {y}^{\prime }{}_{1}{y}_{2}}\right)
$$

$$
= {y}_{1}\left\lbrack  {{y}_{2}^{\prime \prime } + p\left( x\right) {y}_{2}^{\prime }}\right\rbrack   - {y}_{2}\left\lbrack  {{y}_{1}^{\prime \prime } + p\left( x\right) {y}_{1}^{\prime }}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {y}_{1}\left\lbrack  {-q\left( x\right) {y}_{2}}\right\rbrack   - {y}_{2}\left\lbrack  {-q\left( x\right) {y}_{1}}\right\rbrack   = 0.
$$

故 $W$ 满足所给微分方程.

(2) 因 ${W}^{\prime } + p\left( x\right) W = 0$ ,分离变量得 $\frac{\mathrm{d}W}{W} =  - p\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ . 将上式两端分别在

$\left\lbrack  {{W}_{0},W}\right\rbrack$ 与 $\left\lbrack  {{x}_{0},x}\right\rbrack$ 上积分,得

$$
\ln W - \ln {W}_{0} =  - {\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}p\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x,
$$

其中 ${W}_{0} = W\left( {x}_{0}\right)$ . 于是得

$$
W = W\left( {x}_{0}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{x}p\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}.
$$

25 *11. 求下列欧拉方程的通解:

(1) ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } + {3x}{y}^{\prime } + y = 0$ ;

(2) ${x}^{2}{y}^{\prime \prime } - {4x}{y}^{\prime } + {6y} = x$ .

解 (1) 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,即 $t = \ln x$ ,并记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则原方程可化为

$$
\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  + 3\mathrm{D} + 1}\right\rbrack  y = 0,
$$

即 $\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 2\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = 0$ .

该方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} + {2r} + 1 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 1$ ,于是该方程的通解为

$$
y = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-t},
$$

故原方程的通解为

$$
y = \frac{{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}\ln x}{x}.
$$

(2)令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,即 $t = \ln x$ ,并记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则原方程可化为

$$
\left\lbrack  {\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right)  - 4\mathrm{D} + 6}\right\rbrack  y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t},
$$

即 $\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 5\mathrm{D} + 6}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ .

该方程对应齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {5r} + 6 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1} = 2,{r}_{2} = 3$ . 故齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{3t}.
$$

因 $f\left( t\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{t},\lambda  = 1$ 不是特征方程的根,故可令 ${y}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ 是非齐次方程的特解. 代入 $\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} - 5\mathrm{D} + 6}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ 中并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,得 $A = \frac{1}{2}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}.
$$

于是得

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{3t} + \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{t},
$$

即原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{x}^{2} + {C}_{2}{x}^{3} + \frac{x}{2}.
$$

2° 12. 求下列常系数线性微分方程组的通解:

(1) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + 2\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + y = 0, \\  3\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {2x} + 4\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + {3y} = t; \end{array}\right.$ ( 2 ) $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} + 2\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + x + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + y = 0, \\  \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + x + \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{t}^{2}} + 2\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t} + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}. \end{array}\right.$

解 (1) 记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组可表示为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \mathrm{D}x + \left( {2\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = 0, \\  \left( {3\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) x + \left( {4\mathrm{D} + 3}\right) y = t. \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} \mathrm{D} & 2\mathrm{D} + 1 \\  3\mathrm{D} + 2 & 4\mathrm{D} + 3 \end{matrix}\right| x = \left| \begin{matrix} 0 & 2\mathrm{D} + 1 \\  t & 4\mathrm{D} + 3 \end{matrix}\right| ,
$$

即

$$
\left( {2{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 4\mathrm{D} + 2}\right) x =  - t - 2.
$$

③

方程③对应齐次方程的特征方程为 $2{r}^{2} + {4r} + 2 = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1,2} =  - 1$ . 因 $f\left( t\right)  =$ $- t - 2$ ,故令 ${x}^{ * } = {At} + B$ 是③的特解,代入③中,即得 $A = \frac{1}{2},B = 0$ . 故方程③有通解

$$
x = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + \frac{1}{2}t.
$$

又由② $- 2 \times$ ①可得

$$
y =  - \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) x + t
$$

$$
=  - \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2} + {C}_{2}t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - \frac{1}{2},
$$

故方程组的通解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + \frac{1}{2}t, \\  y =  - \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2} + {C}_{2}t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - \frac{1}{2}. \end{array}\right.
$$

(2)记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,方程组可表示为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} \left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 2\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) x + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = 0, \\  \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) x + \left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 2\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \end{array}\right.
$$

即

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {\left( \mathrm{D} + 1\right) }^{2}x + \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y = 0, \\  \left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) x + {\left( \mathrm{D} + 1\right) }^{2}y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \end{array}\right.
$$

①

②

则有

$$
\left| \begin{matrix} {\left( \mathrm{D} + 1\right) }^{2} & \mathrm{D} + 1 \\  \mathrm{D} + 1 & {\left( \mathrm{D} + 1\right) }^{2} \end{matrix}\right| x = \left| \begin{matrix} 0 & \mathrm{D} + 1 \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{t} & {\left( \mathrm{D} + 1\right) }^{2} \end{matrix}\right|
$$

即

$$
\left( {{\mathrm{D}}^{3} + 3{\mathrm{D}}^{2} + 2\mathrm{D}}\right) x =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{t}.
$$

③

方程③对应齐次方程的特征方程为 $r\left( {{r}^{2} + {3r} + 2}\right)  = 0$ ,有根 ${r}_{1} = 0,{r}_{2} =  - 1,{r}_{3} =$ -2. 而 $f\left( t\right)  =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{t},\lambda  = 1$ 不是特征方程的根,故令 ${x}^{ * } = A{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ 是方程③的特解,代入③ 中并消去 ${\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,可得 $A =  - \frac{1}{6}$ ,即 ${x}^{ * } =  - \frac{1}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,于是方程③的通解为

$$
x = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} - \frac{1}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}.
$$

又由方程①得

$$
\left( {\mathrm{D} + 1}\right) y =  - {\left( \mathrm{D} + 1\right) }^{2}x =  - {\mathrm{D}}^{2}x - 2\mathrm{D}x - x
$$

$$
=  - {C}_{1} - {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + \frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{t},
$$

即 ${y}^{\prime } + y =  - {C}_{1} - {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + \frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,可解得

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \mathrm{d}t}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {-{C}_{1} - {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + \frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \mathrm{d}t}\mathrm{\;d}t + {C}_{4}}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-t}\left\lbrack  {\int \left( {-{C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} - {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + \frac{2}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}}\right) \mathrm{d}t + {C}_{4}}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
=  - {C}_{1} + {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + \frac{1}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + {C}_{4}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t}.
$$

故方程组的通解为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} - \frac{1}{6}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \\  y = {C}_{4}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} - {C}_{1} + {C}_{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}} + \frac{1}{3}{\mathrm{e}}^{t}. \end{array}\right.
$$

# 二、全国硕士研究生入学统一考试数学 试题选解

## (一)函数 极限 连续

2.1. (2004. III,IV) 函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{\left| x\right| \sin \left( {x - 2}\right) }{x\left( {x - 1}\right) {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2}}$ 在下列哪个区间内有界 (   ).

(A)(-1,0) (B)(0,1) (C)(1,2) (D)(2,3)

解 因为 $x \rightarrow  1$ 及 $x \rightarrow  2$ 时,均有 $f\left( x\right)  \rightarrow  \infty$ ,所以 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0,1}\right) ,\left( {1,2}\right) ,\left( {2,3}\right)$ 内均无界,故应选 (A).

2. (1998. II) 设数列 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 与 $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 满足 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}{y}_{n} = 0$ ,则下列断言正确的是 (   ).

(A) 若 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 发散,则 $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 必发散 (B) 若 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 无界,则 $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 必有界

(C) 若 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 有界,则 $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 必为无穷小 (D) 若 $\left\{  \frac{1}{{x}_{n}}\right\}$ 为无穷小,则 $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 必为无穷小

解 取 ${x}_{n} = n,{y}_{n} = \frac{1}{{n}^{2}}$ ,则 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}{y}_{n} = 0$ ,且 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 发散,但 $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 收敛,故 (A) 不正确.

取 ${x}_{n} = \left\lbrack  {1 + {\left( -1\right) }^{n}}\right\rbrack  n,{y}_{n} = \left\lbrack  {1 - {\left( -1\right) }^{n}}\right\rbrack  n$ ,则 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}{y}_{n} = 0$ ,且 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}  ,\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 都无界, 故 (B) 不正确.

取 ${x}_{n} = \frac{1}{{n}^{2}},{y}_{n} = n$ ,则 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}{y}_{n} = 0$ ,且 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 有界,但 $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}$ 不是无穷小,故(C)也不正确.

由 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}{y}_{n} = 0$ 知 $\left\{  {{x}_{n}{y}_{n}}\right\}$ 为无穷小 $\left( {n \rightarrow  \infty }\right)$ ,故当 $\left\{  \frac{1}{{x}_{n}}\right\}$ 为无穷小时, $\left\{  {y}_{n}\right\}   =$ $\left\{  {\left( {{x}_{n}{y}_{n}}\right)  \cdot  \frac{1}{{x}_{n}}}\right\}$ 为无穷小,故应选 (D).

2. 3. (2007. I )当 $x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }$ 时,与 $\sqrt{x}$ 等价的无穷小量是(   ).

(A) $1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{x}}$ (B) $\ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - \sqrt{x}}$ (C) $\sqrt{1 + \sqrt{x}} - 1$ (D) $1 - \cos \sqrt{x}$

解 当 $x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }$ 时,有 $1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{x}} =  - \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{\sqrt{x}} - 1}\right)  \sim   - \sqrt{x},\sqrt{1 + \sqrt{x}} - 1 \sim  \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{x},1 - \cos \sqrt{x}$ $\sim  \frac{1}{2}{\left( \sqrt{x}\right) }^{2} = \frac{1}{2}x$ . 利用排除法知应选 (B).

注 本题直接找出 $\ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - \sqrt{x}}$ 的等价无穷小有些困难,但由于另外三个的等价无穷小很容易得到, 因此通过排除法可得到答案. 事实上,

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{\ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - \sqrt{x}}}{\sqrt{x}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - \ln \left( {1 - \sqrt{x}}\right) }{\sqrt{x}}\underset{t \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}{\underbrace{\;\sqrt{x} = t\;}}\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{\ln \left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right)  - \ln \left( {1 - t}\right) }{t}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{\frac{2t}{1 + {t}^{2}} + \frac{1}{1 - t}}{1} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{{2t}\left( {1 - t}\right)  + 1 + {t}^{2}}{\left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right) \left( {1 - t}\right) } = 1.
$$

24. (2009. I ,III) 当 $x \rightarrow  0$ 时, $f\left( x\right)  = x - \sin {ax}$ 与 $g\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2}\ln \left( {1 - {bx}}\right)$ 是等价无穷小, 则(   ).

(A) $a = 1,b =  - \frac{1}{6}$ (B) $a = 1,b = \frac{1}{6}$

(C) $a =  - 1,b =  - \frac{1}{6}$ (D) $a =  - 1,b = \frac{1}{6}$

解 因为 $f\left( x\right)  = x - \sin {ax},g\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2}\ln \left( {1 - {bx}}\right)$ 为等价无穷小,所以

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right) }{g\left( x\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x - \sin {ax}}{{x}^{2}\ln \left( {1 - {bx}}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x - \sin {ax}}{{x}^{2} \cdot  \left( {-{bx}}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - a\cos {ax}}{-{3b}{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{a}^{2}\sin {ax}}{-{6bx}}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{a}^{2} \cdot  {ax}}{-{6bx}} =  - \frac{{a}^{3}}{6b} = 1,
$$

得 ${a}^{3} =  - {6b}$ ,由此排除 (B) (C).

另外, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - a\cos {ax}}{-{3b}{x}^{2}}$ 存在,蕴含了 $1 - a\cos {ax} \rightarrow  0\left( {x \rightarrow  0}\right)$ ,得 $a = 1$ ,排除 (D). 故应选 (A).

25. (2001. II) 设当 $x \rightarrow  0$ 时, $\left( {1 - \cos x}\right) \ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)$ 是比 $x\sin {x}^{n}$ 高阶的无穷小,而 $x\sin {x}^{n}$ 是比 $\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} - 1}\right)$ 高阶的无穷小,则正整数 $n$ 等于 (   ).

(A) 1 (B) 2 (C) 3 (D) 4

解 当 $x \rightarrow  0$ 时, $\left( {1 - \cos x}\right) \ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)  \sim  \frac{1}{2}{x}^{4},x\sin {x}^{n} \sim  {x}^{n + 1},{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} - 1 \sim  {x}^{2}$ ,故应选 (B).

26. ( 2007. I ,Ⅲ )曲线 $y = \frac{1}{x} + \ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right)$ 的渐近线的条数为(   ).

(A) 0 (B) 1 (C) 2 (D) 3

解 因为 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{x} + \ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right) }\right\rbrack   = \infty$ ,所以 $x = 0$ 为垂直渐近线; 又 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   - \infty }}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{x} + \ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right) }\right\rbrack   = 0$ ,所以 $y = 0$ 为水平渐近线; 进一步,

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{y}{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{{x}^{2}} + \frac{\ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right) }{x}}\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{\ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right) }{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}} = 1,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left\lbrack  {y - 1 \cdot  x}\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{x} + \ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right)  - x}\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left\lbrack  {\ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}}\right)  - x}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\left\lbrack  {\ln {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right)  - x}\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}\ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right)  = 0,
$$

于是有斜渐近线: $y = x$ . 故应选 (D).

注 一般来说,有水平渐近线 (即 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}y = c$ ) 就不再考虑斜渐近线,但当 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}y$ 不存在时,就要分别讨论 $x \rightarrow   - \infty$ 和 $x \rightarrow   + \infty$ 两种情况,即左右两侧的渐近线. 本题在 $x < 0$ 的一侧有水平渐近线,而在 $x > 0$ 的一侧有斜渐近线. 关键应注意指数函数 ${\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 当 $x \rightarrow  \infty$ 时极限不存在,必须分 $x \rightarrow   - \infty$ 和 $x \rightarrow   + \infty$ 进行讨论.

27. (2010. I ) 极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left\lbrack  \frac{{x}^{2}}{\left( {x - a}\right) \left( {x + b}\right) }\right\rbrack  }^{x}$ 等于(   ).

(A) 1 (B) $\mathrm{e}$ (C) ${\mathrm{e}}^{a - b}$ (D) ${\mathrm{e}}^{b - a}$

解 因为 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left\lbrack  \frac{{x}^{2}}{\left( {x - a}\right) \left( {x + b}\right) }\right\rbrack  }^{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left\{  {\left\lbrack  1 + \frac{\left( {a - b}\right) x + {ab}}{\left( {x - a}\right) \left( {x + b}\right) }\right\rbrack  }^{\frac{\left( {x - a}\right) \left( {x + b}\right) }{\left( {a - b}\right) x + {ab}}}\right\}  }^{\frac{x\left\lbrack  {\left( {a - b}\right) x + {ab}}\right\rbrack  }{\left( {x - a}\right) \left( {x + b}\right) }} =$ ${\mathrm{e}}^{a - b}$ ,所以应选 (C).

28. (2008. I ) 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内单调有界, $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 为数列,下列命题正确的是 (   ).

(A) 若 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 收敛,则 $\left\{  {f\left( {x}_{n}\right) }\right\}$ 收敛 (B) 若 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 单调,则 $\left\{  {f\left( {x}_{n}\right) }\right\}$ 收敛

(C) 若 $\left\{  {f\left( {x}_{n}\right) }\right\}$ 收敛,则 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 收敛 (D) 若 $\left\{  {f\left( {x}_{n}\right) }\right\}$ 单调,则 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 收敛

解 若 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 单调,则由函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内单调有界知, $\left\{  {f\left( {x}_{n}\right) }\right\}$ 单调有界,从而 $\left\{  {f\left( {x}_{n}\right) }\right\}$ 收敛,故应选 (B).

例 9. (1994. I , II) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {\cot x\left( {\frac{1}{\sin x} - \frac{1}{x}}\right) }\right\rbrack   =$ _____.

解 由等价无穷小代换定理

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\cot x}\right) \left( {\frac{1}{\sin x} - \frac{1}{x}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x - \sin x}{x\sin x\tan x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\frac{1}{6}{x}^{3}}{{x}^{3}} = \frac{1}{6}.
$$

2010. (1999. II) 求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sqrt{1 + \tan x} - \sqrt{1 + \sin x}}{x\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - {x}^{2}}$ .

解 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sqrt{1 + \tan x} - \sqrt{1 + \sin x}}{x\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - {x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\{  {\frac{\tan x - \sin x}{x\left\lbrack  {\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - x}\right\rbrack  } \cdot  \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 + \tan x} + \sqrt{1 + \sin x}}}\right\}$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - \cos x}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - x} = \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sin x}{-\frac{x}{1 + x}} =  - \frac{1}{2}.
$$

1211. (2000. I ) 求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\frac{2 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}}}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{4}{x}}} + \frac{\sin x}{\left| x\right| }}\right)$ .

解 因为

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\left( {\frac{2 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}}}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{4}{x}}} + \frac{\sin x}{\left| x\right| }}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\left( {\frac{2{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{4}{x}} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{3}{x}}}{{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{4}{x}} + 1} + \frac{\sin x}{x}}\right)  = 1,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\left( {\frac{2 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}}}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{4}{x}}} + \frac{\sin x}{\left| x\right| }}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\left( {\frac{2 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}}}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{4}{x}}} - \frac{\sin x}{x}}\right)  = 2 - 1 = 1,
$$

所以

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\frac{2 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}}}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{4}{x}}} + \frac{\sin x}{\left| x\right| }}\right)  = 1.
$$

2012. (1997. I ) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{3\sin x + {x}^{2}\cos \frac{1}{x}}{\left( {1 + \cos x}\right) \ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } =$ _____.

解 因为

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{3\sin x}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{3x}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } = 3,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{x}^{2}\cos \frac{1}{x}}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{x}^{2}\cos \frac{1}{x}}{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}x\cos \frac{1}{x} = 0,
$$

所以

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{3\sin x + {x}^{2}\cos \frac{1}{x}}{\left( {1 + \cos x}\right) \ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{1 + \cos x}\left\lbrack  {\frac{3\sin x}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) } + \frac{{x}^{2}\cos \frac{1}{x}}{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }}\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{2}\left( {3 + 0}\right)  = \frac{3}{2}\text{.}
$$

例 13. (2008. I ) 求极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left\lbrack  {\sin x - \sin \left( {\sin x}\right) }\right\rbrack  \sin x}{{x}^{4}}$ .

解法一 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left\lbrack  {\sin x - \sin \left( {\sin x}\right) }\right\rbrack  \sin x}{{x}^{4}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left\lbrack  \sin x - \sin \left( \sin x\right) \right\rbrack  }{{x}^{3}}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\cos x - \cos \left( {\sin x}\right) \cos x}{3{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - \cos \left( {\sin x}\right) }{3{x}^{2}}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sin \left( {\sin x}\right) \cos x}{6x} = \frac{1}{6}\text{.}
$$

解法二 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left\lbrack  {\sin x - \sin \left( {\sin x}\right) }\right\rbrack  \sin x}{{x}^{4}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left\lbrack  {\sin x - \sin \left( {\sin x}\right) }\right\rbrack  \sin x}{{\sin }^{4}x}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  0}}\frac{t - \sin t}{{t}^{3}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - \cos t}{3{t}^{2}}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sin t}{6t} = \frac{1}{6}\text{.}
$$

例 14. (2011. I ) 求极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left\lbrack  \frac{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }{x}\right\rbrack  }^{\frac{1}{{e}^{x} - 1}}$ .

分析 本题考查极限的计算,属于 ${1}^{\infty }$ 形式的极限. 计算时,先按 ${1}^{\infty }$ 未定式的计算方法将极限式变形, 再综合利用等价无穷小替换、洛必达法则等方法进行计算.

解 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left\lbrack  \frac{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }{x}\right\rbrack  }^{\frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left\lbrack  1 + \frac{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - x}{x}\right\rbrack  }^{\frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - x}{x}\frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}}$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - x}{{x}^{2}}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}^{\frac{1}{1 + x}} - 1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{-x}{{2x}\left( {1 + x}\right) }} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{2}}.
$$

25. 15. (1995. III) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {\frac{1}{{n}^{2} + n + 1} + \frac{2}{{n}^{2} + n + 2} + \cdots  + \frac{n}{{n}^{2} + n + n}}\right)  =$ _____.

解 因为

$$
\frac{n\left( {n + 1}\right) }{2\left( {{n}^{2} + n + n}\right) } \leq  \frac{1}{{n}^{2} + n + 1} + \frac{2}{{n}^{2} + n + 2} + \cdots  + \frac{n}{{n}^{2} + n + n}
$$

$$
\leq  \frac{n\left( {n + 1}\right) }{2\left( {{n}^{2} + n + 1}\right) },
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{n\left( {n + 1}\right) }{2\left( {{n}^{2} + n + 1}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{n\left( {n + 1}\right) }{2\left( {{n}^{2} + n + n}\right) } = \frac{1}{2},
$$

所以由夹逼准则知原式 $= \frac{1}{2}$ .

2516. (1998. I,II) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sqrt{1 + x} + \sqrt{1 - x} - 2}{{x}^{2}} =$ _____.

解法一 利用洛必达法则,

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sqrt{1 + x} + \sqrt{1 - x} - 2}{{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\frac{1}{2\sqrt{1 + x}} - \frac{1}{2\sqrt{1 - x}}}{2x}
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{-\frac{1}{2}} - {\left( 1 - x\right) }^{-\frac{1}{2}}}{x}
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {-\frac{1}{2}{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{-\frac{3}{2}} - \frac{1}{2}{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{-\frac{3}{2}}}\right\rbrack   =  - \frac{1}{4}.
$$

解法二 利用泰勒公式, 因为

$$
\sqrt{1 + x} = 1 + \frac{1}{2}x + \frac{\frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{2} - 1}\right) }{2!}{x}^{2} + o\left( {x}^{2}\right) ,
$$

$$
\sqrt{1 - x} = 1 - \frac{1}{2}x + \frac{\frac{1}{2}\left( {\frac{1}{2} - 1}\right) }{2!}{x}^{2} + o\left( {x}^{2}\right) ,
$$

所以

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sqrt{1 + x} + \sqrt{1 - x} - 2}{{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{-\frac{1}{4}{x}^{2} + o\left( {x}^{2}\right) }{{x}^{2}} =  - \frac{1}{4}.
$$

例 17. (2006. I ) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }{1 - \cos x} =$ _____.

解法一 利用等价无穷小,

$$
