\text{ 原极限 } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{x}^{2}}{\frac{1}{2}{x}^{2}} = 2\text{. }
$$

解法二 利用三角公式及两个重要极限,

原极限 $= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) }{2{\sin }^{2}\frac{x}{2}}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}2 \cdot  \frac{{\left( \frac{x}{2}\right) }^{2}}{{\sin }^{2}\frac{x}{2}} \cdot  \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\ln {\left( 1 + x\right) }^{\frac{1}{x}} = 2 \cdot  1 = 2.
$$

13. 18. (1994. III) 计算 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\tan }^{n}\left( {\frac{\pi }{4} + \frac{2}{n}}\right)$ .

解 因为

$$
\tan \left( {\frac{\pi }{4} + \frac{2}{n}}\right)  = \frac{1 + \tan \frac{2}{n}}{1 - \tan \frac{2}{n}},
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{\tan \frac{2}{n}}{\frac{2}{n}} = 1,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{1}{1 - \tan \frac{2}{n}} = 1,
$$

所以

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\tan }^{n}\left( {\frac{\pi }{4} + \frac{2}{n}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( \frac{1 + \tan \frac{2}{n}}{1 - \tan \frac{2}{n}}\right) }^{n}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( 1 + \frac{2\tan \frac{2}{n}}{1 - \tan \frac{2}{n}}\right) }^{n}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( 1 + \frac{2\tan \frac{2}{n}}{1 - \tan \frac{2}{n}}\right) }^{\frac{1 - {\tan }^{\frac{2}{n}}}{2{\tan }^{\frac{2}{n}}} \cdot  \frac{4{\tan }^{\frac{2}{n}}}{\frac{2}{n}} \cdot  \frac{1}{1 - {\tan }^{\frac{2}{n}}}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{4}.
$$

29 19. (2006. I ) 设数列 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 满足 $0 < {x}_{1} < \pi ,{x}_{n + 1} = \sin {x}_{n}\left( {n = 1,2,\cdots }\right)$ .

(I) 证明 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}$ 存在,并求该极限;

( II ) 计算 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( \frac{{x}_{n + 1}}{{x}_{n}}\right) }^{\frac{1}{{x}_{n}^{2}}}$ .

解 (I) 用归纳法证明 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 单调减少且有下界.

由 $0 < {x}_{1} < \pi$ ,得

$$
0 < {x}_{2} = \sin {x}_{1} < {x}_{1} < \pi ;
$$

设 $0 < {x}_{n} < \pi$ ,则

$$
0 < {x}_{n + 1} = \sin {x}_{n} < {x}_{n} < \pi ,
$$

所以 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 单调减少且有下界,故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}$ 存在.

记 $a = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}$ ,由 ${x}_{n + 1} = \sin {x}_{n}$ 得

$$
a = \sin a,
$$

所以 $a = 0$ ,即 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n} = 0$ .

( II ) 因为

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left( \frac{\sin x}{x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\ln \frac{\sin x}{x}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\ln \frac{\sin x}{x}},
$$

而

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\ln \frac{\sin x}{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{2x}\left( {\frac{\cos x}{\sin x} - \frac{1}{x}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x\cos x - \sin x}{2{x}^{3}}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{-x\sin x}{6{x}^{2}} =  - \frac{1}{6}\text{,}
$$

故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left( \frac{\sin x}{x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{6}}$ ,

又由 (I), $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n} = 0$ ,所以

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( \frac{{x}_{n + 1}}{{x}_{n}}\right) }^{\frac{1}{{x}_{n}^{2}}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( \frac{\sin {x}_{n}}{{x}_{n}}\right) }^{\frac{1}{{x}_{n}^{2}}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left( \frac{\sin x}{x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{{x}^{2}}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{6}}.
$$

220. (2002. V) 设 $0 < {x}_{1} < 3,{x}_{n + 1} = \sqrt{{x}_{n}\left( {3 - {x}_{n}}\right) }\left( {n = 1,2,\cdots }\right)$ ,证明数列 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 的极限存在, 并求此极限.

证 由题设 $0 < {x}_{1} < 3$ 知, ${x}_{1}$ 及 $3 - {x}_{1}$ 均为正数,故

$$
0 < {x}_{2} = \sqrt{{x}_{1}\left( {3 - {x}_{1}}\right) } \leq  \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}_{1} + 3 - {x}_{1}}\right)  = \frac{3}{2}.
$$

设当 $k > 1$ 时, $0 < {x}_{k} \leq  \frac{3}{2}$ ,则

$$
0 < {x}_{k + 1} = \sqrt{{x}_{k}\left( {3 - {x}_{k}}\right) } \leq  \frac{1}{2}\left( {{x}_{k} + 3 - {x}_{k}}\right)  = \frac{3}{2},
$$

故由数学归纳法知,对任意正整数 $n > 1$ ,均有

$$
0 < {x}_{n} \leq  \frac{3}{2},
$$

即数列 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 是有界的.

又当 $n > 1$ 时,

$$
{x}_{n + 1} - {x}_{n} = \sqrt{{x}_{n}\left( {3 - {x}_{n}}\right) } - {x}_{n} = \sqrt{{x}_{n}}\left( {\sqrt{3 - {x}_{n}} - \sqrt{{x}_{n}}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{\sqrt{{x}_{n}}\left( {3 - 2{x}_{n}}\right) }{\sqrt{3 - {x}_{n}} + \sqrt{{x}_{n}}} \geq  0\;\left( {\text{ 因 }0 < {x}_{n} \leq  \frac{3}{2}}\right) ,
$$

故当 $n > 1$ 时, ${x}_{n + 1} \geq  {x}_{n}$ ,即数列 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 单调增加.

根据单调有界极限存在准则知 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}$ 存在.

设 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n} = a$ ,由

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n + 1} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\sqrt{{x}_{n}\left( {3 - {x}_{n}}\right) },
$$

得 $a = \sqrt{a\left( {3 - a}\right) }$ ,从而 $2{a}^{2} - {3a} = 0$ . 解得 $a = \frac{3}{2},a = 0$ . 因 $a = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n} \geq  {x}_{2} > 0$ ,故 $a = 0$ 舍去,得 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n} = \frac{3}{2}$ .

例 21. (1999. I ) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\frac{1}{{x}^{2}} - \frac{1}{x\tan x}}\right)  =$ _____.

解法一 利用洛必达法则,

$$
\text{ 原极限 } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sin x - x\cos x}{{x}^{2}\sin x}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sin x}{2\sin x + x\cos x}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\cos x}{3\cos x - x\sin x} = \frac{1}{3}\text{.}
$$

解法二 利用麦克劳林公式,

原极限 $= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sin x - x\cos x}{{x}^{2}\sin x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x - \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + o\left( {x}^{3}\right)  - x + \frac{1}{2}{x}^{3} + o\left( {x}^{3}\right) }{{x}^{3} + o\left( {x}^{3}\right) }$

$= \frac{1}{3}$ .

解法三 利用等价无穷小代换及洛必达法则,

原极限 $= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\tan x - x}{{x}^{2}\tan x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\tan x - x}{{x}^{3}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\sec }^{2}x - 1}{3{x}^{2}}$

$= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\tan }^{2}x}{3{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{x}^{2}}{3{x}^{2}} = \frac{1}{3}$ .

22. (2005. III,IV) 求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\frac{1 + x}{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}} - \frac{1}{x}}\right)$ .

解 当 $x \rightarrow  0$ 时, $1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} \sim  x$ ,并利用洛必达法则得

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\frac{1 + x}{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}} - \frac{1}{x}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x + {x}^{2} - 1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{x\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right) }
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x + {x}^{2} - 1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{{x}^{2}}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 + {2x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{2x}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{2 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{2} = \frac{3}{2}\text{.}
$$

例 23. (2004. II) 设 $f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{\left( {n - 1}\right) x}{n{x}^{2} + 1}$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 的间断点为 $x =$ _____.

解 因为当 $x \neq  0$ 时,

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{\left( {n - 1}\right) x}{n{x}^{2} + 1} = \frac{1}{x},
$$

所以

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{x},x \neq  0, & \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{x} = \infty , \\  0, & x = 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

从而 $f\left( x\right)$ 的间断点为 $x = 0$ .

22. 24.(2005. II)设函数

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{x - 1}} - 1},
$$

则 (   ).

(A) $x = 0,x = 1$ 都是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第一类间断点

(B) $x = 0,x = 1$ 都是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第二类间断点

(C) $x = 0$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第一类间断点, $x = 1$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第二类间断点

(D) $x = 0$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第二类间断点, $x = 1$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第一类间断点

解 因为

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = \infty ,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  = 0,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)  =  - 1,
$$

所以应选 (D).

225.(2002. II)设函数

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{\tan x}}{\arcsin \frac{x}{2}}, & x > 0, \\  a{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}, & x \leq  0 \end{array}\right.
$$

在 $x = 0$ 处连续,则 $a =$ _____.

解

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{\tan x}}{\arcsin \frac{x}{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{-\tan x}{\frac{x}{2}} =  - 2,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}a{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} = a = f\left( 0\right) .
$$

因 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处连续,故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)$ ,从而得 $a =  - 2$ .

226. (1998. II) 求函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\left( 1 + x\right) }^{\frac{x}{\tan \left( {x - \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) }}$ 在区间 $\left( {0,{2\pi }}\right)$ 内的间断点,并判断其类型.

解 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0,{2\pi }}\right)$ 内的间断点为 $x = \frac{\pi }{4},\frac{3\pi }{4},\frac{5\pi }{4},\frac{7\pi }{4}$ .

在 $x = \frac{\pi }{4}$ 处, $f\left( \frac{\pi }{4}\right)  =  + \infty$ ,在 $x = \frac{5}{4}\pi$ 处, $f\left( \frac{5{\pi }^{ + }}{4}\right)  =  + \infty$ ,故 $x = \frac{\pi }{4},\frac{5\pi }{4}$ 为第二类间断点 (无穷间断点);

在 $x = \frac{3\pi }{4}$ 处, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \frac{3\pi }{4}}}f\left( x\right)  = 1$ ,在 $x = \frac{7}{4}\pi$ 处, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \frac{7\pi }{4}}}f\left( x\right)  = 1$ ,故 $x = \frac{3\pi }{4},\frac{7\pi }{4}$ 为第一类间断点 (可去间断点).

227. (2001. II) 求极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  x}}{\left( \frac{\sin t}{\sin x}\right) }^{\frac{x}{\sin t - \sin x}}$ ,记此极限为 $f\left( x\right)$ ,求函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 的间断点并指出其类型.

解 因为

$$
f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  x}}\frac{x}{\sin t - \sin x}\ln \frac{\sin t}{\sin x}},
$$

而

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  x}}\frac{x}{\sin t - \sin x}\ln \frac{\sin t}{\sin x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  x}}x\frac{\cos t/\sin t}{\cos t} = \frac{x}{\sin x},
$$

故 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{\sin x}}$ .

$f\left( x\right)$ 的间断点为 $x = {k\pi }\left( {k \in  \mathbf{Z}}\right)$ .

在 $x = 0$ 处, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{x}{\sin x}} = \mathrm{e}$ ,故 $x = 0$ 是函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第一类间断点 (可去间断点);

在 $x = {k\pi }\left( {k =  \pm  1, \pm  2,\cdots }\right)$ 处, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {k\pi }}}f\left( x\right)  = \infty$ ,故 $x = {k\pi }\left( {k =  \pm  1, \pm  2,\cdots }\right)$ 是函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 的第二类间断点 (无穷间断点).

28.(1992. IV)设函数

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{\ln \cos \left( {x - 1}\right) }{1 - \sin \frac{\pi }{2}x}, & x \neq  1, \\  1, & x = 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

问函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 1$ 处是否连续? 若不连续,修改函数在 $x = 1$ 处的定义,使之连续.

解 因为

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{\ln \cos \left( {x - 1}\right) }{1 - \sin \frac{\pi }{2}x} = \frac{2}{\pi }\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{\tan \left( {x - 1}\right) }{\cos \frac{\pi }{2}x}
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{\pi }\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{{\sec }^{2}\left( {x - 1}\right) }{-\frac{\pi }{2}\sin \frac{\pi }{2}x} =  - \frac{4}{{\pi }^{2}} \neq  f\left( 1\right) ,
$$

所以函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 1$ 处不连续. 若修改定义,令 $f\left( 1\right)  =  - \frac{4}{{\pi }^{2}}$ ,则函数在 $x = 1$ 处连续.

29. 29. (2003. II)设函数

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{\ln \left( {1 + a{x}^{3}}\right) }{x - \arcsin x}, & x < 0, \\  6, & x = 0, \\  \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} + {x}^{2} - {ax} - 1}{x\sin \frac{x}{4}}, & x > 0, \end{array}\right.
$$

问 $a$ 为何值时, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处连续; $a$ 为何值时, $x = 0$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的可去间断点?

解 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\frac{\ln \left( {1 + a{x}^{3}}\right) }{x - \arcsin x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\frac{a{x}^{3}}{x - \arcsin x}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\frac{{3a}{x}^{2}}{1 - \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{{3a}{x}^{2}}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}} - 1} \cdot  \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\frac{6ax}{\frac{-x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}} =  - {6a},
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} + {x}^{2} - {ax} - 1}{x\sin \frac{x}{4}} = 4\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} + {x}^{2} - {ax} - 1}{{x}^{2}}
$$

$$
= 4\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{a{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} + {2x} - a}{2x} = 2\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\left( {{a}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} + 2}\right)
$$

$$
= 2{a}^{2} + 4\text{.}
$$

令 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)$ ,有 $2{a}^{2} + 4 =  - {6a}$ ,得 $a =  - 1$ 或 $a =  - 2$ .

当 $a =  - 1$ 时, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = 6 = f\left( 0\right) ,f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处连续.

当 $a =  - 2$ 时, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = {12} \neq  f\left( 0\right) ,x = 0$ 是 $f\left( x\right)$ 的可去间断点.

## (二) 一元函数微分学

221. (2012. I) 设函数 $y\left( x\right)  = \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}\right) \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 2}\right) \cdots \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{nx} - n}\right)$ ,其中 $n$ 为正整数,则 ${y}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  =$ (   ).

(A) ${\left( -1\right) }^{n - 1}\left( {n - 1}\right)$ ! (B) ${\left( -1\right) }^{n}\left( {n - 1}\right)$ !

(C) ${\left( -1\right) }^{n - 1}n$ ! (D) ${\left( -1\right) }^{n}n$ !

解 因为 ${y}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{y\left( x\right)  - y\left( 0\right) }{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}\right) \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 2}\right) \cdots \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{nx} - n}\right) }{x}$ .

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 2}\right) \cdots \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{nx} - n}\right)  =  - 1 \times  \left( {-2}\right) \cdots \left( {1 - n}\right)
$$

$$
= {\left( -1\right) }^{n - 1}\left( {n - 1}\right) !\text{,}
$$

所以应选 (A).

22. ( 2001. I )设 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在点 $x = 0$ 可导的充要条件为(   ).

(A) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{{h}^{2}}f\left( {1 - \cos h}\right)$ 存在 (B) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{h}f\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{h}}\right)$ 存在

(C) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{{h}^{2}}f\left( {h - \sin h}\right)$ 存在 (D) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{h}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( h\right) }\right\rbrack$ 存在

解 令 $1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{h} = t$ ,则 $h = \ln \left( {1 - t}\right)$ ,当 $h \rightarrow  0$ 时, $t \rightarrow  0$ ,故

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{h}f\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{h}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( t\right) }{\ln \left( {1 - t}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( t\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{t} \cdot  \frac{t}{\ln \left( {1 - t}\right) }
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{t \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( t\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{t} \cdot  \left( {-1}\right) ,
$$

由导数的定义知,应选 (B). 关于其他三个选项的排除,可用反例说明. 取 $f\left( x\right)  =$ $\left| x\right|$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处不可导,但

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{{h}^{2}}f\left( {1 - \cos h}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left| 1 - \cos h\right| }{{h}^{2}} = \frac{1}{2},
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{{h}^{2}}f\left( {h - \sin h}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\left| h - \sin h\right| }{{h}^{2}} = 0,
$$

故排除(A)和(C).

又取 $f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} 1, & x \geq  0, \\  0, & x < 0, \end{array}\right.$ 则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处不连续,从而 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ 不存在. 但

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{1}{h}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( h\right) }\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{1}{h}\left( {1 - 1}\right)  = 0,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\frac{1}{h}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( h\right) }\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}\frac{1}{h}\left( {0 - 0}\right)  = 0.
$$

即 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1}{h}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( h\right) }\right\rbrack$ 存在,故排除 (D).

3. (2002. I ,II)设函数 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内有界可导,则(   ).

(A) 当 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = 0$ 时,必有 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$

(B) 当 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 存在时,必有 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$

(C) 当 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)  = 0$ 时,必有 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$

(D) 当 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 存在时,必有 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$

解 取 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{\sin {x}^{2}}{x}$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内有界可导,且 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,而 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  =$ $2\cos {x}^{2} - \frac{\sin {x}^{2}}{{x}^{2}},\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 不存在,故排除 (A).

取 $f\left( x\right)  = \sin x$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内有界可导,且 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,而 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \cos x$ , $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 1$ ,故排除 (C) 和 (D). 因此,应选 (B).

注 可直接证明 (B) 为正确选项. 设 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = k \neq  0$ ,不妨设 $k > 0$ ,则存在 $M >$ 0,当 $x > M$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > \frac{k}{2}$ . 由 ${\int }_{M}^{x}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x > {\int }_{M}^{x}\frac{k}{2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ 得, $f\left( x\right)  > \frac{k}{2}\left( {x - M}\right)  + f\left( M\right)$ ,与 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内有界矛盾,故选 (B).

24. (1999. II)曲线 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin {2t}, \\  y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\cos t \end{array}\right.$ 在点(0,1)处的法线方程为_____.

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{{y}_{t}^{\prime }}{{x}_{t}^{\prime }} = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\cos t - {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin t}{{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin {2t} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\cos {2t}} = \frac{\cos t - \sin t}{\sin {2t} + 2\cos {2t}}.
$$

点(0,1)对应参数 $t = 0,{\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right| }_{t = 0} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,于是所求法线方程为

$$
y - 1 =  - {2x},
$$

即 ${2x} + y - 1 = 0$ .

25. (2010. I ) 设 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{-t},y = {\int }_{0}^{t}\ln \left( {1 + {u}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}u$ ,则 ${\left. \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}}\right| }_{t = 0} =$ _____.

解

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{\mathrm{d}y/\mathrm{d}t}{\mathrm{\;d}x/\mathrm{d}t} =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\ln \left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right) ,
$$

$\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right) /\mathrm{d}t}{\mathrm{\;d}x/\mathrm{d}t} =  - \left\lbrack  {{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\ln \left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right)  + {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\frac{2t}{1 + {t}^{2}}}\right\rbrack   \cdot  \left( {-{\mathrm{e}}^{t}}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}\left\lbrack  {\ln \left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right)  + \frac{2t}{1 + {t}^{2}}}\right\rbrack  ,$

于是 ${\left. \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}}\right| }_{t = 0} = 0$ .

26. (2004. II) 设函数 $y\left( x\right)$ 由参数方程

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {t}^{3} + {3t} + 1 \\  y = {t}^{3} - {3t} + 1 \end{array}\right.
$$

确定,则曲线 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 向上凸的 $x$ 取值范围为_____.

解 由题设知

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{{t}^{2} - 1}{{t}^{2} + 1},
$$

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)  \cdot  \frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{4t}{3{\left( {t}^{2} + 1\right) }^{3}}.
$$

令 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} < 0$ ,得 $t < 0$ . 代入 $x = {t}^{3} + {3t} + 1$ 并由单调性知 $x < 1$ ,故所求取值范围为 $\left( {-\infty ,1}\right)$ 或 $( - \infty ,1\rbrack$ .

27. (2011. I ) 曲线 $y = \left( {x - 1}\right) {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2}{\left( x - 3\right) }^{3}{\left( x - 4\right) }^{4}$ 的拐点是(   ).

(A)(1,0) (B)(2,0) (C)(3,0) (D)(4,0)

解 由 $y = \left( {x - 1}\right) {\left( x - 2\right) }^{2}{\left( x - 3\right) }^{3}{\left( x - 4\right) }^{4}$ 可知1,2,3,4分别是 $y = \left( {x - 1}\right)$ ${\left( x - 2\right) }^{2}{\left( x - 3\right) }^{3}{\left( x - 4\right) }^{4} = 0$ 的一、二、三、四重根,故由导数与原函数之间的关系可知

$$
{y}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  \neq  0,\;{y}^{\prime }\left( 2\right)  = {y}^{\prime }\left( 3\right)  = {y}^{\prime }\left( 4\right)  = 0,
$$

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime }\left( 2\right)  \neq  0,\;{y}^{\prime \prime }\left( 3\right)  = {y}^{\prime \prime }\left( 4\right)  = 0,\;{y}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( 3\right)  \neq  0,\;{y}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( 4\right)  = 0,
$$

故(3,0)是一拐点.

注 由 ${y}^{\prime \prime }\left( 3\right)  = 0,{y}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( 3\right)  \neq  0$ 得出(3,0)是一拐点,参阅习题 3-4 中第 16 题的解答.

228. (2002. I) 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 的某邻域内具有一阶连续导数,且 $f\left( 0\right)  \neq  0,{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ $\neq  0$ ,若 ${af}\left( h\right)  + {bf}\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( 0\right)$ 在 $h \rightarrow  0$ 时是比 $h$ 高阶的无穷小,试确定 $a,b$ 的值.

解法一 由题设条件知

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {{af}\left( h\right)  + {bf}\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }\right\rbrack   = \left( {a + b - 1}\right) f\left( 0\right)  = 0,
$$

由于 $f\left( 0\right)  \neq  0$ ,故有 $a + b - 1 = 0$ .

又由洛必达法则, 有

$$
0 = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{af}\left( h\right)  + {bf}\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{h} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{a{f}^{\prime }\left( h\right)  + {2b}{f}^{\prime }\left( {2h}\right) }{1} = \left( {a + {2b}}\right) {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) ,
$$

因 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  \neq  0$ ,故有 $a + {2b} = 0$ .

于是,解得 $a = 2,b =  - 1$ .

解法二 由 $f\left( h\right)$ 在 $h = 0$ 处可导,即

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( h\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{h} = {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) ,
$$

于是

$$
\frac{f\left( h\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{h} = {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  + \alpha ,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\alpha  = 0.
$$

从而有

$$
f\left( h\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) h + {o}_{1}\left( h\right) ,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{o}_{1}\left( h\right) }{h} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\alpha  = 0.
$$

同理有

$$
f\left( {2h}\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) {2h} + {o}_{2}\left( h\right) ,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{o}_{2}\left( h\right) }{h} = 0.
$$

所以

$$
{af}\left( h\right)  + {bf}\left( {2h}\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  = \left( {a + b - 1}\right) f\left( 0\right)  + \left( {a + {2b}}\right) {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) h + o\left( h\right) ,
$$

按题设,当 $h \rightarrow  0$ 时上式右端应是 $h$ 的高阶无穷小,从而

$$
\left( {a + b - 1}\right) f\left( 0\right)  = 0,\;\left( {a + {2b}}\right) {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0,
$$

于是 $a + b - 1 = 0,a + {2b} = 0$ ,得 $a = 2,b =  - 1$ .

9. (2011. I ) 求方程 $k\arctan x - x = 0$ 不同实根的个数,其中 $k$ 为参数.

解 令 $f\left( x\right)  = k\arctan x - x$ ,则 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0,{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{k}{1 + {x}^{2}} - 1 = \frac{k - 1 - {x}^{2}}{1 + {x}^{2}}$ .

(1)当 $k \leq  1$ 时,在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  \leq  0$ ,且等号仅当 $k = 1,x = 0$ 时成立,所以 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 上单调减少,又 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内有且仅有一个零点.

(2)当 $k > 1$ 时,在 $\left( {-\sqrt{k - 1},\sqrt{k - 1}}\right)$ 内 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,所以 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack  - \sqrt{k - 1}$ , $\sqrt{k - 1}\rbrack$ 上单调增加,又 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-\sqrt{k - 1},\sqrt{k - 1}}\right\rbrack$ 上有且只有一个零点; 在 $\left( {-\infty , - \sqrt{k - 1}}\right)$ 及 $\left( {\sqrt{k - 1}, + \infty }\right)$ 内均有 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,所以 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $( - \infty$ , $- \sqrt{k - 1}$ ) 及 $\left( {\sqrt{k - 1}, + \infty }\right)$ 内均单调减少,又 $f\left( {-\sqrt{k - 1}}\right)  < f\left( 0\right)  = 0,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   - \infty }}f\left( x\right)  =$ $+ \infty ,f\left( \sqrt{k - 1}\right)  > f\left( 0\right)  = 0,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  =  - \infty$ . 因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , - \sqrt{k - 1}}\right)$ 及 $\left( {\sqrt{k - 1}, + \infty }\right)$ 内各有一个零点.

综上所述, $k \leq  1$ 时,方程 $k\arctan x - x = 0$ 只有一个实根, $k > 1$ 时,方程 $k\arctan x - x$ $= 0$ 有三个实根.

1510. (2002. I ) 已知两曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 与 $y = {\int }_{0}^{\arctan x}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ 在点(0,0)处的切线相同, 写出此切线方程,并求极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{nf}\left( \frac{2}{n}\right)$ .

解 由已知条件得 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = {\left. \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{-{\left( \arctan x\right) }^{2}}}{1 + {x}^{2}}\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,
$$

故所求切线方程为 $y = x$ .

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{nf}\left( \frac{2}{n}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}2\frac{f\left( \frac{2}{n}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{\frac{2}{n}} = 2{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 2.
$$

1211. (1987. I,II) 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在闭区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上可微,对于 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上的每一个 $x$ ,函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 的值都在开区间(0,1)内,且 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  \neq  1$ ,证明在(0,1)内有且仅有一个 $x$ ,使 $f\left( x\right)  = x.$

证 令 $F\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - x$ ,则 $F\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续. 由于 $0 < f\left( x\right)  < 1$ ,所以 $F\left( 0\right)  =$ $f\left( 0\right)  - 0 > 0,F\left( 1\right)  = f\left( 1\right)  - 1 < 0$ ,故由零点定理知,在(0,1)内至少存在一点 $x$ ,使 $F\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - x = 0$ ,即 $f\left( x\right)  = x$ .

5212. (2010. I) 求 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}\left( {{x}^{2} - t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ 的单调区间与极值.

解 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}\left( {{x}^{2} - t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = {x}^{2}{\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t - {\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,

令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {2x}{\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = 0$ ,得 $x =  - 1,x = 0,x = 1$ .

由 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = 2{\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t + 4{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{4}}$ ,因为

$$
{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\pm 1}\right)  = \frac{4}{\mathrm{e}} > 0,\;{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  =  - 2{\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t < 0,
$$

所以 $x =  - 1,x = 1$ 为 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极小值点,极小值为 $f\left( {\pm 1}\right)  = 0;x = 0$ 为 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极大值点,极大值为 $f\left( 0\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{1}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{1}{2}\left( {1 - \frac{1}{\mathrm{e}}}\right)$ .

因此, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $( - \infty , - 1\rbrack$ 及 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上单调减少, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,0}\right\rbrack$ 及 $\lbrack 1, + \infty )$ 上单调增加.

例 13. (2012. I ) 证明: $x\ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - x} + \cos x \geq  1 + \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}\left( {-1 < x < 1}\right)$ .

证 令 $f\left( x\right)  = x\ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - x} + \cos x - 1 - \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}\left( {-1 < x < 1}\right)$ . 因为 $f\left( {-x}\right)  = f\left( x\right)$ ,所以只要讨论当 $x \geq  0$ 时的情形即可. 又

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - x} + x \cdot  \frac{1 - x}{1 + x} \cdot  \frac{1 - x + \left( {1 + x}\right) }{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}} - \sin x - x
$$

$$
= \ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - x} + \frac{2x}{1 - {x}^{2}} - \sin x - x\;\left( {0 \leq  x < 1}\right) ,
$$

$$
{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1 - x}{1 + x} \cdot  \frac{1 - x + 1 + x}{{\left( 1 - x\right) }^{2}} + \frac{2\left( {1 - {x}^{2}}\right)  - {2x}\left( {-{2x}}\right) }{{\left( 1 - {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}} - \cos x - 1
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{1 - {x}^{2}} + \frac{2 + 2{x}^{2}}{{\left( 1 - {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}} - \cos x - 1
$$

$$
= \frac{4}{{\left( 1 - {x}^{2}\right) }^{2}} - \cos x - 1\;\left( {0 \leq  x < 1}\right) ,
$$

$$
{f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{-4 \cdot  2\left( {1 - {x}^{2}}\right) \left( {-{2x}}\right) }{{\left( 1 - {x}^{2}\right) }^{4}} + \sin x = \frac{16x}{{\left( 1 - {x}^{2}\right) }^{3}} + \sin x\;\left( {0 \leq  x < 1}\right) ,
$$

当 $x \in  \left( {0,1}\right)$ 时, ${f}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,从而 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 单调增加, ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = 2 > 0$ ,由此得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 单调增加, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,又得 $f\left( x\right)$ 单调增加, $f\left( x\right)  > f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,因此当 $x \in  \left( {-1,1}\right)$ 时,

$f\left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,即

$$
x\ln \frac{1 + x}{1 - x} + \cos x \geq  1 + \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}\left( {-1 < x < 1}\right) .
$$

24. (2011. I)证明: (1)对任意正整数 $n$ ,都有 $\frac{1}{n + 1} < \ln \left( {1 + \frac{1}{n}}\right)  < \frac{1}{n}$ ；

(2)设 ${a}_{n} = 1 + \frac{1}{2} + \cdots  + \frac{1}{n} - \ln n\left( {n = 1,2,\cdots }\right)$ ,证明数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 收敛.

解 (1) 令 $\frac{1}{n} = x$ ,则原不等式可化为 $\frac{x}{x + 1} < \ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  < x$ .

先证明 $\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  < x\left( {x > 0}\right)$ .

令 $f\left( x\right)  = x - \ln \left( {1 + x}\right)$ . 由于 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 1 - \frac{1}{1 + x} > 0\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,可知 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上单调增加. 又由于 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,因此当 $x > 0$ 时, $f\left( x\right)  > f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,即 $\ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  <$ $x\left( {x > 0}\right)$ .

再证明 $\frac{x}{x + 1} < \ln \left( {1 + x}\right) \left( {x > 0}\right)$ .

令 $g\left( x\right)  = \ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  - \frac{x}{x + 1}$ . 由于 $g\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{1 + x} - \frac{1}{{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{2}} > 0\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,可知 $g\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上单调增加. 由于 $g\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,因此当 $x > 0$ 时, $g\left( x\right)  > g\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,即 $\frac{x}{x + 1} <$ $\ln \left( {1 + x}\right) \left( {x > 0}\right)$ .

因此,我们证明了 $\frac{x}{x + 1} < \ln \left( {1 + x}\right)  < x\left( {x > 0}\right)$ . 再令 $x = \frac{1}{n}$ ,即可得到所需证明的不等式.

(2) ${a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = \frac{1}{n + 1} - \ln \left( {1 + \frac{1}{n}}\right)$ ,由不等式 $\frac{1}{n + 1} < \ln \left( {1 + \frac{1}{n}}\right)$ 可知: 数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 单调减少.

又由不等式 $\ln \left( {1 + \frac{1}{n}}\right)  < \frac{1}{n}$ 可知:

$$
{a}_{n} = 1 + \frac{1}{2} + \cdots  + \frac{1}{n} - \ln n > \ln \left( {1 + 1}\right)  + \ln \left( {1 + \frac{1}{2}}\right)  + \cdots  + \ln \left( {1 + \frac{1}{n}}\right)  - \ln n
$$

$$
= \ln \left( {n + 1}\right)  - \ln n > 0\text{.}
$$

因此数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 是有界的. 故由单调有界收敛准则可知,数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 收敛.

25. 15. (2007. I ) 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 上具有二阶导数,且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ . 令 ${u}_{n} = f\left( n\right)$ $\left( {n = 1,2,\cdots }\right)$ ,则下列结论正确的是 (   ).

(A) 若 ${u}_{1} > {u}_{2}$ ,则 $\left\{  {u}_{n}\right\}$ 必收敛 (B) 若 ${u}_{1} > {u}_{2}$ ,则 $\left\{  {u}_{n}\right\}$ 必发散

(C) 若 ${u}_{1} < {u}_{2}$ ,则 $\left\{  {u}_{n}\right\}$ 必收敛 (D) 若 ${u}_{1} < {u}_{2}$ ,则 $\left\{  {u}_{n}\right\}$ 必发散

解 设 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{2}$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 上具有二阶导数,且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0,{u}_{1} < {u}_{2}$ ,但 $\left\{  {u}_{n}\right\}   = \left\{  {n}^{2}\right\}$ 发散,故排除(C); 设 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x}$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 上具有二阶导数,且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0,{u}_{1} > {u}_{2}$ ,但 $\left\{  {u}_{n}\right\}   = \left\{  \frac{1}{n}\right\}$ 收敛,故排除 (B); 又设 $f\left( x\right)  =  - \ln x$ ,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $(0$ , $+ \infty )$ 上具有二阶导数,且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0,{u}_{1} > {u}_{2}$ ,但 $\left\{  {u}_{n}\right\}   = \left\{  {-\ln n}\right\}$ 发散,故排除 (A). 因此, 应选 (D).

注 也可直接证明 (D) 为正确选项. 若 ${u}_{1} < {u}_{2}$ ,则存在 $k > 0$ ,使得 ${u}_{2} - {u}_{1} > k > 0$ . 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack$ 上应用拉格朗日中值定理,存在 ${\xi }_{1} \in  \left( {1,2}\right)$ 使得

$$
\frac{{u}_{2} - {u}_{1}}{2 - 1} = \frac{f\left( 2\right)  - f\left( 1\right) }{2 - 1} = {f}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{1}\right)  > k > 0,
$$

又因为在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 上 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,因此 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {{\xi }_{1}, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调增加,于是对任意 $x \in  \left( {{\xi }_{1}, + \infty }\right)$ 有

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > {f}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{1}\right)  > k > 0.
$$

在区间 $\left\lbrack  {{\xi }_{1},x}\right\rbrack$ 上应用拉格朗日中值定理,存在 ${\xi }_{2} \in  \left( {{\xi }_{1},x}\right)$ ,使得

$$
\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {\xi }_{1}\right) }{x - {\xi }_{1}} = {f}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{2}\right)  > k > 0,
$$

即 $f\left( x\right)  = f\left( {\xi }_{1}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{2}\right) \left( {x - {\xi }_{1}}\right)  \rightarrow   + \infty \left( {x \rightarrow   + \infty }\right)$ ,故应选 (D).

2516. (2007. I,III)设函数 $f\left( x\right) ,g\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(a,b)内具有二阶导数且存在相等的最大值, $f\left( a\right)  = g\left( a\right) ,f\left( b\right)  = g\left( b\right)$ ,证明: 存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使得 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  =$ ${g}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)$ .

分析 需要证明的结论与导数有关, 自然联想到用微分中值定理, 事实上, 若令 $F\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - g\left( x\right)$ ,则问题转化为证明 ${F}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,只需对 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 用罗尔定理,关键是找到 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 的端点函数值相等的区间 (特别是两个一阶导数同时为零的点),而利用 $F\left( a\right)  = F\left( b\right)  = 0$ ,若能再找一点 $c \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使得 $F\left( c\right)  = 0$ , 则在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,c}\right\rbrack  ,\left\lbrack  {c,b}\right\rbrack$ 上两次利用罗尔定理有一阶导函数相等的两点,再对 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 用罗尔定理即可.

证 构造辅助函数 $F\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - g\left( x\right)$ ,由题设有 $F\left( a\right)  = F\left( b\right)  = 0$ . 又 $f\left( x\right)$ , $g\left( x\right)$ 在(a,b)内具有相等的最大值,不妨设存在 ${x}_{1} \leq  {x}_{2},{x}_{1},{x}_{2} \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使得

$$
f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = M = \mathop{\max }\limits_{\left\lbrack  a,b\right\rbrack  }f\left( x\right) ,\;g\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = M = \mathop{\max }\limits_{\left\lbrack  a,b\right\rbrack  }g\left( x\right) .
$$

若 ${x}_{1} = {x}_{2}$ ,令 $c = {x}_{1}$ ,则 $F\left( c\right)  = 0$ .

若 ${x}_{1} < {x}_{2}$ ,因 $F\left( {x}_{1}\right)  = f\left( {x}_{1}\right)  - g\left( {x}_{1}\right)  \geq  0,F\left( {x}_{2}\right)  = f\left( {x}_{2}\right)  - g\left( {x}_{2}\right)  \leq  0$ ,从而存在 $c \in  \left\lbrack  {{x}_{1},{x}_{2}}\right\rbrack   \subset  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使 $F\left( c\right)  = 0$ .

在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,c}\right\rbrack  ,\left\lbrack  {c,b}\right\rbrack$ 上分别利用罗尔定理知,存在 ${\xi }_{1} \in  \left( {a,c}\right) ,{\xi }_{2} \in  \left( {c,b}\right)$ , 使得

$$
{F}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{1}\right)  = {F}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{2}\right)  = 0.
$$

再对 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {{\xi }_{1},{\xi }_{2}}\right\rbrack$ 上应用罗尔定理,知存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {{\xi }_{1},{\xi }_{2}}\right)  \subset  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,有

$$
{F}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0,
$$

即 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  = {g}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)$ .

27. (2009. I , III )

(I) 证明拉格朗日中值定理: 若函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在(a,b)内可导,则存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使得 $f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left( {b - a}\right)$ ;

(II) 证明: 若函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处连续,在 $\left( {0,\delta }\right) \left( {\delta  > 0}\right)$ 内可导,且 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  =$ $A$ ,则 ${f}_{ + }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ 存在,且 ${f}_{ + }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = A$ .

证 (I) 作辅助函数 $\varphi \left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - f\left( a\right)  - \frac{f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right) }{b - a}\left( {x - a}\right)$ ,易验证 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ 满足: $\varphi \left( a\right)  = \varphi \left( b\right) ;\varphi \left( x\right)$ 在闭区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在开区间(a,b)内可导,且 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ $= {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - \frac{f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right) }{b - a}.$

根据罗尔定理,可得在(a,b)内至少有一点 $\xi$ ,使 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,即

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  - \frac{f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right) }{b - a} = 0,
$$

所以, $f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left( {b - a}\right)$ .

(II) 任取 ${x}_{0} \in  \left( {0,\delta }\right)$ ,则函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 满足: 在闭区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,{x}_{0}}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,在开区间 $\left( {0,{x}_{0}}\right)$ 内可导,从而由拉格朗日中值定理可得,存在 ${\xi }_{{x}_{0}} \in  \left( {0,{x}_{0}}\right)  \subset  \left( {0,\delta }\right)$ ,使得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{{x}_{0}}\right)  =$ $\frac{f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{{x}_{0} - 0}.$

又由于 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = A$ ,对上式两边取 ${x}_{0} \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }$ 时的极限可得,

$$
{f}_{ + }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{x}_{0} \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}\frac{f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{{x}_{0} - 0} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{x}_{0} \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{{x}_{0}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{\xi }_{{x}_{0}} \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{f}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{{x}_{0}}\right)  = A,
$$

故 ${f}_{ + }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ 存在,且 ${f}_{ + }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = A$ .

2518. (1996. III) 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上具有二阶导数,且 $f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right)  = 0$ , ${f}^{\prime }\left( a\right) {f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  > 0$ ,证明存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ 和 $\eta  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ 及 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right)  = 0$ .

证 先证明存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ . 用反证法.

若不存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ ,则在(a,b)内恒有 $f\left( x\right)  > 0$ (或 $f\left( x\right)  < 0$ ),不妨设 $f\left( x\right)  > 0$ (对 $f\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,类似可证),则

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( a\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {a}^{ + }}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( a\right) }{x - a} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {a}^{ + }}}\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x - a} \geq  0,
$$

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {b}^{ - }}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( b\right) }{x - b} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {b}^{ - }}}\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x - b} \leq  0.
$$

从而 ${f}^{\prime }\left( a\right) {f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  \leq  0$ ,与已知条件矛盾,所以在(a,b)内至少存在一点 $\xi$ , 使 $f\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ .

再证存在 $\eta  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,使 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right)  = 0$ .

由 $f\left( a\right)  = f\left( b\right)  = f\left( \xi \right)$ 及罗尔定理知,存在 ${\eta }_{1} \in  \left( {a,\xi }\right)$ 和 ${\eta }_{2} \in  \left( {\xi ,b}\right)$ ,使 ${f}^{\prime }\left( {\eta }_{1}\right)  =$ ${f}^{\prime }\left( {\eta }_{2}\right)  = 0$ ,再在 $\left\lbrack  {{\eta }_{1},{\eta }_{2}}\right\rbrack$ 上对函数 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 运用罗尔定理,知存在 $\eta  \in  \left( {{\eta }_{1},{\eta }_{2}}\right)  \subset  \left( {a,b}\right)$ , 使 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right)  = 0$ .

1919. 19. (2001. I)设 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 在(-1,1)内具有二阶连续导数且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  \neq  0$ ,试证：

(1)对于(-1,1)内的任一 $x \neq  0$ ,存在惟一的 $\theta \left( x\right)  \in  \left( {0,1}\right)$ ,使 $f\left( x\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  +$ $x{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right)$ 成立;

(2) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\theta \left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2}$ .

证法一 (1) 任给非零 $x \in  \left( {-1,1}\right)$ ,由拉格朗日中值定理得

$$
f\left( x\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  + x{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right) \;\left( {0 < \theta \left( x\right)  < 1}\right) .
$$

因为 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 在(-1,1)内连续且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  \neq  0$ ,所以 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 在(-1,1)内不变号,不妨设 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在(-1,1)内严格单增,故 $\theta \left( x\right)$ 惟一.

(2)由泰勒公式得

$$
f\left( x\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x + \frac{1}{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) {x}^{2},
$$

$\xi$ 在 0 与 $x$ 之间. 所以

$$
x{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right)  = f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x + \frac{1}{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) {x}^{2},
$$

从而

$$
\theta \left( x\right) \frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) }{\theta \left( x\right) x} = \frac{1}{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) .
$$

由于

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) }{\theta \left( x\right) x} = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right) ,\;\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{\xi  \rightarrow  0}}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right) ,
$$

故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\theta \left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2}$ .

证法二 (1) 同证法一(1).

(2)对于非零 $x \in  \left( {-1,1}\right)$ ,由拉格朗日中值定理得

$$
f\left( x\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  + x{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right) \;\left( {0 < \theta \left( x\right)  < 1}\right) ,
$$

所以

$$
\frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) }{x} = \frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x}{{x}^{2}}.
$$

由于

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {\theta \left( x\right) x}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) }{\theta \left( x\right) x} = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right) ,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x}{{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) }{2x} = \frac{1}{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right) ,
$$

故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\theta \left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2}$ .

20. (2005. III ,IV)以下四个命题中,正确的是(   ).

(A) 若 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内连续,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界

(B) 若 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内连续,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界

(C) 若 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界,则 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界

(D) 若 $f\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界

解 若 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界,则存在常数 $M > 0$ ,对任意 $x \in  \left( {0,1}\right) ,\left| {{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) }\right|  \leq$ $M$ . 又当 $x \in  \left( {0,1}\right)$ 时,由拉格朗日中值定理,有

$$
f\left( x\right)  - f\left( \frac{1}{2}\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left( {x - \frac{1}{2}}\right) ,
$$

其中 $\xi$ 介于 $x$ 与 $\frac{1}{2}$ 之间,于是有

$$
\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|  \leq  \left| {f\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }\right|  + M\left| {x - \frac{1}{2}}\right|  < \left| {f\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }\right|  + \frac{1}{2}M,
$$

故应选 (C).

注 本题也可以用排除法. 对选项 (A)、(B),取 $f\left( x\right)  = \ln x$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x},\ln x$ 与 $\frac{1}{x}$ 均在(0,1)内连续,但 $\ln x$ 在(0,1)内无界,故 $\left( \mathrm{A}\right) \text{、}\left( \mathrm{B}\right)$ 均不正确; 对选项(D), 取 $f\left( x\right)  = \sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}},f\left( x\right)$ 在(0,1)内有界,但 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  =  - \frac{x}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}$ 在(0,1)内无界,故(D) 不正确.

2. 21. ( 2001. II )设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack  \left( {a > 0}\right)$ 上具有二阶连续导数, $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ .

(1)写出 $f\left( x\right)$ 的带拉格朗日余项的一阶麦克劳林公式；

(2)证明在 $\left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ 上至少存在一点 $\eta$ ,使

$$
{a}^{3}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right)  = 3{\int }_{-a}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x.
$$

解 (1) 对任意 $x \in  \left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ ,

$$
f\left( x\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x + \frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) }{2!}{x}^{2} = {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x + \frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) }{2!}{x}^{2},
$$

其中 $\xi$ 在 0 与 $x$ 之间.

(2) ${\int }_{-a}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{-a}^{a}{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x\mathrm{\;d}x + {\int }_{-a}^{a}\frac{{x}^{2}}{2!}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-a}^{a}{x}^{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

因为 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,故对任意的 $x \in  \left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ ,有 $m \leq  {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  \leq  M$ ,其中 $M,m$ 分别为 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ 上的最大、最小值,所以有

$$
m{\int }_{0}^{a}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x \leq  {\int }_{-a}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-a}^{a}{x}^{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  M{\int }_{0}^{a}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

即

$$
m \leq  \frac{3}{{a}^{3}}{\int }_{-a}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  M.
$$

因而由 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 的连续性知,至少存在一点 $\eta  \in  \left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ ,使

$$
{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right)  = \frac{3}{{a}^{3}}{\int }_{-a}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x,
$$

即 ${a}^{3}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right)  = 3{\int }_{-a}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

下面我们给出 (2) 的另一种证法.

令 $F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{-x}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ . 因为 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ 上有二阶连续导数,所以 $F\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ 上有三阶连续导数,且

$$
F\left( 0\right)  = 0,\;{F}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0,\;{F}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0.
$$

由泰勒公式知,存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {-a,a}\right)$ ,使得

$$
F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{-x}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{3!}{F}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) {x}^{3},\;\xi  \in  \left( {-a,a}\right) .
$$

由 ${F}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  + {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {-x}\right)$ ,故有

$$
{\int }_{-x}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{3!}\left\lbrack  {{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  + {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {-\xi }\right) }\right\rbrack  {x}^{3},\;\xi  \in  \left( {-a,a}\right) .
$$

又因为 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 连续,所以在 $\xi$ 与 $- \xi$ 之间存在 $\eta$ ,使得 $\frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  + {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {-\xi }\right) }{2} = {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right)$ ,从而

$$
{\int }_{-x}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{3}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right) {x}^{3},\;\eta  \in  \left( {-a,a}\right) .
$$

在上式中令 $x = a$ 即得所证. (按此证法, $\eta$ 可在开区间(-a,a)内取得,比原题结论更精确. )

22. (2006. I ) 设函数 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 具有二阶导数,且 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0,{\Delta x}$ 为自变量 $x$ 在点 ${x}_{0}$ 处的增量, ${\Delta y}$ 与 $\mathrm{d}y$ 分别为 $f\left( x\right)$ 在点 ${x}_{0}$ 处对应的增量与微分,若 ${\Delta x} > 0$ ,则 (   ).

(A) $0 < \mathrm{d}y < {\Delta y}$ (B) $0 < {\Delta y} < \mathrm{d}y$

(C) ${\Delta y} < \mathrm{d}y < 0$ (D) $\mathrm{d}y < {\Delta y} < 0$

解 由一阶泰勒公式

$$
f\left( {{x}_{0} + {\Delta x}}\right)  = f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) {\Delta x} + \frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) }{2!}{\left( \Delta x\right) }^{2},
$$

其中 $\xi$ 介于 ${x}_{0}$ 与 ${x}_{0} + {\Delta x}$ 之间,及已知条件知 $\mathrm{d}y = {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) {\Delta x} > 0,{\Delta y} - \mathrm{d}y =$ $\frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \xi \right) }{2!}{\left( \Delta x\right) }^{2} > 0$ ,故应选 (A).

223. (1990. III) 证明当 $x > 0$ 时,有不等式

$$
\arctan x + \frac{1}{x} > \frac{\pi }{2}.
$$

证 设 $f\left( x\right)  = \arctan x + \frac{1}{x} - \frac{\pi }{2}\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,则

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{1 + {x}^{2}} - \frac{1}{{x}^{2}} < 0,
$$

故函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内单调减少. 又 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,于是

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \arctan x + \frac{1}{x} - \frac{\pi }{2} > 0\;\left( {x > 0}\right) ,
$$

即 $\arctan x + \frac{1}{x} > \frac{\pi }{2}\;\left( {x > 0}\right)$ .

22. 24. (1999. I )试证：当 $x > 0$ 时,

$$
\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x \geq  {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}.
$$

证法一 令 $\varphi \left( x\right)  = \left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x - {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,易知 $\varphi \left( 1\right)  = 0$ . 由于

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {2x}\ln x - x + 2 - \frac{1}{x},{\varphi }^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  = 0,
$$

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = 2\ln x + 1 + \frac{1}{{x}^{2}},
$$

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{2\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) }{{x}^{3}},
$$

故当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, ${\varphi }^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ; 当 $1 < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${\varphi }^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,从而 ${\varphi }^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 1$ 处取得最小值,而 ${\varphi }^{\prime \prime }\left( 1\right)  = 2 > 0$ ,故当 $x \in  \left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 时, ${\varphi }^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,从而 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内单调增加.

又 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,故当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ; 当 $1 < x <  + \infty$ 时, ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ . 从而 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 1$ 处取得最小值,而 $\varphi \left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,故 $\varphi \left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,即当 $x > 0$ 时, $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x \geq  {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}.$

证法二 令 $\varphi \left( x\right)  = \ln x - \frac{x - 1}{x + 1}\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,则

$$
{\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x} - \frac{2}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}} = \frac{{x}^{2} + 1}{x{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}} > 0\;\left( {x > 0}\right) ,
$$

从而 $\varphi \left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内单调增加,而 $\varphi \left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,所以当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, $\varphi \left( x\right)  < 0$ ; 当 $1 < x <  + \infty$ 时, $\varphi \left( x\right)  > 0$ . 于是当 $x > 0$ 时,

$$
\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \varphi \left( x\right)  = \left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x - {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2} \geq  0,
$$

即 $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x \geq  {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}$ .

进一步,我们还可以证明: 当 $x > 0$ 时, $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x \geq  2{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}$ .

事实上,令 $\varphi \left( x\right)  = \ln x - \frac{2\left( {x - 1}\right) }{x + 1}$ ,则 $\varphi \left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,且 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}}{x{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}} > 0$ , $x \neq  1$ . 所以当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, $\varphi \left( x\right)  < 0$ ; 当 $1 < x <  + \infty$ 时, $\varphi \left( x\right)  > 0$ . 故当 $x > 0$ 时, $\left( {x - 1}\right) \varphi \left( x\right)  \geq  0$ ,即有 $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x \geq  2{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}$ .

25. 25. ( 2005. III ,IV )设 $f\left( x\right)  = x\sin x + \cos x$ ,下列命题中正确的是(   ).

(A) $f\left( 0\right)$ 是极大值, $f\left( \frac{\pi }{2}\right)$ 是极小值

(B) $f\left( 0\right)$ 是极小值, $f\left( \frac{\pi }{2}\right)$ 是极大值

(C) $f\left( 0\right)$ 是极大值, $f\left( \frac{\pi }{2}\right)$ 也是极大值

(D) $f\left( 0\right)$ 是极小值, $f\left( \frac{\pi }{2}\right)$ 也是极小值

解 由于 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \sin x + x\cos x - \sin x = x\cos x,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \cos x - x\sin x,{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  =$ ${f}^{\prime }\left( \frac{\pi }{2}\right)  = 0,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = 1 > 0,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \frac{\pi }{2}\right)  =  - \frac{\pi }{2} < 0$ ,故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处取得极小值,在 $x = \frac{\pi }{2}$ 处取得极大值,应选 (B).

26. (2001. II) 设 $\rho  = \rho \left( x\right)$ 是抛物线 $y = \sqrt{x}$ 上任一点 $M\left( {x,y}\right) \left( {x \geq  1}\right)$ 处的曲率半径, $s =$ $s\left( x\right)$ 是该抛物线上介于点 $A\left( {1,1}\right)$ 与 $M$ 之间的弧长,计算 ${3\rho }\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}\rho }{\mathrm{d}{s}^{2}} -$

${\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{\mathrm{d}s}\right) }^{2}$ 的值. (在直角坐标系下曲率公式为 $K = \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}$ .

解 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2\sqrt{x}},{y}^{\prime \prime } =  - \frac{1}{4\sqrt{{x}^{3}}}$ ,所以抛物线在点 $M\left( {x,y}\right)$ 处的曲率半径

$$
\rho  = \rho \left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{K} = \frac{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}}{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| } = \frac{1}{2}{\left( 4x + 1\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}},
$$

抛物线上 $\overset{⏜}{AM}$ 的弧长

$$
s = s\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{1}^{x}\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{1}^{x}\sqrt{1 + \frac{1}{4x}}\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

由参数方程求导公式得

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{\mathrm{d}s} = \frac{\frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{\mathrm{d}x}}{\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}x}} = \frac{\frac{1}{2} \cdot  \frac{3}{2}{\left( 4x + 1\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}} \cdot  4}{\sqrt{1 + \frac{1}{4x}}} = 6\sqrt{x},
$$

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}\rho }{\mathrm{d}{s}^{2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{\mathrm{d}s}\right) \frac{1}{\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}x}} = \frac{6}{2\sqrt{x}} \cdot  \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 + \frac{1}{4x}}} = \frac{6}{\sqrt{{4x} + 1}},
$$

从而

$$
{3\rho }\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}\rho }{\mathrm{d}{s}^{2}} - {\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{\mathrm{d}s}\right) }^{2} = \frac{3}{2}{\left( 4x + 1\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}} \cdot  \frac{6}{\sqrt{{4x} + 1}} - {36x} = 9.
$$

27. (1990. III) 在椭圆 $\frac{{x}^{2}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{{y}^{2}}{{b}^{2}} = 1$ 的第一象限部分上求一点 $P$ ,使该点处的切线、椭圆及两坐标轴所围图形的面积为最小 (其中 $a > 0,b > 0$ ).

解 设所求点为 $P\left( {{x}_{0},{y}_{0}}\right)$ ,则该点处的切线方程为

$$
\frac{x{x}_{0}}{{a}^{2}} + \frac{y{y}_{0}}{{b}^{2}} = 1,
$$

图形面积为

$$
S = \frac{{a}^{2}{b}^{2}}{2{x}_{0}{y}_{0}} - \frac{1}{4}{\pi ab},\;{x}_{0} \in  \left( {0,a}\right) .
$$

设 $A = {x}_{0}{y}_{0} = \frac{b}{a}{x}_{0}\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}_{0}^{2}}$ ,则

$$
{A}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = \frac{b}{a}\left( {\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}_{0}^{2}} - \frac{{x}_{0}^{2}}{\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}_{0}^{2}}}}\right)  = \frac{b\left( {{a}^{2} - 2{x}_{0}^{2}}\right) }{a\sqrt{{a}^{2} - {x}_{0}^{2}}}.
$$

由 ${A}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 0$ ,得 ${x}_{0} = \frac{a}{\sqrt{2}}$ ,易知 $\frac{a}{\sqrt{2}}$ 为 $A$ 的极大值点,即 $S$ 的极小值点,也是 $S$ 的最小值点,此时, ${y}_{0} = \frac{b}{\sqrt{2}}$ . 故所求点为 $P\left( {\frac{a}{\sqrt{2}},\frac{b}{\sqrt{2}}}\right)$ 时,所围图形面积最小.

28. (1993. III) 作半径为 $r$ 的球的外切正圆锥,问此圆锥的高 $h$ 为何值时,其体积最小, 并求出该最小值.

解 设圆锥的底面圆半径为 $R$ (见图研 $2 - 1$ ),则有

$$
{Rh} = \left( {R + \sqrt{{R}^{2} + {h}^{2}}}\right) r,
$$

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_353.jpg?x=606&y=1341&w=391&h=454&r=0"/>

图研 2-1

<!-- Media -->

解得

$$
R = \frac{rh}{\sqrt{{h}^{2} - {2hr}}},
$$

于是圆锥的体积为

$$
V\left( h\right)  = \frac{\pi }{3}{R}^{2}h = \frac{\pi {r}^{2}}{3}\frac{{h}^{2}}{h - {2r}},\;{2r} < h <  + \infty .
$$

由

$$
{V}^{\prime }\left( h\right)  = \frac{\pi {r}^{2}}{3}\frac{{h}^{2} - {4rh}}{{\left( h - 2r\right) }^{2}}
$$

可得 $V\left( h\right)$ 在 $\left( {{2r}, + \infty }\right)$ 内的惟一驻点 $h = {4r}$ ,当 $h = {4r}$ 时, $V$ 取最小值, $V\left( {4r}\right)  = \frac{{8\pi }{r}^{3}}{3}$ .

229. (1994. III) 设 $y = \frac{{x}^{3} + 4}{{x}^{2}}$ ,求

(1)函数的增减区间及极值；(2)函数图像的凹凸区间及拐点；

(3)渐近线; (4)作出其图形.

解 定义域 $\left( {-\infty ,0}\right)  \cup  \left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ . 当 $x =  - \sqrt[3]{4}$ 时, $y = 0$ .

(1)设 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{{x}^{3} + 4}{{x}^{2}}$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 1 - \frac{8}{{x}^{3}}$ ,故驻点为 $x = 2$ . 又

<!-- Media -->

<table><tr><td>$x$</td><td>$\left( {-\infty ,0}\right)$</td><td>(0,2)</td><td>2</td><td>$\left( {2, + \infty }\right)$</td></tr><tr><td>${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$</td><td>+</td><td>-</td><td>0</td><td>+</td></tr><tr><td>$y = f\left( x\right)$ 的图形</td><td> <img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_354.jpg?x=538&y=1089&w=83&h=71&r=0"/> </td><td> <img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_354.jpg?x=765&y=1085&w=80&h=77&r=0"/> </td><td>(2,3)</td><td>9</td></tr></table>

<!-- Media -->

所以, $\left( {-\infty ,0}\right)$ 及 $\left( {2, + \infty }\right)$ 为增区间,(0,2)为减区间, $x = 2$ 为极小值点,极小值为 $f\left( 2\right)  = 3$ .

(2) ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{24}{{x}^{4}} > 0$ ,故 $\left( {-\infty ,0}\right) ,\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 均为凹区间,图像无拐点.

(3) 因

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{x}^{3} + 4}{{x}^{2}} =  + \infty ,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{x}^{3} + 4}{{x}^{3}} = 1 = a,
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\left\lbrack  {f\left( x\right)  - {ax}}\right\rbrack   = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {\frac{{x}^{3} + 4}{{x}^{2}} - x}\right)  = 0 = b,
$$

所以, $x = 0$ 为铅直渐近线, $y = x$ 为斜渐近线.

(4)图形见图研 2-2.

250. (1993. V) 已知某厂生产 $x$ 件产品的成本为

$$
C = {25000} + {200x} + \frac{1}{40}{x}^{2}\text{(元),}
$$

问: (1) 要使平均成本最小, 应生产多少件产品?

(2)若产品以每件 500 元售出,要使利润最大,应生产多少件产品？

解 (1) 设平均成本为 $y$ ,则

$$
y = \frac{25000}{x} + {200} + \frac{x}{40}.
$$

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_355.jpg?x=574&y=259&w=469&h=463&r=0"/>

图研 2-2

<!-- Media -->

由 ${y}^{\prime } =  - \frac{25000}{{x}^{2}} + \frac{1}{40} = 0$ ,得 ${x}_{1} = {1000},{x}_{2} =  - {1000}$ (舍去). 因为 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = {1000}} = 5$ . ${10}^{-5} > 0$ ,所以当 $x = {10}^{3}$ 时, $y$ 取得极小值,也是最小值,因此,要使平均成本最小,应生产 1000 件产品.

(2)利润函数为

$$
L = {500x} - \left( {{25000} + {200x} + \frac{{x}^{2}}{40}}\right)  = {300x} - \frac{{x}^{2}}{40} - {25000},
$$

由 ${L}^{\prime } = {300} - \frac{x}{20} = 0$ ,得 $x = {6000}$ . 因 ${\left. {L}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = {6000}} =  - \frac{1}{20} < 0$ ,所以当 $x = {6000}$ 时, $L$ 取得极大值, 也是最大值, 因此, 要使利润最大, 应生产 6000 件产品.

## (三)一元函数积分学

21. (2006. II) 设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{{x}^{3}}{\int }_{0}^{x}\sin {t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t, & x \neq  0, \\  a, & x = 0 \end{array}\right.$ 在 $x = 0$ 处连续,则 $a =$ _____.

解 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}\sin {t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t}{{x}^{3}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sin {x}^{2}}{3{x}^{2}} = \frac{1}{3}$ ,

因此, $a = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{3}$ .

2. (1999. II) 设 $\alpha \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{5x}\frac{\sin t}{t}\mathrm{\;d}t,\beta \left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{\sin x}{\left( 1 + t\right) }^{\frac{1}{t}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,则当 $x \rightarrow  0$ 时, $\alpha \left( x\right)$ 是 $\beta \left( x\right)$ 的 (   ).

(A) 高阶无穷小 (B) 低阶无穷小

(C) 同阶但不等价的无穷小 (D) 等价无穷小

解 由于

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\alpha \left( x\right) }{\beta \left( x\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{5x}\frac{\sin t}{t}\mathrm{\;d}t}{{\int }_{0}^{\sin x}{\left( 1 + t\right) }^{\frac{1}{t}}\mathrm{\;d}t} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{5 \cdot  \frac{\sin {5x}}{5x}}{\cos x \cdot  {\left( 1 + \sin x\right) }^{\frac{1}{\sin x}}} = \frac{5}{\mathrm{e}},
$$

故选 (C).

2. 3. (2006. II) 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 是奇函数,除 $x = 0$ 外处处连续, $x = 0$ 是其第一类间断点,则 ${\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 是 (   ).

(A) 连续的奇函数 (B) 连续的偶函数

(C) 在 $x = 0$ 间断的奇函数 (D) 在 $x = 0$ 间断的偶函数

解 对于任意的 ${x}_{0}$ ,存在 $a > 0$ ,使得 ${x}_{0} \in  \left( {-a,a}\right)$ ,由条件可知 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ 上有界,设 $\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|  < {M}_{a}\left( {x \in  \left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack  }\right)$ ,记 $F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,当 ${x}_{0} + {\Delta x} \in  \left\lbrack  {-a,a}\right\rbrack$ 时, 有

$$
\left| {F\left( {{x}_{0} + {\Delta x}}\right)  - F\left( {x}_{0}\right) }\right|  = \left| {{\int }_{{x}_{0}}^{{x}_{0} + {\Delta x}}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}\right|  < {M}_{a}\left| {\Delta x}\right| ,
$$

故 ${\Delta x} \rightarrow  0$ 时, $F\left( {{x}_{0} + {\Delta x}}\right)  - F\left( {x}_{0}\right)  \rightarrow  0$ ,即 $F\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 处连续. 又

$$
F\left( {-x}\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{-x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t =  - u{\int }_{0}^{x} - f\left( {-u}\right) \mathrm{d}u = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u = F\left( x\right) ,
$$

所以 $F\left( x\right)$ 是连续的偶函数,故选 (B).

24. (1993. I ,II) 求 $\int \frac{x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{\sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

解 令 $u = \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}$ ,即 $x = \ln \left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right)$ ,因此有

$$
\int \frac{x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{\sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int 2\ln \left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}u = {2u}\ln \left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right)  - 2\int \frac{2{u}^{2}}{{u}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= {2u}\ln \left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right)  - {4u} + 4\arctan u + C
$$

$$
= {2x}\sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1} - 4\sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1} + 4\arctan \sqrt{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1} + C\text{.}
$$

例 5. (1994. I,II,III) 求 $\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin \left( {2x}\right)  + 2\sin x}$ .

解法一

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin \left( {2x}\right)  + 2\sin x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2\sin x\left( {\cos x + 1}\right) } = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\cos x}\right) }{2\left( {{\cos }^{2}x - 1}\right) \left( {\cos x + 1}\right) }
$$

$$
\overset{u = \cos x}{ = }\int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{2\left( {{u}^{2} - 1}\right) \left( {u + 1}\right) }
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{8}\int \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{1 - u} + \frac{1}{1 + u} + \frac{2}{{\left( 1 + u\right) }^{2}}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{8}\left\lbrack  {-\ln \left( {1 - u}\right)  + \ln \left( {1 + u}\right)  - \frac{2}{1 + u}}\right\rbrack   + C
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{8}\ln \frac{1 + \cos x}{1 - \cos x} + \frac{1}{4\left( {1 + \cos x}\right) } + C.
$$

解法二

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sin \left( {2x}\right)  + 2\sin x} = \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2\sin x\left( {\cos x + 1}\right) } = \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( \frac{x}{2}\right) }{\sin \frac{x}{2}{\cos }^{3}\frac{x}{2}}
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\left( {\tan \frac{x}{2}}\right) }{\tan \frac{x}{2}{\cos }^{2}\frac{x}{2}}
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{4}\int \frac{1 + {\tan }^{2}\frac{x}{2}}{\tan \frac{x}{2}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\tan \frac{x}{2}}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{8}{\tan }^{2}\frac{x}{2} + \frac{1}{4}\ln \left| {\tan \frac{x}{2}}\right|  + C.
$$

126. (1989. III) 已知 $f\left( 2\right)  = \frac{1}{2},{f}^{\prime }\left( 2\right)  = 0$ 及 ${\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = 1$ ,求 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {2x}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

解 令 $t = {2x}$ ,则

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}{x}^{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {2x}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{8}{\int }_{0}^{2}{t}^{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{8}{\int }_{0}^{2}{t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\left\lbrack  {{f}^{\prime }\left( t\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{8}{\left\lbrack  {t}^{2}{f}^{\prime }\left( t\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{2} - \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{2}t{f}^{\prime }\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{2}t\mathrm{\;d}\left\lbrack  {f\left( t\right) }\right\rbrack
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{4}{\left\lbrack  tf\left( t\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{2} + \frac{1}{4}{\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{4} + \frac{1}{4} = 0\text{.}
$$

207. (1995. III) 设 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{\sin t}{\pi  - t}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,计算 ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

解 ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\left\lbrack  xf\left( x\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\pi } - {\int }_{0}^{\pi }x{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$

$$
= \pi {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\frac{\sin t}{\pi  - t}\mathrm{\;d}t - {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\frac{x\sin x}{\pi  - x}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\frac{\left( {\pi  - x}\right) \sin x}{\pi  - x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = 2.
$$

8. 8. (1998. II) 计算积分 ${\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| x - {x}^{2}\right| }}$ .

解 注意到 $x = 1$ 是被积函数的瑕点,而

$$
{\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x - {x}^{2}}} = {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\frac{1}{4} - {\left( x - \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2}}} = {\left\lbrack  \arcsin \left( 2x - 1\right) \right\rbrack  }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1} = \arcsin 1 = \frac{\pi }{2}.
$$

$$
{\int }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - x}} = {\int }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{{\left( x - \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} - \frac{1}{4}}} = {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( x - \frac{1}{2} + \sqrt{{\left( x - \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} - \frac{1}{4}}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}} = \ln \left( {2 + \sqrt{3}}\right) .
$$

因此

$$
{\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{\left| x - {x}^{2}\right| }} = {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{x - {x}^{2}}} + {\int }_{1}^{\frac{3}{2}}\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} - x}} = \frac{\pi }{2} + \ln \left( {2 + \sqrt{3}}\right) .
$$

9. 9. (2005. II)设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 连续,且 $f\left( 0\right)  \neq  0$ ,求极限

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}\left( {x - t}\right) f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}{x{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( {x - t}\right) \mathrm{d}t}.
$$

解 ${\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( {x - t}\right) \mathrm{d}t = t - u{\int }_{x}^{0} - f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ , 因此

$$
\text{ 原式 } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{x{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - {\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}{x{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}
$$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {xf}\left( x\right)  - {xf}\left( x\right) }{{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {xf}\left( x\right) }
$$

$$
= \frac{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}{x}}{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}{x} + f\left( x\right) }\right\rbrack  }
$$

$$
= \frac{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right) }{\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  + f\left( 0\right) } = \frac{1}{2}.
$$

210. (2000. II) 设 ${xOy}$ 平面上有正方形 $D = \{ \left( {x,y}\right)  \mid  0 \leq  x \leq  1,0 \leq  y \leq  1\}$ 及直线 $l : x + y =$ $t\left( {t \geq  0}\right)$ . 若 $S\left( t\right)$ 表示正方形 $D$ 位于直线 $l$ 左下方部分的面积,试求 ${\int }_{0}^{x}S\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t(x \geq$ $0)$ .

解 如图研 3-1 可知,

$$
S\left( t\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{2}{t}^{2}, & 0 \leq  t \leq  1, \\   - \frac{1}{2}{t}^{2} + {2t} - 1, & 1 < t \leq  2, \\  1, & t > 2, \end{array}\right.
$$

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_359.jpg?x=560&y=1590&w=438&h=455&r=0"/>

图研 3-1

<!-- Media -->

所以当 $0 \leq  x \leq  1$ 时, ${\int }_{0}^{x}S\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{1}{2}{t}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3}$ ;

当 $1 < x \leq  2$ 时, ${\int }_{0}^{x}S\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{1}S\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{1}^{x}\left( {-\frac{1}{2}{t}^{2} + {2t} - 1}\right) \mathrm{d}t$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + {x}^{2} - x + \frac{1}{3};
$$

当 $x > 2$ 时, ${\int }_{0}^{x}S\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{2}S\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{2}^{x}\mathrm{\;d}t = x - 1$ .

因此

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}S\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3}, & 0 \leq  x \leq  1, \\   - \frac{1}{6}{x}^{3} + {x}^{2} - x + \frac{1}{3}, & 1 < x \leq  2, \\  x - 1, & x > 2. \end{array}\right.
$$

2211. (1992. III) 求曲线 $y = \sqrt{x}$ 的一条切线 $l$ ,使该曲线与切线 $l$ 及直线 $x = 0,x = 2$ 所围成图形面积最小.

解 由 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2\sqrt{x}}$ ,得曲线在 $\left( {t,\sqrt{t}}\right)$ 处的切线方程为

$$
y - \sqrt{t} = \frac{1}{2\sqrt{t}}\left( {x - t}\right) ,
$$

即 $y = \frac{1}{2\sqrt{t}}x + \frac{\sqrt{t}}{2}$ . 所围面积为

$$
S\left( t\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{2}\left( {\frac{1}{2\sqrt{t}}x + \frac{\sqrt{t}}{2} - \sqrt{x}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{\sqrt{t}} + \sqrt{t} - \frac{4\sqrt{2}}{3}.
$$

令 ${S}^{\prime }\left( t\right)  = 0$ ,得 $t = 1$ ,又 ${S}^{\prime \prime }\left( 1\right)  = \frac{1}{2} > 0$ . 故当 $t = 1$ 时,面积取极小值,由于驻点惟一, 因此 $t = 1$ 是最小值点,此时 $l$ 的方程为 $y = \frac{x}{2} + \frac{1}{2}$ .

12. (1993. III) 设平面图形 $A$ 由 ${x}^{2} + {y}^{2} \leq  {2x}$ 与 $y \geq  x$ 所确定,求图形 $A$ 绕直线 $x = 2$ 旋转一周所得旋转体的体积.

解 $A$ 的图形如图研 3-2,取 $y$ 为积分变量,则 $y$ 的变化范围为 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ . 相应于

图研 3-2

$\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上的任一小区间 $\left\lbrack  {y,y + \mathrm{d}y}\right\rbrack$ 的体积元素为

$$
\mathrm{d}V = \left\{  {\pi {\left\lbrack  2 - \left( 1 - \sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}}\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2} - \pi {\left( 2 - y\right) }^{2}}\right\}  \mathrm{d}y
$$

$$
= {2\pi }\left\lbrack  {\sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}} - {\left( y - 1\right) }^{2}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}y\text{,}
$$

因此所求体积为

$$
V = {\int }_{0}^{1}{2\pi }\left\lbrack  {\sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}} - {\left( y - 1\right) }^{2}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}y
$$

$$
= {2\pi }{\left\lbrack  \frac{y}{2}\sqrt{1 - {y}^{2}} + \frac{1}{2}\arcsin y + \frac{{\left( 1 - y\right) }^{3}}{3}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1}
$$

$$
= \frac{{\pi }^{2}}{2} - \frac{2\pi }{3}\text{.}
$$

2313. (1994. III) 求曲线 $y = 3 - \left| {{x}^{2} - 1}\right|$ 与 $x$ 轴围成的封闭图形绕直线 $y = 3$ 旋转所得的旋转体体积.

取 $x$ 为积分变量,记相应于区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 和 $\left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack$ 上的体积分别为 ${V}_{1}$ 和 ${V}_{2}$ ,则它们的体积元素分别为

$$
\mathrm{d}{V}_{1} = \pi \left\{  {{3}^{2} - {\left\lbrack  3 - \left( {x}^{2} + 2\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2}}\right\}  \mathrm{d}x = \pi \left( {8 + 2{x}^{2} - {x}^{4}}\right) \mathrm{d}x,
$$

$$
\mathrm{d}{V}_{2} = \pi \left\{  {{3}^{2} - {\left\lbrack  3 - \left( 4 - {x}^{2}\right) \right\rbrack  }^{2}}\right\}  \mathrm{d}x = \pi \left( {8 + 2{x}^{2} - {x}^{4}}\right) \mathrm{d}x.
$$

由对称性得

$$
V = 2\left( {{V}_{1} + {V}_{2}}\right)  = {2\pi }{\int }_{0}^{1}\left( {8 + 2{x}^{2} - {x}^{4}}\right) \mathrm{d}x + {2\pi }{\int }_{1}^{2}\left( {8 + 2{x}^{2} - {x}^{4}}\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= {2\pi }{\int }_{0}^{2}\left( {8 + 2{x}^{2} - {x}^{4}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{448}{15}\pi .
$$

214. (1991. I,II) 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,(0,1)内可导,且 $3{\int }_{\frac{2}{3}}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = f\left( 0\right)$ ,证明在(0,1)内存在一点 $c$ ,使 ${f}^{\prime }\left( c\right)  = 0$ .

解 由积分中值定理知,在 $\left\lbrack  {\frac{2}{3},1}\right\rbrack$ 上存在一点 ${c}_{1}$ ,使

$$
{\int }_{\frac{2}{3}}^{1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{3}f\left( {c}_{1}\right) ,
$$

从而有 $f\left( {c}_{1}\right)  = f\left( 0\right)$ ,故 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,{c}_{1}}\right\rbrack$ 上满足罗尔定理条件,因此在 $\left( {0,{c}_{1}}\right)$ $\left( { \subset  \left( {0,1}\right) }\right)$ 内存在一点 $c$ ,使 ${f}^{\prime }\left( c\right)  = 0$ ,证毕.

15. 15. (1993. III)设 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,a}\right\rbrack$ 上连续,且 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,证明: $\left| {{\int }_{0}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}\right|  \leq  \frac{M{a}^{2}}{2}$ ,其中 $M = \mathop{\max }\limits_{{0 \leq  x \leq  a}}\left| {{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) }\right| .$

解 由微分中值定理可知: 对于任意 $x \in  \left\lbrack  {0,a}\right\rbrack$ ,存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {0,x}\right)$ ,使得 $f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) x$ ,由条件 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ 得 $f\left( x\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) x$ ,因此有

$$
\left| {{\int }_{0}^{a}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}\right|  \leq  {\int }_{0}^{a}\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right| \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{a}\left| {{f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) x}\right| \mathrm{d}x \leq  {\int }_{0}^{a}{Mx}\mathrm{\;d}x = \frac{M{a}^{2}}{2}.
$$

16. 16. (1999. II)设 $f\left( x\right)$ 是区间 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上单调减少且非负的连续函数, ${a}_{n} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{n}f\left( k\right)  - {\int }_{1}^{n}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x\left( {n = 1,2,\cdots }\right)$ ,证明数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 的极限存在. 解 由于 $f\left( x\right)$ 单调减少,因此

$$
f\left( {k + 1}\right)  \leq  {\int }_{k}^{k + 1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  f\left( k\right) \;\left( {k = 1,2,\cdots }\right) ,
$$

因此有

$$
{a}_{n} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{n}f\left( k\right)  - {\int }_{1}^{n}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{n}f\left( k\right)  - \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{n - 1}}{\int }_{k}^{k + 1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x
$$

$$
= \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 1}}^{{n - 1}}\left\lbrack  {f\left( k\right)  - {\int }_{k}^{k + 1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}\right\rbrack   + f\left( n\right)  \geq  0,
$$

即数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 有下界. 又

$$
{a}_{n + 1} - {a}_{n} = f\left( {n + 1}\right)  - {\int }_{n}^{n + 1}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x \leq  0,
$$

即得数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 单调减少,由单调有界数列必有极限的准则知数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 的极限存在. 27. 7. (2004. II) 设 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{x}^{x + \frac{\pi }{2}}\left| {\sin t}\right| \mathrm{d}t$ ,(1) 证明 $f\left( x\right)$ 是以 $\pi$ 为周期的周期函数； (2) 求 $f\left( x\right)$ 的值域. 解 (1) $f\left( {x + \pi }\right)  = {\int }_{x + \pi }^{x + \frac{3\pi }{2}}\left| {\sin t}\right| \mathrm{d}t$ ,设 $t = u + \pi$ ,则有

$$
f\left( {x + \pi }\right)  = {\int }_{x}^{x + \frac{\pi }{2}}\left| {\sin \left( {u + \pi }\right) }\right| \mathrm{d}u = {\int }_{x}^{x + \frac{\pi }{2}}\left| {\sin u}\right| \mathrm{d}u = f\left( x\right) ,
$$

故 $f\left( x\right)$ 是以 $\pi$ 为周期的周期函数. (2)因为 $\left| {\sin x}\right|$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 上连续,注意到 $f\left( x\right)$ 是以 $\pi$ 为周期的周期函数, 故只需在 $\left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack$ 上讨论 $f\left( x\right)$ 的值域. 因为

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \left| {\sin \left( {x + \frac{\pi }{2}}\right) }\right|  - \left| {\sin x}\right|  = \left| {\cos x}\right|  - \left| {\sin x}\right| ,
$$

令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,解得 ${x}_{1} = \frac{\pi }{4},{x}_{2} = \frac{3\pi }{4}$ ,且

$$
f\left( \frac{\pi }{4}\right)  = {\int }_{\frac{\pi }{4}}^{\frac{3\pi }{4}}\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t = \sqrt{2},
$$

$$
f\left( \frac{3\pi }{4}\right)  = {\int }_{\frac{5\pi }{4}}^{\frac{5\pi }{4}}\left| {\sin t}\right| \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{\frac{3\pi }{4}}^{\pi }\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t - {\int }_{\pi }^{\frac{5\pi }{4}}\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t = 2 - \sqrt{2}.
$$

又

$$
f\left( 0\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sin t\mathrm{\;d}t = 1,\;f\left( \pi \right)  = {\int }_{\pi }^{\frac{3\pi }{2}}\left( {-\sin t}\right) \mathrm{d}t = 1,
$$

因而 $f\left( x\right)$ 的最小值是 $2 - \sqrt{2}$ ,最大值是 $\sqrt{2}$ ,故 $f\left( x\right)$ 的值域是 $\left\lbrack  {2 - \sqrt{2},\sqrt{2}}\right\rbrack$ . 18. 18. (2002. I , II)设

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {2x} + \frac{3}{2}{x}^{2}, &  - 1 \leq  x < 0, \\  \frac{x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1\right) }^{2}}, & 0 \leq  x \leq  1, \end{array}\right.
$$

求函数 $F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{-1}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 的表达式. 解 当 $- 1 \leq  x < 0$ 时,

$$
F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{-1}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{-1}^{x}\left( {{2t} + \frac{3}{2}{t}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  {t}^{2} + \frac{1}{2}{t}^{3}\right\rbrack  }_{-1}^{x} = \frac{1}{2}{x}^{3} + {x}^{2} - \frac{1}{2}\text{.}
$$

当 $0 \leq  x \leq  1$ 时,

$$
F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{-1}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{-1}^{0}\left( {{2t} + \frac{3}{2}{t}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{t{\mathrm{e}}^{t}}{{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{t} + 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  {t}^{2} + \frac{1}{2}{t}^{3}\right\rbrack  }_{-1}^{0} - {\int }_{0}^{x}t\mathrm{\;d}\left( \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + 1}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2} - {\left\lbrack  \frac{t}{{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + 1}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{x} + {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}t =  - \frac{1}{2} - \frac{x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} + {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{-1}{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-t}}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{-t}\right)
$$

$$
=  - \frac{1}{2} - \frac{x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} - {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-t}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{x} =  - \frac{1}{2} - \frac{x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} - \ln \left( {1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}\right)  + \ln 2.
$$

因此

$$
F\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{1}{2}{x}^{3} + {x}^{2} - \frac{1}{2}, &  - 1 \leq  x < 0, \\   - \frac{1}{2} - \frac{x}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1} - \ln \frac{1 + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}}{2}, & 0 \leq  x \leq  1. \end{array}\right.
$$

219. ( 2007. I , III )如图研 3-4,连续函数 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-3, - 2}\right\rbrack  ,\left\lbrack  {2,3}\right\rbrack$ 上的图形分别是直径为 1 的上、下半圆周,在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-2,0}\right\rbrack  ,\left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack$ 的图形分别是直径为 2 的下、上半圆周,设 $F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,则下列结论正确的是 (   ).

(A) $F\left( 3\right)  =  - \frac{3}{4}F\left( {-2}\right)$ (B) $F\left( 3\right)  = \frac{5}{4}F\left( 2\right)$

(C) $F\left( {-3}\right)  = \frac{3}{4}F\left( 2\right)$ (D) $F\left( {-3}\right)  =  - \frac{5}{4}F\left( {-2}\right)$

图 研 3-4
