解 根据定积分的几何意义, 有

$F\left( 2\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\pi ,$

$F\left( 3\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{2}^{3}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{2}\pi  - \frac{1}{2}\pi  \cdot  {\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} = \frac{3}{8}\pi ,$

$F\left( {-2}\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{-2}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - {\int }_{-2}^{0}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{1}{2}\pi ,$

$F\left( {-3}\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{-3}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x =  - \left\lbrack  {{\int }_{-3}^{-2}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x + {\int }_{-2}^{0}f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x}\right\rbrack   =  - \left\lbrack  {\frac{1}{2}\pi {\left( \frac{1}{2}\right) }^{2} - \frac{1}{2}\pi }\right\rbrack   = \frac{3}{8}\pi .$

故选 (C).

20. (2007. I ) ${\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{1}{{x}^{3}}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x =$ _____.

解 作换元 $x = \frac{1}{t}$ ,则

$$
{\int }_{1}^{2}\frac{1}{{x}^{3}}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{x}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1}t{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\mathrm{\;d}t = {\left\lbrack  t{\mathrm{e}}^{t} - {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\right\rbrack  }_{\frac{1}{2}}^{1} = \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{2}}.
$$

221. (2008. I ) 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 是连续函数.

(1)利用定义证明函数 $F\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 可导,且 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)$ ;

(2) 当 $f\left( x\right)$ 是以 2 为周期的周期函数时,证明函数 $G\left( x\right)  = 2{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t -$ $x{\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ 也是以 2 为周期的周期函数.

证 (1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{\Delta x} \rightarrow  0}}\frac{F\left( {x + {\Delta x}}\right)  - F\left( x\right) }{\Delta x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{\Delta x} \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{0}^{x + {\Delta x}}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}{\Delta x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{\Delta x} \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\int }_{x}^{x + {\Delta x}}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}{\Delta x}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{\Delta x} \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( \xi \right) {\Delta x}}{\Delta x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{\Delta x} \rightarrow  0}}f\left( \xi \right)  = f\left( x\right) ,
$$

因此 $F\left( x\right)$ 可导,且 ${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = f\left( x\right)$ .

(2) $G\left( {x + 2}\right)  - G\left( x\right)  = 2\left( {{\int }_{0}^{x + 2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t}\right)  - 2{\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$

$$
= 2{\int }_{x}^{x + 2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t - 2{\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t,
$$

由于 $f\left( x\right)$ 是以 2 为周期的周期函数,故必有 ${\int }_{x}^{x + 2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t = {\int }_{0}^{2}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,因此 $G\left( {x + 2}\right)  -$ $G\left( x\right)  = 0$ ,即 $G\left( x\right)$ 是以 2 为周期的周期函数.

22. (2009. I ) 如图研 3-5,正方形 $\{ \left( {x,y}\right) \left| \right| x\left| { \leq  1,}\right| y \mid   \leq  1\}$ 被其对角线划分为四个区域 ${D}_{k}\left( {k = 1,2,3,4}\right) ,{I}_{k} = {\iint }_{\Omega }y\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x\mathrm{\;d}y$ ,则 $\mathop{\max }\limits_{{1 \leq  k \leq  4}}\left\{  {I}_{k}\right\}   =$ (   ).

(A) ${I}_{1}$ (B) ${I}_{2}$ (C) ${I}_{3}$ (D) ${I}_{4}$

解 记 ${D}_{1}^{ * }$ 和 ${D}_{3}^{ * }$ 为 ${D}_{1}$ 和 ${D}_{3}$ 中 $x \geq  0$ 部分的区域,利用二重积分区域的对称性及被积函数的奇偶性, 可得

$$
{I}_{2} = {I}_{4} = 0,
$$

{I}_{1} = 2{\iint }_{{D}_{1}}y\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x\mathrm{\;d}y > 0,\;{I}_{3} = 2{\iint }_{{D}_{3}}y\cos x\mathrm{\;d}x\mathrm{\;d}y < 0.
