223. (2010. I ) 设 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{-t},y = {\int }_{0}^{t}\ln \left( {1 + {u}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}u$ ,则 ${\left. \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}}\right| }_{t = 0} =$ _____.

解

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t}}{\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t}} =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\ln \left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right) ,
$$

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)  = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}\left\lbrack  {-{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\ln \left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right) }\right\rbrack  /\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t}\left\lbrack  {\ln \left( {1 + {t}^{2}}\right)  + \frac{2t}{1 + {t}^{2}}}\right\rbrack  ,
$$

于是 ${\left. \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}}\right| }_{t = 0} = 0$ .

例24. (2010. I ) ${\int }_{0}^{{\pi }^{2}}\sqrt{x}\cos \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x =$ _____.

解 作换元 $x = {u}^{2}$ ,则

${\int }_{0}^{{\pi }^{2}}\sqrt{x}\cos \sqrt{x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\pi }2{u}^{2}\cos u\mathrm{\;d}u = {\left\lbrack  2{u}^{2}\sin u + 4u\cos u - 4\sin u\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\pi } =  - {4\pi }.$

25. 25. (2010. I ) 求 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}\left( {{x}^{2} - t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ 的单调区间与极值.

解 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}\left( {{x}^{2} - t}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = {x}^{2}{\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t - {\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,

令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {2x}{\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = 0$ ,得 $x =  - 1,0,1$ .

在 $\left( {-\infty , - 1}\right)$ 和(0,1)上可得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $( - \infty , - 1\rbrack$ 和 $\left\lbrack  {0,1}\right\rbrack$ 上单调减少; 在(-1,0)和 $\left( {1, + \infty }\right)$ 上可得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {-1,0}\right\rbrack$ 和 $\lbrack 1, + \infty )$ 上单调增加.

又 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = 2{\int }_{1}^{{x}^{2}}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t + 4{x}^{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{x}^{4}}$ ,得

$$
{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\pm 1}\right)  = 4{\mathrm{e}}^{-1} > 0,\;{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  =  - 2{\int }_{0}^{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t < 0,
$$

所以 $x =  - 1$ 和 $x = 1$ 为 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极小值点,极小值为 $f\left( {\pm 1}\right)  = 0;x = 0$ 为 $f\left( x\right)$ 的极大值点,极大值为 $f\left( 0\right)  =  - {\int }_{1}^{0}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = {\int }_{0}^{1}t{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}t = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{t}^{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = \frac{\mathrm{e} - 1}{2\mathrm{e}}$ .

226. (2010. I ,III) (1) 比较 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\left| {\ln t}\right| {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + t\right) \right\rbrack  }^{n}\mathrm{\;d}t$ 与 ${\int }_{0}^{1}{t}^{n}\left| {\ln t}\right| \mathrm{d}t\left( {n = 1,2,\cdots }\right)$ ;

(2)记 ${u}_{n} = {\int }_{0}^{1}\left| {\ln t}\right| {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + t\right) \right\rbrack  }^{n}\mathrm{\;d}t\left( {n = 1,2,\cdots }\right)$ ,求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{u}_{n}$ .

解 (1) 当 $0 \leq  t \leq  1$ 时, $0 \leq  \ln \left( {1 + t}\right)  \leq  t$ ,故 $\left| {\ln t}\right| {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + t\right) \right\rbrack  }^{n} \leq  {t}^{n}\left| {\ln t}\right|$ ,于是

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}\left| {\ln t}\right| {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + t\right) \right\rbrack  }^{n}\mathrm{\;d}t \leq  {\int }_{0}^{1}{t}^{n}\left| {\ln t}\right| \mathrm{d}t.
$$

(2)由(1)得

$$
0 \leq  {\int }_{0}^{1}\left| {\ln t}\right| {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 + t\right) \right\rbrack  }^{n}\mathrm{\;d}t \leq  {\int }_{0}^{1}{t}^{n}\left| {\ln t}\right| \mathrm{d}t,
$$

而

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}{t}^{n}\left| {\ln t}\right| \mathrm{d}t =  - {\int }_{0}^{1}{t}^{n}\ln t\mathrm{\;d}t =  - {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{n + 1}{t}^{n + 1}\left( \ln t - \frac{1}{n + 1}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = \frac{1}{{\left( n + 1\right) }^{2}},
$$

由夹逼准则得 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{u}_{n} = 0$ .

227. (2011. I ) 设 $I = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \sin x\mathrm{\;d}x,J = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \cot x\mathrm{\;d}x,K = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\ln \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,则 $I,J,K$ 的大小关系是(   ).

(A) $I < J < K$ (B) $I < K < J$ (C) $J < I < K$ (D) $K < J < I$

解 当 $x \in  \left( {0,\frac{\pi }{4}}\right)$ 时, $0 < \sin x < \cos x < \cot x$ ,因此 $\ln \sin x < \ln \cos x < \ln \cot x$ . 故选 (B).

228. (2011. I)曲线 $y = {\int }_{0}^{x}\tan t\mathrm{\;d}t\left( {0 \leq  x \leq  \frac{\pi }{4}}\right)$ 的弧长 $s =$ _____.

$$
\text{解}s = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\sqrt{1 + {\tan }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}}\sec x\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( \sec x + \tan x\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{4}} = \ln \left( {\sqrt{2} + 1}\right) .
$$

229. (2012. I ) 设 ${I}_{k} = {\int }_{\mathrm{e}}^{k\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x\left( {k = 1,2,3}\right)$ ,则有(   ).

(A) ${I}_{1} < {I}_{2} < {I}_{3}$ (B) ${I}_{3} < {I}_{2} < {I}_{1}$

(C) ${I}_{2} < {I}_{3} < {I}_{1}$ (D) ${I}_{2} < {I}_{1} < {I}_{3}$

解 ${I}_{2} - {I}_{1} = {\int }_{\pi }^{2\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x < 0,{I}_{3} - {I}_{2} = {\int }_{2\pi }^{3\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x > 0$ ,

$$
{I}_{3} - {I}_{1} = {\int }_{\pi }^{3\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{\pi }^{2\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x + {\int }_{2\pi }^{3\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

对 ${\int }_{2\pi }^{3\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$ 作换元 $x = \pi  + u$ ,得

$$
{\int }_{2\pi }^{3\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x =  - {\int }_{\pi }^{2\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{\left( u + \pi \right) }^{2}}\sin u\mathrm{\;d}u =  - {\int }_{\pi }^{2\pi }{\mathrm{e}}^{{\left( x + \pi \right) }^{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x,
$$

因此

$$
{I}_{3} - {I}_{1} = {\int }_{\pi }^{2\pi }\left\lbrack  {{\mathrm{e}}^{{x}^{2}} - {\mathrm{e}}^{{\left( x + \pi \right) }^{2}}}\right\rbrack  \sin x\mathrm{\;d}x > 0.
$$

故选 (D).

例 30. (2012. I ) ${\int }_{0}^{2}x\sqrt{{2x} - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x =$ _____.

解 作换元 $x = 1 + \sin u$ ,则

$$
{\int }_{0}^{2}x\sqrt{{2x} - {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{0}^{2}x\sqrt{1 - {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{-\frac{\pi }{2}}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\left( {1 + \sin u}\right) {\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = \frac{\pi }{2}\text{.}
$$

## (四)微分方程

例 1. (1999. I , II) ${y}^{\prime \prime } - {4y} = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ 的通解为_____.

解 此方程对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - 4 = 0$ ,其根为 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  2$ . 又因自由项 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{2x},\lambda  = 2$ 是特征方程的单根,故令 ${y}^{ * } = {Ax}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ 是原方程的特解,代入方程可得 $A = \frac{1}{4}$ ,于是原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2x}} + \frac{x}{4}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}.
$$

22. (2000. I)微分方程 $x{y}^{\prime \prime } + 3{y}^{\prime } = 0$ 的通解为_____.

解 原方程可变形为 $\frac{\mathrm{d}{y}^{\prime }}{{y}^{\prime }} =  - \frac{3}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,积分得 $\ln {y}^{\prime } =  - 3\ln x + \ln {C}_{0}$ ,

即 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{{C}_{0}}{{x}^{3}}$ . 故

$$
y =  - \frac{{C}_{0}}{2}\frac{1}{{x}^{2}} + {C}_{2} = \frac{{C}_{1}}{{x}^{2}} + {C}_{2}.
$$

3. (2001. I ) 设 $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\left( {{C}_{1}\sin x + {C}_{2}\cos x}\right)$ ( ${C}_{1},{C}_{2}$ 为任意常数) 为某二阶常系数线性齐次微分方程的通解,则该微分方程为_____.

解 由所给通解的表达式知, ${r}_{1,2} = 1 \pm  \mathrm{i}$ 是所求微分方程的特征方程的根,于是特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {2r} + 2 = 0$ ,故所求微分方程为

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = 0.
$$

24. (2001. II) 过点 $\left( {\frac{1}{2},0}\right)$ 且满足关系式 ${y}^{\prime }\arcsin x + \frac{y}{\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}} = 1$ 的曲线方程为 _____.

解 将所给关系式改写成 ${y}^{\prime } + \frac{1}{\arcsin x\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}y = \frac{1}{\arcsin x}$ ,由一阶线性微分方程的通解公式, 得

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\arcsin x\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}}\left( {\int \frac{1}{\arcsin x}{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\arcsin x\sqrt{1 - {x}^{2}}}}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right) ,
$$

即

$$
y = \frac{1}{\arcsin x}\left( {x + C}\right) ,
$$

代入初值条件 $x = \frac{1}{2},y = 0$ ,得 $C =  - \frac{1}{2}$ ,故所求曲线的方程为

$$
y = \frac{x - \frac{1}{2}}{\arcsin x}.
$$

25. (2002. I ,II) 微分方程 $y{y}^{\prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime 2} = 0$ 满足初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{1}{2}$ 的特解是_____.

解 令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,且原方程成为 ${yp}\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + {p}^{2} = 0$ ,即

$$
p = 0\text{ 或 }y\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + p = 0.
$$

由于 $p = 0$ 不满足条件 ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,故取 $y\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + p = 0$ . 分离变量后积分得

$$
p = \frac{{C}_{1}}{y},
$$

代入初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1,{\left. p\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{1}{2y},
$$

分离变量后积分得 ${y}^{2} = x + {C}_{2}$ ,代入初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 1$ . 于是有 ${y}^{2} =$ $x + 1$ ,解得特解

$$
y = \sqrt{x + 1}\text{.}
$$

2. (2004. I) 欧拉方程 ${x}^{2}\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} + {4x}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + {2y} = 0\left( {x > 0}\right)$ 的通解为_____.

解 令 $x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}$ ,记 $\mathrm{D} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}$ ,则原方程成为

$$
\mathrm{D}\left( {\mathrm{D} - 1}\right) y + 4\mathrm{D}y + {2y} = 0.
$$

特征方程是 $r\left( {r - 1}\right)  + {4r} + 2 = 0$ ,解得特征根是 ${r}_{1} =  - 1,{r}_{2} =  - 2$ ,故得通解 $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-t} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{2t}}$ ,于是原方程的通解为

$$
y = \frac{{C}_{1}}{x} + \frac{{C}_{2}}{{x}^{2}}.
$$

27. (2004. II) 微分方程 $\left( {y + {x}^{3}}\right) \mathrm{d}x - {2x}\mathrm{\;d}y = 0$ 满足 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = \frac{6}{5}$ 的特解为_____.

解 原方程变形为一阶线性方程

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} - \frac{1}{2x}y = \frac{{x}^{2}}{2},
$$

解得

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{1}{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int \frac{{x}^{2}}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{1}{2x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{5}{x}^{3} + C\sqrt{x}\text{.}
$$

由 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = \frac{6}{5}$ 得 $C = 1$ ,故特解为

$$
y = \frac{1}{5}{x}^{3} + \sqrt{x}.
$$

8. (2005. I,II) 微分方程 $x{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = x\ln x$ 满足 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} =  - \frac{1}{9}$ 的特解为_____.

解 原方程变形为一阶线性方程

$$
{y}^{\prime } + \frac{2}{x}y = \ln x,
$$

解得

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{2}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int \ln x{\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{2}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\left( {\frac{1}{3}{x}^{3}\ln x - \frac{1}{9}{x}^{3} + C}\right) .
$$

由 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} =  - \frac{1}{9}$ ,得 $C = 0$ ,故特解为

$$
y = \frac{x}{3}\left( {\ln x - \frac{1}{3}}\right) .
$$

29. (2009. I ) 若二阶常系数齐次线性微分方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + a{y}^{\prime } + {by} = 0$ 的通解为 $y =$ $\left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,则非齐次方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + a{y}^{\prime } + {by} = x$ 满足条件 $y\left( 0\right)  = 2,{y}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0$ 的解为 $y =$ _____.

解 由常系数线性齐次微分方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + a{y}^{\prime } + {by} = 0$ 的通解为 $y = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 可知 ${y}_{1} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},{y}_{2} = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 为齐次微分方程的两个线性无关的解. 可见齐次方程的特征方程是 ${\left( r - 1\right) }^{2} = {r}^{2} - {2r} + 1 = 0$ ,故齐次微分方程为 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } + y = 0$ .

设非齐次方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } + y = x$ 的特解为 ${y}^{ * } = {Ax} + B$ ,代入方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } + y = x$ ,解得 $A = 1,B = 2$ ,即 ${y}^{ * } = x + 2$ . 故 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 2{y}^{\prime } + y = x$ 的通解为

$$
y = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + x + 2,
$$

且

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2} + {C}_{2}x}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1.
$$

代入初值条件 $y\left( 0\right)  = 2,{y}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 0,{C}_{2} =  - 1$ . 因此所求的解为 $y =  - x{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + x + 2$ .

2. 10. (2011. I) 微分方程 ${y}^{\prime } + y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x$ 满足条件 $y\left( 0\right)  = 0$ 的解为 $y =$ _____.

解 原方程的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int 1\mathrm{\;d}x}\left\lbrack  {\int {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x{\mathrm{e}}^{\int 1\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left\lbrack  {\int \cos x\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right\rbrack   = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left\lbrack  {\sin x + C}\right\rbrack  ,
$$

由 $y\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,得 $C = 0$ ,故所求解为 $y = \sin x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ .

2 11. (1989. I,II) 设线性无关的函数 ${y}_{1},{y}_{2},{y}_{3}$ 都是二阶非齐次方程

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } + p\left( x\right) {y}^{\prime } + q\left( x\right) y = f\left( x\right)
$$

的解, ${C}_{1},{C}_{2}$ 是任意常数,则该非齐次方程的通解是 (   ).

(A) ${C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + {y}_{3}$ (B) ${C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} - \left( {{C}_{1} + {C}_{2}}\right) {y}_{3}$

(C) ${C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} - \left( {1 - {C}_{1} - {C}_{2}}\right) {y}_{3}$ (D) ${C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + \left( {1 - {C}_{1} - {C}_{2}}\right) {y}_{3}$

解 因 ${y}_{1} - {y}_{3}$ 与 ${y}_{2} - {y}_{3}$ 是对应的齐次方程的解,且由 ${y}_{1},{y}_{2},{y}_{3}$ 线性无关可推知 ${y}_{1} - {y}_{3}$ 与 ${y}_{2} - {y}_{3}$ 线性无关,而 ${y}_{3}$ 是非齐次方程的特解,故

$$
y = {C}_{1}\left( {{y}_{1} - {y}_{3}}\right)  + {C}_{2}\left( {{y}_{2} - {y}_{3}}\right)  + {y}_{3} = {C}_{1}{y}_{1} + {C}_{2}{y}_{2} + \left( {1 - {C}_{1} - {C}_{2}}\right) {y}_{3}
$$

是非齐次方程的通解,所以选择 (D).

22. 12. (1989. III) 微分方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} + 1$ 的一个特解应具有形式 (式中 $a,b$ 为常数) (   ).

(A) $a{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + b$ (B) ${ax}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + b$ (C) $a{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {bx}$ (D) ${ax}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {bx}$

解 原方程对应的齐次方程的特征方程的根为 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1$ . 相对于方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ , 因 ${f}_{1}\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x},\lambda  = 1$ 是特征方程的 (单) 根,故该方程的特解应形如 ${y}_{1}^{ * } = {ax}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ .

又相对于方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = 1$ ,因 ${f}_{2}\left( x\right)  = 1,\lambda  = 0$ 不是特征方程的根,故该方程的特解应形如 ${y}_{2}^{ * } = b$ .

按叠加原理,原方程的特解应形如 ${y}^{ * } = {y}_{1}^{ * } + {y}_{2}^{ * } = {ax}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + b$ . 故应选择 (B). 13. ( 2008. I )在下列微分方程中,以 $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}\cos {2x} + {C}_{3}\sin {2x}\left( {{C}_{1},{C}_{2},{C}_{3}}\right.$ 为任意的常数)为通解的是(   ).

(A) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } - {4y} = 0$ (B) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } + {4y} = 0$

(C) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } + {4y} = 0$ (D) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime } + 4{y}^{\prime } - {4y} = 0$

解 由 $y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}\cos {2x} + {C}_{3}\sin {2x}$ 可知微分方程的特征方程的根为 ${\lambda }_{1} = 1$ , ${\lambda }_{2,3} =  \pm  2\mathrm{i}$ ,故对应的特征方程为

$$
\left( {r - 1}\right) \left( {r + 2\mathrm{i}}\right) \left( {r - 2\mathrm{i}}\right)  = \left( {r - 1}\right) \left( {{r}^{2} + 4}\right)
$$

$$
= {r}^{3} - {r}^{2} + {4r} - 4 = 0\text{,}
$$

所以微分方程为 ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime } + 4{y}^{\prime } - {4y} = 0$ . 应选 (D).

14. (1989. I,II,III) 设 $f\left( x\right)  = \sin x - {\int }_{0}^{x}\left( {x - t}\right) f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,其中 $f$ 为连续函数,求 $f\left( x\right)$ .

解 因 $f\left( x\right)  = \sin x - x{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t + {\int }_{0}^{x}{tf}\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t$ ,代入 $x = 0$ ,得 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,

且

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \cos x - {\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) \mathrm{d}t.
$$

代入 $x = 0$ ,得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 1$ . 又

$$
{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  =  - \sin x - f\left( x\right) .
$$

记 $y = f\left( x\right)$ ,即得初值问题

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {y}^{\prime \prime } + y =  - \sin x, \\  {\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 1. \end{array}\right.
$$

上述微分方程对应的齐次方程的特征方程有根 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  \mathrm{i}$ ,而自由项为 $- \sin x,\lambda  +$ $\mathrm{i}\omega  = \mathrm{i}$ 是特征方程的根,故令 ${y}^{ * } = x\left( {A\cos x + B\sin x}\right)$ 是原方程的特解,代入微分方程并比较系数,得 $A = \frac{1}{2},B = 0$ ,即 ${y}^{ * } = \frac{1}{2}x\cos x$ . 于是得通解

$$
y = {C}_{1}\cos x + {C}_{2}\sin x + \frac{1}{2}x\cos x,
$$

且.

$$
{y}^{\prime } =  - {C}_{1}\sin x + {C}_{2}\cos x + \frac{1}{2}\cos x - \frac{1}{2}x\sin x.
$$

由 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ 及 ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 1$ ,得

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {C}_{1} = 0, \\  {C}_{2} + \frac{1}{2} = 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

即 ${C}_{1} = 0,{C}_{2} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,故

$$
y = f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\sin x + \frac{1}{2}x\cos x.
$$

25. 15. (1991. I,II)在上半平面上求一条向下凸的曲线,其上任一点 $P\left( {x,y}\right)$ 处的曲率等于此曲线在该点的法线 ${PQ}$ 长度的倒数 ( $Q$ 是法线与 $x$ 轴的交点),且曲线在点 (1,1)处的切线与 $x$ 轴平行.

解 曲线 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 在点 $P\left( {x,y}\right)$ 处的法线方程为

$$
Y - y =  - \frac{1}{{y}^{\prime }}\left( {X - x}\right) .
$$

令 $Y = 0$ ,得点 $Q$ 的坐标 $\left( {x + y{y}^{\prime },0}\right)$ ,于是

$$
\left| {PQ}\right|  = \sqrt{{\left( y{y}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2}} = \left| y\right| \sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}.
$$

依题意有

$$
\frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{3}{2}}} = \frac{1}{\left| y\right| {\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}}}.
$$

因所求曲线在上半平面上且向下凸,有 $\left| y\right|  = y,\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right|  = {y}^{\prime \prime }$ ,故得微分方程

$$
\frac{{y}^{\prime \prime }}{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}} = \frac{1}{y},
$$

且由题设知 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = 0$ .

令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = p\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}y}$ ,且微分方程降阶为

$$
\frac{p\mathrm{\;d}p}{1 + {p}^{2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y}.
$$

由条件 $y = 1,p = 0$ ,积分 ${\int }_{0}^{p}\frac{p\mathrm{\;d}p}{1 + {p}^{2}} = {\int }_{1}^{y}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y}$ ,得 $\frac{1}{2}\ln \left( {1 + {p}^{2}}\right)  = \ln y$ ,从而

$$
p =  \pm  \sqrt{{y}^{2} - 1},
$$

即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\sqrt{{y}^{2} - 1}} =  \pm  \mathrm{d}x.
$$

积分得

$$
\ln \left( {y + \sqrt{{y}^{2} - 1}}\right)  =  \pm  x + C,
$$

即 $y = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x + C} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\left( {x + C}\right) }}{2}$ . 代入初值条件 $x = 1,y = 1$ ,得 $C =  - 1$ ,故

$$
y = \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x - 1} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-\left( {x - 1}\right) }}{2}.
$$

26. 16. (1995. I ,II)设曲线 $L$ 位于 ${xOy}$ 平面的第一象限内, $L$ 上任一点 $M$ 处的切线与 $y$ 轴总相交,交点记为 $A$ . 已知 $\left| {MA}\right|  = \left| {OA}\right|$ ,且 $L$ 过点 $\left( {\frac{3}{2},\frac{3}{2}}\right)$ ,求 $L$ 的方程.

解 设点 $M$ 的坐标为(x,y),则切线 ${MA}$ 的方程为

$$
Y - y = {y}^{\prime }\left( {X - x}\right) .
$$

令 $X = 0$ ,得 $A$ 的坐标 $\left( {0,y - x{y}^{\prime }}\right)$ .

因 $\left| {MA}\right|  = \left| {OA}\right|$ ,故有

$$
\left| {y - x{y}^{\prime }}\right|  = \sqrt{{\left( x - 0\right) }^{2} + {\left( y - y + x{y}^{\prime }\right) }^{2}},
$$

化简后得

$$
{2y}{y}^{\prime } - \frac{1}{x}{y}^{2} =  - x.
$$

即

$$
{\left( {y}^{2}\right) }^{\prime } - \frac{1}{x}{y}^{2} =  - x.
$$

由一阶线性方程的通解公式解得

$$
{y}^{2} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int  - x{\mathrm{e}}^{-\int \frac{1}{x}\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = x\left( {-x + C}\right)  =  - {x}^{2} + {Cx}.
$$

由于 $L$ 位于第一象限,故取

$$
y = \sqrt{{Cx} - {x}^{2}}.
$$

代入初值条件 $x = \frac{3}{2},y = \frac{3}{2}$ ,得 $C = 3$ . 故 $L$ 的方程为

$$
y = \sqrt{{3x} - {x}^{2}}.
$$

29 17. (1995. III) 设 $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 是微分方程 $x{y}^{\prime } + p\left( x\right) y = x$ 的一个解,求此微分方程满足条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = \ln 2} = 0$ 的特解.

解 将 $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 代入原方程,可得

$$
x{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + p\left( x\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} = x,
$$

故

$$
p\left( x\right)  = x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - x,
$$

即原方程对应的齐次方程为 $x{y}^{\prime } + \left( {x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - x}\right) y = 0$ ,消去 $x$ ,得 ${y}^{\prime } + \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - 1}\right) y = 0$ ,

分离变量并积分得齐次方程的通解为

$$
Y = C{\mathrm{e}}^{x + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}},
$$

于是得原方程的通解为

$$
y = C{\mathrm{e}}^{x + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

由初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = \ln 2} = 0$ ,得 $C \cdot  2{\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{2}} + 2 = 0$ ,即 $C =  - {\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{2}}$ . 故所求特解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{x + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - \frac{1}{2}}.
$$

2518. (1996. III) 设 $f\left( x\right)$ 为连续函数.

(1)求初值问题 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {y}^{\prime } + {ay} = f\left( x\right) , \\  {\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0 \end{array}\right.$ 的解 $y\left( x\right)$ ,其中 $a$ 是正常数;

(2)若 $\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|  \leq  k$ ( $k$ 为常数),证明当 $x \geq  0$ 时,有 $\left| {y\left( x\right) }\right|  \leq  \frac{k}{a}\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}}\right)$ .

解 (1) 方程的通解为

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-\int a\mathrm{\;d}x}\left( {\int f\left( x\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{\int a\mathrm{\;d}x}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\left( {\int f\left( x\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}\mathrm{\;d}x + C}\right)
$$

$$
= {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\left( {F\left( x\right)  + C}\right) ,
$$

其中 $F\left( x\right)$ 是 $f\left( x\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{ax}$ 的一个原函数. 由 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 0$ ,得 $C =  - F\left( 0\right)$ ,故

$$
y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\left\lbrack  {F\left( x\right)  - F\left( 0\right) }\right\rbrack   = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{at}\mathrm{\;d}t.
$$

(2)因 $\left| {f\left( x\right) }\right|  \leq  k$ ,故

$$
\left| y\right|  = {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\left| {{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( t\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{at}\mathrm{\;d}t}\right|  \leq  {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}{\int }_{0}^{x}\left| {f\left( t\right) }\right| {\mathrm{e}}^{at}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

$$
\leq  k{\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}{\int }_{0}^{x}{\mathrm{e}}^{at}\mathrm{\;d}t = k{\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}\frac{1}{a}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{ax} - 1}\right)
$$

$$
= \frac{k}{a}\left( {1 - {\mathrm{e}}^{-{ax}}}\right) .
$$

2519. (1993. I,II)设物体 $A$ 从点(0,1)出发,以常速率 $v$ 沿 $y$ 轴正向运动. 物体 $B$ 从点(-1,0)与 $A$ 同时出发,其速率为 ${2v}$ ,方向始终指向 $A$ . 试建立物体 $B$ 的运动轨迹所满足的微分方程, 并写出初值条件.

解 设物体 $B$ 的运动轨迹的方程为 $y = y\left( x\right)$ ,又设在时刻 $t$ ,物体 $B$ 位于点 (x,y)处,此时物体 $A$ 位于点 $\left( {0,1 + {vt}}\right)$ . 按题意,则如图研 $4 - 1$ 所示,有

$$
{y}^{\prime } = \frac{1 + {vt} - y}{0 - x},
$$

即

$$
y - x{y}^{\prime } - 1 = {vt}. \tag{1}
$$

<!-- Media -->

<img src="https://cdn.noedgeai.com/01940c56-10ad-7326-92af-ec794cfa19d8_375.jpg?x=616&y=264&w=339&h=361&r=0"/>

图研 4-1

<!-- Media -->

又此刻,物体 $B$ 从点(-1,0)行至(x,y)的路程为

$$
{\int }_{-1}^{x}\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {2vt}. \tag{2}
$$

由 (1) 式与 (2) 式消去 ${vt}$ ,得

$$
y - x{y}^{\prime } - 1 = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{-1}^{x}\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

在上式两端对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
{y}^{\prime } - \left( {{y}^{\prime } + x{y}^{\prime \prime }}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}},
$$

即

$$
x{y}^{\prime \prime } + \frac{1}{2}\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}} = 0,
$$

初值条件为 ${\left. y\right| }_{x =  - 1} = 0,{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = 1$ .

20. (1998. II) 利用代换 $y = \frac{u}{\cos x}$ 将方程

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime }\cos x - 2{y}^{\prime }\sin x + {3y}\cos x = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}
$$

化简, 并求出原方程的通解.

解法一 由 $u = y\cos x$ 两端对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
{u}^{\prime } = {y}^{\prime }\cos x - y\sin x,\;{u}^{\prime \prime } = {y}^{\prime \prime }\cos x - 2{y}^{\prime }\sin x - y\cos x.
$$

于是原方程化为 ${u}^{\prime \prime } + {4u} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,其通解为

$$
u = {C}_{1}\cos {2x} + {C}_{2}\sin {2x} + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{5}\left( {{C}_{1},{C}_{2}}\right. \text{为任意常数})\text{.}
$$

从而原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}\frac{\cos {2x}}{\cos x} + 2{C}_{2}\sin x + \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x}}{5\cos x}.
$$

解法二

$$
y = u\sec x,{y}^{\prime } = {u}^{\prime }\sec x + u\sec x \cdot  \tan x,
$$

${y}^{\prime \prime } = {u}^{\prime \prime }\sec x + 2{u}^{\prime }\sec x \cdot  \tan x + u\sec x \cdot  {\tan }^{2}x + u{\sec }^{3}x.$ 代入原方程得 ${u}^{\prime \prime } + {4u} = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ . (下同解法一)

27. (1997. II) 设曲线 $L$ 的极坐标方程为 $\rho  = \rho \left( \theta \right) ,M\left( {\rho ,\theta }\right)$ 为 $L$ 上任一点, ${M}_{0}\left( {2,0}\right)$ 为 $L$ 上一定点. 若极径 $O{M}_{0},{OM}$ 与曲线 $L$ 所围成的面积等于 $L$ 上 ${M}_{0},M$ 两点间弧长的值之一半. 求曲线 $L$ 的方程.

解 由题意得

$$
\frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\theta }{\rho }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}\theta  = \frac{1}{2}{\int }_{0}^{\theta }\sqrt{{\rho }^{2} + {\rho }^{\prime 2}}\mathrm{\;d}\theta ,
$$

上式两端对 $\theta$ 求导,得 ${\rho }^{2} = \sqrt{{\rho }^{2} + {\rho }^{\prime 2}}$ ,即 ${\rho }^{\prime } =  \pm  \rho \sqrt{{\rho }^{2} - 1}$ . 分离变量并积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{\rho \sqrt{{\rho }^{2} - 1}} =  \pm  \int \mathrm{d}\theta
$$

即

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}\rho }{{\rho }^{2}\sqrt{1 - \frac{1}{{\rho }^{2}}}} =  \pm  \int \mathrm{d}\theta ,
$$

得 $- \arcsin \frac{1}{\rho } =  \pm  \theta  + C$ ,代入初值条件 $\theta  = 0,\rho  = 2$ ,得 $C =  - \frac{\pi }{6}$ . 故曲线 $L$ 的方程为 $\arcsin \frac{1}{\rho } = \frac{\pi }{6} \pm  \theta$ ,即

$$
\rho  = \frac{1}{\sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} \pm  \theta }\right) }.
$$

若将 $L$ 表示成直角坐标方程,则由 $\rho \sin \left( {\frac{\pi }{6} \pm  \theta }\right)  = 1$ ,即

$$
\rho \left( {\frac{1}{2}\cos \theta  \pm  \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\sin \theta }\right)  = 1,
$$

得 $x \pm  \sqrt{3}y = 2$ .

22. (1998. II) 设 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 是一向上凸的连续曲线,其上任一点(x,y)处的曲率为 $\frac{1}{\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}}$ . 又此曲线上点(0,1)处的切线方程为 $y = x + 1$ ,求该曲线的方程,并求 $y =$ $y\left( x\right)$ 的极值.

解 因曲线向上凸,故 ${y}^{\prime \prime } \leq  0$ ,曲率 $K = \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( \sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\right) }^{3}} = \frac{-{y}^{\prime \prime }}{{\left( \sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\right) }^{3}}$ ,按题意有

$$
\frac{-{y}^{\prime \prime }}{{\left( \sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}\right) }^{3}} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}}},
$$

即

$$
\frac{{y}^{\prime \prime }}{1 + {y}^{\prime 2}} =  - 1
$$

令 ${y}^{\prime } = p$ ,则上述方程化为 $\frac{{p}^{\prime }}{1 + {p}^{2}} =  - 1$ ,即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{1 + {p}^{2}} =  - \mathrm{d}x,
$$

积分得 $\arctan p = {C}_{1} - x$ .

因 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 在点(0,1)处的切线方程为 $y = x + 1$ ,故 ${\left. p\right| }_{x = 0} = {\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} = 1$ . 由此条件得 $\arctan 1 = {C}_{1}$ ,即 ${C}_{1} = \frac{\pi }{4}$ . 于是

$$
{y}^{\prime } = p = \tan \left( {\frac{\pi }{4} - x}\right) ,
$$

积分得

$$
y = \ln \left\lbrack  {\cos \left( {\frac{\pi }{4} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack   + {C}_{2}.
$$

因曲线过点(0,1),故由 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1$ ,得 ${C}_{2} = 1 - \ln \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2} = 1 + \frac{1}{2}\ln 2$ . 故所求曲线的方程为

$$
y = \ln \left\lbrack  {\cos \left( {\frac{\pi }{4} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack   + 1 + \frac{1}{2}\ln 2.
$$

由于 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 是连续曲线,故 $y = \ln \left\lbrack  {\cos \left( {\frac{\pi }{4} - x}\right) }\right\rbrack   + 1 + \frac{1}{2}\ln 2$ 的定义域为 $- \frac{\pi }{2}$ $< x - \frac{\pi }{4} < \frac{\pi }{2}$ ,即 $- \frac{\pi }{4} < x < \frac{3\pi }{4}$ . 又 $\cos \left( {\frac{\pi }{4} - x}\right)  \leq  1$ . 故当 $x = \frac{\pi }{4}$ 时, $y$ 有极大值 1 $+ \frac{1}{2}\ln 2$ .

23. (1998. III) 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack 1, + \infty )$ 上连续. 若由曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ ,直线 $x = 1$ , $x = t\left( {t > 1}\right)$ 与 $x$ 轴所围成的图形绕 $x$ 轴旋转一周所成的旋转体体积为

$$
V\left( t\right)  = \frac{\pi }{3}\left\lbrack  {{t}^{2}f\left( t\right)  - f\left( 1\right) }\right\rbrack  ,
$$

试求 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 所满足的微分方程,并求该微分方程满足条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 2} = \frac{2}{9}$ 的解.

解 依题意, 有

$$
\pi {\int }_{1}^{t}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \frac{\pi }{3}\left\lbrack  {{t}^{2}f\left( t\right)  - f\left( 1\right) }\right\rbrack  ,
$$

即

$$
3{\int }_{1}^{t}{f}^{2}\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {t}^{2}f\left( t\right)  - f\left( 1\right) .
$$

两端对 $t$ 求导,得 $3{f}^{2}\left( t\right)  = {2tf}\left( t\right)  + {t}^{2}{f}^{\prime }\left( t\right)$ . 将变量 $t$ 用 $x$ 表示,即

$$
{x}^{2}{y}^{\prime } + {2xy} = 3{y}^{2}
$$

为 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 满足的微分方程.

将此方程改写为

$$
{y}^{\prime } + 2\frac{y}{x} = 3{\left( \frac{y}{x}\right) }^{2},
$$

令 $u = \frac{y}{x}$ ,则 ${y}^{\prime } = u + x{u}^{\prime }$ ,且方程成为 $x{u}^{\prime } = {3u}\left( {u - 1}\right)$ ,分离变量并积分

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}u}{u\left( {u - 1}\right) } = 3\int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{x},
$$

得

$$
\ln \left| \frac{u - 1}{u}\right|  = 3\ln \left| x\right|  + \ln {C}_{1},
$$

代入 $u = \frac{y}{x}$ ,得 $\ln \left| \frac{y - x}{y}\right|  = \ln {C}_{1}{\left| x\right| }^{3}$ ,即

$$
\frac{y - x}{y} = C{x}^{3}\;\left( {C =  \pm  {C}_{1}}\right) .
$$

由初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 2} = \frac{2}{9}$ ,得 $C =  - 1$ ,于是由 $\frac{y - x}{y} =  - {x}^{3}$ 解得

$$
y = \frac{x}{{x}^{3} + 1}
$$

22. 24. (2001. IV)设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内连续, $f\left( 1\right)  = \frac{5}{2}$ ,且对所有 $x,t \in  \left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ ,满足条件

$$
{\int }_{1}^{xt}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u = t{\int }_{1}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u + x{\int }_{1}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u,
$$

求 $f\left( x\right)$ .

解 在所给条件等式的两端对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
{tf}\left( {xt}\right)  = {tf}\left( x\right)  + {\int }_{1}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u.
$$

在上式中令 $x = 1$ ,且由 $f\left( 1\right)  = \frac{5}{2}$ ,可得

$$
{tf}\left( t\right)  = \frac{5}{2}t + {\int }_{1}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u. \tag{1}
$$

由于 $t > 0$ 时 $\frac{1}{t}{\int }_{1}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u$ 关于 $t$ 可导,故 $f\left( t\right)  = \frac{5}{2} + \frac{1}{t}{\int }_{1}^{t}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u$ 可导,于是在等式 (1) 两端对 $t$ 求导,得

$$
f\left( t\right)  + t{f}^{\prime }\left( t\right)  = \frac{5}{2} + f\left( t\right) ,
$$

即 ${f}^{\prime }\left( t\right)  = \frac{5}{2t}$ ,积分得 $f\left( t\right)  = \frac{5}{2}\ln t + C$ .

由 $f\left( 1\right)  = \frac{5}{2}$ ,得 $C = \frac{5}{2}$ . 故 $f\left( t\right)  = \frac{5}{2}\ln t + \frac{5}{2}$ ,即

$$
f\left( x\right)  = \frac{5}{2}\left( {\ln x + 1}\right) .
$$

25. (2000. II) 某湖泊的水量为 $V$ ,每年排入湖泊内含污染物 $A$ 的污水量为 $\frac{V}{6}$ ,流入湖泊内不含 $A$ 的水量为 $\frac{V}{6}$ ,流出湖泊的水量为 $\frac{V}{3}$ . 已知 1999 年年底湖中 $A$ 的含量为 $5{m}_{0}$ ,超过国家规定指标. 为了治理污染,从 2000 年初起,限定排入湖泊中含 $A$ 污水的浓度不超过 $\frac{{m}_{0}}{V}$ . 问至多需经过多少年,湖泊中污染物 $A$ 的含量降至 ${m}_{0}$ 以内? (注: 设湖水中 $A$ 的浓度是均匀的.)

解 设从 2000 年年初 (令此时 $t = 0$ ) 开始,第 $t$ 年湖泊中污染物 $A$ 的总量为 $m$ ,浓度为 $\frac{m}{V}$ ,则在时间间隔 $\left\lbrack  {t,t + \mathrm{d}t}\right\rbrack$ 内,排入湖泊中 $A$ 的量为 $\frac{{m}_{0}}{V} \cdot  \frac{V}{6}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{{m}_{0}}{6}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,流出湖泊的水中 $A$ 的量为 $\frac{m}{V} \cdot  \frac{V}{3}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{m}{3}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,因而在此时间间隔内湖泊中污染物 $A$ 的改变量

$$
\mathrm{d}m = \left( {\frac{{m}_{0}}{6} - \frac{m}{3}}\right) \mathrm{d}t.
$$

由分离变量法解得 $m = \frac{{m}_{0}}{2} - C{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{1}{3}}$ ,代入初值条件 ${\left. m\right| }_{t = 0} = 5{m}_{0}$ ,得 $C =  - \frac{9}{2}{m}_{0}$ . 于是

$$
m = \frac{{m}_{0}}{2}\left( {1 + 9{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{t}{3}}}\right) .
$$

令 $m = {m}_{0}$ ,得 $t = 6\ln 3$ ,即至多需经过 $6\ln 3$ 年,湖泊中污染物 $A$ 的含量降至 ${m}_{0}$ 以内.

26. (2003. II) 设位于第一象限的曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 过点 $\left( {\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2},\frac{1}{2}}\right)$ ,其上任一点 $P\left( {x,y}\right)$ 处的法线与 $y$ 轴的交点为 $Q$ ,且线段 ${PQ}$ 被 $x$ 轴平分.

(1)求曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的方程；

(2)已知曲线 $y = \sin x$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack$ 上的弧长为 $l$ ,试用 $l$ 表示曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的弧长 $s$ .

解 (1) 曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 在点 $P\left( {x,y}\right)$ 处的法线方程为

$$
Y - y =  - \frac{1}{{y}^{\prime }}\left( {X - x}\right) ,
$$

其中(X,Y)为法线上任意一点,令 $X = 0$ ,则

$$
Y = y + \frac{x}{{y}^{\prime }},
$$

故 $Q$ 点为 $\left( {0,y + \frac{x}{{y}^{\prime }}}\right)$ . 由题设知 $y + y + \frac{x}{{y}^{\prime }} = 0$ ,即 ${2y}\mathrm{\;d}y + x\mathrm{\;d}x = 0$ . 积分,得 ${x}^{2} + 2{y}^{2} = C$

( $C$ 为任意常数). 由 $y\left| {\;x = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2} = \frac{1}{2}}\right.$ 知 $C = 1$ ,故曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的方程为

$$
{x}^{2} + 2{y}^{2} = 1\text{.}
$$

(2)曲线 $y = \sin x$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,\pi }\right\rbrack$ 上的弧长为

$$
l = 2{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{1 + {\cos }^{2}x}\mathrm{\;d}x.
$$

曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 的参数方程为

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = \cos \theta , \\  y = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}\sin \theta , \end{array}\right.
$$

故

$$
s = {\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{{\sin }^{2}\theta  + \frac{1}{2}{\cos }^{2}\theta }\mathrm{d}\theta  = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{1 + {\sin }^{2}\theta }\mathrm{d}\theta .
$$

令 $\theta  = \frac{\pi }{2} - t$ ,则

$$
s = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}{\int }_{\frac{\pi }{2}}^{0}\sqrt{1 + {\cos }^{2}t}\left( {-\mathrm{d}t}\right)  = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sqrt{1 + {\cos }^{2}t}\mathrm{\;d}t = \frac{l}{2\sqrt{2}} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{4}l.
$$

227. (2003. I,II) 设函数 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 内具有二阶导数,且 ${y}^{\prime } \neq  0$ , $x = x\left( y\right)$ 是 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 的反函数.

( 1 )试将 $x = x\left( y\right)$ 所满足的微分方程 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{y}^{2}} + \left( {y + \sin x}\right) {\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y}\right) }^{3} = 0$ 变换为 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 满足的微分方程;

(2)求变换后的微分方程满足初值条件 $y\left( 0\right)  = 0,{y}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \frac{3}{2}$ 的解.

解 (1) 由反函数导数公式知 $\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} = \frac{1}{{y}^{\prime }}$ ,即

$$
{y}^{\prime }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} = 1.
$$

上式两端关于 $x$ 求导,得 ${y}^{\prime \prime }\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y} + \frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{y}^{2}}{\left( {y}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} = 0$ ,所以

$$
\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}x}{\mathrm{\;d}{y}^{2}} =  - \frac{\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}y}{y}^{\prime \prime }}{{\left( {y}^{\prime }\right) }^{2}} =  - \frac{{y}^{\prime \prime }}{{\left( {y}^{\prime }\right) }^{3}}.
$$

代入原微分方程, 得

$$
{y}^{\prime \prime } - y = \sin x.
$$

( * )

(2)方程(*)所对应的齐次方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = 0$ 的通解为

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}.
$$

设方程 $\left( *\right)$ 的特解为

$$
{y}^{ * } = A\cos x + B\sin x,
$$

代入方程 (*),求得 $A = 0,B =  - \frac{1}{2}$ ,故 ${y}^{ * } =  - \frac{1}{2}\sin x$ ,从而 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - y = \sin x$ 的通解

是

$$
y\left( x\right)  = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - \frac{1}{2}\sin x.
$$

由 $y\left( 0\right)  = 0,{y}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \frac{3}{2}$ ,得 ${C}_{1} = 1,{C}_{2} =  - 1$ ,故所求初值问题的解为

$$
y\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - {\mathrm{e}}^{-x} - \frac{1}{2}\sin x.
$$

28. (2004. I ) 某种飞机在机场降落时, 为了减少滑行距离, 在触地的瞬间, 飞机尾部张开减速伞以增加阻力,使飞机减速并停下. 现有一质量为 ${9000}\mathrm{\;{kg}}$ 的飞机,着陆时的水平速度为 ${700}\mathrm{\;{km}}/\mathrm{h}$ . 经测试,减速伞打开后,飞机所受的总阻力与飞机的速度成正比 (比例系数为 $k = {6.0} \times  {10}^{6}$ ). 问从着陆点算起,飞机滑行的最长距离是多少?

解法一 根据牛顿第二定律,得 $m\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}t} =  - {kv}$ ,即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{v} =  - \frac{k}{m}\mathrm{\;d}t
$$

两端积分得 $\ln v =  - \frac{k}{m}t + \ln C$ ,即 $v = C{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{k}{m}t}$ . 当 $t = 0$ 时, $v = {v}_{0}$ ,有 $C = {v}_{0}$ ,故

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = v = {v}_{0}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{k}{m}t}.
$$

于是飞机滑行的最长距离为

$$
s = {\int }_{0}^{+\infty }{v}_{0}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{k}{m}t}\mathrm{\;d}t =  - {\left. \frac{m{v}_{0}}{k}{\mathrm{e}}^{-\frac{k}{m}t}\right| }_{0}^{+\infty } = \frac{m{v}_{0}}{k} = {1.05}\left( \mathrm{\;{km}}\right) .
$$

解法二 根据牛顿第二定律, 得

$$
m\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}t} =  - {kv},
$$

又 $\frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}s} \cdot  \frac{\mathrm{d}s}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \frac{\mathrm{d}v}{\mathrm{\;d}s} \cdot  v$ ,故有

$$
\mathrm{d}s =  - \frac{m}{k}\mathrm{\;d}v,
$$

积分得 $s =  - \frac{m}{k}v + C$ . 由于 $t = 0$ 时, $s = 0,v = {v}_{0}$ ,故 $C = \frac{m}{k}{v}_{0}$ . 于是得

$$
s =  - \frac{m}{k}\left( {v - {v}_{0}}\right) .
$$

令 $v \rightarrow  0$ (当 $t \rightarrow  \infty$ 时),得

$$
s \rightarrow  \frac{m{v}_{0}}{k} = {1.05}\left( \mathrm{\;{km}}\right) .
$$

129. (2010. I ) 求微分方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } - 3{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = {2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 的通解.

解 原方程对应的齐次方程的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - {3r} + 2 = 0$ ,根为 ${r}_{1} = 1,{r}_{2} = 2$ ,故对应的齐次方程的通解是

$$
Y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}.
$$

由于自由项为 ${2x}{\mathrm{e}}^{x},\lambda  = 1$ 为特征方程的单根,故令非齐次方程的特解 ${y}^{ * } =$ $x\left( {{ax} + b}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} = \left( {a{x}^{2} + {bx}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ ,代入原方程后解得 $a =  - 1,b =  - 2$ ,故 ${y}^{ * } =  - \left( {{x}^{2} + {2x}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ . 从而所求通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - \left( {{x}^{2} + {2x}}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x},
$$

其中 ${C}_{1},{C}_{2}$ 是任意常数.

例 30. (2013. I ) 设数列 $\left\{  {a}_{n}\right\}$ 满足条件: ${a}_{0} = 3,{a}_{1} = 1,{a}_{n - 2} - n\left( {n - 1}\right) {a}_{n} = 0\left( {n \geq  2}\right)$ ,

$S\left( x\right)$ 是幂级数 $\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{a}_{n}{x}^{n}$ 的和函数.

(1)证明: ${S}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  - S\left( x\right)  = 0$ ;

(2) 求 $S\left( x\right)$ 的表达式.

解 (1)当 $n \geq  2$ 时,由

$$
{a}_{n} = \frac{{a}_{n - 2}}{n\left( {n - 1}\right) } = \frac{{a}_{n - 4}}{n\left( {n - 1}\right) \left( {n - 2}\right) \left( {n - 3}\right) } = \cdots  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{{a}_{0}}{n!}, & n = {2m}, \\  \frac{{a}_{1}}{n!}, & n = {2m} + 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

其中, $m = 1,2,\cdots$ ,易见 $\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{a}_{n}{x}^{n}$ 的收敛域是 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ ,即

$$
S\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{a}_{n}{x}^{n},\;x \in  \left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right) .
$$

于是有

$$
{S}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 1}}^{\infty }n{a}_{n}{x}^{n - 1},\;{S}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 2}}^{\infty }n\left( {n - 1}\right) {a}_{n}{x}^{n - 2},
$$

且由条件 ${a}_{n - 2} = n\left( {n - 1}\right) {a}_{n}$ ,得

$$
{S}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 2}}^{\infty }{a}_{n - 2}{x}^{n - 2} = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{a}_{n}{x}^{n} = S\left( x\right) ,
$$

所以, ${S}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  - S\left( x\right)  = 0$ .

(2)二阶常系数齐次线性微分方程 ${S}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  - S\left( x\right)  = 0$ 的特征方程为 ${r}^{2} - 1 = 0$ , 根为 ${r}_{1,2} =  \pm  1$ ,故通解为 $S\left( x\right)  = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ .

由于

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} S\left( 0\right)  = {C}_{1} + {C}_{2} = {a}_{0} = 3, \\  {S}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = {C}_{1} - {C}_{2} = {a}_{1} = 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

故 ${C}_{1} = 2,{C}_{2} = 1$ ,即 $S\left( x\right)  = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{-x},x \in  \left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ .

# 三、同济大学高等数学 试卷选编

## (一) 高等数学(上)期中考试试卷(I)


### 一、填空选择题

1. 设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1 + o\left( x\right)$ ,且 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0$ ,则下列结论正确的是 (   ).

(A) $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处不连续 (B) $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 处连续但不可导

(C) ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 0$ (D) ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 1$

2. 已知函数 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 处的导数 ${f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 2$ ,则当 ${\Delta x} \rightarrow  0$ 时, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 ${x}_{0}$ 处的微分 $\mathrm{d}y$ 是 (   ).

(A) 与 ${\Delta x}$ 等价的无穷小量 (B) 比 ${\Delta x}$ 高阶的无穷小量

(C) 比 ${\Delta x}$ 低阶的无穷小量 (D) 与 ${\Delta x}$ 同阶而非等价的无穷小量

3. 设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{3\sin \left( {x - 1}\right) }{x - 1}, & x < 1, \\  {\mathrm{e}}^{2ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{ax} + 1, & x \geq  1 \end{array}\right.$ 在 $\left( {-\infty , + \infty }\right)$ 上连续,则常数 $a =$ _____.

4. 若 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 1$ ,则 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {-x}\right) }{\ln \left( {1 + {2x}}\right) } =$ _____.

5. 曲线 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin {2t}, \\  y = {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\cos t \end{array}\right.$ 在 $t = 0$ 所对应点处的切线方程为_____.

### 二、计算题

1. 求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - \cos \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}\right) }{\ln \left( {1 - 3{x}^{2}}\right) }$ .

2. 已知函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\tan x}\sin \left( {\cos x}\right)$ ,求 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ .

3. 求 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left( \frac{\tan x}{x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{1 - \cos x}}$ .

4. 设可微函数 $f\left( x\right)  > 0,y = \ln f\left( {x}^{2}\right)$ ,求 $\mathrm{d}y$ .

5. 设函数 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 由方程 $\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + y}\right)  = {x}^{3}y + \sin x$ 确定,求 ${\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right| }_{x = 0}$ .

三、求函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\left( 1 + x\right) }^{\frac{x}{\tan \left( {x - \frac{\pi }{4}}\right) }}$ 在区间 $\left( {0,\pi }\right)$ 内的间断点,并判断间断点类型.

四、已知函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{{x}^{3}}{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}}$ ,求

(1)函数单调区间,函数极值；

(2)函数图形的凹凸区间,函数图形的拐点.

五、求函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{1 + x}$ 在 $x = 0$ 处带拉格朗日余项的 $n$ 阶泰勒展开式.

六、讨论曲线 $y = 4\ln x + k$ 与曲线 $y = {4x} + {\ln }^{4}x$ 的交点个数 ( $k$ 为常数).

七、设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {1,2}\right\rbrack$ 上三阶可导,且 $f\left( 1\right)  = f\left( 2\right)  = 0$ ,令 $F\left( x\right)  = {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}$ $f\left( x\right)$ . 证明: ${F}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ 在区间(1,2)内至少有一个零点.

### 参考答案

一、填空选择题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}f\left( x\right)  = 0 = f\left( 0\right) ,{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x} = 1$ . 故选 (D).

2. $\mathrm{d}y = {f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right) {\Delta x} = {2\Delta x},\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{{\Delta x} \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\Delta x} = 2$ . 故选 (D).

3. $f\left( {1}^{ - }\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}\frac{3\sin \left( {x - 1}\right) }{x - 1} = 3,f\left( {1}^{ + }\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ + }}}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2ax} - {\mathrm{e}}^{ax} + 1}\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{2a} - {\mathrm{e}}^{a} + 1$ . 根据条件 $f\left( {1}^{ - }\right)  = f\left( {1}^{ + }\right)  = f\left( 1\right)$ ,解得 $a = \ln 2$ .

4. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {-x}\right) }{\ln \left( {1 + {2x}}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {-x}\right) }{2x} = \frac{1}{2}\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{x} + \frac{f\left( {-x}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{-x}}\right\rbrack   = 1$ .

5. ${\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right| }_{t = 0} = {\left. \frac{\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}t}}{\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t}}\right| }_{t = 0} = {\left. \frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\cos t - {\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin t}{{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\sin {2t} + 2{\mathrm{e}}^{t}\cos {2t}}\right| }_{t = 0} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,当 $t = 0$ 时, $x = 0,y = 1$ . 所求切线为 $y = \frac{1}{2}x + 1$ .

二、计算题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{1 - \cos \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}\right) }{\ln \left( {1 - 3{x}^{2}}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\frac{1}{2}{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1\right) }^{2}}{-3{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\frac{1}{2}{\left( 2x\right) }^{2}}{-3{x}^{2}} =  - \frac{2}{3}$ .

2. ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\tan x}{\sec }^{2}x\sin \left( {\cos x}\right)  - {\mathrm{e}}^{\tan x}\cos \left( {\cos x}\right) \sin x,{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = \sin 1$ .

3. ${\left( \frac{\tan x}{x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{1 - \cos x}} = {\left\lbrack  {\left( 1 + \frac{\tan x - x}{x}\right) }^{\frac{x}{\tan x - x}}\right\rbrack  }^{\frac{\tan x - x}{x\left( {1 - \cos x}\right) }}$ ,

由于

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\tan x - x}{x\left( {1 - \cos x}\right) } = 2\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\tan x - x}{{x}^{3}} = 2\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\sec }^{2}x - 1}{3{x}^{2}} = 2\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\tan }^{2}x}{3{x}^{2}} = \frac{2}{3},
$$

因此

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left( \frac{\tan x}{x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{1 - \cos x}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{2}{3}}.
$$

4. $\mathrm{d}y = \frac{1}{f\left( {x}^{2}\right) }\mathrm{d}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {x}^{2}\right) }\right\rbrack   = \frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}^{2}\right) }{f\left( {x}^{2}\right) }\mathrm{d}\left( {x}^{2}\right)  = \frac{{2x}{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}^{2}\right) }{f\left( {x}^{2}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$ .

5. 方程 $\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + y}\right)  = {x}^{3}y + \sin x$ 两端对 $x$ 求导,得

$$
\frac{{2x} + \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}}{{x}^{2} + y} = 3{x}^{2}y + {x}^{3}\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} + \cos x,
$$

注意到 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = 1$ ,于是 ${\left. \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right| }_{x = 0} = 1$ .

三、间断点为 $x = \frac{\pi }{4},\frac{3\pi }{4},\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \frac{\pi }{4}}}f\left( x\right)  = 0,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \frac{\pi }{4}}}f\left( x\right)  =  + \infty ,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \frac{3\pi }{4}}}f\left( x\right)  = 1$ . 因此 $x = \frac{\pi }{4}$ 和 $x = \frac{3\pi }{4}$ 分别为 $f\left( x\right)$ 的无穷间断点和可去间断点.

四、(1) 令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{{x}^{2}\left( {x - 3}\right) }{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{3}} = 0$ 得 $x = 0,3$ ,在 $\left( {-\infty ,0}\right) ,\left( {0,1}\right)$ 和 $\left( {3, + \infty }\right)$ 内, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,在(1,3)内, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ . 故函数单调增加区间为 $\left( {-\infty ,1}\right)$ 和 $\lbrack 3, + \infty )$ ,单调减少区间为 $(1,3\rbrack$ ,极小值为 $f\left( 3\right)  = \frac{27}{4}$ ,无极大值.

(2)令 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{6x}{{\left( x - 1\right) }^{4}} = 0$ 得 $x = 0$ ,在 $\left( {-\infty ,0}\right)$ 内, ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,在(0,1)和 $\left( {1, + \infty }\right)$ 内, ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ . 故函数图形的凸区间为 $( - \infty ,0\rbrack$ ,凹区间为 $\lbrack 0,1)$ 和 $\left( {1, + \infty }\right)$ ,函数图形的拐点为(0,0).

五、 ${f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( x\right)  = \frac{{\left( -1\right) }^{n}n!}{{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{n + 1}},{f}^{\left( n\right) }\left( 0\right)  = {\left( -1\right) }^{n}n!$ . 所求的 $n$ 阶泰勒展开式为

$f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{k = 0}}^{n}{\left( -1\right) }^{k}{x}^{k} + \frac{{\left( -1\right) }^{n + 1}}{{\left( 1 + \xi \right) }^{n + 2}}{x}^{n + 1}\;$ (其中 $\xi$ 介于 0 与 $x$ 之间).

六、令 $f\left( x\right)  = {4x} + {\ln }^{4}x - 4\ln x - k\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{4}{x}\left( {x + {\ln }^{3}x - 1}\right)$ . 记 $g\left( x\right)  =$ $x + {\ln }^{3}x - 1$ ,则当 $x > 0$ 时, ${g}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 1 + \frac{3{\ln }^{2}x}{x} > 0$ ,即 $g\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内单调增加. 注意到 $g\left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,因此当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, $g\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,当 $x > 1$ 时, $g\left( x\right)  > 0$ .

于是,当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,当 $x > 1$ 时, ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ . 即当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, $f\left( x\right)$ 单调减少,当 $x > 1$ 时, $f\left( x\right)$ 单调增加.

又 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  =  + \infty ,f\left( 1\right)  = 4 - k,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  =  + \infty$ ,因此当 $f\left( 1\right)  < 0$ ,即 $k > 4$ 时, $f\left( x\right)$ 有 2 个零点,此时两条曲线的交点为 2 个; 当 $f\left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,即 $k = 4$ 时, $f\left( x\right)$ 仅有 1 个零点 $x = 1$ ,此时两条曲线的交点只有 1 个; 当 $f\left( 1\right)  > 0$ ,即 $k < 4$ 时, $f\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,此时两条曲线没有交点.

七、 $F\left( 1\right)  = F\left( 2\right)  = 0$ ,由罗尔定理可知,存在 ${\xi }_{1} \in  \left( {1,2}\right)$ ,使得 ${F}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{1}\right)  = 0$ .

${F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 2\left( {x - 1}\right) f\left( x\right)  + {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ ,于是 ${F}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  = {F}^{\prime }\left( {\xi }_{1}\right)  = 0$ ,由罗尔定理可知,存在 ${\xi }_{2} \in  \left( {1,{\xi }_{1}}\right)  \subset  \left( {1,2}\right)$ ,使得 ${F}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\xi }_{2}\right)  = 0$ .

${F}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  = {2f}\left( x\right)  + 4\left( {x - 1}\right) {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  + {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)$ ,于是 ${F}^{\prime \prime }\left( 1\right)  = {F}^{\prime \prime }\left( {\xi }_{2}\right)  = 0$ ,由罗尔定理可知,存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {1,{\xi }_{2}}\right)  \subset  \left( {1,2}\right)$ ,使得 ${F}^{\prime \prime \prime }\left( \xi \right)  = 0$ .

## (二)高等数学(上)期中考试试卷(Ⅱ)



### 一、填空题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {\sqrt{{n}^{2} + {4n} + 3} - \sqrt{{n}^{2} + n + 2}}\right)  =$ _____.

2. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left( \frac{1 - {2x}}{1 + x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{x}} =$ _____.

3. 已知 $y = x\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right)$ ,则它在 $x = 1$ 处的微分 ${\left. \mathrm{d}y\right| }_{x = 1} =$ _____.

4. 若函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-1,4}\right\rbrack$ 上可导, $f\left( {-1}\right)  = 2,f\left( 4\right)  =  - 1$ ,则在区间 $( - 1$ , 4) 内至少有一点 $\xi$ ,使得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  =$ _____.

### 二、选择题
5. 极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}{x}_{n}$ 存在是数列 $\left\{  {x}_{n}\right\}$ 单调有界的 (   ).

(A) 充分条件 (B) 必要条件 (C) 充要条件 (D) 无关条件

6. 对于区间 $I$ 上的二阶可导函数 $f\left( x\right) ,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ 是函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $I$ 上单调减少的(   ).

(A) 充分条件 (B) 必要条件 (C) 充要条件 (D) 无关条件

7. 函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 可导的充分条件是 (   ).

(A) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {x}^{2}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{{x}^{2} - 0}$ 存在 (B) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {x}^{3}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{{x}^{3}}$ 存在

(C) ${f}_{ - }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ 与 ${f}_{ + }^{\prime }\left( 0\right)$ 存在 (D) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {\sin x}\right) }{x}$ 存在

8. 已知 $f\left( x\right)  = x\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} - 2}\right) \left( {{x}^{2} - 4}\right)$ ,导函数 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-1,2}\right\rbrack$ 上零点的个数至少为 (   ) .

(A) 1 个 (B) 2 个 (C) 3 个 (D) 4 个

### 三、计算题

1. 计算极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}n\left( {1 - \cos \frac{1}{2\sqrt{n}}}\right)$ .

2. 求由参数方程 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} x = t{\mathrm{e}}^{t}, \\  y = {\mathrm{e}}^{2t} + 1 \end{array}\right.$ 所确定的函数 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 的二阶导数 $\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}}$ .

3. 求极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sqrt[3]{1 + {x}^{3}} - \sqrt{1 - 3{x}^{2}}}{{\sin }^{2}x}$ .

4. 函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\lbrack 0, + \infty )$ 上有二阶导数,且 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0,{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  > 0$ . 证明: $\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x}$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调增加.

三、求曲线 $2{x}^{2} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x - y} = {y}^{2} + 2$ 在点(1,1)处的切线方程,并求由该方程所确定函数 $y = y\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 1$ 处的二阶导数 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 1}$ .

四、讨论 $y = x\sqrt{x - 1}$ 的单调性与函数图形的凹凸性,并求出曲线的拐点.

五、求函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \tan \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}\right)$ 带佩亚诺余项的二阶麦克劳林公式,并计算极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\tan \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}\right)  - {2x}}{{x}^{2}}.$

六、设 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\lbrack 1, + \infty )$ 上单调,证明 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)$ 存在的充要条件是 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\lbrack 1, + \infty )$ 上有界.

### 参考答案



1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\left( {\sqrt{{n}^{2} + {4n} + 3} - \sqrt{{n}^{2} + n + 2}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{{3n} + 1}{\sqrt{{n}^{2} + {4n} + 3} + \sqrt{{n}^{2} + n + 2}}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}\frac{3 + \frac{1}{n}}{\sqrt{1 + \frac{4}{n} + \frac{3}{{n}^{2}}} + \sqrt{1 + \frac{1}{n} + \frac{2}{{n}^{2}}}} = \frac{3}{2}\text{.}
$$

2. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left( \frac{1 - {2x}}{1 + x}\right) }^{\frac{1}{x}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}{\left\lbrack  {\left( 1 + \frac{-{3x}}{1 + x}\right) }^{\frac{1 + x}{-{3x}}}\right\rbrack  }^{\frac{-3}{1 + x}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-3}$ .

3. ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = {\left. \left( \ln \left( {x}^{2} + 1\right)  + \frac{2{x}^{2}}{{x}^{2} + 1}\right) \right| }_{x = 1} = 1 + \ln 2,{\left. \mathrm{d}y\right| }_{x = 1} = \left( {1 + \ln 2}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

4. ${f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  = \frac{f\left( 4\right)  - f\left( {-1}\right) }{4 - \left( {-1}\right) } =  - \frac{3}{5}$ .

5. 由于单调有界数列必有极限, 故选 (B).

6. 由于 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ 只能得到 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 单调减少 (例如 $y =  - {x}^{2}$ 满足条件但没有单调性), 故选 (D).

7. 由于

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {x}^{2}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{{x}^{2} - 0} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{x - 0},
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {x}^{3}\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{{x}^{3}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }{x - 0},
$$

${f}^{\prime } - \left( 0\right)$ 与 ${f}^{\prime } + \left( 0\right)$ 存在而不相等时, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 不可导, $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {\sin x}\right) }{x}$ 存在且 $f\left( 0\right)$ 不存在或不等于 0 时, $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 0$ 不可导. 故选 (B).

8. 由于 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {-1,2}\right\rbrack$ 上有 5 个零点 $x =  - 1,0,1,\sqrt{2},2$ ,由罗尔定理可知在 $\left( {-1,0}\right) ,\left( {0,1}\right) ,\left( {1,\sqrt{2}}\right)$ 和 $\left( {\sqrt{2},2}\right)$ 内各至少有一个零点. 故选 (D). 二、计算下列各题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}n\left( {1 - \cos \frac{1}{2\sqrt{n}}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}n \cdot  \frac{1}{2}{\left( \frac{1}{2\sqrt{n}}\right) }^{2} = \frac{1}{8}$ .

2. $\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x} = \frac{2{\mathrm{e}}^{2t}}{{\mathrm{e}}^{t} + t{\mathrm{e}}^{t}} = \frac{2{\mathrm{e}}^{t}}{1 + t},\frac{{\mathrm{d}}^{2}y}{\mathrm{\;d}{x}^{2}} = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}\left( \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{\;d}x}\right)  = \frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}t}\left( \frac{2{\mathrm{e}}^{t}}{t + 1}\right) /\frac{\mathrm{d}x}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \frac{2t}{{\left( t + 1\right) }^{3}}$ .

3. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\sqrt[3]{1 + {x}^{3}} - \sqrt{1 - 3{x}^{2}}}{{\sin }^{2}x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\left( 1 + {x}^{3}\right) }^{\frac{1}{3}} - {\left( 1 - 3{x}^{2}\right) }^{\frac{1}{2}}}{{x}^{2}}$

$$
= \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{x}^{2}{\left( 1 + {x}^{3}\right) }^{-\frac{2}{3}} + {3x}{\left( 1 - 3{x}^{2}\right) }^{-\frac{1}{2}}}{2x} = \frac{3}{2}.
$$

4. 记 $F\left( x\right)  = \frac{f\left( x\right) }{x}$ ,则

$$
{F}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{x{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - f\left( x\right) }{{x}^{2}} = \frac{x{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - \left\lbrack  {f\left( x\right)  - f\left( 0\right) }\right\rbrack  }{{x}^{2}}
$$

$$
= \frac{x{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  - x{f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) }{{x}^{2}} = \frac{\left( {x - \xi }\right) {f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right) }{x} > 0,
$$

其中 $\xi ,\eta  \in  \left( {0,x}\right)$ ,故 $\frac{f\left( x\right) }{x}$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调增加.

三、在等式 $2{x}^{2} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x - y} = {y}^{2} + 2$ 两端分别对 $x$ 求导得

$$
{4x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x - y}\left( {1 - {y}^{\prime }}\right)  = {\left. 2y{y}^{\prime },\;{y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = {\left. \frac{{4x} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x - y}}{{2y} + {\mathrm{e}}^{x - y}}\right| }_{\left( 1,1\right) } = \frac{5}{3}.
$$

所求切线方程为

$$
y - 1 = \frac{5}{3}\left( {x - 1}\right) ,
$$

即 ${5x} - {3y} - 2 = 0$ . 等式两端再次对 $x$ 求导得 $4 + {\mathrm{e}}^{x - y}{\left( 1 - {y}^{\prime }\right) }^{2} - {y}^{\prime \prime }{\mathrm{e}}^{x - y} = 2\left( {{y}^{\prime 2} + y{y}^{\prime \prime }}\right)$ , 由 $x = y = 1$ 以及 ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = \frac{5}{3}$ ,得到 ${\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 1} =  - \frac{10}{27}$ .

四、显然函数定义域为 $x \geq  1$ . 由 ${y}^{\prime } = \frac{{3x} - 2}{2\sqrt{x - 1}} > 0$ 知函数在 $\left( {1, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调增加.

令 ${y}^{\prime \prime } = \frac{{3x} - 4}{4{\left( x - 1\right) }^{3/2}} = 0$ 得 $x = \frac{4}{3}$ . 当 $1 < x < \frac{4}{3}$ 时, ${y}^{\prime \prime } < 0$ ,曲线是凸的; 当 $x > \frac{4}{3}$ 时, ${y}^{\prime \prime } > 0$ ,曲线是凹的. 曲线的拐点为 $\left( {\frac{4}{3},\frac{4\sqrt{3}}{9}}\right)$ .

五、 $f\left( 0\right)  = 0,{f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right)  = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}{\sec }^{2}\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}\right) {\left. \right| }_{x = 0} = 2$ ,

$$
{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right)  = {\left. \left\lbrack  4{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}{\sec }^{2}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1\right)  + 8{\mathrm{e}}^{4x}{\sec }^{2}\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1\right) \tan \left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1\right) \right\rbrack  \right| }_{x = 0} = 4,
$$

$$
f\left( x\right)  = f\left( 0\right)  + {f}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) x + \frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( 0\right) }{2}{x}^{2} + o\left( {x}^{2}\right)  = {2x} + 2{x}^{2} + o\left( {x}^{2}\right) .
$$

$$
\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{\tan \left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} - 1}\right)  - {2x}}{{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{2{x}^{2} + o\left( {x}^{2}\right) }{{x}^{2}} = 2.
$$

六、不妨设 $f\left( x\right)$ 单调增加.

必要性:

当 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)$ 存在时,记 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = A$ ,则 $f\left( 1\right)  \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  A$ ,即 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\lbrack 1, + \infty )$ 上有界.

充分性:

当 $f\left( x\right)$ 在区间 $\lbrack 1, + \infty )$ 上有界时,则 $f\left( n\right)$ 是单调增加且有界的数列,故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}f\left( n\right)$ 存在,记 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}f\left( n\right)  = A$ .

由单调增加得 $f\left( \left\lbrack  x\right\rbrack  \right)  \leq  f\left( x\right)  \leq  f\left( {\left\lbrack  x\right\rbrack   + 1}\right)$ ,而 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( \left\lbrack  x\right\rbrack  \right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( {\left\lbrack  x\right\rbrack   + 1}\right)  =$ $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}f\left( n\right)  = A$ ,由夹逼准则可知 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)$ 存在,且 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow   + \infty }}f\left( x\right)  = A$ .

## (三)高等数学(上)期末考试试卷(Ⅰ)



### 一、填空题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{\ln x} =$ _____.

2. 曲线 ${xy} = 2$ 在点(1,2)的曲率为_____.

3. 函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {x}^{3} - {3x} + 1$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack$ 上的最大值为_____.

4. $\int \frac{\ln \tan x}{{\cos }^{2}x\tan x}\mathrm{\;d}x =$ _____.

5. ${\int }_{-{4\pi }}^{4\pi }\left( {x + 1}\right) \left| {\sin x}\right| \mathrm{d}x =$ _____.

6. 微分方程 ${y}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}^{\prime } + {2y} = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\cos x$ 的特解形式可表示为 ${y}^{ * } =$ _____(只需写出形式, 不必确定其中系数).

### 二、选择题

1. 当 $x \rightarrow   + \infty$ 时,函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{x}\sin x$ 是 (   ).

(A) 无穷小 (B) 无穷大

(C) 有界量, 但不是无穷小 (D) 无界的, 但不是无穷大

2. 设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ (其中 $b - a = 1$ ) 上具有二阶导数,且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,下列不等式正确的是 (   ).

(A) ${f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( a\right)  < f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)$ (B) ${f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  < f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( a\right)$

(C) $f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( a\right)$ (D) ${f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  < f\left( a\right)  - f\left( b\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( a\right)$

3. 函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {a,b}\right\rbrack$ 上(   ).

(A) 可导必有界 (B) 有界必可积

(C) 可积必连续 (D) 连续必可导

4. 具有特解 $y = x{\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 及 $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{-x}$ 的三阶常系数齐次线性微分方程是 (   ).

(A) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime } - y = 0$ (B) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime \prime } + {y}^{\prime } + y = 0$

(C) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime } + y = 0$ (D) ${y}^{\prime \prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime \prime } - {y}^{\prime } - y = 0$

### 三、解答题

1. 求极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}}\right)$ .

2. 设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\left( {x}^{2} + 2\right) }^{{x}^{2} - 1}$ ,求 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)$ .

3. 计算反常积分 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{x + 1}{x\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}x$ .

4. 求由圆 ${\left( x - 5\right) }^{2} + {y}^{2} = {16}$ 所围图形绕 $y$ 轴旋转而成的旋转体体积.

四、设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 2$ 处连续,且 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {2 - x}\right)  - 3}{2\sin x} = 5$ . 试证 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 2$ 处可导,并求曲线 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 在横坐标为 $x = 2$ 的点处的切线方程.

五、设函数 $f\left( x\right)  = {\int }_{0}^{x}\frac{\sin t}{\pi  - t}\mathrm{\;d}t$ ,求定积分 ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

六、设函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 内可导,且满足 ${\int }_{0}^{1}f\left( {tx}\right) \mathrm{d}t = {2f}\left( x\right)  + 1$ 及 $f\left( 1\right)  = 1$ , 求 $f\left( x\right)$ .

七、证明: 当 $x > 0$ 时, $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x \geq  {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}$ .

### 参考答案

一、填空题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{\left( 1 + x\right) }^{\ln x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {0}^{ + }}}{\left\lbrack  {\left( 1 + x\right) }^{\frac{1}{x}}\right\rbrack  }^{x\ln x} = {\mathrm{e}}^{0} = 1$ .

2. ${\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 1} =  - {\left. \frac{1}{{x}^{2}}\right| }_{x = 1} =  - 1,{\left. {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }_{x = 1} = {\left. \frac{2}{{x}^{3}}\right| }_{x = 1} = 2$ ,所求曲率

$$
K = {\left. \frac{\left| {y}^{\prime \prime }\right| }{{\left( 1 + {y}^{\prime 2}\right) }^{3/2}}\right| }_{x = 1} = \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}.
$$

3. 令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = 3{x}^{2} - 3 = 0$ 得 $x = 1,f\left( 0\right)  = 1,f\left( 1\right)  =  - 1,f\left( 2\right)  = 3$ ,所求最大值为 $f\left( 2\right)  = 3$ .

4. $\int \frac{\ln \tan x}{{\cos }^{2}x\tan x}\mathrm{\;d}x = \int \frac{\ln \tan x}{\tan x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\tan x}\right)  = \frac{1}{2}{\left( \ln \tan x\right) }^{2} + C$ .

5. ${\int }_{-{4\pi }}^{4\pi }\left( {x + 1}\right) \left| {\sin x}\right| \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{-{4\pi }}^{4\pi }x\left| {\sin x}\right| \mathrm{d}x + {\int }_{-{4\pi }}^{4\pi }\left| {\sin x}\right| \mathrm{d}x = 2{\int }_{0}^{4\pi }\left| {\sin x}\right| \mathrm{d}x =$ ${16}{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = {16}.$

6. 由于 $- 1 + \mathrm{i}$ 为特征方程的根,因此可设 ${y}^{ * } = x{\mathrm{e}}^{-x}\left( {a\cos x + b\sin x}\right)$ .

二、选择题

1. 因为 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}f\left( {n\pi }\right)  = 0,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{n \rightarrow  \infty }}f\left( {{2n\pi } + \frac{\pi }{2}}\right)  =  + \infty$ . 故选 (D).

2. 由拉格朗日中值定理可知,存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {a,b}\right)$ ,满足 $f\left( b\right)  - f\left( a\right)  = \left( {b - a}\right) {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  =$ ${f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)$ . 又根据条件可知 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 单调减少,因此 ${f}^{\prime }\left( b\right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right)  < {f}^{\prime }\left( a\right)$ . 故选 (B).

3. 由于可导必连续,在闭区间上连续的函数一定有界. 故选 (A).

4. 根据条件, $r =  - 1$ 为特征方程的单根, $r = 1$ 为特征方程的二重根,因此特征方程为 $\left( {r + 1}\right) {\left( r - 1\right) }^{2} = {r}^{3} - {r}^{2} - r + 1 = 0$ . 故选 (C).

 三、解答题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{1}{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}}\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - x - 1}{x\left( {{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}\right) } = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - x - 1}{{x}^{2}} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - 1}{2x} = \frac{1}{2}$ .

2. $f\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 2}\right) },{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = {\mathrm{e}}^{\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 2}\right) }\left\lbrack  {{2x}\ln \left( {{x}^{2} + 2}\right)  + \frac{{2x}\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) }{{x}^{2} + 2}}\right\rbrack$ , 故 ${f}^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  = 2\ln 3$ .

3. ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{x + 1}{x\left( {{x}^{2} + 1}\right) }\mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\left( {\frac{1}{x} - \frac{x - 1}{{x}^{2} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\left\lbrack  \ln \frac{x}{\sqrt{{x}^{2} + 1}} + \arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{+\infty } = \frac{\pi }{4} +$

$\frac{1}{2}\ln 2$ .

4. 将曲线方程写成 $x = 5 \pm  \sqrt{{16} - {y}^{2}}$ ,因此所求体积为

$$
V = \pi {\int }_{-4}^{4}{\left( 5 + \sqrt{{16} - {y}^{2}}\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}y - \pi {\int }_{-4}^{4}{\left( 5 - \sqrt{{16} - {y}^{2}}\right) }^{2}\mathrm{\;d}y = {20\pi }{\int }_{-4}^{4}\sqrt{{16} - {y}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}y
$$

$$
= {40\pi }{\int }_{0}^{4}\sqrt{{16} - {y}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}y,
$$

作换元 $y = 4\sin u$ 得, $V = {640\pi }{\int }_{0}^{\frac{\pi }{2}}{\cos }^{2}u\mathrm{\;d}u = {160}{\pi }^{2}$ .

四、由条件得 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\left\lbrack  {f\left( {2 - x}\right)  - 3}\right\rbrack   = 0$ ,即 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  2}}f\left( x\right)  = 3$ ,再由连续性得 $f\left( 2\right)  = 3$ . 而

$$
{f}^{\prime }\left( 2\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {2 - x}\right)  - f\left( 2\right) }{-x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {2 - x}\right)  - 3}{2\sin x} \cdot  \frac{2\sin x}{-x} =  - {10},
$$

即 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $x = 2$ 处可导. 所求切线方程为 $y - 3 =  - {10}\left( {x - 2}\right)$ ,即 $y =  - {10x} + {23}$ .

五、 ${\int }_{0}^{\pi }f\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\left\lbrack  xf\left( x\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{\pi } - {\int }_{0}^{\pi }x{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \mathrm{d}x = \pi {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\frac{\sin t}{\pi  - t}\mathrm{\;d}t - {\int }_{0}^{\pi }\frac{x\sin x}{\pi  - x}\mathrm{\;d}x =$

${\int }_{0}^{\pi }\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = 2$ .

六、作换元 $t = \frac{u}{x}$ ,则 ${\int }_{0}^{1}f\left( {tx}\right) \mathrm{d}t = \frac{1}{x}{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u$ ,故原等式为

$$
{\int }_{0}^{x}f\left( u\right) \mathrm{d}u = {2xf}\left( x\right)  + x,
$$

上式两端对 $x$ 求导,得 $f\left( x\right)  = {2f}\left( x\right)  + {2x}{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  + 1$ ,故 $y = f\left( x\right)$ 满足微分方程

$$
\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {y}^{\prime } =  - \frac{y + 1}{2x}, \\  {\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = 1, \end{array}\right.
$$

分离变量后两端积分, 得

$$
\int \frac{\mathrm{d}y}{y + 1} =  - \int \frac{\mathrm{d}x}{2x},
$$

即 $\ln \left( {y + 1}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{2}\ln x + C$ ,根据条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 1} = 1$ 解得 $C = \ln 2$ . 因此 $y = f\left( x\right)  = \frac{2}{\sqrt{x}} - 1$ .

七、记 $f\left( x\right)  = \ln x - \frac{x - 1}{x + 1}\left( {x > 0}\right)$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \frac{1}{x} - \frac{2}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}} = \frac{{x}^{2} + 1}{{\left( x + 1\right) }^{2}} > 0$ ,因此 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left( {0, + \infty }\right)$ 上单调增加.

注意到 $f\left( 1\right)  = 0$ ,因此当 $0 < x < 1$ 时, $f\left( x\right)  < 0$ ,即 $\ln x < \frac{x - 1}{x + 1}$ 或 $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x > (x$ $- 1{)}^{2}$ ; 当 $x > 1$ 时, $f\left( x\right)  > 0$ ,即 $\ln x > \frac{x - 1}{x + 1}$ 或 $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x > {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}$ .

综合可得,当 $x > 0$ 时, $\left( {{x}^{2} - 1}\right) \ln x \geq  {\left( x - 1\right) }^{2}$ .

## (四)高等数学(上)期末考试试卷(Ⅱ)



### 一、填空选择题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( \frac{x + 1}{x - 2}\right) }^{x} =$ _____.

2. 若极限 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {{x}_{0} - {2h}}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{h} = 3$ ,则 ${f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  =$ _____.

3. ${\int }_{-2}^{2}\left( {{x}^{2} + {x}^{3}\sqrt{4 - {x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x =$ _____.

4. $\int \sin x{\mathrm{e}}^{2\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x =$ _____.

5. 微分方程 $4{y}^{\prime \prime } - 4{y}^{\prime } + y = 0$ 的通解为 $y =$ _____.

6. 记 ${I}_{1} = {\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\sin }^{4}x\mathrm{\;d}x,{I}_{2} = {\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\sin }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x,{I}_{3} = {\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x,{I}_{4} = {\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }x{\sin }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ ,则这 4 项积分的大小关系为(   ).

(A) ${I}_{2} > {I}_{1} > {I}_{3} > {I}_{4}$ (B) ${I}_{3} > {I}_{2} > {I}_{1} > {I}_{4}$

(C) ${I}_{4} > {I}_{1} > {I}_{3} > {I}_{2}$ (D) ${I}_{1} > {I}_{2} > {I}_{4} > {I}_{3}$

7. 下列反常积分中收敛的是(   ).

(A) ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 2}\mathrm{\;d}x$ (B) ${\int }_{\mathrm{e}}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{x\sqrt{\ln x + 2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$

(C) ${\int }_{-\infty }^{+\infty }\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x$ (D) ${\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{1}{x - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x$

8. 若函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right)  - \ln 2}{{x}^{3} - 1}, & x \neq  1, \\  a, & x = 1 \end{array}\right.$ 在 $x = 1$ 连续,则常数 $a =$ (   ).

(A) $\frac{2}{3}$ (B) $- \frac{2}{3}$

(C) $- \frac{1}{3}$ (D) $\frac{1}{3}$

### 二、计算题

1. 计算由曲线 $y = \sqrt{x + 2}$ 与直线 $x - {3y} + 4 = 0$ 所围平面图形的面积.

2. 若函数 $u\left( x\right)$ 与 $v\left( x\right)$ 具有 $n$ 阶导数,试写出计算函数 $u\left( x\right) v\left( x\right)$ 的 $n$ 阶导数的莱布尼茨公式,并求 $x{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}$ 的 10 阶导数.

3. 求函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \left( {{x}^{2} + x - 5}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x}$ 的单调区间以及函数的极值.

4. 计算反常积分 ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) }{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x$ .

5. 求微分方程 $\left\{  \begin{array}{l} {y}^{\prime \prime } + 2{y}^{\prime } - {3y} = 1, \\  {\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{2}{3},{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} =  - 7 \end{array}\right.$ 的解.

### 三、解答题

三、一薄片铅直放入水中,其形状与位置由曲线 $x = {y}^{2} - 1$ 与直线 $x - {2y} - 2 = 0$ 所围成的图形确定,其中 $x$ 轴平行于水面且位于水面下 $1\mathrm{\;m}$ 深处, $y$ 轴铅直向上,试求该薄片的一侧所受的水压力 (假设水的密度为 $\mu$ ).

四、求积分 ${\int }_{0}^{1}\sqrt{x}\ln \left( {x + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x$ .

五、(1) 试求常数 $a,b$ ,使得函数 $f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {x}^{2}, & 0 \leq  x \leq  1, \\  {ax} + b, & 1 < x \leq  2 \end{array}\right.$ 在区间 $\left\lbrack  {0,2}\right\rbrack$ 上可导; (2) 由该曲线段绕 $y$ 轴旋转形成一个容器,如果每单位时间向该容器均匀地注入体积为 ${v}_{0}$ 的水,试求该容器自开始注入水至溢出前水深为 $h$ 时水面的上升速度.

六、要建一个容积为 14 、侧面为圆柱面、顶部接着一个半球形的仓库 (不含底部). 已知顶部单位面积的造价是其侧面圆柱面部分造价的 3 倍, 试求该仓库的底圆半径, 使得该仓库的造价最省.

七、函数 $f\left( x\right)$ 在 $\left\lbrack  {{x}_{0}, + \infty }\right)$ 上具有二阶导数,并且 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ . 对于任意 $x > {x}_{0}$ ,由拉格朗日中值定理,存在 $\xi  \in  \left( {{x}_{0},x}\right)$ ,使得 $f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left( {x - {x}_{0}}\right)$ . 证明: $\xi$ 定义了 $\left( {{x}_{0}, + \infty }\right)$ 内的一个单调增加函数.

### 参考答案

 一、填空选择题

1. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left( \frac{x + 1}{x - 2}\right) }^{x} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  \infty }}{\left\lbrack  {\left( 1 + \frac{3}{x - 2}\right) }^{\frac{x - 2}{3}}\right\rbrack  }^{\frac{3x}{x - 2}} = {\mathrm{e}}^{3}$ .

2. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {{x}_{0} - {2h}}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{h} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{h \rightarrow  0}}\frac{f\left( {{x}_{0} - {2h}}\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{-{2h}} \cdot  \left( {-2}\right)  =  - 2{f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = 3$ ,得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( {x}_{0}\right)  =  - \frac{3}{2}.$

3. ${\int }_{-2}^{2}\left( {{x}^{2} + {x}^{3}\sqrt{4 - {x}^{2}}}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{-2}^{2}{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{3}{x}^{3}\right\rbrack  }_{-2}^{2} = \frac{16}{3}$ .

4. $\int \sin x{\mathrm{e}}^{2\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}x =  - \int {\mathrm{e}}^{2\cos x}\mathrm{\;d}\left( {\cos x}\right)  =  - \frac{1}{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{2\cos x} + C$ .

5. 特征方程为 $4{r}^{2} - {4r} + 1 = 0$ ,得重根 ${r}_{1,2} = \frac{1}{2}$ ,因此通解为 $y = {\mathrm{e}}^{\frac{1}{2}x}\left( {{C}_{1}x + {C}_{2}}\right)$ .

6. 因为 $\left| x\right|  \geq  \left| {\sin x}\right| ,1 \geq  \left| {\sin x}\right|$ ,所以 ${\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}x > {\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\sin }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x > {\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }{\sin }^{4}x\mathrm{\;d}x >$ $0 = {\int }_{-\pi }^{\pi }x{\sin }^{2}x\mathrm{\;d}x$ . 故选 (B).

7. ${\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{{x}^{2} + 2}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\arctan \frac{x}{\sqrt{2}}\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{+\infty } = \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\left( {\frac{\pi }{2} - \arctan \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}\right)$ ,

$$
{\int }_{\mathrm{e}}^{+\infty }\frac{1}{x\sqrt{\ln x + 2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  2\sqrt{\ln x + 2}\right\rbrack  }_{\mathrm{e}}^{+\infty } =  + \infty ,
$$

${\int }_{0}^{t}\sin x\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  -\cos x\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{t} = 1 - \cos t$ ,当 $t \rightarrow   + \infty$ 时极限不存在,

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{1}{x - 1}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\left\lbrack  \ln \left( 1 - x\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} =  - \infty .
$$

故选 (A).

8. $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  1}}\frac{\frac{2x}{1 + {x}^{2}}}{3{x}^{2}} = \frac{1}{3} = f\left( 1\right)  = a$ . 故选 (D).

 二、计算题

1. 联立方程 $y = \sqrt{x + 2}$ 和 $x - {3y} + 4 = 0$ 解得交点为(-1,1)和(2,2),因此所求面积为

$$
A = {\int }_{1}^{2}\left\lbrack  {{3y} - 4 - \left( {{y}^{2} - 2}\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}y = {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{3}{y}^{3} + \frac{3}{2}{y}^{2} - 2y\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{2} = \frac{1}{6}.
$$

2. 记 $u = u\left( x\right) ,v = v\left( x\right)$ ,则

$$
{\left( uv\right) }^{\left( n\right) } = u{v}^{\left( n\right) } + n{u}^{\prime }{v}^{\left( n - 1\right) } + \frac{n\left( {n - 1}\right) }{2}{u}^{\prime \prime }{v}^{\left( n - 2\right) } + \cdots  + {\mathrm{C}}_{n}^{k}{u}^{\left( k\right) }{v}^{\left( n - k\right) } + \cdots  + {u}^{\left( n\right) }v,
$$

${\left( x{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\right) }^{\left( {10}\right) } = x{\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\right) }^{\left( {10}\right) } + {10} \cdot  1 \cdot  {\left( {\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\right) }^{\left( 9\right) } = x \cdot  {2}^{10}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} + {10} \cdot  {2}^{9}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x} = {2}^{10}{\mathrm{e}}^{2x}\left( {x + 5}\right) .$

3. 令 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)  = \left( {{x}^{2} + {3x} - 4}\right) {\mathrm{e}}^{x} = 0$ 解得 ${x}_{1} =  - 4$ 和 ${x}_{2} = 1$ .

<!-- Media -->

<table><tr><td>$x$</td><td>$\left( {-\infty , - 4}\right)$</td><td>-4</td><td>(-4,1)</td><td>1</td><td>$\left( {1, + \infty }\right)$</td></tr><tr><td>${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$</td><td>+</td><td>0</td><td>-</td><td>0</td><td>+</td></tr><tr><td>函数 $f\left( x\right)$</td><td>单调增加</td><td>$x =  - 4$ 为极大值点</td><td>单调减少</td><td>$x = 1$ 为极小值点</td><td>单调增加</td></tr></table>

<!-- Media -->

因此, $\left( {-\infty , - 4\rbrack \text{和}\lbrack 1, + \infty }\right)$ 为单调增加区间, $\left\lbrack  {-4,1}\right\rbrack$ 为单调减少区间. 函数的极大值为 $f\left( {-4}\right)  = 7{\mathrm{e}}^{-4}$ ,极小值为 $f\left( 1\right)  =  - 3\mathrm{e}$ .

$$
\text{4.}{\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{\ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) }{{x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x = {\int }_{1}^{+\infty } - \ln \left( {1 + {x}^{2}}\right) \mathrm{d}\left( \frac{1}{x}\right)
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  -\frac{1}{x}\ln \left( 1 + {x}^{2}\right) \right\rbrack  }_{1}^{+\infty } + {\int }_{1}^{+\infty }\frac{2}{1 + {x}^{2}}\mathrm{\;d}x
$$

$$
= \ln 2 + {\left\lbrack  2\arctan x\right\rbrack  }_{1}^{+\infty } = \ln 2 + \frac{\pi }{2}.
$$

5. 特征方程为 ${r}^{2} + {2r} - 3 = 0$ ,根为 ${r}_{1} =  - 3$ 和 ${r}_{2} = 1$ ,因此所对应的齐次线性微分方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x}.
$$

设非齐次线性微分方程的特解为 ${y}^{ * } = a$ ,代入方程解得 $a =  - \frac{1}{3}$ ,因此原方程的通解为

$$
y = {C}_{1}{\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}} + {C}_{2}{\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \frac{1}{3}.
$$

由初值条件 ${\left. y\right| }_{x = 0} = \frac{2}{3},{\left. {y}^{\prime }\right| }_{x = 0} =  - 7$ 解得 ${C}_{1} = 2,{C}_{2} =  - 1$ ,因此所求解为

$$
y = 2{\mathrm{e}}^{-{3x}} - {\mathrm{e}}^{x} - \frac{1}{3}.
$$

三、联立方程 $x = {y}^{2} - 1$ 和 $x - {2y} - 2 = 0$ ,解得交点(0, - 1)和(8,3),因此所求水压力为

$$
F = {\int }_{-1}^{1}{\mu g}\left( {1 - y}\right) \left\lbrack  {{2y} + 2 - \left( {{y}^{2} - 1}\right) }\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}y = {\mu g}{\int }_{-1}^{1}\left( {{y}^{3} - 3{y}^{2} - y + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}y
$$

$$
= {2\mu g}{\int }_{0}^{1}\left( {-3{y}^{2} + 3}\right) \mathrm{d}y = {4\mu g}\left( \mathrm{\;N}\right) .
$$

四、令 $u = \sqrt{x}$ ,即 $x = {u}^{2}$ ,则

$$
{\int }_{0}^{1}\sqrt{x}\ln \left( {x + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}x = {\int }_{0}^{1}2{u}^{2}\ln \left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}u = \frac{2}{3}{\int }_{0}^{1}\ln \left( {{u}^{2} + 1}\right) \mathrm{d}{u}^{3}
$$

$$
= {\left\lbrack  \frac{2}{3}{u}^{3}\ln \left( {u}^{2} + 1\right) \right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} - \frac{4}{3}{\int }_{0}^{1}\frac{{u}^{4}}{{u}^{2} + 1}\mathrm{\;d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{3}\ln 2 - \frac{4}{3}{\int }_{0}^{1}\left( {{u}^{2} - 1 + \frac{1}{{u}^{2} + 1}}\right) \mathrm{d}u
$$

$$
= \frac{2}{3}\ln 2 - \frac{4}{3}{\left\lbrack  \frac{1}{3}{u}^{3} - u + \arctan u\right\rbrack  }_{0}^{1} = \frac{2}{3}\ln 2 + \frac{8}{9} - \frac{\pi }{3}\text{.}
$$

五、(1) $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)  = 1,\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  = a + b$ ,由可导必连续,故 $\mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}f\left( x\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ + }}}f\left( x\right)  =$ $f\left( 1\right)$ ,得 $a + b = 1$ ;

${f}^{\prime } - \left( 1\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}\frac{{x}^{2} - 1}{x - 1} = 2,{f}^{\prime } + \left( 1\right)  = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ - }}}\frac{{ax} + b - 1}{x - 1} = \mathop{\lim }\limits_{{x \rightarrow  {1}^{ + }}}\frac{{ax} - a}{x - 1} = a$ ,由于可导,故 ${f}_{ - }^{\prime }\left( 1\right)  = {f}_{ + }^{\prime }\left( 1\right)$ ,得 $a = 2,b =  - 1$ .

( 2 )由 ( 1 ) 得 $h = f\left( x\right)  = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {x}^{2}, & 0 \leq  x \leq  1, \\  {2x} - 1, & 1 < x \leq  2, \end{array}\right.$ 根据元素法可知 $\mathrm{d}V = \pi {x}^{2}\mathrm{\;d}h$ ,故

$$
{v}_{0} = \frac{\mathrm{d}V}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \pi {x}^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \left\{  {\begin{array}{ll} {\pi h}\frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\mathrm{\;d}t}, & 0 < x \leq  1, \\  \pi {\left( \frac{h + 1}{2}\right) }^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\mathrm{\;d}t}, & 1 < x < 2 \end{array} = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} {\pi h}\frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\mathrm{\;d}t}, & 0 < h \leq  1, \\  \pi {\left( \frac{h + 1}{2}\right) }^{2}\frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\mathrm{\;d}t}, & 1 < h < 3, \end{array}\right. }\right.
$$

即

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}h}{\mathrm{\;d}t} = \left\{  \begin{array}{ll} \frac{{v}_{0}}{\pi h}, & 0 < h \leq  1, \\  \frac{4{v}_{0}}{\pi {\left( h + 1\right) }^{2}}, & 1 < h < 3. \end{array}\right.
$$

六、设圆柱面的高为 $h$ ,底半径为 $r$ ,则容积为 $\pi {r}^{2}h + \frac{2}{3}\pi {r}^{3} = {14}$ ,解得 $h = \frac{14}{\pi {r}^{2}} - \frac{2}{3}r$ .

如果侧面单位面积的造价为 $k$ ,则顶部单位面积的造价为 ${3k}$ ,总造价为

$$
p = k \cdot  {2\pi rh} + {3k} \cdot  {2\pi }{r}^{2} = {2k\pi r}\left( {\frac{14}{\pi {r}^{2}} - \frac{2}{3}r}\right)  + {6k\pi }{r}^{2} = {2k}\left( {\frac{14}{r} + \frac{7}{3}\pi {r}^{2}}\right) ,
$$

令

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}p}{\mathrm{\;d}r} = {2k}\left( {-\frac{14}{{r}^{2}} + \frac{14}{3}{\pi r}}\right)  = \frac{28k\pi }{3{r}^{2}}\left( {{r}^{3} - \frac{3}{\pi }}\right)  = 0
$$

得惟一驻点 $r = \sqrt[3]{\frac{3}{\pi }}$ ,显然该点为极小值点,也是最小值点. 即底圆半径为 $\sqrt[3]{\frac{3}{\pi }}$ 时,该仓库的造价最省.

七、由条件 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  < 0$ 得 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 单调减少,因此满足拉格朗日中值定理 $f\left( x\right)  -$ $f\left( {x}_{0}\right)  = {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left( {x - {x}_{0}}\right)$ 的 $\xi$ 是惟一的,因此 $\xi$ 定义了 $\left( {{x}_{0}, + \infty }\right)$ 上的一个函数 $\xi  = \xi \left( x\right)$ .

由于 ${f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 单调减少,因此 $y = {f}^{\prime }\left( x\right)$ 存在反函数 $x = \varphi \left( y\right)$ ,从而

$$
\xi  = \varphi \left( \frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{x - {x}_{0}}\right) .
$$

又根据反函数的可导性结论可知,当 ${f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right)  \neq  0$ 时, $x = \varphi \left( y\right)$ 可导,且 ${\varphi }^{\prime }\left( y\right)  = \frac{1}{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( x\right) } <$

0 . 于是

$$
\frac{\mathrm{d}\xi }{\mathrm{d}x} = {\varphi }^{\prime }\left( \frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{x - {x}_{0}}\right) {\left\lbrack  \frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{x - {x}_{0}}\right\rbrack  }^{\prime },
$$

$$
{\left\lbrack  \frac{f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }{x - {x}_{0}}\right\rbrack  }^{\prime } = \frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \left( {x - {x}_{0}}\right)  - \left\lbrack  {f\left( x\right)  - f\left( {x}_{0}\right) }\right\rbrack  }{{\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{2}}
$$

$$
= \frac{{f}^{\prime }\left( x\right) \left( {x - {x}_{0}}\right)  - {f}^{\prime }\left( \xi \right) \left( {x - {x}_{0}}\right) }{{\left( x - {x}_{0}\right) }^{2}} = \frac{{f}^{\prime \prime }\left( \eta \right) \left( {x - \xi }\right) }{x - {x}_{0}} < 0\;\text{(其中}\eta  \in  \left( {\xi ,x}\right) \text{),}
$$

故 $\frac{\mathrm{d}\xi }{\mathrm{d}x} > 0$ ,即 $\xi$ 在 $\left( {{x}_{0}, + \infty }\right)$ 内单调增加. College Mathematics Guidance Series 大学数学学习辅导丛书
